// =====================================================
// MODULE 2 — MASTER RUNNER
// PURPOSE:
// Runs the full Stocks Overseer Advisor system in the
// correct order using the clean GoogleFinance structure.
// =====================================================

function runFullOverseerUpdate() {

  // OPTIMISATION — reset main conditional formatting and clear charts before rebuild.
  resetWorkbookConditionalFormattingQuiet();
  cleanupChartsBeforeRebuild();

  // =====================================================
  // OPTIMISED FULL RUNNER — v44
  // PURPOSE:
  // Runs the workbook in a cleaner order to reduce rework,
  // avoid stale dashboard references, and prevent destructive
  // UI refreshes from wiping advanced visual modules.
  // =====================================================

  // STEP 1 — Ensure required headers exist.
  addCleanGoogleFinanceColumns();
  ensureExpandedGoogleFinanceHeaders();

  // STEP 2 — Refresh GoogleFinance formulas and allow formulas to calculate.
  setupGoogleFinanceOnly();
  SpreadsheetApp.flush();

  // STEP 3 — Recalculate clean metrics and derived fields.
  recalculateCleanGoogleFinanceMetrics();
  fillRemainingGoogleFinanceDerivedInputFields();
  fillExistingAutomatableInputFields();

  // STEP 4 — Generate investment decision outputs.
  runCleanWatchlistSignalEngine();
  runCleanPortfolioAllocationEngine();

  // STEP 5 — Data quality, ticker suggestions, and logs.
  runTickerDataQualityCheckOptimised();
  runTickerFormatSuggestionEngine();
  updateErrorLogSheet();
  updateSystemLog();

  // STEP 6 — Refresh historical data before dashboard uses it.
  createHistoricalPriceSheet();
  refreshOptimizedHistorySummary();

  // STEP 7 — Build operational Dashboard in dependency order.
  createCleanDashboard();
  createDashboardKpiScorecards();
  reserveDashboardKpiSpace();
  refreshExecutiveSummaryBanner();
  createDashboardTop10DecisionView();
  refreshTop10MiniCharts();
  createOptimizedDashboardHistoricalSnapshot();
  addHistoricalSnapshotPerformanceNote();
  createDashboardTickerCountSummary();
  createDashboardNavigationStatusPanel();
  createUnsupportedTickerDashboard();
  createTickerSuggestionDashboard();
  createDashboardRiskHeatmap();
  addDashboardRiskHeatmapInsightNote();
  createDashboardSystemLogPanel();
  createDashboardErrorLogPanel();
  createDashboardUserZonePanel();
  createDashboardManualInputReminderPanel();
  createFundamentalImportDashboardPanel();
  createDashboardFundamentalValidationPanel();
  createDashboardBadgeLegendPanel();
  createDashboardRowHighlightLegendPanel();
  createDashboardAlertCentrePanel();

  // STEP 8 — Refresh supporting sheets and views.
  createUserInputGuideSheet();
  createVisualLegendSheet();
  createFundamentalImportSheet();
  refreshManagementView();
  refreshDecisionSupportSheets();
  refreshExecutiveCharts();
  refreshGainDividendCalculatorWithGuide();
  refreshCalculatorUiGraphics();
  refreshCalculatorAutoFillEnhancement();
  refreshCalculatorTickerSelectionAutoFillPatch();
  refreshCalculatorUserInputYellowHighlight();
  refreshAdvancedUiGraphicsPackage();
  refreshScenarioAlertsOnboardingPackage();

  // STEP 9 — Formatting and visual polish.
  formatInputSheet();
  formatDashboard();
  formatHistorySheet();
  applyColourIndicatorsAndConditionalFormatting();
  applyHistoricalSnapshotConditionalFormatting();
  applyDashboardStatusPanelFormatting();
  applyDashboardErrorLogPanelFormatting();
  applyUnsupportedTickerDashboardFormatting();
  applyTop10DecisionViewFormatting();
  applyDashboardThemeAndSectionStyling();
  refreshDashboardSidebarColourFix();
  applyDashboardKpiScorecardFormatting();
  applyDashboardRiskHeatmapFormatting();
  applyRecommendationBadgeStyling();
  applyConditionalRowHighlighting();
  applyVisualInputUpgrade();
  applyWorkbookLayoutOptimisation();
  refreshPrintLayout();
  refreshUiEnhancementModules();

  // STEP 10 — Final chart refresh and quiet master polish.
  createImprovedDashboardCharts();
  runMasterUiPolishCleanupQuiet();
  refreshOptimisationSupportPackage();
  refreshStagedRebuildSupport();
  createCalculatorOnboardingAuditSheet();
  refreshOptimisedOnboardingWizard();

  SpreadsheetApp.getUi()
    .alert("Optimised full Overseer update completed successfully.");
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 3 — GOOGLEFINANCE FORMULA ENGINE
// PURPOSE:
// Uses ticker values from the Input sheet to fill available
// GoogleFinance market data fields.
// =====================================================

function setupGoogleFinanceOnly() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sh = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);

  if (!sh) throw new Error("Sheet not found: " + SHEET_NAME);

  const headers = getHeaders(sh);
  const tickerCol = getCol(headers, "Ticker");

  for (let r = 2; r <= sh.getLastRow(); r++) {
    const ticker = sh.getRange(r, tickerCol).getValue();
    if (!ticker) continue;

    const tickerCell = sh.getRange(r, tickerCol).getA1Notation();

    // =====================================================
    // COMPANY NAME
    // GOOGLEFINANCE supported
    // =====================================================

    setFormula(
      sh,
      headers,
      r,
      "Company",
      `=IFERROR(IF(${tickerCell}="","",GOOGLEFINANCE(${tickerCell},"name")),"")`
    );

    // =====================================================
    // CURRENCY
    // GOOGLEFINANCE supported
    // =====================================================

    setFormula(
      sh,
      headers,
      r,
      "Currency",
      `=IFERROR(IF(${tickerCell}="","",GOOGLEFINANCE(${tickerCell},"currency")),"")`
    );

    // GoogleFinance-supported market data.
    setFormula(sh, headers, r, "Share Price", `=IFERROR(IF(${tickerCell}="","",GOOGLEFINANCE(${tickerCell},"price")),"")`);
    setFormula(sh, headers, r, "Market Cap", `=IFERROR(IF(${tickerCell}="","",GOOGLEFINANCE(${tickerCell},"marketcap")),"")`);
    setFormula(sh, headers, r, "PE Ratio", `=IFERROR(IF(${tickerCell}="","",GOOGLEFINANCE(${tickerCell},"pe")),"")`);
    setFormula(sh, headers, r, "EPS", `=IFERROR(IF(${tickerCell}="","",GOOGLEFINANCE(${tickerCell},"eps")),"")`);
    setFormula(sh, headers, r, "Beta", `=IFERROR(IF(${tickerCell}="","",GOOGLEFINANCE(${tickerCell},"beta")),"")`);
    setFormula(sh, headers, r, "52 Week High", `=IFERROR(IF(${tickerCell}="","",GOOGLEFINANCE(${tickerCell},"high52")),"")`);
    setFormula(sh, headers, r, "52 Week Low", `=IFERROR(IF(${tickerCell}="","",GOOGLEFINANCE(${tickerCell},"low52")),"")`);

    // =====================================================
    // ADDITIONAL GOOGLEFINANCE-SUPPORTED MARKET DATA
    // =====================================================

    setFormula(sh, headers, r, "Open Price", `=IFERROR(IF(${tickerCell}="","",GOOGLEFINANCE(${tickerCell},"priceopen")),"")`);

    setFormula(sh, headers, r, "Day High", `=IFERROR(IF(${tickerCell}="","",GOOGLEFINANCE(${tickerCell},"high")),"")`);

    setFormula(sh, headers, r, "Day Low", `=IFERROR(IF(${tickerCell}="","",GOOGLEFINANCE(${tickerCell},"low")),"")`);

    setFormula(sh, headers, r, "Trade Time", `=IFERROR(IF(${tickerCell}="","",GOOGLEFINANCE(${tickerCell},"tradetime")),"")`);

    setFormula(sh, headers, r, "Data Delay", `=IFERROR(IF(${tickerCell}="","",GOOGLEFINANCE(${tickerCell},"datadelay")),"")`);

    setFormula(sh, headers, r, "Average Volume", `=IFERROR(IF(${tickerCell}="","",GOOGLEFINANCE(${tickerCell},"volumeavg")),"")`);

    setValue(sh, headers, r, "Data Source", "GOOGLEFINANCE only");
    setValue(sh, headers, r, "Last Updated", new Date());
    setValue(sh, headers, r, "Remarks", "GoogleFinance market data formula refreshed.");
  }
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 4 — CLEAN COLUMN ENGINE
// PURPOSE:
// Adds clean GoogleFinance-derived metric columns.
// These columns avoid misleading use of legacy headers.
// =====================================================

function addCleanGoogleFinanceColumns() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");

  const newHeaders = [
    "Implied Shares Outstanding",
    "Earnings Yield %",
    "Upside to 52W High %",
    "Downside to 52W Low %",
    "52W Price Position %",
    "GoogleFinance Score",
    "Beta Risk Group",
    "Momentum Signal"
  ];

  let headers = getHeaders(input);

  newHeaders.forEach(header => {
    if (!headers.includes(header)) {
      const nextCol = input.getLastColumn() + 1;
      input.getRange(1, nextCol).setValue(header);
      headers = getHeaders(input);
    }
  });

  input.getRange(1, 1, 1, input.getLastColumn()).setFontWeight("bold");
  input.autoResizeColumns(1, input.getLastColumn());
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 5 — CLEAN GOOGLEFINANCE METRIC CALCULATION
// PURPOSE:
// Calculates metrics that can be derived from ticker-only
// GoogleFinance data.
// =====================================================

function recalculateCleanGoogleFinanceMetrics() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");

  const data = input.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];

  // Source columns.
  const tickerCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker");
  const priceCol = colIndex(headers, "Share Price");
  const marketCapCol = colIndex(headers, "Market Cap");
  const epsCol = colIndex(headers, "EPS");
  const peCol = colIndex(headers, "PE Ratio");
  const betaCol = colIndex(headers, "Beta");
  const high52Col = colIndex(headers, "52 Week High");
  const low52Col = colIndex(headers, "52 Week Low");

  // Clean output columns.
  const impliedSharesCol = colIndex(headers, "Implied Shares Outstanding");
  const earningsYieldCol = colIndex(headers, "Earnings Yield %");
  const upside52Col = colIndex(headers, "Upside to 52W High %");
  const downside52Col = colIndex(headers, "Downside to 52W Low %");
  const position52Col = colIndex(headers, "52W Price Position %");
  const scoreCol = colIndex(headers, "GoogleFinance Score");
  const betaRiskCol = colIndex(headers, "Beta Risk Group");
  const momentumCol = colIndex(headers, "Momentum Signal");

  // Optional compatibility columns from the original sheet.
  const sharesCol = colIndex(headers, "Shares Outstanding");
  const legacyScoreCol = colIndex(headers, "Overall Investment Score");
  const scenarioCol = colIndex(headers, "Scenario");
  const volatilityCol = colIndex(headers, "Volatility %");

  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {
    const row = data[r];
    if (!row[tickerCol]) continue;

    const price = num(row[priceCol]);
    const marketCap = num(row[marketCapCol]);
    const eps = num(row[epsCol]);
    const pe = num(row[peCol]);
    const beta = num(row[betaCol]);
    const high52 = num(row[high52Col]);
    const low52 = num(row[low52Col]);

    const impliedShares = safeDiv(marketCap, price);
    const earningsYield = safeDiv(eps, price);
    const upsideToHigh = safeDiv(high52 - price, price);
    const downsideToLow = safeDiv(price - low52, price);
    const pricePosition = safeDiv(price - low52, high52 - low52);

    const betaRiskGroup = classifyBetaRisk(beta);
    const momentumSignal = classifyMomentum(pricePosition);
    const gfScore = scoreGoogleFinance(pe, beta, pricePosition, earningsYield);

    const rowNumber = r + 1;

    // Clean outputs.
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, impliedSharesCol, impliedShares);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, earningsYieldCol, earningsYield);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, upside52Col, upsideToHigh);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, downside52Col, downsideToLow);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, position52Col, pricePosition);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, scoreCol, gfScore);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, betaRiskCol, betaRiskGroup);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, momentumCol, momentumSignal);

    // Compatibility outputs.
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, sharesCol, impliedShares);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, legacyScoreCol, gfScore);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, scenarioCol, momentumSignal + " / " + betaRiskGroup);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, volatilityCol, beta);

    setValue(input, headers, rowNumber, "Data Source", "GOOGLEFINANCE + Clean Derived Metrics");
    setValue(input, headers, rowNumber, "Last Updated", new Date());
    setValue(input, headers, rowNumber, "Remarks", "Clean metrics calculated from GoogleFinance market data.");
  }

  formatCleanMetricColumns(input);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 6 — CLEAN WATCHLIST SIGNAL ENGINE
// PURPOSE:
// Generates Final Recommendation and Watchlist Status
// using clean GoogleFinance-derived columns.
// =====================================================

function runCleanWatchlistSignalEngine() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");

  const data = input.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];

  const tickerCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker");
  const peCol = colIndex(headers, "PE Ratio");
  const scoreCol = colIndex(headers, "GoogleFinance Score");
  const earningsYieldCol = colIndex(headers, "Earnings Yield %");
  const upsideCol = colIndex(headers, "Upside to 52W High %");
  const betaRiskCol = colIndex(headers, "Beta Risk Group");
  const momentumCol = colIndex(headers, "Momentum Signal");

  const recommendationCol = colIndex(headers, "Final Recommendation");
  const watchlistCol = colIndex(headers, "Watchlist Status");
  const valuationScoreCol = colIndex(headers, "Valuation Score");
  const financialStrengthScoreCol = colIndex(headers, "Financial Strength Score");
  const remarksCol = colIndex(headers, "Remarks");

  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {
    const row = data[r];
    if (!row[tickerCol]) continue;

    const pe = num(row[peCol]);
    const score = num(row[scoreCol]);
    const earningsYield = num(row[earningsYieldCol]);
    const upside = num(row[upsideCol]);
    const betaRisk = row[betaRiskCol];
    const momentum = row[momentumCol];

    let recommendation = "HOLD / MONITOR";
    let watchlist = "WATCHLIST";
    let remark = "Monitor until stronger valuation, risk, or momentum signal appears.";

    const valuationScore = calculateValuationProxyScore(pe, earningsYield);
    const financialStrengthScore = calculateFinancialStrengthProxyScore(betaRisk, score);

    if (
      score >= 75 &&
      valuationScore >= 70 &&
      betaRisk !== "VERY HIGH RISK" &&
      upside >= 0.10
    ) {
      recommendation = "BUY CANDIDATE";
      watchlist = "HIGH PRIORITY";
      remark = "Strong GoogleFinance score, acceptable valuation proxy, and upside to 52W high.";
    } else if (
      score >= 60 &&
      valuationScore >= 50 &&
      betaRisk !== "VERY HIGH RISK"
    ) {
      recommendation = "ACCUMULATE / STUDY";
      watchlist = "MEDIUM PRIORITY";
      remark = "Moderate clean score; suitable for further study before entry.";
    } else if (
      betaRisk === "VERY HIGH RISK" ||
      score < 45
    ) {
      recommendation = "AVOID / HIGH RISK";
      watchlist = "LOW PRIORITY";
      remark = "High risk or weak GoogleFinance-derived score.";
    } else if (
      momentum === "NEAR 52W LOW" &&
      betaRisk !== "VERY HIGH RISK"
    ) {
      recommendation = "VALUE WATCH";
      watchlist = "WATCHLIST";
      remark = "Near 52W low; possible value watch but requires fundamental confirmation.";
    }

    const rowNumber = r + 1;
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, recommendationCol, recommendation);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, watchlistCol, watchlist);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, valuationScoreCol, valuationScore);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, financialStrengthScoreCol, financialStrengthScore);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, remarksCol, remark);
  }
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 7 — CLEAN PORTFOLIO ALLOCATION ENGINE
// PURPOSE:
// Suggests allocation using GoogleFinance Score,
// beta risk, momentum, and recommendation.
// =====================================================

function runCleanPortfolioAllocationEngine() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");

  const data = input.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];

  const tickerCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker");
  const scoreCol = colIndex(headers, "GoogleFinance Score");
  const betaRiskCol = colIndex(headers, "Beta Risk Group");
  const momentumCol = colIndex(headers, "Momentum Signal");
  const recommendationCol = colIndex(headers, "Final Recommendation");

  const allocationCol = colIndex(headers, "Portfolio Allocation %");
  const remarksCol = colIndex(headers, "Remarks");

  const stocks = [];

  // Clear prior allocations first.
  if (allocationCol >= 0) {
    input.getRange(2, allocationCol + 1, Math.max(input.getLastRow() - 1, 1), 1).clearContent();
  }

  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {
    const row = data[r];
    if (!row[tickerCol]) continue;

    const ticker = row[tickerCol];
    const score = num(row[scoreCol]);
    const betaRisk = row[betaRiskCol];
    const momentum = row[momentumCol];
    const recommendation = row[recommendationCol];

    const isEligible =
      recommendation === "BUY CANDIDATE" ||
      recommendation === "ACCUMULATE / STUDY" ||
      recommendation === "HOLD / MONITOR" ||
      recommendation === "VALUE WATCH";

    if (!isEligible) continue;

    const allocationScore =
      score *
      riskMultiplier(betaRisk) *
      recommendationMultiplier(recommendation) *
      momentumMultiplier(momentum);

    stocks.push({
      rowNumber: r + 1,
      ticker,
      allocationScore
    });
  }

  if (stocks.length === 0) return;

  const totalScore = stocks.reduce((sum, s) => sum + s.allocationScore, 0);
  if (!totalScore) return;

  // First pass with a 15% cap.
  let capped = [];
  let uncapped = [];

  stocks.forEach(s => {
    const rawAllocation = s.allocationScore / totalScore;

    if (rawAllocation > 0.15) {
      capped.push({ ...s, allocation: 0.15 });
    } else {
      uncapped.push({ ...s, rawAllocation });
    }
  });

  // Redistribute remaining allocation among uncapped stocks.
  const cappedTotal = capped.reduce((sum, s) => sum + s.allocation, 0);
  const remainingAllocation = Math.max(1 - cappedTotal, 0);
  const uncappedTotalScore = uncapped.reduce((sum, s) => sum + s.allocationScore, 0);

  const finalStocks = [
    ...capped,
    ...uncapped.map(s => ({
      ...s,
      allocation: uncappedTotalScore > 0
        ? (s.allocationScore / uncappedTotalScore) * remainingAllocation
        : 0
    }))
  ];

  finalStocks.forEach(s => {
    setCellByIndex(input, s.rowNumber, allocationCol, s.allocation);
    setCellByIndex(
      input,
      s.rowNumber,
      remarksCol,
      "Clean allocation based on GoogleFinance score, beta risk, momentum, and recommendation."
    );
  });

  if (allocationCol >= 0) {
    input.getRange(2, allocationCol + 1, input.getLastRow() - 1, 1)
      .setNumberFormat("0.00%");
  }
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 8 — CLEAN DASHBOARD
// PURPOSE:
// Builds the complete dashboard using clean columns.
// This replaces older scattered dashboard sections.
// =====================================================

function createCleanDashboard() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);
  let dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");
  if (!dash) dash = ss.insertSheet(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  // Clear full Dashboard so old fixed-position sections do not remain.
  dash.clear();

  const data = input.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];
  const stocks = getCleanStockObjects(data, headers);

  dash.getRange("A1").setValue("Stocks Overseer Advisor Dashboard");

  if (stocks.length === 0) {
    dash.getRange("A3").setValue("No valid stock data found.");
    return;
  }

  // =====================================================
  // DYNAMIC DASHBOARD LAYOUT
  // PURPOSE:
  // Prevents overlap when ticker count increases.
  // =====================================================

  let row = 8; // Start below Module 53 KPI scorecards and Module 60 executive banner

  createSummaryCards_(dash, stocks, row);
  row += 6;

  // Reserve space for Module 45 Top 10 Decision View near the top.
  row += 18; // Reserved space for Module 45 Top 10 Decision View

  row += 2;
  row = createRankingTable_(dash, stocks, row);

  row += 3;
  row = createWatchlistTable_(dash, stocks, row);

  row += 3;
  row = createPortfolioTable_(dash, stocks, row);

  row += 3;
  row = createConcentrationCheck_(dash, stocks, row);

  row += 2;
  row = createRiskGrouping_(dash, stocks, row);

  // Store next available dashboard row for other modules.
  PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties()
    .setProperty("DASHBOARD_NEXT_ROW", String(row + 3));
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 8A — DASHBOARD SUMMARY CARDS
// PURPOSE:
// Creates high-level decision cards.
// =====================================================

function createSummaryCards_(dash, stocks, startRow) {
  const topScore = [...stocks].sort((a, b) => b.score - a.score)[0];
  const highestEarningsYield = [...stocks].sort((a, b) => b.earningsYield - a.earningsYield)[0];
  const highestUpside = [...stocks].sort((a, b) => b.upside - a.upside)[0];
  const strongestMomentum = [...stocks].sort((a, b) => b.position - a.position)[0];
  const near52Low = [...stocks].sort((a, b) => a.position - b.position)[0];
  const buyCandidate = stocks.find(s => s.recommendation === "BUY CANDIDATE");

  const cards = [
    ["Top Score", topScore.ticker, topScore.score, "GoogleFinance Score"],
    ["Highest Earnings Yield", highestEarningsYield.ticker, highestEarningsYield.earningsYield, "Earnings Yield"],
    ["Highest 52W Upside", highestUpside.ticker, highestUpside.upside, "Upside to 52W High"],
    ["Strongest Momentum", strongestMomentum.ticker, strongestMomentum.position, "52W Position"],
    ["Nearest 52W Low", near52Low.ticker, near52Low.position, "52W Position"],
    ["Buy Candidate", buyCandidate ? buyCandidate.ticker : "N/A", buyCandidate ? buyCandidate.score : "N/A", "Score"]
  ];

  let col = 1;
  cards.forEach(card => {
    dash.getRange(startRow, col).setValue(card[0]);
    dash.getRange(startRow + 1, col).setValue(card[1]);
    dash.getRange(startRow + 2, col).setValue(card[2]);
    dash.getRange(startRow + 3, col).setValue(card[3]);
    col += 2;
  });

  dash.getRange(startRow, 1, 1, 12).setFontWeight("bold");
  dash.getRange(startRow + 2, 3, 1, 3).setNumberFormat("0.00%");
  dash.getRange(startRow + 2, 7, 1, 3).setNumberFormat("0.00%");
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 8B — CLEAN RANKING TABLE
// PURPOSE:
// Creates ranking by GoogleFinance Score.
// =====================================================

function createRankingTable_(dash, stocks, startRow) {
  const table = [
    [
      "Rank",
      "Ticker",
      "Share Price",
      "PE Ratio",
      "Beta",
      "Earnings Yield %",
      "Upside to 52W High %",
      "52W Position %",
      "Beta Risk Group",
      "Momentum Signal",
      "GoogleFinance Score"
    ]
  ];

  const sorted = [...stocks].sort((a, b) => b.score - a.score);

  sorted.forEach((s, i) => {
    table.push([
      i + 1,
      s.ticker,
      s.price,
      s.pe,
      s.beta,
      s.earningsYield,
      s.upside,
      s.position,
      s.betaRisk,
      s.momentum,
      s.score
    ]);
  });

  dash.getRange(startRow, 1).setValue("Clean GoogleFinance Ranking Dashboard");
  dash.getRange(startRow + 2, 1, table.length, table[0].length).setValues(table);
  dash.getRange(startRow + 2, 1, 1, table[0].length).setFontWeight("bold");
  dash.getRange(startRow + 3, 6, Math.max(table.length - 1, 1), 3).setNumberFormat("0.00%");

  PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties()
    .setProperty("DASHBOARD_RANKING_START", String(startRow + 3));

  return startRow + 2 + table.length;
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 8C — CLEAN WATCHLIST TABLE
// PURPOSE:
// Creates recommendation and watchlist table.
// =====================================================

function createWatchlistTable_(dash, stocks, startRow) {
  const table = [
    [
      "Ticker",
      "Share Price",
      "PE Ratio",
      "GoogleFinance Score",
      "Earnings Yield %",
      "Upside to 52W High %",
      "Beta Risk Group",
      "Momentum Signal",
      "Watchlist Status",
      "Final Recommendation",
      "Remarks"
    ]
  ];

  [...stocks].sort((a, b) => b.score - a.score).forEach(s => {
    table.push([
      s.ticker,
      s.price,
      s.pe,
      s.score,
      s.earningsYield,
      s.upside,
      s.betaRisk,
      s.momentum,
      s.watchlist,
      s.recommendation,
      s.remarks
    ]);
  });

  dash.getRange(startRow, 1).setValue("Clean Watchlist Dashboard Table");
  dash.getRange(startRow + 2, 1, table.length, table[0].length).setValues(table);
  dash.getRange(startRow + 2, 1, 1, table[0].length).setFontWeight("bold");
  dash.getRange(startRow + 3, 5, Math.max(table.length - 1, 1), 2).setNumberFormat("0.00%");

  PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties()
    .setProperty("DASHBOARD_WATCHLIST_START", String(startRow + 3));

  return startRow + 2 + table.length;
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 8D — CLEAN PORTFOLIO TABLE
// PURPOSE:
// Creates portfolio allocation dashboard table.
// =====================================================

function createPortfolioTable_(dash, stocks, startRow) {
  const portfolioStocks = stocks
    .filter(s => s.allocation > 0)
    .sort((a, b) => b.allocation - a.allocation);

  const table = [
    [
      "Ticker",
      "Share Price",
      "GoogleFinance Score",
      "Beta Risk Group",
      "Momentum Signal",
      "Final Recommendation",
      "Suggested Allocation %"
    ]
  ];

  portfolioStocks.forEach(s => {
    table.push([
      s.ticker,
      s.price,
      s.score,
      s.betaRisk,
      s.momentum,
      s.recommendation,
      s.allocation
    ]);
  });

  dash.getRange(startRow, 1).setValue("Clean Portfolio Allocation Dashboard");
  dash.getRange(startRow + 2, 1, table.length, table[0].length).setValues(table);
  dash.getRange(startRow + 2, 1, 1, table[0].length).setFontWeight("bold");
  dash.getRange(startRow + 3, 7, Math.max(table.length - 1, 1), 1).setNumberFormat("0.00%");

  PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties()
    .setProperty("DASHBOARD_PORTFOLIO_START", String(startRow + 3));

  return startRow + 2 + table.length;
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 8E — PORTFOLIO CONCENTRATION CHECK
// PURPOSE:
// Checks top 1, top 3, and top 5 allocation concentration.
// =====================================================

function createConcentrationCheck_(dash, stocks, startRow) {
  const allocations = stocks
    .filter(s => s.allocation > 0)
    .sort((a, b) => b.allocation - a.allocation);

  const totalAllocation = allocations.reduce((sum, s) => sum + s.allocation, 0);
  const top1 = allocations[0] ? allocations[0].allocation : 0;
  const top3 = allocations.slice(0, 3).reduce((sum, s) => sum + s.allocation, 0);
  const top5 = allocations.slice(0, 5).reduce((sum, s) => sum + s.allocation, 0);

  let concentrationRisk = "BALANCED";

  if (top1 > 0.20 || top3 > 0.50) {
    concentrationRisk = "HIGH CONCENTRATION";
  } else if (top1 > 0.15 || top3 > 0.40) {
    concentrationRisk = "MODERATE CONCENTRATION";
  }

  const table = [
    ["Metric", "Value"],
    ["Total Allocation", totalAllocation],
    ["Top 1 Weight", top1],
    ["Top 3 Weight", top3],
    ["Top 5 Weight", top5],
    ["Risk Level", concentrationRisk]
  ];

  dash.getRange(startRow, 1).setValue("Portfolio Concentration Check");
  dash.getRange(startRow + 2, 1, table.length, table[0].length).setValues(table);
  dash.getRange(startRow + 2, 1, 1, table[0].length).setFontWeight("bold");
  dash.getRange(startRow + 3, 2, 4, 1).setNumberFormat("0.00%");

  return startRow + 2 + table.length;
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 8F — RISK GROUPING DASHBOARD
// PURPOSE:
// Groups allocation by beta risk group.
// =====================================================

function createRiskGrouping_(dash, stocks, startRow) {
  const groups = {
    "LOW RISK": { count: 0, allocation: 0 },
    "MODERATE RISK": { count: 0, allocation: 0 },
    "HIGH RISK": { count: 0, allocation: 0 },
    "VERY HIGH RISK": { count: 0, allocation: 0 },
    "NO BETA DATA": { count: 0, allocation: 0 }
  };

  stocks.forEach(s => {
    const group = groups[s.betaRisk] ? s.betaRisk : "NO BETA DATA";
    groups[group].count += 1;
    groups[group].allocation += s.allocation;
  });

  const table = [["Risk Group", "Stock Count", "Total Allocation %"]];

  Object.keys(groups).forEach(group => {
    table.push([group, groups[group].count, groups[group].allocation]);
  });

  dash.getRange(startRow, 1).setValue("Risk Grouping Dashboard");
  dash.getRange(startRow + 2, 1, table.length, table[0].length).setValues(table);
  dash.getRange(startRow + 2, 1, 1, table[0].length).setFontWeight("bold");
  dash.getRange(startRow + 3, 3, table.length - 1, 1).setNumberFormat("0.00%");

  PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties()
    .setProperty("DASHBOARD_RISK_START", String(startRow + 3));

  return startRow + 2 + table.length;
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 33 — FILL REMAINING GOOGLEFINANCE-DERIVED INPUT FIELDS
// PURPOSE:
// Fills remaining Input sheet fields that can be reasonably
// calculated from existing GOOGLEFINANCE outputs and clean
// derived metrics.
// IMPORTANT:
// This does NOT fill true financial statement fields such as
// Revenue, EBITDA, Debt, Cash Flow, ROIC, etc.
// =====================================================

function fillRemainingGoogleFinanceDerivedInputFields() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) {
    throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");
  }

  const data = input.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];

  // Source columns
  const tickerCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker");
  const priceCol = colIndex(headers, "Share Price");
  const marketCapCol = colIndex(headers, "Market Cap");
  const epsCol = colIndex(headers, "EPS");
  const peCol = colIndex(headers, "PE Ratio");
  const betaCol = colIndex(headers, "Beta");
  const high52Col = colIndex(headers, "52 Week High");
  const low52Col = colIndex(headers, "52 Week Low");
  const gfScoreCol = colIndex(headers, "GoogleFinance Score");
  const earningsYieldCol = colIndex(headers, "Earnings Yield %");
  const upsideCol = colIndex(headers, "Upside to 52W High %");
  const downsideCol = colIndex(headers, "Downside to 52W Low %");
  const positionCol = colIndex(headers, "52W Price Position %");
  const betaRiskCol = colIndex(headers, "Beta Risk Group");
  const momentumCol = colIndex(headers, "Momentum Signal");

  // Output / compatibility columns
  const sharesCol = colIndex(headers, "Shares Outstanding");
  const impliedSharesCol = colIndex(headers, "Implied Shares Outstanding");
  const valuationScoreCol = colIndex(headers, "Valuation Score");
  const financialStrengthScoreCol = colIndex(headers, "Financial Strength Score");
  const overallScoreCol = colIndex(headers, "Overall Investment Score");
  const scenarioCol = colIndex(headers, "Scenario");
  const volatilityCol = colIndex(headers, "Volatility %");
  const marginSafetyCol = colIndex(headers, "Margin of Safety %");
  const expectedCagrCol = colIndex(headers, "Expected 10Y CAGR %");
  const maxDrawdownCol = colIndex(headers, "Max Drawdown %");
  const watchlistCol = colIndex(headers, "Watchlist Status");
  const recommendationCol = colIndex(headers, "Final Recommendation");
  const remarksCol = colIndex(headers, "Remarks");

  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {

    const row = data[r];

    if (!row[tickerCol]) continue;

    const rowNumber = r + 1;

    const price = num(row[priceCol]);
    const marketCap = num(row[marketCapCol]);
    const eps = num(row[epsCol]);
    const pe = num(row[peCol]);
    const beta = num(row[betaCol]);
    const high52 = num(row[high52Col]);
    const low52 = num(row[low52Col]);

    let gfScore = num(row[gfScoreCol]);
    let earningsYield = num(row[earningsYieldCol]);
    let upside = num(row[upsideCol]);
    let downside = num(row[downsideCol]);
    let position = num(row[positionCol]);
    let betaRisk = row[betaRiskCol];
    let momentum = row[momentumCol];

    // Recalculate if clean columns are empty
    const impliedShares = safeDiv(marketCap, price);

    if (!earningsYield) {
      earningsYield = safeDiv(eps, price);
    }

    if (!upside) {
      upside = safeDiv(high52 - price, price);
    }

    if (!downside) {
      downside = safeDiv(price - low52, price);
    }

    if (!position) {
      position = safeDiv(price - low52, high52 - low52);
    }

    if (!betaRisk) {
      betaRisk = classifyBetaRisk(beta);
    }

    if (!momentum) {
      momentum = classifyMomentum(position);
    }

    if (!gfScore) {
      gfScore = scoreGoogleFinance(pe, beta, position, earningsYield);
    }

    const valuationScore = calculateValuationProxyScore(pe, earningsYield);
    const financialStrengthScore = calculateFinancialStrengthProxyScore(betaRisk, gfScore);

    // Fill share count fields
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, sharesCol, impliedShares);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, impliedSharesCol, impliedShares);

    // Fill clean derived values if missing or needing refresh
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, earningsYieldCol, earningsYield);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, upsideCol, upside);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, downsideCol, downside);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, positionCol, position);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, betaRiskCol, betaRisk);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, momentumCol, momentum);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, gfScoreCol, gfScore);

    // Fill proxy scoring fields
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, valuationScoreCol, valuationScore);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, financialStrengthScoreCol, financialStrengthScore);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, overallScoreCol, gfScore);

    // Fill compatibility/proxy columns from original model
    // Note: These are proxies, not true institutional metrics.
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, scenarioCol, momentum + " / " + betaRisk);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, volatilityCol, beta);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, marginSafetyCol, upside);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, expectedCagrCol, earningsYield);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, maxDrawdownCol, -downside);

    // Fill watchlist and recommendation only if blank
    if (watchlistCol >= 0 && !row[watchlistCol]) {
      setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, watchlistCol, "WATCHLIST");
    }

    if (recommendationCol >= 0 && !row[recommendationCol]) {
      setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, recommendationCol, "HOLD / MONITOR");
    }

    if (remarksCol >= 0) {
      setCellByIndex(
        input,
        rowNumber,
        remarksCol,
        "Remaining GoogleFinance-derived fields filled. True fundamentals remain blank."
      );
    }
  }

  formatRemainingGoogleFinanceDerivedFields(input);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 33A — FORMAT REMAINING GOOGLEFINANCE-DERIVED FIELDS
// PURPOSE:
// Applies number and percentage formatting to Module 33 outputs.
// =====================================================

function formatRemainingGoogleFinanceDerivedFields(input) {

  const headers = getHeaders(input);
  const lastRow = Math.max(input.getLastRow() - 1, 1);

  const percentageHeaders = [
    "Earnings Yield %",
    "Upside to 52W High %",
    "Downside to 52W Low %",
    "52W Price Position %",
    "Margin of Safety %",
    "Expected 10Y CAGR %",
    "Max Drawdown %",
    "Volatility %"
  ];

  percentageHeaders.forEach(header => {
    const c = colIndex(headers, header);
    if (c >= 0) {
      input.getRange(2, c + 1, lastRow, 1).setNumberFormat("0.00%");
    }
  });

  const numberHeaders = [
    "Shares Outstanding",
    "Implied Shares Outstanding",
    "GoogleFinance Score",
    "Overall Investment Score",
    "Valuation Score",
    "Financial Strength Score"
  ];

  numberHeaders.forEach(header => {
    const c = colIndex(headers, header);
    if (c >= 0) {
      input.getRange(2, c + 1, lastRow, 1).setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");
    }
  });

  input.autoResizeColumns(1, input.getLastColumn());
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 34 — EXISTING FIELD AUTO-CALCULATION ENGINE
// PURPOSE:
// Fill existing Input sheet columns that can be calculated
// from current GoogleFinance outputs and clean derived metrics.
// This module does NOT fabricate true fundamentals.
// =====================================================

function fillExistingAutomatableInputFields() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) {
    throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");
  }

  const data = input.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];

  // =====================================================
  // SOURCE COLUMNS
  // =====================================================

  const tickerCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker");
  const priceCol = colIndex(headers, "Share Price");
  const marketCapCol = colIndex(headers, "Market Cap");
  const epsCol = colIndex(headers, "EPS");
  const peCol = colIndex(headers, "PE Ratio");
  const betaCol = colIndex(headers, "Beta");
  const high52Col = colIndex(headers, "52 Week High");
  const low52Col = colIndex(headers, "52 Week Low");
  const gfScoreCol = colIndex(headers, "GoogleFinance Score");
  const earningsYieldCol = colIndex(headers, "Earnings Yield %");
  const upsideCol = colIndex(headers, "Upside to 52W High %");
  const downsideCol = colIndex(headers, "Downside to 52W Low %");
  const positionCol = colIndex(headers, "52W Price Position %");
  const betaRiskCol = colIndex(headers, "Beta Risk Group");
  const momentumCol = colIndex(headers, "Momentum Signal");

  // =====================================================
  // EXISTING OUTPUT COLUMNS
  // =====================================================

  const sharesCol = colIndex(headers, "Shares Outstanding");
  const impliedSharesCol = colIndex(headers, "Implied Shares Outstanding");
  const valuationScoreCol = colIndex(headers, "Valuation Score");
  const financialStrengthScoreCol = colIndex(headers, "Financial Strength Score");
  const overallScoreCol = colIndex(headers, "Overall Investment Score");
  const managementScoreCol = colIndex(headers, "Management Score");
  const moatScoreCol = colIndex(headers, "Moat Score");
  const scenarioCol = colIndex(headers, "Scenario");
  const volatilityCol = colIndex(headers, "Volatility %");
  const marginSafetyCol = colIndex(headers, "Margin of Safety %");
  const expectedCagrCol = colIndex(headers, "Expected 10Y CAGR %");
  const maxDrawdownCol = colIndex(headers, "Max Drawdown %");
  const buyTargetCol = colIndex(headers, "Buy Target Price");
  const sellTargetCol = colIndex(headers, "Sell Target Price");
  const watchlistCol = colIndex(headers, "Watchlist Status");
  const recommendationCol = colIndex(headers, "Final Recommendation");
  const remarksCol = colIndex(headers, "Remarks");

  // Conditionally calculated fields if supporting existing data is available
  const bookValuePerShareCol = colIndex(headers, "Book Value Per Share");
  const pbRatioCol = colIndex(headers, "PB Ratio");
  const dividendPerShareCol = colIndex(headers, "Dividend Per Share");
  const dividendYieldCol = colIndex(headers, "Dividend Yield %");
  const payoutRatioCol = colIndex(headers, "Payout Ratio %");
  const retentionRatioCol = colIndex(headers, "Retention Ratio %");
  const totalDebtCol = colIndex(headers, "Total Debt");
  const cashCol = colIndex(headers, "Cash & Equivalents");
  const netDebtCol = colIndex(headers, "Net Debt");
  const ebitdaCol = colIndex(headers, "EBITDA");
  const netDebtEbitdaCol = colIndex(headers, "Net Debt/EBITDA");
  const currentAssetsCol = colIndex(headers, "Current Assets");
  const currentLiabilitiesCol = colIndex(headers, "Current Liabilities");
  const currentRatioCol = colIndex(headers, "Current Ratio");
  const netIncomeCol = colIndex(headers, "Net Income");
  const equityCol = colIndex(headers, "Shareholder Equity");
  const assetsCol = colIndex(headers, "Total Assets");
  const roeCol = colIndex(headers, "ROE %");
  const roaCol = colIndex(headers, "ROA %");

  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {

    const row = data[r];

    if (!row[tickerCol]) continue;

    const rowNumber = r + 1;

    // =====================================================
    // READ SOURCE VALUES
    // =====================================================

    const price = num(row[priceCol]);
    const marketCap = num(row[marketCapCol]);
    const eps = num(row[epsCol]);
    const pe = num(row[peCol]);
    const beta = num(row[betaCol]);
    const high52 = num(row[high52Col]);
    const low52 = num(row[low52Col]);

    let gfScore = num(row[gfScoreCol]);
    let earningsYield = num(row[earningsYieldCol]);
    let upside = num(row[upsideCol]);
    let downside = num(row[downsideCol]);
    let position = num(row[positionCol]);
    let betaRisk = row[betaRiskCol];
    let momentum = row[momentumCol];

    // =====================================================
    // RECALCULATE IF CLEAN FIELDS ARE EMPTY
    // =====================================================

    const impliedShares = safeDiv(marketCap, price);

    if (!earningsYield) earningsYield = safeDiv(eps, price);
    if (!upside) upside = safeDiv(high52 - price, price);
    if (!downside) downside = safeDiv(price - low52, price);
    if (!position) position = safeDiv(price - low52, high52 - low52);
    if (!betaRisk) betaRisk = classifyBetaRisk(beta);
    if (!momentum) momentum = classifyMomentum(position);
    if (!gfScore) gfScore = scoreGoogleFinance(pe, beta, position, earningsYield);

    const valuationScore = calculateValuationProxyScore(pe, earningsYield);
    const financialStrengthScore = calculateFinancialStrengthProxyScore(betaRisk, gfScore);

    // =====================================================
    // FILL EXISTING GOOGLEFINANCE-DERIVED FIELDS
    // =====================================================

    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, sharesCol, impliedShares);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, impliedSharesCol, impliedShares);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, earningsYieldCol, earningsYield);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, upsideCol, upside);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, downsideCol, downside);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, positionCol, position);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, gfScoreCol, gfScore);

    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, valuationScoreCol, valuationScore);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, financialStrengthScoreCol, financialStrengthScore);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, overallScoreCol, gfScore);

    // Management and Moat scores cannot be truly calculated from GoogleFinance.
    // These are neutral placeholders only if the cells are blank.
    if (managementScoreCol >= 0 && row[managementScoreCol] === "") {
      setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, managementScoreCol, 50);
    }

    if (moatScoreCol >= 0 && row[moatScoreCol] === "") {
      setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, moatScoreCol, 50);
    }

    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, scenarioCol, momentum + " / " + betaRisk);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, volatilityCol, beta);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, marginSafetyCol, upside);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, expectedCagrCol, earningsYield);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, maxDrawdownCol, -downside);

    // Proxy targets:
    // Buy Target Price = 52W High
    // Sell Target Price = 52W Low
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, buyTargetCol, high52);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, sellTargetCol, low52);

    // =====================================================
    // CONDITIONALLY CALCULATED EXISTING FIELDS
    // Only fills if supporting fields already exist.
    // =====================================================

    const bvps = num(row[bookValuePerShareCol]);
    const dps = num(row[dividendPerShareCol]);
    const totalDebt = num(row[totalDebtCol]);
    const cash = num(row[cashCol]);
    const ebitda = num(row[ebitdaCol]);
    const currentAssets = num(row[currentAssetsCol]);
    const currentLiabilities = num(row[currentLiabilitiesCol]);
    const netIncome = num(row[netIncomeCol]);
    const equity = num(row[equityCol]);
    const assets = num(row[assetsCol]);

    if (pbRatioCol >= 0 && bvps > 0) {
      setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, pbRatioCol, safeDiv(price, bvps));
    }

    if (dividendYieldCol >= 0 && dps > 0) {
      setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, dividendYieldCol, safeDiv(dps, price));
    }

    if (payoutRatioCol >= 0 && dps > 0 && eps > 0) {
      const payout = safeDiv(dps, eps);
      setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, payoutRatioCol, payout);
      setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, retentionRatioCol, 1 - payout);
    }

    if (netDebtCol >= 0 && (totalDebt || cash)) {
      const netDebt = totalDebt - cash;
      setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, netDebtCol, netDebt);

      if (netDebtEbitdaCol >= 0 && ebitda > 0) {
        setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, netDebtEbitdaCol, safeDiv(netDebt, ebitda));
      }
    }

    if (currentRatioCol >= 0 && currentAssets > 0 && currentLiabilities > 0) {
      setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, currentRatioCol, safeDiv(currentAssets, currentLiabilities));
    }

    if (roeCol >= 0 && netIncome && equity) {
      setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, roeCol, safeDiv(netIncome, equity));
    }

    if (roaCol >= 0 && netIncome && assets) {
      setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, roaCol, safeDiv(netIncome, assets));
    }

    // =====================================================
    // STATUS FIELDS
    // =====================================================

    if (watchlistCol >= 0 && row[watchlistCol] === "") {
      setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, watchlistCol, "WATCHLIST");
    }

    if (recommendationCol >= 0 && row[recommendationCol] === "") {
      setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, recommendationCol, "HOLD / MONITOR");
    }

    if (remarksCol >= 0) {
      setCellByIndex(
        input,
        rowNumber,
        remarksCol,
        "Existing automatable fields updated from GoogleFinance-derived data. True fundamentals remain blank."
      );
    }
  }

  formatExistingAutomatableFields(input);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 34A — FORMAT EXISTING AUTOMATABLE FIELDS
// PURPOSE:
// Applies correct number and percentage formats.
// =====================================================

function formatExistingAutomatableFields(input) {

  const headers = getHeaders(input);
  const lastRow = Math.max(input.getLastRow() - 1, 1);

  const percentageHeaders = [
    "Earnings Yield %",
    "Upside to 52W High %",
    "Downside to 52W Low %",
    "52W Price Position %",
    "Margin of Safety %",
    "Expected 10Y CAGR %",
    "Max Drawdown %",
    "Volatility %",
    "Dividend Yield %",
    "Payout Ratio %",
    "Retention Ratio %",
    "ROE %",
    "ROA %",
    "Current Ratio"
  ];

  percentageHeaders.forEach(header => {
    const c = colIndex(headers, header);
    if (c >= 0) {
      const format = header === "Current Ratio" ? "#,##0.00" : "0.00%";
      input.getRange(2, c + 1, lastRow, 1).setNumberFormat(format);
    }
  });

  const numberHeaders = [
    "Shares Outstanding",
    "Implied Shares Outstanding",
    "GoogleFinance Score",
    "Overall Investment Score",
    "Valuation Score",
    "Financial Strength Score",
    "Management Score",
    "Moat Score",
    "PB Ratio",
    "Net Debt",
    "Net Debt/EBITDA",
    "Buy Target Price",
    "Sell Target Price"
  ];

  numberHeaders.forEach(header => {
    const c = colIndex(headers, header);
    if (c >= 0) {
      input.getRange(2, c + 1, lastRow, 1).setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");
    }
  });

  input.autoResizeColumns(1, input.getLastColumn());
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 9 — HISTORICAL PRICE ENGINE
// PURPOSE:
// Pulls one-year daily close prices into the History sheet.
// =====================================================

function createHistoricalPriceSheet() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);
  let history = ss.getSheetByName(HISTORY_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");
  if (!history) history = ss.insertSheet(HISTORY_SHEET_NAME);

  history.clear();

  const data = input.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];
  const tickerCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker");

  history.getRange("A1").setValue("Ticker");
  history.getRange("B1").setValue("Historical Close Price Formula");

  let outputRow = 2;

  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {
    const ticker = data[r][tickerCol];
    if (!ticker) continue;

    history.getRange(outputRow, 1).setValue(ticker);
    history.getRange(outputRow, 2)
      .setFormula(`=IFERROR(GOOGLEFINANCE(A${outputRow},"close",TODAY()-365,TODAY(),"DAILY"),"")`);

    // GoogleFinance returns around 250 trading rows plus headers.
    // This spacing prevents datasets from overlapping.
    outputRow += 270;
  }

  history.getRange("A1:B1").setFontWeight("bold");
  history.autoResizeColumns(1, 2);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 10 — INPUT FORMATTING ENGINE
// PURPOSE:
// Formats the Input sheet, including clean columns.
// =====================================================

function formatInputSheet() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");

  const headers = getHeaders(input);
  const lastRow = Math.max(input.getLastRow() - 1, 1);

  input.getDataRange().setFontFamily("Arial");
  input.setFrozenRows(1);
  input.getRange(1, 1, 1, input.getLastColumn()).setFontWeight("bold");

  const numberHeaders = [
    "Share Price",
    "Market Cap",
    "Shares Outstanding",
    "Implied Shares Outstanding",
    "PE Ratio",
    "EPS",
    "Beta",
    "Average Volume",
    "52 Week High",
    "52 Week Low",
    "GoogleFinance Score",
    "Overall Investment Score",
    "Valuation Score",
    "Financial Strength Score"
  ];

  numberHeaders.forEach(header => {
    const c = colIndex(headers, header);
    if (c >= 0) {
      input.getRange(2, c + 1, lastRow, 1).setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");
    }
  });

  const percentageHeaders = [
    "Earnings Yield %",
    "Upside to 52W High %",
    "Downside to 52W Low %",
    "52W Price Position %",
    "Portfolio Allocation %",
    "Volatility %",
    "Margin of Safety %",
    "Expected 10Y CAGR %",
    "Max Drawdown %"
  ];

  percentageHeaders.forEach(header => {
    const c = colIndex(headers, header);
    if (c >= 0) {
      input.getRange(2, c + 1, lastRow, 1).setNumberFormat("0.00%");
    }
  });

  input.autoResizeColumns(1, input.getLastColumn());
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 11 — DASHBOARD FORMATTING ENGINE
// PURPOSE:
// Formats the Dashboard sheet.
// =====================================================

function formatDashboard() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!dash) throw new Error("Dashboard sheet not found.");

  dash.getDataRange().setFontFamily("Arial");
  dash.setFrozenRows(1);

  dash.getRange("A1")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(16);

  styleDashboardSectionTitles_(dash);

  dash.autoResizeColumns(1, Math.max(dash.getLastColumn(), 20));
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 12 — HISTORY FORMATTING ENGINE
// PURPOSE:
// Formats the History sheet.
// =====================================================

function formatHistorySheet() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const history = ss.getSheetByName(HISTORY_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!history) return;

  history.getDataRange().setFontFamily("Arial");
  history.setFrozenRows(1);
  history.getRange("A1:B1").setFontWeight("bold");
  history.autoResizeColumns(1, 2);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 13 — DATA OBJECT BUILDER
// PURPOSE:
// Converts Input sheet rows into clean stock objects.
// =====================================================

function getCleanStockObjects(data, headers) {
  const tickerCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker");
  const priceCol = colIndex(headers, "Share Price");
  const peCol = colIndex(headers, "PE Ratio");
  const betaCol = colIndex(headers, "Beta");
  const scoreCol = colIndex(headers, "GoogleFinance Score");
  const earningsYieldCol = colIndex(headers, "Earnings Yield %");
  const upsideCol = colIndex(headers, "Upside to 52W High %");
  const downsideCol = colIndex(headers, "Downside to 52W Low %");
  const positionCol = colIndex(headers, "52W Price Position %");
  const betaRiskCol = colIndex(headers, "Beta Risk Group");
  const momentumCol = colIndex(headers, "Momentum Signal");
  const recommendationCol = colIndex(headers, "Final Recommendation");
  const watchlistCol = colIndex(headers, "Watchlist Status");
  const allocationCol = colIndex(headers, "Portfolio Allocation %");
  const remarksCol = colIndex(headers, "Remarks");

  const stocks = [];

  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {
    const row = data[r];

    if (!row[tickerCol]) continue;

    stocks.push({
      ticker: row[tickerCol],
      price: num(row[priceCol]),
      pe: num(row[peCol]),
      beta: num(row[betaCol]),
      score: num(row[scoreCol]),
      earningsYield: num(row[earningsYieldCol]),
      upside: num(row[upsideCol]),
      downside: num(row[downsideCol]),
      position: num(row[positionCol]),
      betaRisk: row[betaRiskCol],
      momentum: row[momentumCol],
      recommendation: row[recommendationCol],
      watchlist: row[watchlistCol],
      allocation: num(row[allocationCol]),
      remarks: row[remarksCol]
    });
  }

  return stocks;
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 14 — SCORING HELPERS
// PURPOSE:
// Shared logic for risk, momentum, valuation, and scoring.
// =====================================================

function classifyBetaRisk(beta) {
  if (!beta || beta <= 0) return "NO BETA DATA";
  if (beta <= 0.7) return "LOW RISK";
  if (beta <= 1.2) return "MODERATE RISK";
  if (beta <= 1.8) return "HIGH RISK";
  return "VERY HIGH RISK";
}

function classifyMomentum(pricePosition) {
  if (pricePosition === "" || pricePosition == null) return "NO DATA";
  if (pricePosition >= 0.80) return "STRONG MOMENTUM";
  if (pricePosition >= 0.60) return "POSITIVE TREND";
  if (pricePosition >= 0.40) return "NEUTRAL";
  if (pricePosition >= 0.20) return "WEAK";
  return "NEAR 52W LOW";
}

function scoreGoogleFinance(pe, beta, pricePosition, earningsYield) {
  let score = 0;

  // PE valuation score.
  if (pe > 0 && pe <= 10) score += 30;
  else if (pe > 10 && pe <= 20) score += 22;
  else if (pe > 20 && pe <= 30) score += 12;
  else if (pe > 30) score += 5;

  // Beta risk score.
  if (beta > 0 && beta <= 0.7) score += 25;
  else if (beta > 0.7 && beta <= 1.2) score += 18;
  else if (beta > 1.2 && beta <= 1.8) score += 10;
  else if (beta > 1.8) score += 3;

  // 52-week position score.
  if (pricePosition >= 0 && pricePosition <= 0.35) score += 25;
  else if (pricePosition > 0.35 && pricePosition <= 0.65) score += 15;
  else if (pricePosition > 0.65) score += 8;

  // Earnings yield score.
  if (earningsYield > 0.10) score += 20;
  else if (earningsYield > 0.06) score += 15;
  else if (earningsYield > 0.03) score += 8;
  else if (earningsYield > 0) score += 3;

  return score;
}

function calculateValuationProxyScore(pe, earningsYield) {
  if (pe > 0 && pe <= 10 && earningsYield >= 0.08) return 90;
  if (pe > 10 && pe <= 15 && earningsYield >= 0.06) return 75;
  if (pe > 15 && pe <= 25 && earningsYield >= 0.04) return 60;
  if (pe > 25 || pe <= 0) return 35;
  return 50;
}

function calculateFinancialStrengthProxyScore(betaRisk, score) {
  if (betaRisk === "LOW RISK" && score >= 75) return 85;
  if (betaRisk === "MODERATE RISK" && score >= 65) return 70;
  if (betaRisk === "HIGH RISK") return 45;
  if (betaRisk === "VERY HIGH RISK") return 25;
  return 50;
}

function riskMultiplier(betaRisk) {
  if (betaRisk === "LOW RISK") return 1.25;
  if (betaRisk === "MODERATE RISK") return 1.00;
  if (betaRisk === "HIGH RISK") return 0.65;
  if (betaRisk === "VERY HIGH RISK") return 0.25;
  return 0.50;
}

function recommendationMultiplier(recommendation) {
  if (recommendation === "BUY CANDIDATE") return 1.30;
  if (recommendation === "ACCUMULATE / STUDY") return 1.00;
  if (recommendation === "HOLD / MONITOR") return 0.60;
  if (recommendation === "VALUE WATCH") return 0.50;
  return 0;
}

function momentumMultiplier(momentum) {
  if (momentum === "STRONG MOMENTUM") return 1.10;
  if (momentum === "POSITIVE TREND") return 1.00;
  if (momentum === "NEAR 52W LOW") return 0.85;
  return 0.90;
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 36 — DASHBOARD HISTORICAL PRICE SNAPSHOT
// PURPOSE:
// Adds share price snapshots to the Dashboard sheet:
// Current Price, 1 Year Ago, 3 Years Ago, 5 Years Ago,
// and 10 Years Ago using GOOGLEFINANCE historical lookup.
// =====================================================

function createDashboardHistoricalPriceSnapshot() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) {
    throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");
  }

  if (!dash) {
    throw new Error("Dashboard sheet not found.");
  }

  const data = input.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];

  const tickerCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker");
  const priceCol = colIndex(headers, "Share Price");

  // =====================================================
  // DYNAMIC DASHBOARD LOCATION
  // Appends below the last table created by createCleanDashboard().
  // =====================================================

  const props = PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties();
  const startRow = Number(props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_NEXT_ROW")) || findNextDashboardRow_(dash, 1, 12);
  const startCol = 1;

  // Clear a safe area below this section only.
  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, 200, 10).clearContent();

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol)
    .setValue("Historical Share Price Snapshot");

  const tableHeaders = [
    "Ticker",
    "Current Price",
    "Price 1Y Ago",
    "Price 3Y Ago",
    "Price 5Y Ago",
    "Price 10Y Ago",
    "1Y Return %",
    "3Y Return %",
    "5Y Return %",
    "10Y Return %"
  ];

  dash.getRange(startRow + 2, startCol, 1, tableHeaders.length)
    .setValues([tableHeaders]);

  let outputRow = startRow + 3;

  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {

    const row = data[r];
    const ticker = row[tickerCol];

    if (!ticker) continue;

    const currentPrice = row[priceCol];

    dash.getRange(outputRow, startCol).setValue(ticker);
    dash.getRange(outputRow, startCol + 1).setValue(currentPrice);

    dash.getRange(outputRow, startCol + 2)
      .setFormula(`=IFERROR(INDEX(GOOGLEFINANCE(A${outputRow},"price",TODAY()-365,TODAY()-365),2,2),"")`);

    dash.getRange(outputRow, startCol + 3)
      .setFormula(`=IFERROR(INDEX(GOOGLEFINANCE(A${outputRow},"price",TODAY()-365*3,TODAY()-365*3),2,2),"")`);

    dash.getRange(outputRow, startCol + 4)
      .setFormula(`=IFERROR(INDEX(GOOGLEFINANCE(A${outputRow},"price",TODAY()-365*5,TODAY()-365*5),2,2),"")`);

    dash.getRange(outputRow, startCol + 5)
      .setFormula(`=IFERROR(INDEX(GOOGLEFINANCE(A${outputRow},"price",TODAY()-365*10,TODAY()-365*10),2,2),"")`);

    dash.getRange(outputRow, startCol + 6)
      .setFormula(`=IFERROR((B${outputRow}-C${outputRow})/C${outputRow},"")`);

    dash.getRange(outputRow, startCol + 7)
      .setFormula(`=IFERROR((B${outputRow}-D${outputRow})/D${outputRow},"")`);

    dash.getRange(outputRow, startCol + 8)
      .setFormula(`=IFERROR((B${outputRow}-E${outputRow})/E${outputRow},"")`);

    dash.getRange(outputRow, startCol + 9)
      .setFormula(`=IFERROR((B${outputRow}-F${outputRow})/F${outputRow},"")`);

    outputRow++;
  }

  const rowCount = Math.max(outputRow - (startRow + 3), 1);

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol)
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(12)
    .setBackground("#d9e2f3")
    .setFontColor("#1f2933");

  dash.getRange(startRow + 2, startCol, 1, tableHeaders.length)
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff");

  dash.getRange(startRow + 3, startCol + 1, rowCount, 5)
    .setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");

  dash.getRange(startRow + 3, startCol + 6, rowCount, 4)
    .setNumberFormat("0.00%");

  dash.autoResizeColumns(startCol, tableHeaders.length);

  props.setProperty("DASHBOARD_HISTORY_START", String(startRow + 3));
  props.setProperty("DASHBOARD_NEXT_ROW", String(outputRow + 3));
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 36A — HISTORICAL RETURN CONDITIONAL FORMATTING
// PURPOSE:
// Adds green/red colour scale to historical return columns.
// =====================================================

function applyHistoricalSnapshotConditionalFormatting() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!dash) return;

  const props = PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties();
  const historyStart = Number(props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_HISTORY_START")) || findSectionDataStart_(dash, "Historical Share Price Snapshot", 2);

  if (!historyStart) return;

  const rows = detectTableLength(dash, historyStart, 1);
  if (rows <= 0) return;

  const rules = dash.getConditionalFormatRules();

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .setGradientMinpointWithValue("#f4cccc", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "-0.30")
      .setGradientMidpointWithValue("#fff2cc", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "0")
      .setGradientMaxpointWithValue("#d9ead3", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "0.30")
      .setRanges([dash.getRange(historyStart, 7, rows, 4)])
      .build()
  );

  dash.setConditionalFormatRules(rules);
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 40 — DASHBOARD TICKER COUNT + DATA COVERAGE SUMMARY
// PURPOSE:
// Adds a Dashboard summary showing total tickers, valid priced
// tickers, missing price data, scored tickers, allocated tickers,
// and recommendation counts.
// =====================================================

function createDashboardTickerCountSummary() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) {
    throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");
  }

  if (!dash) {
    throw new Error("Dashboard sheet not found.");
  }

  const data = input.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];

  const tickerCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker");
  const priceCol = colIndex(headers, "Share Price");
  const scoreCol = colIndex(headers, "GoogleFinance Score");
  const allocationCol = colIndex(headers, "Portfolio Allocation %");
  const recommendationCol = colIndex(headers, "Final Recommendation");
  const watchlistCol = colIndex(headers, "Watchlist Status");
  const statusCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker Data Status");

  let totalTickers = 0;
  let pricedTickers = 0;
  let missingPrice = 0;
  let scoredTickers = 0;
  let allocatedTickers = 0;

  let buyCandidates = 0;
  let accumulateStudy = 0;
  let holdMonitor = 0;
  let avoidHighRisk = 0;
  let valueWatch = 0;

  let highPriority = 0;
  let mediumPriority = 0;
  let lowPriority = 0;

  let tickerStatusOk = 0;
  let tickerStatusWarning = 0;

  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {

    const row = data[r];
    const ticker = row[tickerCol];

    if (!ticker) continue;

    totalTickers++;

    const price = num(row[priceCol]);
    const score = num(row[scoreCol]);
    const allocation = num(row[allocationCol]);
    const recommendation = row[recommendationCol];
    const watchlist = row[watchlistCol];
    const status = statusCol >= 0 ? row[statusCol] : "";

    if (price > 0) pricedTickers++;
    else missingPrice++;

    if (score > 0) scoredTickers++;
    if (allocation > 0) allocatedTickers++;

    if (recommendation === "BUY CANDIDATE") buyCandidates++;
    else if (recommendation === "ACCUMULATE / STUDY") accumulateStudy++;
    else if (recommendation === "HOLD / MONITOR") holdMonitor++;
    else if (recommendation === "AVOID / HIGH RISK") avoidHighRisk++;
    else if (recommendation === "VALUE WATCH") valueWatch++;

    if (watchlist === "HIGH PRIORITY") highPriority++;
    else if (watchlist === "MEDIUM PRIORITY") mediumPriority++;
    else if (watchlist === "LOW PRIORITY") lowPriority++;

    if (status === "OK") tickerStatusOk++;
    else if (status) tickerStatusWarning++;
  }

  const pricedCoverage = totalTickers > 0 ? pricedTickers / totalTickers : 0;
  const scoredCoverage = totalTickers > 0 ? scoredTickers / totalTickers : 0;
  const allocatedCoverage = totalTickers > 0 ? allocatedTickers / totalTickers : 0;

  const table = [
    ["Metric", "Count / Value"],
    ["Total Tickers", totalTickers],
    ["Priced Tickers", pricedTickers],
    ["Missing Price Data", missingPrice],
    ["Price Coverage %", pricedCoverage],
    ["Scored Tickers", scoredTickers],
    ["Score Coverage %", scoredCoverage],
    ["Allocated Tickers", allocatedTickers],
    ["Allocation Coverage %", allocatedCoverage],
    ["Buy Candidates", buyCandidates],
    ["Accumulate / Study", accumulateStudy],
    ["Hold / Monitor", holdMonitor],
    ["Avoid / High Risk", avoidHighRisk],
    ["Value Watch", valueWatch],
    ["High Priority", highPriority],
    ["Medium Priority", mediumPriority],
    ["Low Priority", lowPriority],
    ["Ticker Status OK", tickerStatusOk],
    ["Ticker Status Warning", tickerStatusWarning]
  ];

  // Fixed right-side panel to avoid overlap with left dashboard tables.
  const startRow = 3;
  const startCol = 14; // Column N

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, 25, 4).clearContent();

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol)
    .setValue("Ticker Count + Data Coverage Summary");

  dash.getRange(startRow + 2, startCol, table.length, table[0].length)
    .setValues(table);

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol)
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(12)
    .setBackground("#d9e2f3")
    .setFontColor("#1f2933");

  dash.getRange(startRow + 2, startCol, 1, table[0].length)
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff");

  dash.getRange(startRow + 6, startCol + 1).setNumberFormat("0.00%");
  dash.getRange(startRow + 8, startCol + 1).setNumberFormat("0.00%");
  dash.getRange(startRow + 10, startCol + 1).setNumberFormat("0.00%");

  dash.autoResizeColumns(startCol, 4);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 35 — COLOUR INDICATORS + CONDITIONAL FORMATTING
// PURPOSE:
// Adds visual colour indicators and conditional formatting
// to Input and Dashboard sheets.
// =====================================================

function applyColourIndicatorsAndConditionalFormatting() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) {
    throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");
  }

  // Apply Input conditional formatting
  applyInputConditionalFormatting_(input);

  // Apply Dashboard visual formatting if Dashboard exists
  if (dash) {
    applyDashboardConditionalFormatting_(dash);
  }
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 35A — INPUT CONDITIONAL FORMATTING
// PURPOSE:
// Applies traffic-light colour formatting to key Input
// analytical columns.
// =====================================================

function applyInputConditionalFormatting_(input) {

  const headers = getHeaders(input);
  const lastRow = Math.max(input.getLastRow(), 2);
  const rules = [];

  // Clear existing conditional format rules first
  input.setConditionalFormatRules([]);

  // =====================================================
  // SCORE COLOUR SCALE
  // Green = strong, yellow = medium, red = weak
  // =====================================================

  [
    "GoogleFinance Score",
    "Overall Investment Score",
    "Valuation Score",
    "Financial Strength Score"
  ].forEach(header => {

    const c = colIndex(headers, header);

    if (c >= 0) {
      const range = input.getRange(2, c + 1, lastRow - 1, 1);

      rules.push(
        SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
          .setGradientMinpointWithValue("#f4cccc", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "0")
          .setGradientMidpointWithValue("#fff2cc", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "50")
          .setGradientMaxpointWithValue("#d9ead3", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "100")
          .setRanges([range])
          .build()
      );
    }
  });

  // =====================================================
  // PORTFOLIO ALLOCATION COLOUR SCALE
  // Larger allocation = stronger green shade
  // =====================================================

  const allocationCol = colIndex(headers, "Portfolio Allocation %");

  if (allocationCol >= 0) {
    const range = input.getRange(2, allocationCol + 1, lastRow - 1, 1);

    rules.push(
      SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
        .setGradientMinpointWithValue("#ffffff", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "0")
        .setGradientMaxpointWithValue("#b6d7a8", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "0.15")
        .setRanges([range])
        .build()
    );
  }

  // =====================================================
  // EARNINGS YIELD COLOUR SCALE
  // High earnings yield = green
  // Negative earnings yield = red
  // =====================================================

  const earningsYieldCol = colIndex(headers, "Earnings Yield %");

  if (earningsYieldCol >= 0) {
    const range = input.getRange(2, earningsYieldCol + 1, lastRow - 1, 1);

    rules.push(
      SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
        .setGradientMinpointWithValue("#f4cccc", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "-0.10")
        .setGradientMidpointWithValue("#fff2cc", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "0.04")
        .setGradientMaxpointWithValue("#d9ead3", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "0.10")
        .setRanges([range])
        .build()
    );
  }

  // =====================================================
  // UPSIDE TO 52W HIGH COLOUR SCALE
  // Higher upside = green
  // =====================================================

  const upsideCol = colIndex(headers, "Upside to 52W High %");

  if (upsideCol >= 0) {
    const range = input.getRange(2, upsideCol + 1, lastRow - 1, 1);

    rules.push(
      SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
        .setGradientMinpointWithValue("#ffffff", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "0")
        .setGradientMidpointWithValue("#fff2cc", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "0.20")
        .setGradientMaxpointWithValue("#d9ead3", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "0.50")
        .setRanges([range])
        .build()
    );
  }

  // =====================================================
  // 52W PRICE POSITION COLOUR SCALE
  // Near 52W low = green for potential value watch
  // Near 52W high = red/orange for stretched price
  // =====================================================

  const positionCol = colIndex(headers, "52W Price Position %");

  if (positionCol >= 0) {
    const range = input.getRange(2, positionCol + 1, lastRow - 1, 1);

    rules.push(
      SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
        .setGradientMinpointWithValue("#d9ead3", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "0")
        .setGradientMidpointWithValue("#fff2cc", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "0.50")
        .setGradientMaxpointWithValue("#f4cccc", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "1")
        .setRanges([range])
        .build()
    );
  }

  // =====================================================
  // BETA RISK GROUP TEXT COLOURS
  // =====================================================

  const betaRiskCol = colIndex(headers, "Beta Risk Group");

  if (betaRiskCol >= 0) {
    const range = input.getRange(2, betaRiskCol + 1, lastRow - 1, 1);

    rules.push(
      SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
        .whenTextEqualTo("LOW RISK")
        .setBackground("#d9ead3")
        .setFontColor("#274e13")
        .setRanges([range])
        .build()
    );

    rules.push(
      SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
        .whenTextEqualTo("MODERATE RISK")
        .setBackground("#fff2cc")
        .setFontColor("#7f6000")
        .setRanges([range])
        .build()
    );

    rules.push(
      SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
        .whenTextEqualTo("HIGH RISK")
        .setBackground("#fce5cd")
        .setFontColor("#783f04")
        .setRanges([range])
        .build()
    );

    rules.push(
      SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
        .whenTextEqualTo("VERY HIGH RISK")
        .setBackground("#f4cccc")
        .setFontColor("#990000")
        .setRanges([range])
        .build()
    );
  }

  // =====================================================
  // MOMENTUM SIGNAL TEXT COLOURS
  // =====================================================

  const momentumCol = colIndex(headers, "Momentum Signal");

  if (momentumCol >= 0) {
    const range = input.getRange(2, momentumCol + 1, lastRow - 1, 1);

    rules.push(
      SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
        .whenTextEqualTo("STRONG MOMENTUM")
        .setBackground("#d9ead3")
        .setFontColor("#274e13")
        .setRanges([range])
        .build()
    );

    rules.push(
      SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
        .whenTextEqualTo("POSITIVE TREND")
        .setBackground("#d0e0e3")
        .setFontColor("#0c343d")
        .setRanges([range])
        .build()
    );

    rules.push(
      SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
        .whenTextEqualTo("NEAR 52W LOW")
        .setBackground("#fff2cc")
        .setFontColor("#7f6000")
        .setRanges([range])
        .build()
    );
  }

  // =====================================================
  // FINAL RECOMMENDATION TEXT COLOURS
  // =====================================================

  const recommendationCol = colIndex(headers, "Final Recommendation");

  if (recommendationCol >= 0) {
    const range = input.getRange(2, recommendationCol + 1, lastRow - 1, 1);

    rules.push(
      SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
        .whenTextEqualTo("BUY CANDIDATE")
        .setBackground("#b6d7a8")
        .setFontColor("#274e13")
        .setRanges([range])
        .build()
    );

    rules.push(
      SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
        .whenTextEqualTo("ACCUMULATE / STUDY")
        .setBackground("#d9ead3")
        .setFontColor("#274e13")
        .setRanges([range])
        .build()
    );

    rules.push(
      SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
        .whenTextEqualTo("HOLD / MONITOR")
        .setBackground("#fff2cc")
        .setFontColor("#7f6000")
        .setRanges([range])
        .build()
    );

    rules.push(
      SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
        .whenTextEqualTo("AVOID / HIGH RISK")
        .setBackground("#f4cccc")
        .setFontColor("#990000")
        .setRanges([range])
        .build()
    );

    rules.push(
      SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
        .whenTextEqualTo("VALUE WATCH")
        .setBackground("#cfe2f3")
        .setFontColor("#073763")
        .setRanges([range])
        .build()
    );
  }

  // =====================================================
  // WATCHLIST STATUS TEXT COLOURS
  // =====================================================

  const watchlistCol = colIndex(headers, "Watchlist Status");

  if (watchlistCol >= 0) {
    const range = input.getRange(2, watchlistCol + 1, lastRow - 1, 1);

    rules.push(
      SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
        .whenTextEqualTo("HIGH PRIORITY")
        .setBackground("#b6d7a8")
        .setFontColor("#274e13")
        .setRanges([range])
        .build()
    );

    rules.push(
      SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
        .whenTextEqualTo("MEDIUM PRIORITY")
        .setBackground("#fff2cc")
        .setFontColor("#7f6000")
        .setRanges([range])
        .build()
    );

    rules.push(
      SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
        .whenTextEqualTo("LOW PRIORITY")
        .setBackground("#f4cccc")
        .setFontColor("#990000")
        .setRanges([range])
        .build()
    );
  }

  input.setConditionalFormatRules(rules);

  // =====================================================
  // HEADER AND STATIC VISUAL FORMATTING
  // =====================================================

  input.getRange(1, 1, 1, input.getLastColumn())
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  input.setFrozenRows(1);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 35B — DASHBOARD CONDITIONAL FORMATTING
// PURPOSE:
// Adds visual colour indicators to dashboard tables.
// =====================================================

function applyDashboardConditionalFormatting_(dash) {

  const rules = [];
  dash.setConditionalFormatRules([]);

  const props = PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties();

  const rankingStart = Number(props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_RANKING_START")) || findSectionDataStart_(dash, "Clean GoogleFinance Ranking Dashboard", 2);
  const watchlistStart = Number(props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_WATCHLIST_START")) || findSectionDataStart_(dash, "Clean Watchlist Dashboard Table", 2);
  const portfolioStart = Number(props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_PORTFOLIO_START")) || findSectionDataStart_(dash, "Clean Portfolio Allocation Dashboard", 2);
  const historyStart = Number(props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_HISTORY_START")) || findSectionDataStart_(dash, "Historical Share Price Snapshot", 2);

  if (rankingStart) {
    const rankingRows = detectTableLength(dash, rankingStart, 2);
    if (rankingRows > 0) {
      rules.push(
        SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
          .setGradientMinpointWithValue("#f4cccc", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "0")
          .setGradientMidpointWithValue("#fff2cc", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "50")
          .setGradientMaxpointWithValue("#d9ead3", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "100")
