          .setRanges([dash.getRange(rankingStart, 11, rankingRows, 1)])
          .build()
      );
    }
  }

  if (portfolioStart) {
    const portfolioRows = detectTableLength(dash, portfolioStart, 1);
    if (portfolioRows > 0) {
      rules.push(
        SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
          .setGradientMinpointWithValue("#ffffff", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "0")
          .setGradientMaxpointWithValue("#b6d7a8", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "0.15")
          .setRanges([dash.getRange(portfolioStart, 7, portfolioRows, 1)])
          .build()
      );
    }
  }

  if (watchlistStart) {
    const watchlistRows = detectTableLength(dash, watchlistStart, 1);
    if (watchlistRows > 0) {
      const recommendationRange = dash.getRange(watchlistStart, 10, watchlistRows, 1);

      rules.push(
        SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
          .whenTextEqualTo("BUY CANDIDATE")
          .setBackground("#b6d7a8")
          .setFontColor("#274e13")
          .setRanges([recommendationRange])
          .build()
      );

      rules.push(
        SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
          .whenTextEqualTo("ACCUMULATE / STUDY")
          .setBackground("#d9ead3")
          .setFontColor("#274e13")
          .setRanges([recommendationRange])
          .build()
      );

      rules.push(
        SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
          .whenTextEqualTo("HOLD / MONITOR")
          .setBackground("#fff2cc")
          .setFontColor("#7f6000")
          .setRanges([recommendationRange])
          .build()
      );

      rules.push(
        SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
          .whenTextEqualTo("AVOID / HIGH RISK")
          .setBackground("#f4cccc")
          .setFontColor("#990000")
          .setRanges([recommendationRange])
          .build()
      );
    }
  }

  if (historyStart) {
    const historyRows = detectTableLength(dash, historyStart, 1);
    if (historyRows > 0) {
      rules.push(
        SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
          .setGradientMinpointWithValue("#f4cccc", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "-0.30")
          .setGradientMidpointWithValue("#fff2cc", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "0")
          .setGradientMaxpointWithValue("#d9ead3", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "0.30")
          .setRanges([dash.getRange(historyStart, 7, historyRows, 4)])
          .build()
      );
    }
  }

  dash.setConditionalFormatRules(rules);

  dash.getRange("A1")
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(16);

  styleDashboardSectionTitles_(dash);
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 37 — REQUIRED HEADER + DATA QUALITY ENGINE
// PURPOSE:
// 1. Adds missing headers required for expanded GoogleFinance automation.
// 2. Checks ticker data quality and flags rows with missing market data.
// =====================================================

function ensureExpandedGoogleFinanceHeaders() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) {
    throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");
  }

  const requiredHeaders = [
    "Open Price",
    "Day High",
    "Day Low",
    "Trade Time",
    "Data Delay",
    "Current Volume",
    "Ticker Data Status"
  ];

  let headers = getHeaders(input);

  requiredHeaders.forEach(header => {

    if (!headers.includes(header)) {
      const nextCol = input.getLastColumn() + 1;
      input.getRange(1, nextCol).setValue(header);
      headers = getHeaders(input);
    }
  });

  input.getRange(1, 1, 1, input.getLastColumn())
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  input.autoResizeColumns(1, input.getLastColumn());
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 37A — TICKER DATA QUALITY CHECK
// PURPOSE:
// Flags unsupported, incomplete, or weak GoogleFinance results.
// This helps identify tickers that may need format correction.
// =====================================================

function runTickerDataQualityCheck() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) {
    throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");
  }

  const data = input.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];

  const tickerCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker");
  const priceCol = colIndex(headers, "Share Price");
  const marketCapCol = colIndex(headers, "Market Cap");
  const epsCol = colIndex(headers, "EPS");
  const peCol = colIndex(headers, "PE Ratio");
  const betaCol = colIndex(headers, "Beta");
  const high52Col = colIndex(headers, "52 Week High");
  const low52Col = colIndex(headers, "52 Week Low");
  const statusCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker Data Status");
  const remarksCol = colIndex(headers, "Remarks");

  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {

    const row = data[r];

    if (!row[tickerCol]) continue;

    const rowNumber = r + 1;

    const price = num(row[priceCol]);
    const marketCap = num(row[marketCapCol]);
    const eps = row[epsCol];
    const pe = row[peCol];
    const beta = row[betaCol];
    const high52 = num(row[high52Col]);
    const low52 = num(row[low52Col]);

    let status = "OK";
    let issues = [];

    if (!price) issues.push("NO PRICE DATA");
    if (!marketCap) issues.push("NO MARKET CAP");
    if (eps === "" || eps == null) issues.push("NO EPS DATA");
    if (pe === "" || pe == null) issues.push("NO PE DATA");
    if (beta === "" || beta == null) issues.push("NO BETA DATA");
    if (!high52 || !low52) issues.push("NO 52W RANGE DATA");

    if (issues.length > 0) {
      status = issues.join(" | ");
    }

    if (!price && !marketCap && !high52 && !low52) {
      status = "CHECK TICKER FORMAT";
    }

    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, statusCol, status);

    if (remarksCol >= 0 && status !== "OK") {
      setCellByIndex(
        input,
        rowNumber,
        remarksCol,
        "Data quality warning: " + status
      );
    }
  }

  formatTickerDataQualityStatus(input);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 37B — FORMAT TICKER DATA STATUS
// PURPOSE:
// Applies visual formatting to ticker status column.
// =====================================================

function formatTickerDataQualityStatus(input) {

  const headers = getHeaders(input);
  const statusCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker Data Status");

  if (statusCol < 0) return;

  const lastRow = Math.max(input.getLastRow(), 2);
  const range = input.getRange(2, statusCol + 1, lastRow - 1, 1);

  const rules = input.getConditionalFormatRules();

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("OK")
      .setBackground("#d9ead3")
      .setFontColor("#274e13")
      .setRanges([range])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextContains("CHECK TICKER FORMAT")
      .setBackground("#f4cccc")
      .setFontColor("#990000")
      .setRanges([range])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextContains("NO PRICE DATA")
      .setBackground("#fce5cd")
      .setFontColor("#783f04")
      .setRanges([range])
      .build()
  );

  input.setConditionalFormatRules(rules);
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 38 — HISTORY SUMMARY SHEET
// PURPOSE:
// Creates a compact historical price summary sheet.
// This is lighter than the raw History sheet and better
// for dashboard analytics.
// =====================================================

function createHistorySummarySheet() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) {
    throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");
  }

  let summary = ss.getSheetByName("History Summary");

  if (!summary) {
    summary = ss.insertSheet("History Summary");
  }

  summary.clear();

  const data = input.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];

  const tickerCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker");
  const priceCol = colIndex(headers, "Share Price");

  const outputHeaders = [
    "Ticker",
    "Current Price",
    "Price 1Y Ago",
    "Price 3Y Ago",
    "Price 5Y Ago",
    "Price 10Y Ago",
    "1Y Return %",
    "3Y Return %",
    "5Y Return %",
    "10Y Return %"
  ];

  summary.getRange(1, 1, 1, outputHeaders.length)
    .setValues([outputHeaders]);

  let outputRow = 2;

  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {

    const row = data[r];
    const ticker = row[tickerCol];

    if (!ticker) continue;

    const currentPrice = row[priceCol];

    summary.getRange(outputRow, 1).setValue(ticker);
    summary.getRange(outputRow, 2).setValue(currentPrice);

    // Historical price formulas.
    // INDEX extracts the historical close returned by GOOGLEFINANCE.
    summary.getRange(outputRow, 3)
      .setFormula(`=IFERROR(INDEX(GOOGLEFINANCE(A${outputRow},"price",TODAY()-365,TODAY()-365),2,2),"")`);

    summary.getRange(outputRow, 4)
      .setFormula(`=IFERROR(INDEX(GOOGLEFINANCE(A${outputRow},"price",TODAY()-365*3,TODAY()-365*3),2,2),"")`);

    summary.getRange(outputRow, 5)
      .setFormula(`=IFERROR(INDEX(GOOGLEFINANCE(A${outputRow},"price",TODAY()-365*5,TODAY()-365*5),2,2),"")`);

    summary.getRange(outputRow, 6)
      .setFormula(`=IFERROR(INDEX(GOOGLEFINANCE(A${outputRow},"price",TODAY()-365*10,TODAY()-365*10),2,2),"")`);

    // Return calculations.
    summary.getRange(outputRow, 7)
      .setFormula(`=IFERROR((B${outputRow}-C${outputRow})/C${outputRow},"")`);

    summary.getRange(outputRow, 8)
      .setFormula(`=IFERROR((B${outputRow}-D${outputRow})/D${outputRow},"")`);

    summary.getRange(outputRow, 9)
      .setFormula(`=IFERROR((B${outputRow}-E${outputRow})/E${outputRow},"")`);

    summary.getRange(outputRow, 10)
      .setFormula(`=IFERROR((B${outputRow}-F${outputRow})/F${outputRow},"")`);

    outputRow++;
  }

  formatHistorySummarySheet(summary);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 38A — HISTORY SUMMARY FORMATTING
// PURPOSE:
// Formats the compact History Summary sheet.
// =====================================================

function formatHistorySummarySheet(summary) {

  const lastRow = Math.max(summary.getLastRow(), 2);

  summary.getDataRange().setFontFamily("Arial");
  summary.setFrozenRows(1);

  summary.getRange(1, 1, 1, summary.getLastColumn())
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  summary.getRange(2, 2, lastRow - 1, 5)
    .setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");

  summary.getRange(2, 7, lastRow - 1, 4)
    .setNumberFormat("0.00%");

  summary.autoResizeColumns(1, summary.getLastColumn());

  // Conditional formatting for returns
  const rules = [];

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .setGradientMinpointWithValue("#f4cccc", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "-0.30")
      .setGradientMidpointWithValue("#fff2cc", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "0")
      .setGradientMaxpointWithValue("#d9ead3", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "0.30")
      .setRanges([summary.getRange(2, 7, lastRow - 1, 4)])
      .build()
  );

  summary.setConditionalFormatRules(rules);
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 39 — IMPROVED DASHBOARD CHART ENGINE
// PURPOSE:
// Creates adaptive Dashboard charts using the clean dashboard
// and History Summary data where available.
// =====================================================

function createImprovedDashboardCharts() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);
  const historySummary = ss.getSheetByName("History Summary");

  if (!dash) {
    throw new Error("Dashboard sheet not found.");
  }

  dash.getCharts().forEach(chart => dash.removeChart(chart));

  const props = PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties();

  const rankingStart = Number(props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_RANKING_START")) || findSectionDataStart_(dash, "Clean GoogleFinance Ranking Dashboard", 2);
  const portfolioStart = Number(props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_PORTFOLIO_START")) || findSectionDataStart_(dash, "Clean Portfolio Allocation Dashboard", 2);
  const riskStart = Number(props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_RISK_START")) || findSectionDataStart_(dash, "Risk Grouping Dashboard", 2);

  const chartCol = 14; // Column N, right side panel

  const rankingRows = rankingStart ? detectTableLength(dash, rankingStart, 2) : 0;

  if (rankingRows > 1) {

    const scoreChart = dash.newChart()
      .setChartType(Charts.ChartType.BAR)
      .addRange(dash.getRange(rankingStart, 2, rankingRows, 1))
      .addRange(dash.getRange(rankingStart, 11, rankingRows, 1))
      .setPosition(25, chartCol, 0, 0)
      .setOption("title", "GoogleFinance Score Ranking")
      .setOption("legend", { position: "none" })
      .setOption("height", 350)
      .setOption("width", 620)
      .build();

    dash.insertChart(scoreChart);
  }

  const portfolioRows = portfolioStart ? detectTableLength(dash, portfolioStart, 1) : 0;

  if (portfolioRows > 1) {

    const allocationChart = dash.newChart()
      .setChartType(Charts.ChartType.PIE)
      .addRange(dash.getRange(portfolioStart, 1, portfolioRows, 1))
      .addRange(dash.getRange(portfolioStart, 7, portfolioRows, 1))
      .setPosition(44, chartCol, 0, 0)
      .setOption("title", "Suggested Portfolio Allocation")
      .setOption("height", 350)
      .setOption("width", 620)
      .build();

    dash.insertChart(allocationChart);
  }

  const riskRows = riskStart ? detectTableLength(dash, riskStart, 1) : 0;

  if (riskRows > 1) {

    const riskChart = dash.newChart()
      .setChartType(Charts.ChartType.COLUMN)
      .addRange(dash.getRange(riskStart, 1, riskRows, 1))
      .addRange(dash.getRange(riskStart, 3, riskRows, 1))
      .setPosition(63, chartCol, 0, 0)
      .setOption("title", "Portfolio Allocation by Risk Group")
      .setOption("legend", { position: "none" })
      .setOption("height", 350)
      .setOption("width", 620)
      .build();

    dash.insertChart(riskChart);
  }

  if (historySummary) {

    const historyRows = Math.max(historySummary.getLastRow() - 1, 0);

    if (historyRows > 1) {

      const historicalReturnChart = dash.newChart()
        .setChartType(Charts.ChartType.COLUMN)
        .addRange(historySummary.getRange(2, 1, historyRows, 1))
        .addRange(historySummary.getRange(2, 7, historyRows, 4))
        .setPosition(82, chartCol, 0, 0)
        .setOption("title", "Historical Returns: 1Y / 3Y / 5Y / 10Y")
        .setOption("height", 380)
        .setOption("width", 720)
        .build();

      dash.insertChart(historicalReturnChart);
    }
  }
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 41 — DASHBOARD NAVIGATION + STATUS PANEL
// PURPOSE:
// Adds a professional status and navigation panel at the
// top-right of the Dashboard sheet.
// =====================================================

function createDashboardNavigationStatusPanel() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");
  if (!dash) throw new Error("Dashboard sheet not found.");

  const data = input.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];

  const tickerCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker");
  const priceCol = colIndex(headers, "Share Price");
  const scoreCol = colIndex(headers, "GoogleFinance Score");
  const allocationCol = colIndex(headers, "Portfolio Allocation %");
  const recommendationCol = colIndex(headers, "Final Recommendation");
  const statusCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker Data Status");

  let totalTickers = 0;
  let pricedTickers = 0;
  let missingPrice = 0;
  let scoredTickers = 0;
  let allocatedTickers = 0;
  let buyCandidates = 0;
  let dataWarnings = 0;

  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {
    const row = data[r];

    if (!row[tickerCol]) continue;

    totalTickers++;

    const price = num(row[priceCol]);
    const score = num(row[scoreCol]);
    const allocation = num(row[allocationCol]);
    const recommendation = row[recommendationCol];
    const status = statusCol >= 0 ? row[statusCol] : "";

    if (price > 0) pricedTickers++;
    else missingPrice++;

    if (score > 0) scoredTickers++;
    if (allocation > 0) allocatedTickers++;
    if (recommendation === "BUY CANDIDATE") buyCandidates++;

    if (status && status !== "OK") dataWarnings++;
  }

  const priceCoverage = totalTickers > 0 ? pricedTickers / totalTickers : 0;
  const scoreCoverage = totalTickers > 0 ? scoredTickers / totalTickers : 0;

  const startRow = 3;
  const startCol = 14; // Column N

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, 35, 6).clearContent();

  const statusTable = [
    ["Overseer Status Panel", ""],
    ["Last Update", new Date()],
    ["Total Tickers", totalTickers],
    ["Priced Tickers", pricedTickers],
    ["Missing Price Data", missingPrice],
    ["Price Coverage %", priceCoverage],
    ["Scored Tickers", scoredTickers],
    ["Score Coverage %", scoreCoverage],
    ["Allocated Tickers", allocatedTickers],
    ["Buy Candidates", buyCandidates],
    ["Data Warnings", dataWarnings]
  ];

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, statusTable.length, 2)
    .setValues(statusTable);

  const props = PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties();

  const navStartRow = startRow + 13;

  const navTable = [
    ["Dashboard Navigation", "Start Row"],
    ["Summary Cards", 3],
    ["Top 10 Decision View", props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_TOP10_START") || ""],
    ["Ranking Table", props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_RANKING_START") || ""],
    ["Watchlist Table", props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_WATCHLIST_START") || ""],
    ["Portfolio Allocation", props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_PORTFOLIO_START") || ""],
    ["Risk Grouping", props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_RISK_START") || ""],
    ["Historical Snapshot", props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_HISTORY_START") || ""],
    ["Unsupported Tickers", props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_UNSUPPORTED_START") || ""],
    ["Ticker Suggestions", props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_TICKER_SUGGESTION_START") || ""],
    ["Risk Heatmap", props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_RISK_HEATMAP_START") || ""]
  ];

  dash.getRange(navStartRow, startCol, navTable.length, 2)
    .setValues(navTable);

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, 1, 2)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  dash.getRange(navStartRow, startCol, 1, 2)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  dash.getRange(startRow + 1, startCol + 1)
    .setNumberFormat("dd/mm/yyyy hh:mm");

  dash.getRange(startRow + 5, startCol + 1)
    .setNumberFormat("0.00%");

  dash.getRange(startRow + 7, startCol + 1)
    .setNumberFormat("0.00%");

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, statusTable.length, 2)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  dash.getRange(navStartRow, startCol, navTable.length, 2)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  dash.autoResizeColumns(startCol, 6);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 41A — STATUS PANEL CONDITIONAL FORMATTING
// PURPOSE:
// Adds colour cues for coverage, missing price data,
// and data warnings.
// =====================================================

function applyDashboardStatusPanelFormatting() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!dash) return;

  const rules = dash.getConditionalFormatRules();

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenNumberGreaterThan(0)
      .setBackground("#f4cccc")
      .setFontColor("#990000")
      .setRanges([dash.getRange("O7")])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenNumberGreaterThan(0)
      .setBackground("#fce5cd")
      .setFontColor("#783f04")
      .setRanges([dash.getRange("O13")])
      .build()
  );

  dash.setConditionalFormatRules(rules);
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 42 — UNSUPPORTED / MISSING DATA TICKER DASHBOARD
// PURPOSE:
// Creates a clear Dashboard section showing tickers that
// may need correction because GOOGLEFINANCE did not return
// usable data.
// =====================================================

function createUnsupportedTickerDashboard() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) {
    throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");
  }

  if (!dash) {
    throw new Error("Dashboard sheet not found.");
  }

  const data = input.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];

  const tickerCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker");
  const companyCol = colIndex(headers, "Company");
  const priceCol = colIndex(headers, "Share Price");
  const marketCapCol = colIndex(headers, "Market Cap");
  const peCol = colIndex(headers, "PE Ratio");
  const epsCol = colIndex(headers, "EPS");
  const betaCol = colIndex(headers, "Beta");
  const high52Col = colIndex(headers, "52 Week High");
  const low52Col = colIndex(headers, "52 Week Low");
  const statusCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker Data Status");

  const rows = [
    [
      "Ticker",
      "Company",
      "Share Price",
      "Market Cap",
      "PE Ratio",
      "EPS",
      "Beta",
      "52W High",
      "52W Low",
      "Ticker Data Status",
      "Suggested Action"
    ]
  ];

  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {

    const row = data[r];
    const ticker = row[tickerCol];

    if (!ticker) continue;

    const price = num(row[priceCol]);
    const marketCap = num(row[marketCapCol]);
    const high52 = num(row[high52Col]);
    const low52 = num(row[low52Col]);

    const status = statusCol >= 0 ? row[statusCol] : "";

    const hasMajorIssue =
      !price ||
      !marketCap ||
      !high52 ||
      !low52 ||
      status === "CHECK TICKER FORMAT" ||
      String(status).indexOf("NO PRICE DATA") >= 0;

    if (!hasMajorIssue) continue;

    let action = "Review ticker format / exchange prefix";

    if (String(ticker).indexOf("KLSE:") === 0) {
      action = "Malaysia ticker may require KLSE format check";
    } else if (String(ticker).indexOf("SWX:") === 0) {
      action = "Swiss ticker may require GoogleFinance-supported symbol";
    } else if (String(ticker).indexOf("NYSE:") === 0 || String(ticker).indexOf("NASDAQ:") === 0) {
      action = "Check if ticker is supported or use alternate listing";
    }

    rows.push([
      ticker,
      companyCol >= 0 ? row[companyCol] : "",
      row[priceCol],
      row[marketCapCol],
      peCol >= 0 ? row[peCol] : "",
      epsCol >= 0 ? row[epsCol] : "",
      betaCol >= 0 ? row[betaCol] : "",
      row[high52Col],
      row[low52Col],
      status,
      action
    ]);
  }

  // =====================================================
  // DYNAMIC DASHBOARD LOCATION
  // Adds this section after the latest dashboard section.
  // =====================================================

  const props = PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties();
  const startRow = Number(props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_NEXT_ROW")) || findNextDashboardRow_(dash, 1, 12);
  const startCol = 1;

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, Math.max(rows.length + 5, 20), rows[0].length)
    .clearContent();

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol)
    .setValue("Unsupported / Missing Data Ticker Dashboard");

  dash.getRange(startRow + 2, startCol, rows.length, rows[0].length)
    .setValues(rows);

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol)
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(12)
    .setBackground("#fce5cd")
    .setFontColor("#783f04");

  dash.getRange(startRow + 2, startCol, 1, rows[0].length)
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff");

  const dataRows = Math.max(rows.length - 1, 1);

  dash.getRange(startRow + 3, startCol + 2, dataRows, 7)
    .setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");

  dash.autoResizeColumns(startCol, rows[0].length);

  props.setProperty("DASHBOARD_UNSUPPORTED_START", String(startRow + 3));
  props.setProperty("DASHBOARD_NEXT_ROW", String(startRow + rows.length + 6));
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 42A — UNSUPPORTED TICKER CONDITIONAL FORMATTING
// PURPOSE:
// Highlights problematic tickers and suggested actions.
// =====================================================

function applyUnsupportedTickerDashboardFormatting() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!dash) return;

  const props = PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties();
  const startRow = Number(props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_UNSUPPORTED_START"));

  if (!startRow) return;

  const rows = detectTableLength(dash, startRow, 1);

  if (rows <= 0) return;

  const rules = dash.getConditionalFormatRules();

  const statusRange = dash.getRange(startRow, 10, rows, 1);
  const actionRange = dash.getRange(startRow, 11, rows, 1);

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextContains("CHECK TICKER FORMAT")
      .setBackground("#f4cccc")
      .setFontColor("#990000")
      .setRanges([statusRange])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextContains("NO PRICE DATA")
      .setBackground("#fce5cd")
      .setFontColor("#783f04")
      .setRanges([statusRange])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextContains("Review ticker")
      .setBackground("#fff2cc")
      .setFontColor("#7f6000")
      .setRanges([actionRange])
      .build()
  );

  dash.setConditionalFormatRules(rules);
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 43 — SYSTEM LOG + REFRESH TIMESTAMP ENGINE
// PURPOSE:
// Creates and updates a System Log sheet each time the
// full Overseer update runs.
// Tracks:
// - Last run timestamp
// - Total ticker count
// - Priced ticker count
// - Missing price count
// - Scored ticker count
// - Allocated ticker count
// - Buy candidate count
// - Data warning count
// - Dashboard next available row
// =====================================================

function updateSystemLog() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) {
    throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");
  }

  let log = ss.getSheetByName("System Log");

  if (!log) {
    log = ss.insertSheet("System Log");
  }

  const data = input.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];

  const tickerCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker");
  const priceCol = colIndex(headers, "Share Price");
  const scoreCol = colIndex(headers, "GoogleFinance Score");
  const allocationCol = colIndex(headers, "Portfolio Allocation %");
  const recommendationCol = colIndex(headers, "Final Recommendation");
  const statusCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker Data Status");

  let totalTickers = 0;
  let pricedTickers = 0;
  let missingPrice = 0;
  let scoredTickers = 0;
  let allocatedTickers = 0;
  let buyCandidates = 0;
  let dataWarnings = 0;

  const warningTickers = [];

  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {

    const row = data[r];
    const ticker = row[tickerCol];

    if (!ticker) continue;

    totalTickers++;

    const price = num(row[priceCol]);
    const score = num(row[scoreCol]);
    const allocation = num(row[allocationCol]);
    const recommendation = row[recommendationCol];
    const status = statusCol >= 0 ? row[statusCol] : "";

    if (price > 0) pricedTickers++;
    else missingPrice++;

    if (score > 0) scoredTickers++;
    if (allocation > 0) allocatedTickers++;
    if (recommendation === "BUY CANDIDATE") buyCandidates++;

    if (status && status !== "OK") {
      dataWarnings++;
      warningTickers.push(ticker + " (" + status + ")");
    }
  }

  const priceCoverage = totalTickers > 0 ? pricedTickers / totalTickers : 0;
  const scoreCoverage = totalTickers > 0 ? scoredTickers / totalTickers : 0;
  const allocationCoverage = totalTickers > 0 ? allocatedTickers / totalTickers : 0;

  const props = PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties();
  const dashboardNextRow = props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_NEXT_ROW") || "";

  // =====================================================
  // CREATE HEADER IF EMPTY
  // =====================================================

  if (log.getLastRow() === 0) {
    log.getRange(1, 1, 1, 13).setValues([[
      "Timestamp",
      "Total Tickers",
      "Priced Tickers",
      "Missing Price",
      "Price Coverage %",
      "Scored Tickers",
      "Score Coverage %",
      "Allocated Tickers",
      "Allocation Coverage %",
      "Buy Candidates",
      "Data Warnings",
      "Dashboard Next Row",
      "Warning Details"
    ]]);
  }

  // =====================================================
  // APPEND LATEST RUN
  // =====================================================

  log.appendRow([
    new Date(),
    totalTickers,
    pricedTickers,
    missingPrice,
    priceCoverage,
    scoredTickers,
    scoreCoverage,
    allocatedTickers,
    allocationCoverage,
    buyCandidates,
    dataWarnings,
    dashboardNextRow,
    warningTickers.slice(0, 20).join(" | ")
  ]);

  formatSystemLog(log);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 43A — FORMAT SYSTEM LOG
// PURPOSE:
// Formats the System Log sheet for readability.
// =====================================================

function formatSystemLog(log) {

  const lastRow = Math.max(log.getLastRow(), 2);
  const lastCol = Math.max(log.getLastColumn(), 13);

  log.getDataRange().setFontFamily("Arial");
  log.setFrozenRows(1);

  log.getRange(1, 1, 1, lastCol)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  log.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 1)
    .setNumberFormat("dd/mm/yyyy hh:mm:ss");

  log.getRange(2, 5, lastRow - 1, 1)
    .setNumberFormat("0.00%");

  log.getRange(2, 7, lastRow - 1, 1)
    .setNumberFormat("0.00%");

  log.getRange(2, 9, lastRow - 1, 1)
    .setNumberFormat("0.00%");

  log.autoResizeColumns(1, lastCol);

  // Conditional formatting
  const rules = [];

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenNumberGreaterThan(0)
      .setBackground("#f4cccc")
      .setFontColor("#990000")
      .setRanges([log.getRange(2, 4, lastRow - 1, 1)])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenNumberGreaterThan(0)
      .setBackground("#fce5cd")
      .setFontColor("#783f04")
      .setRanges([log.getRange(2, 11, lastRow - 1, 1)])
      .build()
  );

  log.setConditionalFormatRules(rules);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 43B — DASHBOARD LOG SUMMARY PANEL
// PURPOSE:
// Adds latest System Log status into the Dashboard
// right-side panel below the navigation/status panel.
// =====================================================

function createDashboardSystemLogPanel() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);
  const log = ss.getSheetByName("System Log");

  if (!dash || !log || log.getLastRow() < 2) return;

  const lastRow = log.getLastRow();
  const latest = log.getRange(lastRow, 1, 1, 13).getValues()[0];

  const startRow = 25;
  const startCol = 14; // Column N

  const table = [
    ["Latest System Log", ""],
    ["Timestamp", latest[0]],
    ["Total Tickers", latest[1]],
    ["Priced Tickers", latest[2]],
    ["Missing Price", latest[3]],
    ["Price Coverage %", latest[4]],
    ["Data Warnings", latest[10]]
  ];

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, 10, 3).clearContent();

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, table.length, 2)
    .setValues(table);

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, 1, 2)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  dash.getRange(startRow + 1, startCol + 1)
    .setNumberFormat("dd/mm/yyyy hh:mm:ss");

  dash.getRange(startRow + 5, startCol + 1)
    .setNumberFormat("0.00%");

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, table.length, 2)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  dash.autoResizeColumns(startCol, 3);
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 44 — TICKER FORMAT SUGGESTION ENGINE
// PURPOSE:
// Adds clearer correction suggestions for unsupported or
// missing-data tickers.
// This helps users fix GOOGLEFINANCE ticker formats faster.
// =====================================================

function runTickerFormatSuggestionEngine() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) {
    throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");
  }

  // Ensure suggestion column exists
  ensureTickerSuggestionHeader(input);

  const data = input.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];

  const tickerCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker");
  const priceCol = colIndex(headers, "Share Price");
  const companyCol = colIndex(headers, "Company");
  const statusCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker Data Status");
  const suggestionCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker Format Suggestion");
  const remarksCol = colIndex(headers, "Remarks");

  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {

    const row = data[r];
    const ticker = row[tickerCol];

    if (!ticker) continue;

    const rowNumber = r + 1;
    const price = num(row[priceCol]);
    const company = companyCol >= 0 ? row[companyCol] : "";
    const status = statusCol >= 0 ? row[statusCol] : "";

    let suggestion = "OK";

    if (price > 0 && company) {
      suggestion = "OK - GoogleFinance data available";
    } else {
      suggestion = buildTickerSuggestion_(ticker, status);
    }

    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, suggestionCol, suggestion);

    if (remarksCol >= 0 && suggestion !== "OK - GoogleFinance data available") {
      setCellByIndex(
        input,
        rowNumber,
        remarksCol,
        "Ticker suggestion: " + suggestion
      );
    }
  }

  formatTickerSuggestionColumn(input);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 44A — ENSURE TICKER SUGGESTION HEADER
// PURPOSE:
// Adds Ticker Format Suggestion column if missing.
// =====================================================

function ensureTickerSuggestionHeader(input) {

  let headers = getHeaders(input);

  if (!headers.includes("Ticker Format Suggestion")) {
    const nextCol = input.getLastColumn() + 1;
    input.getRange(1, nextCol).setValue("Ticker Format Suggestion");
  }

  input.getRange(1, 1, 1, input.getLastColumn())
    .setFontWeight("bold");
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 44B — BUILD TICKER SUGGESTION
// PURPOSE:
// Provides practical ticker-format guidance based on common
// GOOGLEFINANCE exchange prefix issues.
// =====================================================

function buildTickerSuggestion_(ticker, status) {

  const t = String(ticker).trim().toUpperCase();

  if (!t) return "Blank ticker";

  if (String(status).indexOf("CHECK TICKER FORMAT") >= 0) {
    return "Check exchange prefix or unsupported ticker in GOOGLEFINANCE";
  }

  if (t.indexOf(":") < 0) {
    return "Add exchange prefix, e.g. NYSE:XXX, NASDAQ:XXX, KLSE:XXX";
  }

  if (t.indexOf("KLSE:") === 0) {
    return "Malaysia ticker: verify GOOGLEFINANCE support; try exact Bursa symbol without suffix";
  }

  if (t.indexOf("SWX:") === 0) {
    return "Swiss ticker: verify GOOGLEFINANCE exchange support; try VTX: or SIX: alternative if needed";
  }

  if (t.indexOf("EPA:") === 0) {
    return "Euronext Paris ticker: verify GOOGLEFINANCE support; try EPA symbol or alternate listing";
  }

  if (t.indexOf("HKG:") === 0) {
    return "Hong Kong ticker: check leading zero format, e.g. HKG:0700";
  }

  if (t.indexOf("KRX:") === 0) {
    return "Korea ticker: verify KRX code and leading zeros";
  }

  if (t.indexOf("NYSE:") === 0 || t.indexOf("NASDAQ:") === 0) {
    return "US ticker: check if symbol is listed, delisted, renamed, or unsupported by GOOGLEFINANCE";
  }

  if (String(status).indexOf("NO PRICE DATA") >= 0) {
    return "No price data returned; review ticker format and exchange prefix";
  }

  return "Review ticker format / exchange prefix";
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 44C — DASHBOARD TICKER SUGGESTIONS
// PURPOSE:
// Adds a compact dashboard table showing problematic tickers
// and their correction suggestions.
// =====================================================

function createTickerSuggestionDashboard() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input || !dash) return;

  const data = input.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];

  const tickerCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker");
  const companyCol = colIndex(headers, "Company");
  const priceCol = colIndex(headers, "Share Price");
  const statusCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker Data Status");
  const suggestionCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker Format Suggestion");

  const rows = [
    ["Ticker", "Company", "Price", "Data Status", "Ticker Format Suggestion"]
  ];

  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {

    const row = data[r];

    if (!row[tickerCol]) continue;

    const price = num(row[priceCol]);
    const status = statusCol >= 0 ? row[statusCol] : "";
    const suggestion = suggestionCol >= 0 ? row[suggestionCol] : "";

    const needsReview =
      !price ||
      status !== "OK" ||
      (suggestion && String(suggestion).indexOf("OK") !== 0);

    if (!needsReview) continue;

    rows.push([
      row[tickerCol],
      companyCol >= 0 ? row[companyCol] : "",
      row[priceCol],
      status,
      suggestion
    ]);
  }

  const props = PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties();
  const startRow = Number(props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_NEXT_ROW")) || findNextDashboardRow_(dash, 1, 12);
  const startCol = 1;

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, Math.max(rows.length + 5, 20), rows[0].length)
    .clearContent();

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol)
    .setValue("Ticker Format Suggestions");

  dash.getRange(startRow + 2, startCol, rows.length, rows[0].length)
    .setValues(rows);

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol)
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(12)
    .setBackground("#fce5cd")
    .setFontColor("#783f04");

  dash.getRange(startRow + 2, startCol, 1, rows[0].length)
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff");

  const dataRows = Math.max(rows.length - 1, 1);

  dash.getRange(startRow + 3, startCol + 2, dataRows, 1)
    .setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");

  dash.autoResizeColumns(startCol, rows[0].length);

  props.setProperty("DASHBOARD_TICKER_SUGGESTION_START", String(startRow + 3));
  props.setProperty("DASHBOARD_NEXT_ROW", String(startRow + rows.length + 6));
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 44D — FORMAT TICKER SUGGESTION COLUMN
// PURPOSE:
// Applies colour formatting to the suggestion column.
// =====================================================

function formatTickerSuggestionColumn(input) {

  const headers = getHeaders(input);
  const suggestionCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker Format Suggestion");

  if (suggestionCol < 0) return;

  const lastRow = Math.max(input.getLastRow(), 2);
  const range = input.getRange(2, suggestionCol + 1, lastRow - 1, 1);
  const rules = input.getConditionalFormatRules();

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextContains("OK")
      .setBackground("#d9ead3")
      .setFontColor("#274e13")
      .setRanges([range])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextContains("Check")
      .setBackground("#f4cccc")
      .setFontColor("#990000")
      .setRanges([range])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextContains("verify")
      .setBackground("#fff2cc")
      .setFontColor("#7f6000")
      .setRanges([range])
      .build()
  );

  input.setConditionalFormatRules(rules);
  input.autoResizeColumns(1, input.getLastColumn());
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 45 — DASHBOARD TOP 10 DECISION VIEW
// PURPOSE:
// Adds a concise executive decision table to the Dashboard.
// This gives a quick Top 10 view based on:
// - GoogleFinance Score
// - Final Recommendation
// - Earnings Yield
// - Upside to 52W High
// - Beta Risk Group
// - Portfolio Allocation
// =====================================================

function createDashboardTop10DecisionView() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) {
    throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");
  }

  if (!dash) {
    throw new Error("Dashboard sheet not found.");
  }

  const data = input.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];

  const tickerCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker");
  const companyCol = colIndex(headers, "Company");
  const priceCol = colIndex(headers, "Share Price");
  const peCol = colIndex(headers, "PE Ratio");
  const scoreCol = colIndex(headers, "GoogleFinance Score");
  const earningsYieldCol = colIndex(headers, "Earnings Yield %");
  const upsideCol = colIndex(headers, "Upside to 52W High %");
  const betaRiskCol = colIndex(headers, "Beta Risk Group");
  const momentumCol = colIndex(headers, "Momentum Signal");
  const allocationCol = colIndex(headers, "Portfolio Allocation %");
  const recommendationCol = colIndex(headers, "Final Recommendation");
  const watchlistCol = colIndex(headers, "Watchlist Status");
  const statusCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker Data Status");

  const stocks = [];

  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {

    const row = data[r];

    if (!row[tickerCol]) continue;

    const price = num(row[priceCol]);
    const score = num(row[scoreCol]);

    // Exclude tickers with no usable market data.
    if (!price || !score) continue;

    stocks.push({
      ticker: row[tickerCol],
      company: companyCol >= 0 ? row[companyCol] : "",
      price: price,
      pe: num(row[peCol]),
      score: score,
      earningsYield: num(row[earningsYieldCol]),
      upside: num(row[upsideCol]),
      betaRisk: row[betaRiskCol],
      momentum: row[momentumCol],
      allocation: num(row[allocationCol]),
      recommendation: row[recommendationCol],
      watchlist: row[watchlistCol],
      status: statusCol >= 0 ? row[statusCol] : ""
    });
  }

  // =====================================================
  // DECISION SORTING
  // Priority:
  // 1. BUY CANDIDATE
  // 2. ACCUMULATE / STUDY
  // 3. Higher score
  // 4. Higher allocation
  // =====================================================

  const recommendationRank = {
    "BUY CANDIDATE": 5,
    "ACCUMULATE / STUDY": 4,
    "VALUE WATCH": 3,
    "HOLD / MONITOR": 2,
    "AVOID / HIGH RISK": 1
  };

  stocks.sort((a, b) => {
    const recA = recommendationRank[a.recommendation] || 0;
    const recB = recommendationRank[b.recommendation] || 0;

    if (recB !== recA) return recB - recA;
    if (b.score !== a.score) return b.score - a.score;
    return b.allocation - a.allocation;
  });

  const top10 = stocks.slice(0, 10);

  const rows = [
    [
      "Rank",
      "Ticker",
      "Company",
      "Price",
      "PE",
      "Score",
      "Earnings Yield %",
      "Upside to 52W High %",
      "Beta Risk",
      "Momentum",
      "Allocation %",
      "Recommendation",
      "Watchlist"
    ]
  ];

  top10.forEach((s, i) => {
    rows.push([
      i + 1,
      s.ticker,
      s.company,
      s.price,
      s.pe,
      s.score,
      s.earningsYield,
      s.upside,
      s.betaRisk,
      s.momentum,
      s.allocation,
      s.recommendation,
      s.watchlist
    ]);
  });

  // =====================================================
  // DASHBOARD LOCATION
  // Fixed near top left, below summary cards, before full tables.
  // This is intentionally short and does not create overlap.
  // =====================================================

  const startRow = 9;
  const startCol = 1;

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, 15, rows[0].length)
    .clearContent();

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol)
    .setValue("Top 10 Decision View");

  dash.getRange(startRow + 2, startCol, rows.length, rows[0].length)
    .setValues(rows);

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol)
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(12)
    .setBackground("#d9e2f3")
    .setFontColor("#1f2933");

  dash.getRange(startRow + 2, startCol, 1, rows[0].length)
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff");

  const dataRows = Math.max(rows.length - 1, 1);

  dash.getRange(startRow + 3, startCol + 3, dataRows, 3)
    .setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");

  dash.getRange(startRow + 3, startCol + 6, dataRows, 2)
    .setNumberFormat("0.00%");

  dash.getRange(startRow + 3, startCol + 10, dataRows, 1)
    .setNumberFormat("0.00%");

  dash.autoResizeColumns(startCol, rows[0].length);

  PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties()
    .setProperty("DASHBOARD_TOP10_START", String(startRow + 3));
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 45A — TOP 10 DECISION VIEW FORMATTING
// PURPOSE:
// Adds colour formatting to Top 10 Recommendation and Score.
// =====================================================

function applyTop10DecisionViewFormatting() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!dash) return;

  const props = PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties();
  const startRow = Number(props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_TOP10_START")) || 12;

  const rows = detectTableLength(dash, startRow, 2);
  if (rows <= 0) return;

  const rules = dash.getConditionalFormatRules();

  const scoreRange = dash.getRange(startRow, 6, rows, 1);
  const recommendationRange = dash.getRange(startRow, 12, rows, 1);
  const betaRiskRange = dash.getRange(startRow, 9, rows, 1);

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .setGradientMinpointWithValue("#f4cccc", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "0")
      .setGradientMidpointWithValue("#fff2cc", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "50")
      .setGradientMaxpointWithValue("#d9ead3", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "100")
      .setRanges([scoreRange])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("BUY CANDIDATE")
      .setBackground("#b6d7a8")
      .setFontColor("#274e13")
      .setRanges([recommendationRange])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("ACCUMULATE / STUDY")
      .setBackground("#d9ead3")
      .setFontColor("#274e13")
      .setRanges([recommendationRange])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("VALUE WATCH")
      .setBackground("#cfe2f3")
      .setFontColor("#073763")
      .setRanges([recommendationRange])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("LOW RISK")
      .setBackground("#d9ead3")
      .setFontColor("#274e13")
      .setRanges([betaRiskRange])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("HIGH RISK")
      .setBackground("#fce5cd")
      .setFontColor("#783f04")
      .setRanges([betaRiskRange])
      .build()
  );

  dash.setConditionalFormatRules(rules);
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 46 — HISTORICAL SNAPSHOT OPTIMIZATION
// PURPOSE:
// Optimizes the Dashboard historical snapshot by reading from
// the compact History Summary sheet instead of placing many
// GOOGLEFINANCE formulas directly in the Dashboard.
// BENEFIT:
// - Faster Dashboard
// - Less formula duplication
// - Lower risk of overlapping array formulas
// - Cleaner separation between data and presentation
// =====================================================

function createOptimizedDashboardHistoricalSnapshot() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);
  const summary = ss.getSheetByName("History Summary");

  if (!dash) {
    throw new Error("Dashboard sheet not found.");
  }

  if (!summary) {
    throw new Error("History Summary sheet not found. Run createHistorySummarySheet() first.");
  }

  const summaryData = summary.getDataRange().getValues();

  if (summaryData.length < 2) {
    return;
  }

  const headers = summaryData[0];

  const tickerCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker");
  const currentCol = colIndex(headers, "Current Price");
  const price1YCol = colIndex(headers, "Price 1Y Ago");
  const price3YCol = colIndex(headers, "Price 3Y Ago");
  const price5YCol = colIndex(headers, "Price 5Y Ago");
  const price10YCol = colIndex(headers, "Price 10Y Ago");
  const return1YCol = colIndex(headers, "1Y Return %");
  const return3YCol = colIndex(headers, "3Y Return %");
  const return5YCol = colIndex(headers, "5Y Return %");
  const return10YCol = colIndex(headers, "10Y Return %");

  const rows = [
    [
      "Ticker",
      "Current Price",
      "Price 1Y Ago",
      "Price 3Y Ago",
      "Price 5Y Ago",
      "Price 10Y Ago",
      "1Y Return %",
      "3Y Return %",
      "5Y Return %",
      "10Y Return %"
    ]
  ];

  for (let r = 1; r < summaryData.length; r++) {

    const row = summaryData[r];

    if (!row[tickerCol]) continue;

    rows.push([
      row[tickerCol],
      row[currentCol],
      row[price1YCol],
      row[price3YCol],
      row[price5YCol],
      row[price10YCol],
      row[return1YCol],
      row[return3YCol],
      row[return5YCol],
      row[return10YCol]
    ]);
  }

  const props = PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties();
  const startRow = Number(props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_NEXT_ROW")) || findNextDashboardRow_(dash, 1, 12);
  const startCol = 1;

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, Math.max(rows.length + 5, 20), rows[0].length)
    .clearContent();

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol)
    .setValue("Historical Share Price Snapshot");

  dash.getRange(startRow + 2, startCol, rows.length, rows[0].length)
    .setValues(rows);

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol)
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(12)
    .setBackground("#d9e2f3")
    .setFontColor("#1f2933");

  dash.getRange(startRow + 2, startCol, 1, rows[0].length)
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff");

  const dataRows = Math.max(rows.length - 1, 1);

  dash.getRange(startRow + 3, startCol + 1, dataRows, 5)
    .setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");

  dash.getRange(startRow + 3, startCol + 6, dataRows, 4)
    .setNumberFormat("0.00%");

  dash.autoResizeColumns(startCol, rows[0].length);

  props.setProperty("DASHBOARD_HISTORY_START", String(startRow + 3));
  props.setProperty("DASHBOARD_NEXT_ROW", String(startRow + rows.length + 6));
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 46A — HISTORY SUMMARY FORMULA OPTIMIZATION
// PURPOSE:
// Adds formulas only to History Summary sheet and keeps
// Dashboard formula-light.
// =====================================================

function refreshOptimizedHistorySummary() {

  // This wrapper keeps naming clear in the master runner.
  // It uses the existing Module 38 function.
  createHistorySummarySheet();
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 46B — HISTORICAL SNAPSHOT PERFORMANCE NOTE
// PURPOSE:
// Adds a small note to Dashboard explaining that historical
// values are sourced from History Summary.
// =====================================================

function addHistoricalSnapshotPerformanceNote() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!dash) return;

  const props = PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties();
  const historyStart = Number(props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_HISTORY_START"));

  if (!historyStart) return;

  const noteRow = historyStart - 2;

  dash.getRange(noteRow, 12)
    .setValue("Source: History Summary")
    .setFontStyle("italic")
    .setFontColor("#666666");
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 47 — ERROR LOG SHEET
// PURPOSE:
// Creates a dedicated Error Log sheet for data issues,
// ticker problems, missing GoogleFinance outputs,
// and dashboard/system warnings.
// This is separate from System Log:
// - System Log = run summary
// - Error Log = row-level and ticker-level issues
// =====================================================

function updateErrorLogSheet() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) {
    throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");
  }

  let errorLog = ss.getSheetByName("Error Log");

  if (!errorLog) {
    errorLog = ss.insertSheet("Error Log");
  }

  errorLog.clear();

  const data = input.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];

  const tickerCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker");
  const companyCol = colIndex(headers, "Company");
  const priceCol = colIndex(headers, "Share Price");
  const marketCapCol = colIndex(headers, "Market Cap");
  const peCol = colIndex(headers, "PE Ratio");
  const epsCol = colIndex(headers, "EPS");
  const betaCol = colIndex(headers, "Beta");
  const high52Col = colIndex(headers, "52 Week High");
  const low52Col = colIndex(headers, "52 Week Low");
  const statusCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker Data Status");
  const suggestionCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker Format Suggestion");
  const recommendationCol = colIndex(headers, "Final Recommendation");

  const rows = [
    [
      "Timestamp",
      "Row",
      "Ticker",
      "Company",
      "Issue Type",
      "Severity",
      "Details",
      "Suggested Action"
    ]
  ];

  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {

    const row = data[r];
    const ticker = row[tickerCol];

    if (!ticker) continue;

    const sheetRow = r + 1;
    const company = companyCol >= 0 ? row[companyCol] : "";
    const price = num(row[priceCol]);
    const marketCap = num(row[marketCapCol]);
    const pe = peCol >= 0 ? row[peCol] : "";
    const eps = epsCol >= 0 ? row[epsCol] : "";
    const beta = betaCol >= 0 ? row[betaCol] : "";
    const high52 = num(row[high52Col]);
    const low52 = num(row[low52Col]);
    const status = statusCol >= 0 ? row[statusCol] : "";
    const suggestion = suggestionCol >= 0 ? row[suggestionCol] : "";
    const recommendation = recommendationCol >= 0 ? row[recommendationCol] : "";

    // =====================================================
    // CRITICAL — No price data
    // =====================================================

    if (!price) {
      rows.push([
        new Date(),
        sheetRow,
        ticker,
        company,
        "Missing Share Price",
        "CRITICAL",
        "GOOGLEFINANCE did not return a valid share price.",
        suggestion || "Check ticker format / exchange prefix."
      ]);
    }

    // =====================================================
    // HIGH — No market cap
    // =====================================================

    if (!marketCap) {
      rows.push([
        new Date(),
        sheetRow,
        ticker,
        company,
        "Missing Market Cap",
        "HIGH",
        "Market Cap is missing, so shares outstanding and size category may be unreliable.",
        suggestion || "Check GoogleFinance support for this ticker."
      ]);
    }

    // =====================================================
    // MEDIUM — No PE / EPS data
    // =====================================================

    if (pe === "" || pe == null) {
      rows.push([
        new Date(),
        sheetRow,
        ticker,
        company,
        "Missing PE Ratio",
        "MEDIUM",
        "PE Ratio is missing. Valuation score may rely on limited data.",
        "Review if company has negative earnings or unsupported PE data."
      ]);
    }

    if (eps === "" || eps == null) {
      rows.push([
        new Date(),
        sheetRow,
        ticker,
        company,
        "Missing EPS",
        "MEDIUM",
        "EPS is missing. Earnings Yield cannot be calculated properly.",
        "Review earnings data or import fundamentals manually later."
      ]);
    }

    // =====================================================
    // MEDIUM — No Beta data
    // =====================================================

    if (beta === "" || beta == null) {
      rows.push([
        new Date(),
        sheetRow,
        ticker,
        company,
        "Missing Beta",
        "MEDIUM",
        "Beta is missing. Risk bucket defaults may be limited.",
        "Review ticker support or manually input beta if needed."
      ]);
    }

    // =====================================================
    // HIGH — No 52-week range
    // =====================================================

    if (!high52 || !low52) {
      rows.push([
        new Date(),
        sheetRow,
        ticker,
        company,
        "Missing 52W Range",
        "HIGH",
        "52 Week High / Low missing. Momentum and upside calculations may be unavailable.",
        "Check ticker format or GoogleFinance support."
      ]);
    }

    // =====================================================
    // HIGH — Data status warning
    // =====================================================

    if (status && status !== "OK") {
      rows.push([
        new Date(),
        sheetRow,
        ticker,
        company,
        "Ticker Data Status Warning",
        "HIGH",
        status,
        suggestion || "Review ticker data status."
      ]);
    }

    // =====================================================
    // INFO — Avoid recommendation
    // =====================================================

    if (recommendation === "AVOID / HIGH RISK") {
      rows.push([
        new Date(),
        sheetRow,
        ticker,
        company,
        "Avoid / High Risk Flag",
        "INFO",
        "Ticker is classified as AVOID / HIGH RISK by the watchlist engine.",
        "Review score, beta risk, PE, EPS, and 52W position."
      ]);
    }
  }

  // =====================================================
  // WRITE ERROR LOG
  // =====================================================

  errorLog.getRange(1, 1, rows.length, rows[0].length)
    .setValues(rows);

  formatErrorLogSheet(errorLog);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 47A — FORMAT ERROR LOG SHEET
// PURPOSE:
// Formats Error Log for readability and severity scanning.
// =====================================================

function formatErrorLogSheet(errorLog) {

  const lastRow = Math.max(errorLog.getLastRow(), 2);
  const lastCol = Math.max(errorLog.getLastColumn(), 8);

  errorLog.getDataRange().setFontFamily("Arial");
  errorLog.setFrozenRows(1);

  errorLog.getRange(1, 1, 1, lastCol)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  errorLog.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 1)
    .setNumberFormat("dd/mm/yyyy hh:mm:ss");

  errorLog.autoResizeColumns(1, lastCol);

  const rules = [];

  const severityRange = errorLog.getRange(2, 6, lastRow - 1, 1);

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("CRITICAL")
      .setBackground("#f4cccc")
      .setFontColor("#990000")
      .setRanges([severityRange])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("HIGH")
      .setBackground("#fce5cd")
      .setFontColor("#783f04")
      .setRanges([severityRange])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("MEDIUM")
      .setBackground("#fff2cc")
      .setFontColor("#7f6000")
      .setRanges([severityRange])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("INFO")
      .setBackground("#d9ead3")
      .setFontColor("#274e13")
      .setRanges([severityRange])
      .build()
  );

  errorLog.setConditionalFormatRules(rules);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 47B — DASHBOARD ERROR LOG SUMMARY PANEL
// PURPOSE:
// Shows latest Error Log counts on Dashboard right panel.
// =====================================================

function createDashboardErrorLogPanel() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);
  const errorLog = ss.getSheetByName("Error Log");

  if (!dash || !errorLog || errorLog.getLastRow() < 2) return;

  const data = errorLog.getDataRange().getValues();

  let critical = 0;
  let high = 0;
  let medium = 0;
  let info = 0;

  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {
    const severity = data[r][5];

    if (severity === "CRITICAL") critical++;
    else if (severity === "HIGH") high++;
    else if (severity === "MEDIUM") medium++;
    else if (severity === "INFO") info++;
  }

  const startRow = 34;
  const startCol = 14; // Column N

  const table = [
    ["Error Log Summary", ""],
    ["Critical", critical],
    ["High", high],
    ["Medium", medium],
    ["Info", info],
    ["Total Issues", critical + high + medium + info]
  ];

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, 10, 3).clearContent();

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, table.length, 2)
    .setValues(table);

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, 1, 2)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, table.length, 2)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  dash.autoResizeColumns(startCol, 3);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 47C — ERROR LOG DASHBOARD FORMATTING
// PURPOSE:
// Adds colour cues to the dashboard error summary.
// =====================================================

function applyDashboardErrorLogPanelFormatting() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!dash) return;

  const rules = dash.getConditionalFormatRules();

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenNumberGreaterThan(0)
      .setBackground("#f4cccc")
      .setFontColor("#990000")
      .setRanges([dash.getRange("O35")])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenNumberGreaterThan(0)
      .setBackground("#fce5cd")
      .setFontColor("#783f04")
      .setRanges([dash.getRange("O36")])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenNumberGreaterThan(0)
      .setBackground("#fff2cc")
      .setFontColor("#7f6000")
      .setRanges([dash.getRange("O37")])
      .build()
  );

  dash.setConditionalFormatRules(rules);
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 48 — INPUT PROTECTION / USER ZONE
// PURPOSE:
// Protects calculated/formula columns in the Input sheet
// while keeping the Ticker column editable for manual input.
// IMPORTANT:
// Apps Script protections follow Google Sheets permissions.
// The owner can always edit protected ranges.
// =====================================================

function applyInputProtectionUserZone() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) {
    throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");
  }

  const headers = getHeaders(input);
  const tickerCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker") + 1;

  if (tickerCol <= 0) {
    throw new Error("Ticker column not found.");
  }

  // =====================================================
  // STEP 1 — REMOVE OLD PROTECTIONS CREATED BY THIS SCRIPT
  // =====================================================

  const protections = input.getProtections(SpreadsheetApp.ProtectionType.RANGE);

  protections.forEach(p => {
    const description = p.getDescription();
    if (description && description.indexOf("Overseer Protected") >= 0) {
      p.remove();
    }
  });

  // =====================================================
  // STEP 2 — PROTECT ALL NON-TICKER COLUMNS
  // This leaves only Ticker column editable.
  // =====================================================

  const lastCol = input.getLastColumn();
  const lastRow = Math.max(input.getMaxRows(), 2);

  for (let c = 1; c <= lastCol; c++) {

    if (c === tickerCol) continue;

    const range = input.getRange(1, c, lastRow, 1);

    const protection = range.protect()
      .setDescription("Overseer Protected - Calculated / Formula Column");

    // Warning-only mode allows editing after warning.
    // Change to false later if you want hard protection.
    protection.setWarningOnly(true);
  }

  // =====================================================
  // STEP 3 — STYLE USER INPUT COLUMN
  // =====================================================

  input.getRange(1, tickerCol)
    .setBackground("#0b5394")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  input.getRange(2, tickerCol, Math.max(input.getLastRow() - 1, 1), 1)
    .setBackground("#d9eaf7");

  // =====================================================
  // STEP 4 — ADD USER GUIDE NOTE
  // =====================================================

  input.getRange(1, tickerCol)
    .setNote("Manual input zone: enter ticker only. Example: NYSE:KO, NASDAQ:MSFT, HKG:0700.");

  input.autoResizeColumns(1, input.getLastColumn());
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 48A — REMOVE INPUT PROTECTION
// PURPOSE:
// Removes Overseer-created protections if you need to edit
// all columns manually.
// =====================================================

function removeInputProtectionUserZone() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) {
    throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");
  }

  const protections = input.getProtections(SpreadsheetApp.ProtectionType.RANGE);

  protections.forEach(p => {
    const description = p.getDescription();
    if (description && description.indexOf("Overseer Protected") >= 0) {
      p.remove();
    }
  });

  SpreadsheetApp.getUi()
    .alert("Overseer input protections removed.");
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 48B — USER INPUT GUIDE SHEET
// PURPOSE:
// Creates a simple guide sheet explaining which areas are
// manual and which are automated.
// =====================================================

function createUserInputGuideSheet() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  let guide = ss.getSheetByName("User Guide");

  if (!guide) {
    guide = ss.insertSheet("User Guide");
  }

  guide.clear();

  const rows = [
    ["Stocks Overseer Advisor — User Input Guide", ""],
    ["Manual Input Required", "Ticker only"],
    ["Main Editable Column", "Input sheet > Ticker"],
    ["Example Tickers", "NYSE:KO, NASDAQ:MSFT, HKG:0700, EPA:MC"],
    ["Do Not Manually Edit", "Formula/calculated columns unless intentionally overriding"],
    ["Main Run Function", "runFullOverseerUpdate"],
    ["Remove Protection Function", "removeInputProtectionUserZone"],
    ["Protection Mode", "Warning only — user can still edit after warning"],
    ["Recommended Workflow", "1. Add ticker > 2. Run full update > 3. Review Dashboard / Error Log"],
    ["Notes", "GoogleFinance may not support every exchange/ticker format."]
  ];

  guide.getRange(1, 1, rows.length, 2)
    .setValues(rows);

  guide.getRange("A1:B1")
    .merge()
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(14);

  guide.getRange(2, 1, rows.length - 1, 1)
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  guide.getDataRange()
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  guide.autoResizeColumns(1, 2);
}

// =====================================================
// MODULE 49 — VISUAL INPUT UPGRADE / MANUAL INPUT HIGHLIGHT
// PURPOSE:
// Visually separates manual input cells from automated cells.
// Highlights:
// - Ticker column as the only required manual input
// - Formula / calculated columns as automated
// - Empty ticker cells as input-ready cells
// - Dashboard reminder panel for user workflow
// =====================================================

function applyVisualInputUpgrade() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) {
    throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");
  }

  const headers = getHeaders(input);
  const tickerCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker") + 1;

  if (tickerCol <= 0) {
    throw new Error("Ticker column not found.");
  }

  const lastRow = Math.max(input.getMaxRows(), 100);
  const lastCol = input.getLastColumn();

  // =====================================================
  // STEP 1 — BASE SHEET STYLE
  // =====================================================

  input.getDataRange()
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setVerticalAlignment("middle");

  input.setFrozenRows(1);
  input.setFrozenColumns(tickerCol);

  // Header row style
  input.getRange(1, 1, 1, lastCol)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  // =====================================================
  // STEP 2 — MANUAL INPUT COLUMN HIGHLIGHT
  // Ticker is the primary user-editable field.
  // =====================================================

  input.getRange(1, tickerCol)
    .setValue("Ticker")
    .setBackground("#0b5394")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setNote("MANUAL INPUT REQUIRED: Enter ticker only. Examples: NYSE:KO, NASDAQ:MSFT, HKG:0700.");

  input.getRange(2, tickerCol, lastRow - 1, 1)
    .setBackground("#d9eaf7")
    .setFontColor("#000000")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true, "#0b5394", SpreadsheetApp.BorderStyle.SOLID);

  // =====================================================
  // STEP 3 — AUTOMATED COLUMN SHADING
  // All non-ticker columns are automated / calculated zones.
  // =====================================================

  for (let c = 1; c <= lastCol; c++) {

    if (c === tickerCol) continue;

    input.getRange(1, c)
      .setNote("AUTOMATED / CALCULATED: This column is filled by GOOGLEFINANCE or Apps Script where data is available.");

    input.getRange(2, c, lastRow - 1, 1)
      .setBackground("#f7f7f7");
  }

  // =====================================================
  // STEP 4 — KEY OUTPUT COLUMN COLOUR GROUPS
  // Creates visual grouping for important decision columns.
  // =====================================================

  colourHeaderGroup_(input, headers, [
    "Company",
    "Currency",
    "Share Price",
    "Market Cap",
    "PE Ratio",
    "EPS",
    "Beta",
    "52 Week High",
    "52 Week Low",
    "Average Volume"
  ], "#d9ead3", "#274e13");

  colourHeaderGroup_(input, headers, [
    "Implied Shares Outstanding",
    "Earnings Yield %",
    "Upside to 52W High %",
    "Downside to 52W Low %",
    "52W Price Position %",
    "GoogleFinance Score",
    "Beta Risk Group",
    "Momentum Signal"
  ], "#d9e2f3", "#1c4587");

  colourHeaderGroup_(input, headers, [
    "Watchlist Status",
    "Final Recommendation",
    "Portfolio Allocation %",
    "Valuation Score",
    "Financial Strength Score",
    "Overall Investment Score",
    "Remarks"
  ], "#fff2cc", "#7f6000");

  colourHeaderGroup_(input, headers, [
    "Ticker Data Status",
    "Ticker Format Suggestion",
    "Data Source",
    "Last Updated"
  ], "#fce5cd", "#783f04");

  // =====================================================
  // STEP 5 — EMPTY TICKER INPUT READY CELLS
  // Adds a soft border to blank ticker cells.
  // =====================================================

  const tickerValues = input.getRange(2, tickerCol, lastRow - 1, 1).getValues();

  for (let i = 0; i < tickerValues.length; i++) {

    const cell = input.getRange(i + 2, tickerCol);

    if (!tickerValues[i][0]) {
      cell
        .setBackground("#eef7ff")
        .setNote("Ready for manual ticker input.");
    }
  }

  // =====================================================
  // STEP 6 — DATA VALIDATION HELP TEXT FOR TICKER COLUMN
  // Allows flexible ticker input while showing guidance.
  // =====================================================

  const tickerRule = SpreadsheetApp.newDataValidation()
    .requireTextIsNotEqualTo("")
    .setAllowInvalid(true)
    .setHelpText("Enter ticker with exchange prefix where possible. Examples: NYSE:KO, NASDAQ:MSFT, HKG:0700, EPA:MC.")
    .build();

  input.getRange(2, tickerCol, lastRow - 1, 1)
    .setDataValidation(tickerRule);

  input.autoResizeColumns(1, lastCol);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 49A — COLOUR HEADER GROUP HELPER
// PURPOSE:
// Applies header colour groups by header names.
// =====================================================

function colourHeaderGroup_(sheet, headers, headerNames, bg, font) {

  headerNames.forEach(header => {

    const c = colIndex(headers, header);

    if (c >= 0) {
      sheet.getRange(1, c + 1)
        .setBackground(bg)
        .setFontColor(font)
        .setFontWeight("bold");
    }
  });
}

// =====================================================

function createFundamentalImportSheet() {

  if (!importSheet) {
