}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 50A — IMPORT FUNDAMENTALS INTO INPUT
// PURPOSE:
// Maps manually pasted financial fundamentals from
// Fundamental Import into matching rows in Input sheet.
// =====================================================

function importManualFundamentalsToInput() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);
  const importSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Fundamental Import");

  if (!input) {
    throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");
  }

  if (!importSheet) {
    throw new Error("Fundamental Import sheet not found. Run createFundamentalImportSheet() first.");
  }

  const inputData = input.getDataRange().getValues();
  const inputHeaders = inputData[0];

  const importData = importSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const importHeaders = importData[0];

  const inputTickerCol = colIndex(inputHeaders, "Ticker");
  const importTickerCol = colIndex(importHeaders, "Ticker");

  if (inputTickerCol < 0 || importTickerCol < 0) {
    throw new Error("Ticker column missing in Input or Fundamental Import sheet.");
  }

  // Create ticker-to-row lookup for Input sheet
  const inputRowMap = {};

  for (let r = 1; r < inputData.length; r++) {
    const ticker = inputData[r][inputTickerCol];
    if (ticker) {
      inputRowMap[String(ticker).trim().toUpperCase()] = r + 1;
    }
  }

  // Headers that can be imported directly if they exist in both sheets
  const importableHeaders = [
    "Fiscal Year",
    "Revenue",
    "Cost of Revenue",
    "Gross Profit",
    "Operating Expenses",
    "EBITDA",
    "EBIT",
    "Interest Expense",
    "Pre-Tax Income",
    "Net Income",
    "Diluted EPS",
    "Operating Cash Flow",
    "Capital Expenditure (Capex)",
    "Free Cash Flow",
    "Cash & Equivalents",
    "Short-Term Debt",
    "Long-Term Debt",
    "Total Debt",
    "Total Assets",
    "Total Liabilities",
    "Shareholder Equity",
    "Inventory",
    "Accounts Receivable",
    "Accounts Payable",
    "Current Assets",
    "Current Liabilities",
    "Dividends Paid",
    "Dividend Per Share",
    "Book Value Per Share",
    "R&D Expense",
    "SG&A Expense",
    "Employee Count",
    "Notes"
  ];

  let importedCount = 0;
  let unmatchedCount = 0;

  for (let r = 1; r < importData.length; r++) {

    const importRow = importData[r];
    const ticker = importRow[importTickerCol];

    if (!ticker) continue;

    const key = String(ticker).trim().toUpperCase();
    const inputRowNumber = inputRowMap[key];

    if (!inputRowNumber) {
      unmatchedCount++;
      continue;
    }

    importableHeaders.forEach(header => {

      const importCol = colIndex(importHeaders, header);
      const inputCol = colIndex(inputHeaders, header);

      if (importCol >= 0 && inputCol >= 0) {
        const value = importRow[importCol];

        if (value !== "" && value != null) {
          input.getRange(inputRowNumber, inputCol + 1).setValue(value);
        }
      }
    });

    // Mark data source
    const sourceCol = colIndex(inputHeaders, "Data Source");
    if (sourceCol >= 0) {
      input.getRange(inputRowNumber, sourceCol + 1)
        .setValue("GOOGLEFINANCE + Manual Fundamental Import");
    }

    const remarksCol = colIndex(inputHeaders, "Remarks");
    if (remarksCol >= 0) {
      input.getRange(inputRowNumber, remarksCol + 1)
        .setValue("Manual fundamentals imported from Fundamental Import sheet.");
    }

    importedCount++;
  }

  // After import, calculate fundamental ratios
  calculateImportedFundamentalRatios();

  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert(
    "Manual fundamental import completed.\nImported rows: " +
    importedCount +
    "\nUnmatched tickers: " +
    unmatchedCount
  );
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 50B — CALCULATE IMPORTED FUNDAMENTAL RATIOS
// PURPOSE:
// Calculates ratios that require manually imported
// financial statement data.
// =====================================================

function calculateImportedFundamentalRatios() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) {
    throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");
  }

  const data = input.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];

  const tickerCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker");

  const revenueCol = colIndex(headers, "Revenue");
  const grossProfitCol = colIndex(headers, "Gross Profit");
  const ebitdaCol = colIndex(headers, "EBITDA");
  const ebitCol = colIndex(headers, "EBIT");
  const netIncomeCol = colIndex(headers, "Net Income");
  const ocfCol = colIndex(headers, "Operating Cash Flow");
  const capexCol = colIndex(headers, "Capital Expenditure (Capex)");
  const fcfCol = colIndex(headers, "Free Cash Flow");
  const totalDebtCol = colIndex(headers, "Total Debt");
  const cashCol = colIndex(headers, "Cash & Equivalents");
  const assetsCol = colIndex(headers, "Total Assets");
  const liabilitiesCol = colIndex(headers, "Total Liabilities");
  const equityCol = colIndex(headers, "Shareholder Equity");
  const currentAssetsCol = colIndex(headers, "Current Assets");
  const currentLiabilitiesCol = colIndex(headers, "Current Liabilities");
  const inventoryCol = colIndex(headers, "Inventory");
  const arCol = colIndex(headers, "Accounts Receivable");
  const apCol = colIndex(headers, "Accounts Payable");
  const interestExpenseCol = colIndex(headers, "Interest Expense");
  const marketCapCol = colIndex(headers, "Market Cap");
  const sharePriceCol = colIndex(headers, "Share Price");
  const epsCol = colIndex(headers, "EPS");
  const dpsCol = colIndex(headers, "Dividend Per Share");
  const bvpsCol = colIndex(headers, "Book Value Per Share");

  const grossMarginCol = colIndex(headers, "Gross Margin %");
  const ebitdaMarginCol = colIndex(headers, "EBITDA Margin %");
  const operatingMarginCol = colIndex(headers, "Operating Margin %");
  const netMarginCol = colIndex(headers, "Net Margin %");
  const roeCol = colIndex(headers, "ROE %");
  const roaCol = colIndex(headers, "ROA %");
  const debtEquityCol = colIndex(headers, "Debt-to-Equity");
  const currentRatioCol = colIndex(headers, "Current Ratio");
  const interestCoverageCol = colIndex(headers, "Interest Coverage");
  const assetTurnoverCol = colIndex(headers, "Asset Turnover");
  const inventoryTurnoverCol = colIndex(headers, "Inventory Turnover");
  const receivableDaysCol = colIndex(headers, "Receivable Days");
  const payableDaysCol = colIndex(headers, "Payable Days");
  const fcfYieldCol = colIndex(headers, "FCF Yield %");
  const dividendYieldCol = colIndex(headers, "Dividend Yield %");
  const payoutRatioCol = colIndex(headers, "Payout Ratio %");
  const retentionRatioCol = colIndex(headers, "Retention Ratio %");
  const pbRatioCol = colIndex(headers, "PB Ratio");
  const netDebtCol = colIndex(headers, "Net Debt");
  const netDebtEbitdaCol = colIndex(headers, "Net Debt/EBITDA");
  const cashConversionCol = colIndex(headers, "Cash Conversion Ratio");

  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {

    const row = data[r];
    if (!row[tickerCol]) continue;

    const rowNumber = r + 1;

    const revenue = num(row[revenueCol]);
    const grossProfit = num(row[grossProfitCol]);
    const ebitda = num(row[ebitdaCol]);
    const ebit = num(row[ebitCol]);
    const netIncome = num(row[netIncomeCol]);
    const ocf = num(row[ocfCol]);
    const capex = num(row[capexCol]);
    let fcf = num(row[fcfCol]);
    const totalDebt = num(row[totalDebtCol]);
    const cash = num(row[cashCol]);
    const assets = num(row[assetsCol]);
    const liabilities = num(row[liabilitiesCol]);
    const equity = num(row[equityCol]);
    const currentAssets = num(row[currentAssetsCol]);
    const currentLiabilities = num(row[currentLiabilitiesCol]);
    const inventory = num(row[inventoryCol]);
    const ar = num(row[arCol]);
    const ap = num(row[apCol]);
    const interestExpense = Math.abs(num(row[interestExpenseCol]));
    const marketCap = num(row[marketCapCol]);
    const sharePrice = num(row[sharePriceCol]);
    const eps = num(row[epsCol]);
    const dps = num(row[dpsCol]);
    const bvps = num(row[bvpsCol]);

    // Calculate FCF if blank and OCF / Capex exist
    if (!fcf && (ocf || capex)) {
      fcf = ocf - Math.abs(capex);
      setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, fcfCol, fcf);
    }

    // Margins
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, grossMarginCol, safeDiv(grossProfit, revenue));
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, ebitdaMarginCol, safeDiv(ebitda, revenue));
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, operatingMarginCol, safeDiv(ebit, revenue));
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, netMarginCol, safeDiv(netIncome, revenue));

    // Profitability
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, roeCol, safeDiv(netIncome, equity));
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, roaCol, safeDiv(netIncome, assets));

    // Balance sheet ratios
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, debtEquityCol, safeDiv(totalDebt, equity));
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, currentRatioCol, safeDiv(currentAssets, currentLiabilities));
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, assetTurnoverCol, safeDiv(revenue, assets));

    // Coverage
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, interestCoverageCol, safeDiv(ebit, interestExpense));

    // Working capital efficiency
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, inventoryTurnoverCol, safeDiv(revenue, inventory));
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, receivableDaysCol, safeDiv(ar, revenue) * 365);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, payableDaysCol, safeDiv(ap, revenue) * 365);

    // Market / valuation ratios from imported fundamentals
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, fcfYieldCol, safeDiv(fcf, marketCap));
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, dividendYieldCol, safeDiv(dps, sharePrice));
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, pbRatioCol, safeDiv(sharePrice, bvps));

    const payoutRatio = safeDiv(dps, eps);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, payoutRatioCol, payoutRatio);
    if (payoutRatio !== "") {
      setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, retentionRatioCol, 1 - payoutRatio);
    }

    const netDebt = totalDebt - cash;
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, netDebtCol, netDebt);
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, netDebtEbitdaCol, safeDiv(netDebt, ebitda));

    // Cash conversion
    setCellByIndex(input, rowNumber, cashConversionCol, safeDiv(ocf, netIncome));
  }

  formatImportedFundamentalRatios(input);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 50C — FORMAT IMPORTED FUNDAMENTAL RATIOS
// PURPOSE:
// Applies formatting to manually imported fundamental fields.
// =====================================================

function formatImportedFundamentalRatios(input) {

  const headers = getHeaders(input);
  const lastRow = Math.max(input.getLastRow() - 1, 1);

  const percentageHeaders = [
    "Gross Margin %",
    "EBITDA Margin %",
    "Operating Margin %",
    "Net Margin %",
    "ROE %",
    "ROA %",
    "FCF Yield %",
    "Dividend Yield %",
    "Payout Ratio %",
    "Retention Ratio %"
  ];

  percentageHeaders.forEach(header => {
    const c = colIndex(headers, header);
    if (c >= 0) {
      input.getRange(2, c + 1, lastRow, 1).setNumberFormat("0.00%");
    }
  });

  const numberHeaders = [
    "Debt-to-Equity",
    "Current Ratio",
    "Interest Coverage",
    "Asset Turnover",
    "Inventory Turnover",
    "Receivable Days",
    "Payable Days",
    "PB Ratio",
    "Net Debt",
    "Net Debt/EBITDA",
    "Cash Conversion Ratio"
  ];

  numberHeaders.forEach(header => {
    const c = colIndex(headers, header);
    if (c >= 0) {
      input.getRange(2, c + 1, lastRow, 1).setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");
    }
  });

  input.autoResizeColumns(1, input.getLastColumn());
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 50D — FUNDAMENTAL IMPORT DASHBOARD PANEL
// PURPOSE:
// Adds a simple Dashboard panel explaining manual import use.
// =====================================================

function createFundamentalImportDashboardPanel() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!dash) return;

  const startRow = 62;
  const startCol = 14; // Column N

  const table = [
    ["Fundamental Import Layer", ""],
    ["Purpose", "Manual financial statement import"],
    ["Sheet", "Fundamental Import"],
    ["Required Key", "Ticker must match Input"],
    ["Run Import", "importManualFundamentalsToInput"],
    ["Ratios Calculated", "Margins, ROE, ROA, Debt, FCF Yield"],
    ["GoogleFinance Limitation", "Does not provide full statements"]
  ];

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, 12, 4).clearContent();

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, table.length, 2)
    .setValues(table);

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, 1, 2)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  dash.getRange(startRow + 1, startCol, table.length - 1, 1)
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setBackground("#fff2cc");

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, table.length, 2)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  dash.autoResizeColumns(startCol, 4);
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 51 — MANUAL FUNDAMENTAL IMPORT VALIDATION
// PURPOSE:
// Validates the "Fundamental Import" sheet before importing.
// Checks:
// - Missing ticker
// - Duplicate ticker
// - Ticker not found in Input
// - Non-numeric values in numeric fields
// - Negative values in fields that are usually positive
// - Missing source
// =====================================================

function validateFundamentalImportSheet() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);
  const importSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Fundamental Import");

  if (!input) {
    throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");
  }

  if (!importSheet) {
    throw new Error("Fundamental Import sheet not found. Run createFundamentalImportSheet() first.");
  }

  let validation = ss.getSheetByName("Fundamental Import Validation");

  if (!validation) {
    validation = ss.insertSheet("Fundamental Import Validation");
  }

  validation.clear();

  const inputData = input.getDataRange().getValues();
  const inputHeaders = inputData[0];

  const importData = importSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const importHeaders = importData[0];

  const inputTickerCol = colIndex(inputHeaders, "Ticker");
  const importTickerCol = colIndex(importHeaders, "Ticker");
  const sourceCol = colIndex(importHeaders, "Source");

  if (inputTickerCol < 0 || importTickerCol < 0) {
    throw new Error("Ticker column missing in Input or Fundamental Import sheet.");
  }

  // Build valid ticker set from Input sheet
  const validTickers = {};
  for (let r = 1; r < inputData.length; r++) {
    const ticker = inputData[r][inputTickerCol];
    if (ticker) {
      validTickers[String(ticker).trim().toUpperCase()] = true;
    }
  }

  // Numeric fields expected in Fundamental Import
  const numericHeaders = [
    "Revenue",
    "Cost of Revenue",
    "Gross Profit",
    "Operating Expenses",
    "EBITDA",
    "EBIT",
    "Interest Expense",
    "Pre-Tax Income",
    "Net Income",
    "Diluted EPS",
    "Operating Cash Flow",
    "Capital Expenditure (Capex)",
    "Free Cash Flow",
    "Cash & Equivalents",
    "Short-Term Debt",
    "Long-Term Debt",
    "Total Debt",
    "Total Assets",
    "Total Liabilities",
    "Shareholder Equity",
    "Inventory",
    "Accounts Receivable",
    "Accounts Payable",
    "Current Assets",
    "Current Liabilities",
    "Dividends Paid",
    "Dividend Per Share",
    "Book Value Per Share",
    "R&D Expense",
    "SG&A Expense",
    "Employee Count"
  ];

  // These fields are normally positive. Negative values are flagged.
  const usuallyPositiveHeaders = [
    "Revenue",
    "Gross Profit",
    "EBITDA",
    "Operating Cash Flow",
    "Free Cash Flow",
    "Cash & Equivalents",
    "Total Assets",
    "Shareholder Equity",
    "Current Assets",
    "Current Liabilities",
    "Dividend Per Share",
    "Book Value Per Share",
    "Employee Count"
  ];

  const seenTickers = {};

  const rows = [
    [
      "Timestamp",
      "Import Row",
      "Ticker",
      "Issue Type",
      "Severity",
      "Field",
      "Value",
      "Suggested Action"
    ]
  ];

  for (let r = 1; r < importData.length; r++) {

    const row = importData[r];
    const sheetRow = r + 1;
    const ticker = row[importTickerCol];

    // Skip fully blank rows
    if (row.every(v => v === "" || v == null)) continue;

    if (!ticker) {
      rows.push([
        new Date(),
        sheetRow,
        "",
        "Missing Ticker",
        "CRITICAL",
        "Ticker",
        "",
        "Add ticker that matches Input sheet exactly."
      ]);
      continue;
    }

    const tickerKey = String(ticker).trim().toUpperCase();

    if (seenTickers[tickerKey]) {
      rows.push([
        new Date(),
        sheetRow,
        ticker,
        "Duplicate Ticker",
        "HIGH",
        "Ticker",
        ticker,
        "Remove duplicate row or keep only the latest fiscal year."
      ]);
    }

    seenTickers[tickerKey] = true;

    if (!validTickers[tickerKey]) {
      rows.push([
        new Date(),
        sheetRow,
        ticker,
        "Ticker Not Found In Input",
        "CRITICAL",
        "Ticker",
        ticker,
        "Add ticker to Input sheet or correct ticker spelling."
      ]);
    }

    if (sourceCol >= 0 && !row[sourceCol]) {
      rows.push([
        new Date(),
        sheetRow,
        ticker,
        "Missing Source",
        "MEDIUM",
        "Source",
        "",
        "Add source such as annual report, 10-K, company filing, or manual note."
      ]);
    }

    numericHeaders.forEach(header => {

      const c = colIndex(importHeaders, header);
      if (c < 0) return;

      const value = row[c];

      if (value === "" || value == null) return;

      if (isNaN(value)) {
        rows.push([
          new Date(),
          sheetRow,
          ticker,
          "Non-Numeric Value",
          "HIGH",
          header,
          value,
          "Use plain numbers only. Remove commas, text, currency symbols, or notes."
        ]);
        return;
      }

      const numericValue = Number(value);

      if (usuallyPositiveHeaders.includes(header) && numericValue < 0) {
        rows.push([
          new Date(),
          sheetRow,
          ticker,
          "Unusual Negative Value",
          "MEDIUM",
          header,
          numericValue,
          "Check whether this should be negative. Some fields are usually positive."
        ]);
      }
    });
  }

  if (rows.length === 1) {
    rows.push([
      new Date(),
      "",
      "",
      "Validation Passed",
      "OK",
      "",
      "",
      "No validation issues found."
    ]);
  }

  validation.getRange(1, 1, rows.length, rows[0].length)
    .setValues(rows);

  formatFundamentalImportValidationSheet(validation);

  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert(
    "Fundamental Import validation completed.\nIssues found: " + (rows.length - 2 >= 0 ? rows.length - 1 : 0)
  );
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 51A — FORMAT FUNDAMENTAL IMPORT VALIDATION SHEET
// PURPOSE:
// Formats validation output and severity colours.
// =====================================================

function formatFundamentalImportValidationSheet(validation) {

  const lastRow = Math.max(validation.getLastRow(), 2);
  const lastCol = Math.max(validation.getLastColumn(), 8);

  validation.getDataRange().setFontFamily("Arial");
  validation.setFrozenRows(1);

  validation.getRange(1, 1, 1, lastCol)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  validation.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 1)
    .setNumberFormat("dd/mm/yyyy hh:mm:ss");

  validation.autoResizeColumns(1, lastCol);

  const rules = [];
  const severityRange = validation.getRange(2, 5, lastRow - 1, 1);

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("CRITICAL")
      .setBackground("#f4cccc")
      .setFontColor("#990000")
      .setRanges([severityRange])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("HIGH")
      .setBackground("#fce5cd")
      .setFontColor("#783f04")
      .setRanges([severityRange])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("MEDIUM")
      .setBackground("#fff2cc")
      .setFontColor("#7f6000")
      .setRanges([severityRange])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("OK")
      .setBackground("#d9ead3")
      .setFontColor("#274e13")
      .setRanges([severityRange])
      .build()
  );

  validation.setConditionalFormatRules(rules);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 51B — SAFE IMPORT AFTER VALIDATION
// PURPOSE:
// Runs validation first, then imports only if no CRITICAL
// validation errors are found.
// =====================================================

function validateThenImportManualFundamentals() {

  validateFundamentalImportSheet();

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const validation = ss.getSheetByName("Fundamental Import Validation");

  if (!validation || validation.getLastRow() < 2) {
    throw new Error("Validation sheet missing or empty.");
  }

  const data = validation.getDataRange().getValues();

  let criticalCount = 0;

  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {
    if (data[r][4] === "CRITICAL") {
      criticalCount++;
    }
  }

  if (criticalCount > 0) {
    SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert(
      "Import stopped.\nCritical validation issues found: " +
      criticalCount +
      "\nPlease review Fundamental Import Validation sheet."
    );
    return;
  }

  importManualFundamentalsToInput();
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 51C — DASHBOARD FUNDAMENTAL VALIDATION PANEL
// PURPOSE:
// Shows validation summary on Dashboard.
// =====================================================

function createDashboardFundamentalValidationPanel() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);
  const validation = ss.getSheetByName("Fundamental Import Validation");

  if (!dash || !validation || validation.getLastRow() < 2) return;

  const data = validation.getDataRange().getValues();

  let critical = 0;
  let high = 0;
  let medium = 0;
  let ok = 0;

  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {

    const severity = data[r][4];

    if (severity === "CRITICAL") critical++;
    else if (severity === "HIGH") high++;
    else if (severity === "MEDIUM") medium++;
    else if (severity === "OK") ok++;
  }

  const startRow = 73;
  const startCol = 14; // Column N

  const table = [
    ["Fundamental Import Validation", ""],
    ["Critical", critical],
    ["High", high],
    ["Medium", medium],
    ["OK", ok],
    ["Safe Import Function", "validateThenImportManualFundamentals"]
  ];

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, 10, 4).clearContent();

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, table.length, 2)
    .setValues(table);

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, 1, 2)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, table.length, 2)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  dash.autoResizeColumns(startCol, 4);
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 52 — DASHBOARD THEME + SECTION STYLING
// PURPOSE:
// Applies a polished finance-dashboard visual theme.
// Includes:
// - Dark dashboard title bar
// - Styled section headers
// - Alternating row colours
// - Table borders
// - Consistent number alignment
// - Improved row heights and spacing
// =====================================================

function applyDashboardThemeAndSectionStyling() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!dash) {
    throw new Error("Dashboard sheet not found.");
  }

  const lastRow = Math.max(dash.getLastRow(), 1);
  const lastCol = Math.max(dash.getLastColumn(), 20);

  // =====================================================
  // BASE THEME
  // =====================================================

  dash.getDataRange()
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setFontSize(10)
    .setVerticalAlignment("middle");

  dash.setFrozenRows(1);

  // Dashboard title
  dash.getRange("A1:L1")
    .merge()
    .setValue("Stocks Overseer Advisor Dashboard")
    .setBackground("#111827")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(16)
    .setHorizontalAlignment("left");

  dash.setRowHeight(1, 34);

  // Light background across working dashboard canvas
  dash.getRange(2, 1, lastRow, lastCol)
    .setBackground("#ffffff");

  // =====================================================
  // STYLE ALL SECTION TITLES BY TEXT
  // =====================================================

  const sectionTitles = [
    "Top 10 Decision View",
    "Clean GoogleFinance Ranking Dashboard",
    "Clean Watchlist Dashboard Table",
    "Clean Portfolio Allocation Dashboard",
    "Portfolio Concentration Check",
    "Risk Grouping Dashboard",
    "Historical Share Price Snapshot",
    "Unsupported / Missing Data Ticker Dashboard",
    "Ticker Format Suggestions",
    "Ticker Count + Data Coverage Summary",
    "Overseer Status Panel",
    "Dashboard Navigation",
    "Latest System Log",
    "Error Log Summary",
    "User Zone",
    "Manual Input Reminder",
    "Fundamental Import Layer",
    "Fundamental Import Validation"
  ];

  sectionTitles.forEach(title => {
    styleSectionTitleByText_(dash, title);
  });

  // =====================================================
  // STYLE KNOWN TABLE HEADER ROWS
  // Uses header keywords to detect table headers dynamically.
  // =====================================================

  styleRowsContainingText_(dash, "Rank", "#1f2933", "#ffffff");
  styleRowsContainingText_(dash, "Ticker", "#1f2933", "#ffffff");
  styleRowsContainingText_(dash, "Metric", "#1f2933", "#ffffff");
  styleRowsContainingText_(dash, "Risk Group", "#1f2933", "#ffffff");

  // =====================================================
  // APPLY TABLE BANDING TO MAIN LEFT-SIDE TABLES
  // =====================================================

  applyDashboardBandingForSection_(dash, "Clean GoogleFinance Ranking Dashboard", 2, 11);
  applyDashboardBandingForSection_(dash, "Clean Watchlist Dashboard Table", 2, 11);
  applyDashboardBandingForSection_(dash, "Clean Portfolio Allocation Dashboard", 2, 7);
  applyDashboardBandingForSection_(dash, "Historical Share Price Snapshot", 2, 10);
  applyDashboardBandingForSection_(dash, "Unsupported / Missing Data Ticker Dashboard", 2, 11);
  applyDashboardBandingForSection_(dash, "Ticker Format Suggestions", 2, 5);
  applyDashboardBandingForSection_(dash, "Top 10 Decision View", 2, 13);

  // =====================================================
  // RIGHT-SIDE PANEL STYLE
  // =====================================================

  styleRightSidePanels_(dash);

  // =====================================================
  // NUMBER ALIGNMENT AND WIDTHS
  // =====================================================

  dash.getDataRange()
    .setWrap(false);

  // Keep remarks readable when present
  dash.autoResizeColumns(1, lastCol);

  // Make important columns easier to scan
  setSafeColumnWidth_(dash, 1, 130);   // A
  setSafeColumnWidth_(dash, 2, 120);   // B
  setSafeColumnWidth_(dash, 3, 160);   // C
  setSafeColumnWidth_(dash, 11, 220);  // K remarks / long column
  setSafeColumnWidth_(dash, 14, 190);  // N right panels
  setSafeColumnWidth_(dash, 15, 220);  // O right panels

  // Row height
  dash.setRowHeights(2, Math.max(lastRow - 1, 1), 24);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 52A — STYLE SECTION TITLE BY TEXT
// PURPOSE:
// Finds a section title cell and applies a strong visual style.
// =====================================================

function styleSectionTitleByText_(sheet, title) {

  const cell = sheet.createTextFinder(title)
    .matchEntireCell(true)
    .findNext();

  if (!cell) return;

  cell
    .setBackground("#d9e2f3")
    .setFontColor("#1f2933")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(12)
    .setHorizontalAlignment("left");

  sheet.setRowHeight(cell.getRow(), 28);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 52B — STYLE ROWS CONTAINING TEXT
// PURPOSE:
// Applies style to table header rows containing a keyword.
// =====================================================

function styleRowsContainingText_(sheet, text, bg, font) {

  const matches = sheet.createTextFinder(text)
    .matchCase(false)
    .findAll();

  matches.forEach(cell => {

    const row = cell.getRow();
    const lastCol = Math.max(sheet.getLastColumn(), 20);

    // Avoid styling title row too broadly.
    if (row <= 1) return;

    // Main dashboard tables should only style A:M.
    // This prevents colour clash in the right sidebar area N:Z.
    const scopedCols = Math.min(lastCol, 13);
    sheet.getRange(row, 1, 1, scopedCols)
      .setBackground(bg)
      .setFontColor(font)
      .setFontWeight("bold");
  });
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 52C — APPLY SECTION BANDING
// PURPOSE:
// Adds alternating row background and borders to tables.
// sectionTitle = text of the section header.
// headerOffset = rows below section title where table header starts.
// tableWidth = number of table columns.
// =====================================================

function applyDashboardBandingForSection_(sheet, sectionTitle, headerOffset, tableWidth) {

  const titleCell = sheet.createTextFinder(sectionTitle)
    .matchEntireCell(true)
    .findNext();

  if (!titleCell) return;

  const headerRow = titleCell.getRow() + headerOffset;
  const dataStartRow = headerRow + 1;

  const rows = detectTableLength(sheet, dataStartRow, 1);

  if (rows <= 0) return;

  // Header row
  sheet.getRange(headerRow, 1, 1, tableWidth)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  // Borders
  sheet.getRange(headerRow, 1, rows + 1, tableWidth)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true, "#d9d9d9", SpreadsheetApp.BorderStyle.SOLID);

  // Alternating row colours
  for (let i = 0; i < rows; i++) {
    const bg = i % 2 === 0 ? "#ffffff" : "#f8fafc";
    sheet.getRange(dataStartRow + i, 1, 1, tableWidth)
      .setBackground(bg);
  }
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 52D — STYLE RIGHT SIDE PANELS
// PURPOSE:
// Applies borders and subtle backgrounds to right-side panels.
// =====================================================

function styleRightSidePanels_(dash) {

  const panelTitles = [
    "Ticker Count + Data Coverage Summary",
    "Overseer Status Panel",
    "Dashboard Navigation",
    "Latest System Log",
    "Error Log Summary",
    "User Zone",
    "Manual Input Reminder",
    "Fundamental Import Layer",
    "Fundamental Import Validation"
  ];

  panelTitles.forEach(title => {

    const cell = dash.createTextFinder(title)
      .matchEntireCell(true)
      .findNext();

    if (!cell) return;

    const row = cell.getRow();
    const col = cell.getColumn();

    cell
      .setBackground("#111827")
      .setFontColor("#ffffff")
      .setFontWeight("bold");

    dash.getRange(row, col, 8, 2)
      .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true, "#d9d9d9", SpreadsheetApp.BorderStyle.SOLID);

    dash.getRange(row + 1, col, 7, 1)
      .setBackground("#f3f6fa")
      .setFontWeight("bold");

    dash.getRange(row + 1, col + 1, 7, 1)
      .setBackground("#ffffff");
  });
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 52E — SAFE COLUMN WIDTH SETTER
// PURPOSE:
// Prevents errors when target column does not exist.
// =====================================================

function setSafeColumnWidth_(sheet, col, width) {
  if (sheet.getMaxColumns() >= col) {
    sheet.setColumnWidth(col, width);
  }
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 53 — KPI SCORECARDS WITH COLOUR BANDS
// PURPOSE:
// Adds large executive KPI scorecards to the Dashboard.
// These cards make key portfolio/data quality metrics visible:
// - Total tickers
// - Priced coverage
// - Missing price data
// - Buy candidates
// - Allocation coverage
// - Data warnings
// =====================================================

function createDashboardKpiScorecards() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) {
    throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");
  }

  if (!dash) {
    throw new Error("Dashboard sheet not found.");
  }

  const data = input.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];

  const tickerCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker");
  const priceCol = colIndex(headers, "Share Price");
  const scoreCol = colIndex(headers, "GoogleFinance Score");
  const allocationCol = colIndex(headers, "Portfolio Allocation %");
  const recommendationCol = colIndex(headers, "Final Recommendation");
  const statusCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker Data Status");

  let totalTickers = 0;
  let pricedTickers = 0;
  let missingPrice = 0;
  let scoredTickers = 0;
  let allocatedTickers = 0;
  let buyCandidates = 0;
  let dataWarnings = 0;

  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {

    const row = data[r];

    if (!row[tickerCol]) continue;

    totalTickers++;

    const price = num(row[priceCol]);
    const score = num(row[scoreCol]);
    const allocation = num(row[allocationCol]);
    const recommendation = row[recommendationCol];
    const status = statusCol >= 0 ? row[statusCol] : "";

    if (price > 0) pricedTickers++;
    else missingPrice++;

    if (score > 0) scoredTickers++;
    if (allocation > 0) allocatedTickers++;
    if (recommendation === "BUY CANDIDATE") buyCandidates++;

    if (status && status !== "OK") dataWarnings++;
  }

  const pricedCoverage = totalTickers > 0 ? pricedTickers / totalTickers : 0;
  const scoredCoverage = totalTickers > 0 ? scoredTickers / totalTickers : 0;
  const allocationCoverage = totalTickers > 0 ? allocatedTickers / totalTickers : 0;

  // =====================================================
  // KPI CARD LOCATION
  // Placed near the top, below title, above existing summary cards.
  // =====================================================

  const startRow = 2;
  const startCol = 1;

  // Clear top KPI area only
  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, 4, 13).clearContent();

  const cards = [
    {
      title: "Total Tickers",
      value: totalTickers,
      subtitle: "Tracked universe",
      type: "number",
      colour: "#d9e2f3"
    },
    {
      title: "Priced Coverage",
      value: pricedCoverage,
      subtitle: pricedTickers + " / " + totalTickers + " priced",
      type: "percent",
      colour: pricedCoverage >= 0.95 ? "#d9ead3" : "#fff2cc"
    },
    {
      title: "Missing Price",
      value: missingPrice,
      subtitle: "Needs review",
      type: "number",
      colour: missingPrice === 0 ? "#d9ead3" : "#f4cccc"
    },
    {
      title: "Buy Candidates",
      value: buyCandidates,
      subtitle: "High conviction watch",
      type: "number",
      colour: buyCandidates > 0 ? "#d9ead3" : "#fff2cc"
    },
    {
      title: "Allocation Coverage",
      value: allocationCoverage,
      subtitle: allocatedTickers + " allocated",
      type: "percent",
      colour: allocationCoverage >= 0.80 ? "#d9ead3" : "#fff2cc"
    },
    {
      title: "Data Warnings",
      value: dataWarnings,
      subtitle: "Quality flags",
      type: "number",
      colour: dataWarnings === 0 ? "#d9ead3" : "#fce5cd"
    }
  ];

  let col = startCol;

  cards.forEach(card => {

    // Each card uses 2 columns
    const cardRange = dash.getRange(startRow, col, 4, 2);

    cardRange
      .setBackground(card.colour)
      .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true, "#d9d9d9", SpreadsheetApp.BorderStyle.SOLID);

    dash.getRange(startRow, col, 1, 2)
      .merge()
      .setValue(card.title)
      .setFontWeight("bold")
      .setFontSize(10)
      .setHorizontalAlignment("center")
      .setBackground("#1f2933")
      .setFontColor("#ffffff");

    dash.getRange(startRow + 1, col, 2, 2)
      .merge()
      .setValue(card.value)
      .setFontWeight("bold")
      .setFontSize(16)
      .setHorizontalAlignment("center")
      .setVerticalAlignment("middle")
      .setBackground(card.colour)
      .setFontColor("#111827");

    dash.getRange(startRow + 3, col, 1, 2)
      .merge()
      .setValue(card.subtitle)
      .setFontSize(9)
      .setHorizontalAlignment("center")
      .setFontColor("#374151")
      .setBackground(card.colour);

    if (card.type === "percent") {
      dash.getRange(startRow + 1, col)
        .setNumberFormat("0.00%");
    }

    col += 2;
  });

  dash.setRowHeight(startRow, 24);
  dash.setRowHeight(startRow + 1, 32);
  dash.setRowHeight(startRow + 2, 32);
  dash.setRowHeight(startRow + 3, 24);

  PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties()
    .setProperty("DASHBOARD_KPI_START", String(startRow));
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 53A — KPI SCORECARD CONDITIONAL FORMATTING
// PURPOSE:
// Adds extra colour rules to KPI scorecards where helpful.
// =====================================================

function applyDashboardKpiScorecardFormatting() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!dash) return;

  const rules = dash.getConditionalFormatRules();

  // Missing Price card value area: E3:F4
  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenNumberGreaterThan(0)
      .setBackground("#f4cccc")
      .setFontColor("#990000")
      .setRanges([dash.getRange("E3:F4")])
      .build()
  );

  // Data Warnings card value area: K3:L4
  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenNumberGreaterThan(0)
      .setBackground("#fce5cd")
      .setFontColor("#783f04")
      .setRanges([dash.getRange("K3:L4")])
      .build()
  );

  dash.setConditionalFormatRules(rules);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 53B — KPI CARD LAYOUT OFFSET
// PURPOSE:
// Creates extra vertical spacing so KPI cards do not overlap
// with existing summary cards.
// =====================================================

function reserveDashboardKpiSpace() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!dash) return;

  // This simply ensures the top area has enough row height.
  for (let r = 2; r <= 5; r++) {
    dash.setRowHeight(r, 28);
  }
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 54 — RISK HEATMAP
// PURPOSE:
// Creates a visual heatmap matrix on the Dashboard showing
// stock count by GoogleFinance Score band and Beta Risk Group.
// This helps identify portfolio quality concentration.
// =====================================================

function createDashboardRiskHeatmap() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) {
    throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");
  }

  if (!dash) {
    throw new Error("Dashboard sheet not found.");
  }

  const data = input.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];

  const tickerCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker");
  const scoreCol = colIndex(headers, "GoogleFinance Score");
  const betaRiskCol = colIndex(headers, "Beta Risk Group");

  const scoreBands = [
    "80–100",
    "60–79",
    "40–59",
    "20–39",
    "0–19",
    "No Score"
  ];

  const riskGroups = [
    "LOW RISK",
    "MODERATE RISK",
    "HIGH RISK",
    "VERY HIGH RISK",
    "NO BETA DATA"
  ];

  const matrix = {};

  scoreBands.forEach(band => {
    matrix[band] = {};
    riskGroups.forEach(group => {
      matrix[band][group] = 0;
    });
  });

  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {

    const row = data[r];

    if (!row[tickerCol]) continue;

    const score = num(row[scoreCol]);
    const betaRisk = riskGroups.includes(row[betaRiskCol])
      ? row[betaRiskCol]
      : "NO BETA DATA";

    const band = getScoreBandForHeatmap_(score);

    matrix[band][betaRisk]++;
  }

  const table = [
    ["Score Band", ...riskGroups, "Total"]
  ];

  scoreBands.forEach(band => {

    let rowTotal = 0;
    const row = [band];

    riskGroups.forEach(group => {
      const count = matrix[band][group];
      row.push(count);
      rowTotal += count;
    });

    row.push(rowTotal);
    table.push(row);
  });

  // Add total row
  const totalRow = ["Total"];

  riskGroups.forEach((group, index) => {
    let total = 0;

    scoreBands.forEach(band => {
      total += matrix[band][group];
    });

    totalRow.push(total);
  });

  totalRow.push(totalRow.slice(1).reduce((sum, v) => sum + v, 0));
  table.push(totalRow);

  // =====================================================
  // DASHBOARD LOCATION
  // Add after latest dashboard section.
  // =====================================================

  const props = PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties();
  const startRow = Number(props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_NEXT_ROW")) || findNextDashboardRow_(dash, 1, 12);
  const startCol = 1;

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, 15, table[0].length)
    .clearContent();

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol)
    .setValue("Risk Heatmap — Score Band vs Beta Risk");

  dash.getRange(startRow + 2, startCol, table.length, table[0].length)
    .setValues(table);

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol)
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(12)
    .setBackground("#d9e2f3")
    .setFontColor("#1f2933");

  dash.getRange(startRow + 2, startCol, 1, table[0].length)
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff");

  dash.getRange(startRow + 2, startCol, table.length, table[0].length)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true, "#d9d9d9", SpreadsheetApp.BorderStyle.SOLID);

  dash.autoResizeColumns(startCol, table[0].length);

  props.setProperty("DASHBOARD_RISK_HEATMAP_START", String(startRow + 3));
  props.setProperty("DASHBOARD_NEXT_ROW", String(startRow + table.length + 6));
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 54A — SCORE BAND HELPER
// PURPOSE:
// Converts GoogleFinance Score into score band labels.
// =====================================================

function getScoreBandForHeatmap_(score) {

  if (!score || score <= 0) return "No Score";
  if (score >= 80) return "80–100";
  if (score >= 60) return "60–79";
  if (score >= 40) return "40–59";
  if (score >= 20) return "20–39";
  return "0–19";
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 54B — RISK HEATMAP FORMATTING
// PURPOSE:
// Applies heatmap-style colour gradient to the matrix counts.
// =====================================================

function applyDashboardRiskHeatmapFormatting() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!dash) return;

  const props = PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties();
  const startRow = Number(props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_RISK_HEATMAP_START"));

  if (!startRow) return;

  // Matrix count area excludes first label column and total row/column.
  const heatmapRange = dash.getRange(startRow, 2, 6, 5);

  const rules = dash.getConditionalFormatRules();

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .setGradientMinpointWithValue("#ffffff", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "0")
      .setGradientMidpointWithValue("#fff2cc", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "5")
      .setGradientMaxpointWithValue("#d9ead3", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "15")
      .setRanges([heatmapRange])
      .build()
  );

  // Highlight high-risk concentration.
  const highRiskRange = dash.getRange(startRow, 4, 6, 2);

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenNumberGreaterThan(5)
      .setBackground("#f4cccc")
      .setFontColor("#990000")
      .setRanges([highRiskRange])
      .build()
  );

  dash.setConditionalFormatRules(rules);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 54C — RISK HEATMAP INSIGHT NOTE
// PURPOSE:
// Adds a short interpretation note under the heatmap.
// =====================================================

function addDashboardRiskHeatmapInsightNote() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!dash) return;

  const props = PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties();
  const startRow = Number(props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_RISK_HEATMAP_START"));

  if (!startRow) return;

  const noteRow = startRow + 9;

  dash.getRange(noteRow, 1)
    .setValue("Heatmap guide: Prefer more stocks in 80–100 / Low-to-Moderate Risk. Review concentration in High / Very High Risk.")
    .setFontStyle("italic")
    .setFontColor("#666666");
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 55 — RECOMMENDATION BADGE STYLING
// PURPOSE:
// Applies badge-style visual formatting to recommendation,
// watchlist, risk, and momentum fields across Input and Dashboard.
// This improves readability and makes investment actions easier
// to scan visually.
// =====================================================

function applyRecommendationBadgeStyling() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (input) {
    applyInputRecommendationBadges_(input);
  }

  if (dash) {
    applyDashboardRecommendationBadges_(dash);
  }
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 55A — INPUT BADGE STYLING
// PURPOSE:
// Badge-style formatting for Input sheet columns.
// =====================================================

function applyInputRecommendationBadges_(input) {

  const headers = getHeaders(input);
  const lastRow = Math.max(input.getLastRow(), 2);
  const rules = input.getConditionalFormatRules();

  const recommendationCol = colIndex(headers, "Final Recommendation");
  const watchlistCol = colIndex(headers, "Watchlist Status");
  const betaRiskCol = colIndex(headers, "Beta Risk Group");
  const momentumCol = colIndex(headers, "Momentum Signal");

  if (recommendationCol >= 0) {
    addRecommendationBadgeRules_(rules, input.getRange(2, recommendationCol + 1, lastRow - 1, 1));
    input.getRange(1, recommendationCol + 1)
      .setBackground("#ffe599")
      .setFontColor("#7f6000")
      .setFontWeight("bold");
  }

  if (watchlistCol >= 0) {
    addWatchlistBadgeRules_(rules, input.getRange(2, watchlistCol + 1, lastRow - 1, 1));
    input.getRange(1, watchlistCol + 1)
      .setBackground("#fff2cc")
      .setFontColor("#7f6000")
      .setFontWeight("bold");
  }

  if (betaRiskCol >= 0) {
    addRiskBadgeRules_(rules, input.getRange(2, betaRiskCol + 1, lastRow - 1, 1));
  }

  if (momentumCol >= 0) {
    addMomentumBadgeRules_(rules, input.getRange(2, momentumCol + 1, lastRow - 1, 1));
  }

  input.setConditionalFormatRules(rules);

  // Center badge columns for better badge appearance.
  [
    recommendationCol,
    watchlistCol,
    betaRiskCol,
    momentumCol
  ].forEach(c => {
    if (c >= 0) {
      input.getRange(2, c + 1, lastRow - 1, 1)
        .setHorizontalAlignment("center")
        .setFontWeight("bold");
    }
  });
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 55B — DASHBOARD BADGE STYLING
// PURPOSE:
// Badge-style formatting for Dashboard recommendation tables.
// =====================================================

function applyDashboardRecommendationBadges_(dash) {

  const rules = dash.getConditionalFormatRules();

  const props = PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties();

  const top10Start = Number(props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_TOP10_START")) || 0;
  const watchlistStart = Number(props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_WATCHLIST_START")) || 0;
  const portfolioStart = Number(props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_PORTFOLIO_START")) || 0;
  const rankingStart = Number(props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_RANKING_START")) || 0;

  // Top 10 Decision View
  if (top10Start) {
    const rows = detectTableLength(dash, top10Start, 2);
    if (rows > 0) {
      addRiskBadgeRules_(rules, dash.getRange(top10Start, 9, rows, 1));
      addMomentumBadgeRules_(rules, dash.getRange(top10Start, 10, rows, 1));
      addRecommendationBadgeRules_(rules, dash.getRange(top10Start, 12, rows, 1));
      addWatchlistBadgeRules_(rules, dash.getRange(top10Start, 13, rows, 1));

      dash.getRange(top10Start, 9, rows, 5)
        .setHorizontalAlignment("center")
        .setFontWeight("bold");
    }
  }

  // Watchlist Table
  if (watchlistStart) {
    const rows = detectTableLength(dash, watchlistStart, 1);
    if (rows > 0) {
      addRiskBadgeRules_(rules, dash.getRange(watchlistStart, 7, rows, 1));
      addMomentumBadgeRules_(rules, dash.getRange(watchlistStart, 8, rows, 1));
      addWatchlistBadgeRules_(rules, dash.getRange(watchlistStart, 9, rows, 1));
      addRecommendationBadgeRules_(rules, dash.getRange(watchlistStart, 10, rows, 1));

      dash.getRange(watchlistStart, 7, rows, 4)
        .setHorizontalAlignment("center")
        .setFontWeight("bold");
    }
  }

  // Portfolio Table
  if (portfolioStart) {
    const rows = detectTableLength(dash, portfolioStart, 1);
    if (rows > 0) {
      addRiskBadgeRules_(rules, dash.getRange(portfolioStart, 4, rows, 1));
      addMomentumBadgeRules_(rules, dash.getRange(portfolioStart, 5, rows, 1));
      addRecommendationBadgeRules_(rules, dash.getRange(portfolioStart, 6, rows, 1));

      dash.getRange(portfolioStart, 4, rows, 3)
        .setHorizontalAlignment("center")
        .setFontWeight("bold");
    }
  }

  // Ranking Table
  if (rankingStart) {
    const rows = detectTableLength(dash, rankingStart, 2);
    if (rows > 0) {
      addRiskBadgeRules_(rules, dash.getRange(rankingStart, 9, rows, 1));
      addMomentumBadgeRules_(rules, dash.getRange(rankingStart, 10, rows, 1));

      dash.getRange(rankingStart, 9, rows, 2)
        .setHorizontalAlignment("center")
        .setFontWeight("bold");
    }
  }

  dash.setConditionalFormatRules(rules);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 55C — BADGE RULE HELPERS
// PURPOSE:
// Reusable conditional formatting rules for badges.
// =====================================================

function addRecommendationBadgeRules_(rules, range) {

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("BUY CANDIDATE")
      .setBackground("#38761d")
      .setFontColor("#ffffff")
      .setBold(true)
      .setRanges([range])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("ACCUMULATE / STUDY")
      .setBackground("#6aa84f")
      .setFontColor("#ffffff")
      .setBold(true)
      .setRanges([range])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("VALUE WATCH")
      .setBackground("#3c78d8")
      .setFontColor("#ffffff")
      .setBold(true)
      .setRanges([range])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("HOLD / MONITOR")
      .setBackground("#f1c232")
      .setFontColor("#000000")
      .setBold(true)
      .setRanges([range])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("AVOID / HIGH RISK")
      .setBackground("#cc0000")
      .setFontColor("#ffffff")
      .setBold(true)
      .setRanges([range])
      .build()
  );
}

function addMomentumBadgeRules_(rules, range) {

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("STRONG MOMENTUM")
      .setBackground("#38761d")
      .setFontColor("#ffffff")
      .setBold(true)
      .setRanges([range])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("POSITIVE TREND")
      .setBackground("#6aa84f")
      .setFontColor("#ffffff")
      .setBold(true)
      .setRanges([range])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("NEUTRAL")
      .setBackground("#d9d9d9")
      .setFontColor("#000000")
      .setBold(true)
      .setRanges([range])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("WEAK")
      .setBackground("#fce5cd")
      .setFontColor("#783f04")
      .setBold(true)
      .setRanges([range])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("NEAR 52W LOW")
      .setBackground("#cfe2f3")
      .setFontColor("#073763")
      .setBold(true)
      .setRanges([range])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("NO DATA")
      .setBackground("#d9d9d9")
      .setFontColor("#666666")
      .setBold(true)
      .setRanges([range])
      .build()
  );
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 55D — DASHBOARD BADGE LEGEND PANEL
// PURPOSE:
// Adds a small badge legend on the Dashboard right panel.
// =====================================================

function createDashboardBadgeLegendPanel() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!dash) return;

  const startRow = 84;
  const startCol = 14; // Column N

  const table = [
    ["Badge Legend", ""],
    ["BUY CANDIDATE", "Strongest action candidate"],
    ["ACCUMULATE / STUDY", "Further review / staged entry"],
    ["VALUE WATCH", "Potential value but confirm fundamentals"],
    ["HOLD / MONITOR", "Watch but not urgent"],
    ["AVOID / HIGH RISK", "Avoid or deep review"],
    ["LOW RISK", "Lower beta risk"],
    ["VERY HIGH RISK", "High volatility / risk"]
  ];

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, 12, 4).clearContent();

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, table.length, 2)
    .setValues(table);

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, 1, 2)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  dash.getRange(startRow + 1, startCol, table.length - 1, 1)
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, table.length, 2)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  // Manual colouring of legend label cells
  dash.getRange(startRow + 1, startCol).setBackground("#38761d").setFontColor("#ffffff");
  dash.getRange(startRow + 2, startCol).setBackground("#6aa84f").setFontColor("#ffffff");
  dash.getRange(startRow + 3, startCol).setBackground("#3c78d8").setFontColor("#ffffff");
  dash.getRange(startRow + 4, startCol).setBackground("#f1c232").setFontColor("#000000");
  dash.getRange(startRow + 5, startCol).setBackground("#cc0000").setFontColor("#ffffff");
  dash.getRange(startRow + 6, startCol).setBackground("#d9ead3").setFontColor("#274e13");
  dash.getRange(startRow + 7, startCol).setBackground("#cc0000").setFontColor("#ffffff");

  dash.autoResizeColumns(startCol, 4);
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 56 — TOP 10 MINI CHARTS / IN-CELL DATA BARS
// PURPOSE:
// Adds compact visual bar indicators to the Top 10 Decision View.
// Uses SPARKLINE bars for:
// - GoogleFinance Score
// - Earnings Yield
// - Upside to 52W High
// - Portfolio Allocation
// This improves executive scanning without adding heavy charts.
// =====================================================

function createTop10MiniCharts() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!dash) {
    throw new Error("Dashboard sheet not found.");
  }

  const props = PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties();
  const top10Start = Number(props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_TOP10_START")) || 0;

  if (!top10Start) return;

  const rowCount = detectTableLength(dash, top10Start, 2);

  if (rowCount <= 0) return;

  // =====================================================
  // EXISTING TOP 10 COLUMNS
  // Based on Module 45 table:
  // F = Score
  // G = Earnings Yield
  // H = Upside
  // K = Allocation
  // =====================================================

  const chartStartCol = 14; // Column N
  const headerRow = top10Start - 1;

  // Clear previous mini chart area
  dash.getRange(headerRow - 1, chartStartCol, rowCount + 3, 5).clearContent();

  dash.getRange(headerRow - 1, chartStartCol)
    .setValue("Top 10 Mini Visuals");

  const miniHeaders = [
    "Ticker",
    "Score Bar",
    "Yield Bar",
    "Upside Bar",
    "Allocation Bar"
  ];

  dash.getRange(headerRow, chartStartCol, 1, miniHeaders.length)
    .setValues([miniHeaders]);

  for (let i = 0; i < rowCount; i++) {

    const row = top10Start + i;

    // Ticker reference from Top 10 table, column B
    dash.getRange(row, chartStartCol)
      .setFormula(`=B${row}`);

    // Score bar: Score is 0–100, column F
    dash.getRange(row, chartStartCol + 1)
      .setFormula(`=IFERROR(SPARKLINE(F${row},{"charttype","bar";"max",100}),"")`);

    // Earnings Yield bar: cap visual at 15%, column G
    dash.getRange(row, chartStartCol + 2)
      .setFormula(`=IFERROR(SPARKLINE(G${row},{"charttype","bar";"max",0.15}),"")`);

    // Upside bar: cap visual at 100%, column H
    dash.getRange(row, chartStartCol + 3)
      .setFormula(`=IFERROR(SPARKLINE(H${row},{"charttype","bar";"max",1}),"")`);

    // Allocation bar: cap visual at 15%, column K
    dash.getRange(row, chartStartCol + 4)
      .setFormula(`=IFERROR(SPARKLINE(K${row},{"charttype","bar";"max",0.15}),"")`);
  }

  // =====================================================
  // FORMAT MINI CHART AREA
  // =====================================================

  dash.getRange(headerRow - 1, chartStartCol)
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(12)
    .setBackground("#d9e2f3")
    .setFontColor("#1f2933");

  dash.getRange(headerRow, chartStartCol, 1, miniHeaders.length)
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  dash.getRange(top10Start, chartStartCol, rowCount, miniHeaders.length)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true, "#d9d9d9", SpreadsheetApp.BorderStyle.SOLID);

  dash.getRange(top10Start, chartStartCol, rowCount, 1)
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  dash.setColumnWidth(chartStartCol, 110);
  dash.setColumnWidth(chartStartCol + 1, 120);
  dash.setColumnWidth(chartStartCol + 2, 120);
  dash.setColumnWidth(chartStartCol + 3, 120);
  dash.setColumnWidth(chartStartCol + 4, 120);

  PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties()
    .setProperty("DASHBOARD_TOP10_MINICHART_START", String(top10Start));
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 56A — TOP 10 MINI CHART LEGEND
// PURPOSE:
// Adds a quick explanation below the mini chart table.
// =====================================================

function addTop10MiniChartLegend() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!dash) return;

  const props = PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties();
  const top10Start = Number(props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_TOP10_MINICHART_START")) || 0;

  if (!top10Start) return;

  const rowCount = detectTableLength(dash, top10Start, 14);
  const legendRow = top10Start + rowCount + 1;
  const startCol = 14;

  dash.getRange(legendRow, startCol, 2, 5).clearContent();

  dash.getRange(legendRow, startCol)
    .setValue("Mini bars are visual guides only: Score max 100, Yield max 15%, Upside max 100%, Allocation max 15%.")
    .setFontStyle("italic")
    .setFontColor("#666666");

  dash.getRange(legendRow, startCol, 1, 5).merge();
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 56B — TOP 10 MINI CHART REFRESH WRAPPER
// PURPOSE:
// Runs all mini chart visual functions together.
// =====================================================

function refreshTop10MiniCharts() {
  createTop10MiniCharts();
  addTop10MiniChartLegend();
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 57 — FREEZE / COLUMN WIDTH / ROW HEIGHT OPTIMISATION
// PURPOSE:
// Improves workbook usability and readability by standardising:
// - frozen rows / columns
// - column widths
// - row heights
// - text wrapping
// - alignment
// across Input, Dashboard, History Summary, System Log,
// Error Log, User Guide, Visual Legend, and import sheets.
// =====================================================

function applyWorkbookLayoutOptimisation() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);
  const history = ss.getSheetByName("History");
  const historySummary = ss.getSheetByName("History Summary");
  const systemLog = ss.getSheetByName("System Log");
  const errorLog = ss.getSheetByName("Error Log");
  const userGuide = ss.getSheetByName("User Guide");
  const visualLegend = ss.getSheetByName("Visual Legend");
  const fundamentalImport = ss.getSheetByName("Fundamental Import");
  const fundamentalValidation = ss.getSheetByName("Fundamental Import Validation");

  if (input) optimiseInputSheetLayout_(input);
  if (dash) optimiseDashboardLayout_(dash);
  if (history) optimiseLargeDataSheetLayout_(history);
  if (historySummary) optimiseSummarySheetLayout_(historySummary);
  if (systemLog) optimiseLogSheetLayout_(systemLog);
  if (errorLog) optimiseLogSheetLayout_(errorLog);
  if (userGuide) optimiseGuideSheetLayout_(userGuide);
  if (visualLegend) optimiseGuideSheetLayout_(visualLegend);
  if (fundamentalImport) optimiseImportSheetLayout_(fundamentalImport);
  if (fundamentalValidation) optimiseLogSheetLayout_(fundamentalValidation);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 57A — INPUT SHEET LAYOUT OPTIMISATION
// PURPOSE:
// Makes Input easier to use as a ticker-control sheet.
// =====================================================

function optimiseInputSheetLayout_(input) {

  const headers = getHeaders(input);
  const lastRow = Math.max(input.getLastRow(), 2);
  const lastCol = input.getLastColumn();

  input.setFrozenRows(1);

  const tickerCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker") + 1;

  if (tickerCol > 0) {
    input.setFrozenColumns(tickerCol);
    input.setColumnWidth(tickerCol, 130);
  }

  input.getDataRange()
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setFontSize(10)
    .setVerticalAlignment("middle");

  input.getRange(1, 1, 1, lastCol)
    .setWrap(true)
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  input.setRowHeight(1, 46);

  // Important column widths
  setColumnWidthByHeader_(input, headers, "Company", 220);
  setColumnWidthByHeader_(input, headers, "Ticker", 130);
  setColumnWidthByHeader_(input, headers, "Share Price", 100);
  setColumnWidthByHeader_(input, headers, "Market Cap", 140);
  setColumnWidthByHeader_(input, headers, "PE Ratio", 90);
  setColumnWidthByHeader_(input, headers, "EPS", 90);
  setColumnWidthByHeader_(input, headers, "Beta", 80);
  setColumnWidthByHeader_(input, headers, "52 Week High", 110);
  setColumnWidthByHeader_(input, headers, "52 Week Low", 110);
  setColumnWidthByHeader_(input, headers, "GoogleFinance Score", 120);
  setColumnWidthByHeader_(input, headers, "Final Recommendation", 170);
  setColumnWidthByHeader_(input, headers, "Watchlist Status", 150);
  setColumnWidthByHeader_(input, headers, "Ticker Data Status", 220);
  setColumnWidthByHeader_(input, headers, "Ticker Format Suggestion", 300);
  setColumnWidthByHeader_(input, headers, "Remarks", 320);

  // Standard data row height
  input.setRowHeights(2, Math.max(lastRow - 1, 1), 24);

  // Wrap only long text fields
  wrapColumnsByHeader_(input, headers, [
    "Remarks",
    "Notes",
    "Investment Thesis",
    "Risk Notes",
    "Ticker Data Status",
    "Ticker Format Suggestion"
  ]);

  input.autoResizeRows(1, 1);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 57B — DASHBOARD LAYOUT OPTIMISATION
// PURPOSE:
// Improves Dashboard reading experience.
// =====================================================

function optimiseDashboardLayout_(dash) {

  const lastRow = Math.max(dash.getLastRow(), 1);
  const lastCol = Math.max(dash.getLastColumn(), 20);

  dash.setFrozenRows(1);

  dash.getDataRange()
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setFontSize(10)
    .setVerticalAlignment("middle");

  // Main left-side dashboard table widths
  dash.setColumnWidth(1, 95);   // Rank / Ticker / Metric
  dash.setColumnWidth(2, 130);  // Ticker
  dash.setColumnWidth(3, 190);  // Company / Price
  dash.setColumnWidth(4, 105);
  dash.setColumnWidth(5, 105);
  dash.setColumnWidth(6, 115);
  dash.setColumnWidth(7, 130);
  dash.setColumnWidth(8, 130);
  dash.setColumnWidth(9, 140);
  dash.setColumnWidth(10, 150);
  dash.setColumnWidth(11, 260);
  dash.setColumnWidth(12, 130);
  dash.setColumnWidth(13, 130);

  // Right-side panel widths
  dash.setColumnWidth(14, 210);
  dash.setColumnWidth(15, 240);
  dash.setColumnWidth(16, 120);
  dash.setColumnWidth(17, 120);
  dash.setColumnWidth(18, 120);

  // General row heights
  dash.setRowHeights(2, Math.max(lastRow - 1, 1), 24);

  // More height for KPI area if present
  for (let r = 2; r <= 5; r++) {
    dash.setRowHeight(r, 32);
  }

  // Keep title large
  dash.setRowHeight(1, 34);

  // Wrap text in long right-side panels
  dash.getRange(1, 14, lastRow, Math.max(lastCol - 13, 1))
    .setWrap(true);

  // Make table areas readable
  dash.getRange(1, 1, lastRow, lastCol)
    .setVerticalAlignment("middle");
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 57C — LARGE DATA SHEET LAYOUT
// PURPOSE:
// Optimises large sheets like History without heavy formatting.
// =====================================================

function optimiseLargeDataSheetLayout_(sheet) {

  const lastCol = Math.max(sheet.getLastColumn(), 1);

  sheet.setFrozenRows(1);
  sheet.setFrozenColumns(1);

  sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, lastCol)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  sheet.getDataRange()
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setFontSize(9);

  sheet.setColumnWidth(1, 120);

  for (let c = 2; c <= Math.min(lastCol, 30); c++) {
    sheet.setColumnWidth(c, 100);
  }
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 57D — SUMMARY SHEET LAYOUT
// PURPOSE:
// Optimises compact summary tables.
// =====================================================

function optimiseSummarySheetLayout_(sheet) {

  const lastRow = Math.max(sheet.getLastRow(), 2);
  const lastCol = Math.max(sheet.getLastColumn(), 1);

  sheet.setFrozenRows(1);
  sheet.setFrozenColumns(1);

  sheet.getDataRange()
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setFontSize(10)
    .setVerticalAlignment("middle");

  sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, lastCol)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  sheet.setRowHeight(1, 34);
  sheet.setRowHeights(2, Math.max(lastRow - 1, 1), 24);

  sheet.autoResizeColumns(1, lastCol);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 57E — LOG SHEET LAYOUT
// PURPOSE:
// Optimises System Log, Error Log, and validation logs.
// =====================================================

function optimiseLogSheetLayout_(sheet) {

  const lastRow = Math.max(sheet.getLastRow(), 2);
  const lastCol = Math.max(sheet.getLastColumn(), 1);

  sheet.setFrozenRows(1);

  sheet.getDataRange()
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setFontSize(10)
    .setVerticalAlignment("top");

  sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, lastCol)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  sheet.setRowHeight(1, 34);
  sheet.setRowHeights(2, Math.max(lastRow - 1, 1), 28);

  sheet.getDataRange().setWrap(true);

  sheet.autoResizeColumns(1, lastCol);

  // Make common long columns readable
  for (let c = 1; c <= lastCol; c++) {
    if (sheet.getColumnWidth(c) > 350) {
      sheet.setColumnWidth(c, 350);
    }
  }
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 57F — GUIDE / LEGEND SHEET LAYOUT
// PURPOSE:
// Makes guide sheets presentation-friendly.
// =====================================================

function optimiseGuideSheetLayout_(sheet) {

  const lastRow = Math.max(sheet.getLastRow(), 1);
  const lastCol = Math.max(sheet.getLastColumn(), 2);

  sheet.setFrozenRows(1);

  sheet.getDataRange()
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setFontSize(11)
    .setVerticalAlignment("middle")
    .setWrap(true);

  sheet.setRowHeights(1, lastRow, 28);

  sheet.setColumnWidth(1, 260);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(2, 520);

  if (lastCol > 2) {
    sheet.autoResizeColumns(3, lastCol - 2);
  }
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 57G — FUNDAMENTAL IMPORT SHEET LAYOUT
// PURPOSE:
// Makes manual fundamental import easier to paste and review.
// =====================================================

function optimiseImportSheetLayout_(sheet) {

  const lastCol = Math.max(sheet.getLastColumn(), 1);

  sheet.setFrozenRows(1);
  sheet.setFrozenColumns(1);

  sheet.getDataRange()
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setFontSize(10)
    .setVerticalAlignment("middle");

  sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, lastCol)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center")
    .setWrap(true);

  sheet.setRowHeight(1, 46);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(1, 130);

  for (let c = 2; c <= lastCol; c++) {
    sheet.setColumnWidth(c, 140);
  }
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 57H — HELPER: SET COLUMN WIDTH BY HEADER
// =====================================================

function setColumnWidthByHeader_(sheet, headers, header, width) {
  const c = colIndex(headers, header);
  if (c >= 0) {
    sheet.setColumnWidth(c + 1, width);
  }
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 57I — HELPER: WRAP COLUMNS BY HEADER
// =====================================================

function wrapColumnsByHeader_(sheet, headers, headerNames) {

  const lastRow = Math.max(sheet.getLastRow(), 2);

  headerNames.forEach(header => {
    const c = colIndex(headers, header);
    if (c >= 0) {
      sheet.getRange(1, c + 1, lastRow, 1).setWrap(true);
    }
  });
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 58 — DASHBOARD PRINT LAYOUT
// PURPOSE:
// Creates a print/report-friendly Dashboard layout.
// Useful when exporting Dashboard to PDF or presenting to
// management.
// Applies:
// - hidden gridlines
// - clean page-like layout
// - print area helper notes
// - report title/date block
// - simplified section styling
// =====================================================

function applyDashboardPrintLayout() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!dash) {
    throw new Error("Dashboard sheet not found.");
  }

  const lastRow = Math.max(dash.getLastRow(), 1);
  const lastCol = Math.max(dash.getLastColumn(), 20);

  // Hide gridlines for presentation feel
  dash.setHiddenGridlines(true);

  // Base report style
  dash.getDataRange()
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setFontSize(9)
    .setVerticalAlignment("middle");

  // Report title area
  dash.getRange("A1:L1")
    .merge()
    .setValue("Stocks Overseer Advisor — Investment Dashboard")
    .setBackground("#111827")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(16)
    .setHorizontalAlignment("left");

  dash.setRowHeight(1, 36);

  // Add report timestamp
  dash.getRange("N1")
    .setValue("Report Generated");

  dash.getRange("O1")
    .setValue(new Date())
    .setNumberFormat("dd/mm/yyyy hh:mm");

  dash.getRange("N1:O1")
    .setBackground("#111827")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  // Standard page-friendly widths
  const widths = {
    1: 85,
    2: 120,
    3: 160,
    4: 90,
    5: 90,
    6: 105,
    7: 115,
    8: 115,
    9: 130,
    10: 140,
    11: 220,
    12: 120,
    13: 120,
    14: 200,
    15: 230,
    16: 120,
    17: 120,
    18: 120
  };

  Object.keys(widths).forEach(c => {
    const col = Number(c);
    if (dash.getMaxColumns() >= col) {
      dash.setColumnWidth(col, widths[c]);
    }
  });

  // Clean row heights
  dash.setRowHeights(2, Math.max(lastRow - 1, 1), 22);

  // Preserve KPI / title area row height
  for (let r = 1; r <= 6; r++) {
    dash.setRowHeight(r, r === 1 ? 36 : 28);
  }

  // Add light page border around main used area
  dash.getRange(1, 1, lastRow, Math.min(lastCol, 18))
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, false, false, "#e5e7eb", SpreadsheetApp.BorderStyle.SOLID);

  // Freeze top row for on-screen navigation
  dash.setFrozenRows(1);

  // Print guidance panel
  createDashboardPrintGuidePanel();
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 58A — DASHBOARD PRINT GUIDE PANEL
// PURPOSE:
// Adds a panel explaining how to export as PDF.
// =====================================================

function createDashboardPrintGuidePanel() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!dash) return;

  const startRow = 96;
  const startCol = 14; // Column N

  const table = [
    ["Print / PDF Guide", ""],
    ["Best Export", "File > Download > PDF"],
    ["Orientation", "Landscape"],
    ["Scale", "Fit to width"],
    ["Margins", "Narrow"],
    ["Gridlines", "Off"],
    ["Recommended", "Export Dashboard only"]
  ];

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, 10, 4).clearContent();

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, table.length, 2)
    .setValues(table);

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, 1, 2)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  dash.getRange(startRow + 1, startCol, table.length - 1, 1)
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setBackground("#f3f6fa");

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, table.length, 2)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  dash.autoResizeColumns(startCol, 4);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 58B — CREATE EXECUTIVE PRINT SUMMARY SHEET
// PURPOSE:
// Creates a compact print-ready Executive Summary sheet
// with key KPI cards and Top 10 table only.
// This is lighter and better for PDF export.
// =====================================================

function createExecutivePrintSummarySheet() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) {
    throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");
  }

  let printSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Executive Summary");

  if (!printSheet) {
    printSheet = ss.insertSheet("Executive Summary");
  }

  printSheet.clear();
  printSheet.setHiddenGridlines(true);

  const data = input.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];

  const tickerCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker");
  const companyCol = colIndex(headers, "Company");
  const priceCol = colIndex(headers, "Share Price");
  const peCol = colIndex(headers, "PE Ratio");
  const scoreCol = colIndex(headers, "GoogleFinance Score");
  const earningsYieldCol = colIndex(headers, "Earnings Yield %");
  const upsideCol = colIndex(headers, "Upside to 52W High %");
  const betaRiskCol = colIndex(headers, "Beta Risk Group");
  const allocationCol = colIndex(headers, "Portfolio Allocation %");
  const recommendationCol = colIndex(headers, "Final Recommendation");
  const statusCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker Data Status");

  let totalTickers = 0;
  let pricedTickers = 0;
  let missingPrice = 0;
  let buyCandidates = 0;
  let dataWarnings = 0;

  const stocks = [];

  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {

    const row = data[r];

    if (!row[tickerCol]) continue;

    totalTickers++;

    const price = num(row[priceCol]);
    const score = num(row[scoreCol]);
    const recommendation = row[recommendationCol];
    const status = statusCol >= 0 ? row[statusCol] : "";

    if (price > 0) pricedTickers++;
    else missingPrice++;

    if (recommendation === "BUY CANDIDATE") buyCandidates++;
    if (status && status !== "OK") dataWarnings++;

    if (price && score) {
      stocks.push({
        ticker: row[tickerCol],
        company: companyCol >= 0 ? row[companyCol] : "",
        price: price,
        pe: num(row[peCol]),
        score: score,
        earningsYield: num(row[earningsYieldCol]),
        upside: num(row[upsideCol]),
        betaRisk: row[betaRiskCol],
        allocation: num(row[allocationCol]),
        recommendation: recommendation
      });
    }
  }

  const priceCoverage = totalTickers > 0 ? pricedTickers / totalTickers : 0;

  // Title
  printSheet.getRange("A1:J1")
    .merge()
    .setValue("Stocks Overseer Advisor — Executive Summary")
    .setBackground("#111827")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(16);

  printSheet.getRange("A2")
    .setValue("Generated");

  printSheet.getRange("B2")
    .setValue(new Date())
    .setNumberFormat("dd/mm/yyyy hh:mm");

  // KPI table
  const kpi = [
    ["Metric", "Value"],
    ["Total Tickers", totalTickers],
    ["Priced Tickers", pricedTickers],
    ["Missing Price Data", missingPrice],
    ["Price Coverage %", priceCoverage],
    ["Buy Candidates", buyCandidates],
    ["Data Warnings", dataWarnings]
  ];

  printSheet.getRange(4, 1, kpi.length, 2)
    .setValues(kpi);

  printSheet.getRange(4, 1, 1, 2)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  printSheet.getRange(8, 2)
    .setNumberFormat("0.00%");

  // Top 10
  const recommendationRank = {
    "BUY CANDIDATE": 5,
    "ACCUMULATE / STUDY": 4,
    "VALUE WATCH": 3,
    "HOLD / MONITOR": 2,
    "AVOID / HIGH RISK": 1
  };

  stocks.sort((a, b) => {
    const recA = recommendationRank[a.recommendation] || 0;
    const recB = recommendationRank[b.recommendation] || 0;

    if (recB !== recA) return recB - recA;
    if (b.score !== a.score) return b.score - a.score;
    return b.allocation - a.allocation;
  });

  const top10 = stocks.slice(0, 10);

  const topTable = [
    [
      "Rank",
      "Ticker",
      "Company",
      "Price",
      "PE",
      "Score",
      "Earnings Yield %",
      "52W Upside %",
      "Beta Risk",
      "Recommendation"
    ]
  ];

  top10.forEach((s, i) => {
    topTable.push([
      i + 1,
      s.ticker,
      s.company,
      s.price,
      s.pe,
      s.score,
      s.earningsYield,
      s.upside,
      s.betaRisk,
      s.recommendation
    ]);
  });

  printSheet.getRange(13, 1)
    .setValue("Top 10 Decision View")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(12)
    .setBackground("#d9e2f3");

  printSheet.getRange(15, 1, topTable.length, topTable[0].length)
    .setValues(topTable);

  printSheet.getRange(15, 1, 1, topTable[0].length)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");
