  printSheet.getRange(16, 4, Math.max(topTable.length - 1, 1), 3)
    .setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");

  printSheet.getRange(16, 7, Math.max(topTable.length - 1, 1), 2)
    .setNumberFormat("0.00%");

  printSheet.getRange(4, 1, kpi.length, 2)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  printSheet.getRange(15, 1, topTable.length, topTable[0].length)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  printSheet.getDataRange()
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setFontSize(10)
    .setVerticalAlignment("middle");

  printSheet.setFrozenRows(1);
  printSheet.autoResizeColumns(1, 10);

  // Better print widths
  printSheet.setColumnWidth(1, 70);
  printSheet.setColumnWidth(2, 120);
  printSheet.setColumnWidth(3, 220);
  printSheet.setColumnWidth(10, 170);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 58C — PRINT LAYOUT REFRESH WRAPPER
// PURPOSE:
// Runs all print-layout functions together.
// =====================================================

function refreshPrintLayout() {
  applyDashboardPrintLayout();
  createExecutivePrintSummarySheet();
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 59 — CONDITIONAL ROW HIGHLIGHTING
// PURPOSE:
// Highlights entire rows based on key decision/status fields.
// Applies to:
// - Input sheet
// - Dashboard Top 10 table
// - Dashboard Watchlist table
// - Dashboard Unsupported Ticker table
// This makes BUY / AVOID / missing-data rows much easier to scan.
// =====================================================

function applyConditionalRowHighlighting() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (input) {
    applyInputRowHighlighting_(input);
  }

  if (dash) {
    applyDashboardRowHighlighting_(dash);
  }
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 59A — INPUT ROW HIGHLIGHTING
// PURPOSE:
// Highlights entire Input rows using formula-based rules.
// Priority:
// 1. Missing ticker / no price data
// 2. Avoid / high risk
// 3. Buy candidate
// 4. Accumulate / study
// 5. Value watch
// =====================================================

function applyInputRowHighlighting_(input) {

  const headers = getHeaders(input);
  const lastRow = Math.max(input.getLastRow(), 2);
  const lastCol = input.getLastColumn();

  const tickerCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker") + 1;
  const priceCol = colIndex(headers, "Share Price") + 1;
  const recommendationCol = colIndex(headers, "Final Recommendation") + 1;
  const statusCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker Data Status") + 1;

  if (tickerCol <= 0 || recommendationCol <= 0) return;

  const range = input.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, lastCol);
  const rules = input.getConditionalFormatRules();

  // No price data / ticker format warning
  if (priceCol > 0) {
    rules.push(
      SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
        .whenFormulaSatisfied(`=AND($${columnLetter_(tickerCol)}2<>"",$${columnLetter_(priceCol)}2="")`)
        .setBackground("#f4cccc")
        .setFontColor("#990000")
        .setRanges([range])
        .build()
    );
  }

  // Ticker data status warning
  if (statusCol > 0) {
    rules.push(
      SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
        .whenFormulaSatisfied(`=AND($${columnLetter_(statusCol)}2<>"",$${columnLetter_(statusCol)}2<>"OK")`)
        .setBackground("#fce5cd")
        .setFontColor("#783f04")
        .setRanges([range])
        .build()
    );
  }

  // Avoid / high risk
  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenFormulaSatisfied(`=$${columnLetter_(recommendationCol)}2="AVOID / HIGH RISK"`)
      .setBackground("#f4cccc")
      .setFontColor("#990000")
      .setRanges([range])
      .build()
  );

  // Buy candidate
  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenFormulaSatisfied(`=$${columnLetter_(recommendationCol)}2="BUY CANDIDATE"`)
      .setBackground("#d9ead3")
      .setFontColor("#274e13")
      .setRanges([range])
      .build()
  );

  // Accumulate / study
  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenFormulaSatisfied(`=$${columnLetter_(recommendationCol)}2="ACCUMULATE / STUDY"`)
      .setBackground("#eef7e9")
      .setFontColor("#274e13")
      .setRanges([range])
      .build()
  );

  // Value watch
  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenFormulaSatisfied(`=$${columnLetter_(recommendationCol)}2="VALUE WATCH"`)
      .setBackground("#e8f1fb")
      .setFontColor("#073763")
      .setRanges([range])
      .build()
  );

  input.setConditionalFormatRules(rules);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 59B — DASHBOARD ROW HIGHLIGHTING
// PURPOSE:
// Applies row highlighting to key dashboard decision tables.
// =====================================================

function applyDashboardRowHighlighting_(dash) {

  const props = PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties();
  const rules = dash.getConditionalFormatRules();

  // Top 10 table: recommendation column = L / 12
  const top10Start = Number(props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_TOP10_START")) || 0;
  if (top10Start) {
    const rows = detectTableLength(dash, top10Start, 2);
    if (rows > 0) {
      const top10Range = dash.getRange(top10Start, 1, rows, 13);
      addDashboardDecisionRowRules_(rules, top10Range, top10Start, 12);
    }
  }

  // Watchlist table: recommendation column = J / 10
  const watchlistStart = Number(props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_WATCHLIST_START")) || 0;
  if (watchlistStart) {
    const rows = detectTableLength(dash, watchlistStart, 1);
    if (rows > 0) {
      const watchlistRange = dash.getRange(watchlistStart, 1, rows, 11);
      addDashboardDecisionRowRules_(rules, watchlistRange, watchlistStart, 10);
    }
  }

  // Portfolio table: recommendation column = F / 6
  const portfolioStart = Number(props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_PORTFOLIO_START")) || 0;
  if (portfolioStart) {
    const rows = detectTableLength(dash, portfolioStart, 1);
    if (rows > 0) {
      const portfolioRange = dash.getRange(portfolioStart, 1, rows, 7);
      addDashboardDecisionRowRules_(rules, portfolioRange, portfolioStart, 6);
    }
  }

  // Unsupported ticker table: status column = J / 10
  const unsupportedStart = Number(props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_UNSUPPORTED_START")) || 0;
  if (unsupportedStart) {
    const rows = detectTableLength(dash, unsupportedStart, 1);
    if (rows > 0) {
      const unsupportedRange = dash.getRange(unsupportedStart, 1, rows, 11);

      rules.push(
        SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
          .whenFormulaSatisfied(`=$J${unsupportedStart}<>""`)
          .setBackground("#fce5cd")
          .setFontColor("#783f04")
          .setRanges([unsupportedRange])
          .build()
      );
    }
  }

  dash.setConditionalFormatRules(rules);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 59C — DASHBOARD DECISION ROW RULE HELPER
// PURPOSE:
// Adds recommendation-based row rules to a dashboard range.
// =====================================================

function addDashboardDecisionRowRules_(rules, range, startRow, recommendationCol) {

  const recLetter = columnLetter_(recommendationCol);

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenFormulaSatisfied(`=$${recLetter}${startRow}="BUY CANDIDATE"`)
      .setBackground("#eaf4e4")
      .setFontColor("#274e13")
      .setRanges([range])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenFormulaSatisfied(`=$${recLetter}${startRow}="ACCUMULATE / STUDY"`)
      .setBackground("#f3faee")
      .setFontColor("#274e13")
      .setRanges([range])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenFormulaSatisfied(`=$${recLetter}${startRow}="VALUE WATCH"`)
      .setBackground("#edf5ff")
      .setFontColor("#073763")
      .setRanges([range])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenFormulaSatisfied(`=$${recLetter}${startRow}="HOLD / MONITOR"`)
      .setBackground("#fffaf0")
      .setFontColor("#7f6000")
      .setRanges([range])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenFormulaSatisfied(`=$${recLetter}${startRow}="AVOID / HIGH RISK"`)
      .setBackground("#fce8e6")
      .setFontColor("#990000")
      .setRanges([range])
      .build()
  );
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 59D — COLUMN LETTER HELPER
// PURPOSE:
// Converts a 1-based column number to Google Sheets letter.
// Example: 1 = A, 27 = AA.
// =====================================================

function columnLetter_(column) {

  let temp = "";
  let letter = "";

  while (column > 0) {
    temp = (column - 1) % 26;
    letter = String.fromCharCode(temp + 65) + letter;
    column = (column - temp - 1) / 26;
  }

  return letter;
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 59E — ROW HIGHLIGHTING LEGEND PANEL
// PURPOSE:
// Adds a Dashboard legend explaining row highlight colours.
// =====================================================

function createDashboardRowHighlightLegendPanel() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!dash) return;

  const startRow = 106;
  const startCol = 14; // Column N

  const table = [
    ["Row Highlight Legend", ""],
    ["Green row", "Buy Candidate / Accumulate"],
    ["Blue row", "Value Watch"],
    ["Yellow row", "Hold / Monitor"],
    ["Red row", "Avoid / Missing data"],
    ["Orange row", "Ticker data warning"]
  ];

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, 10, 4).clearContent();

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, table.length, 2)
    .setValues(table);

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, 1, 2)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  dash.getRange(startRow + 1, startCol, 1, 1).setBackground("#eaf4e4");
  dash.getRange(startRow + 2, startCol, 1, 1).setBackground("#edf5ff");
  dash.getRange(startRow + 3, startCol, 1, 1).setBackground("#fffaf0");
  dash.getRange(startRow + 4, startCol, 1, 1).setBackground("#fce8e6");
  dash.getRange(startRow + 5, startCol, 1, 1).setBackground("#fce5cd");

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, table.length, 2)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  dash.autoResizeColumns(startCol, 4);
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 60 — EXECUTIVE SUMMARY BANNER
// PURPOSE:
// Adds a one-line executive summary banner at the top of
// Dashboard to quickly communicate portfolio/data status.
// The banner is generated from:
// - Total ticker count
// - Price coverage
// - Missing price data
// - Buy candidates
// - Data warnings
// - High-risk / avoid count
// =====================================================

function createExecutiveSummaryBanner() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) {
    throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");
  }

  if (!dash) {
    throw new Error("Dashboard sheet not found.");
  }

  const data = input.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];

  const tickerCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker");
  const priceCol = colIndex(headers, "Share Price");
  const recommendationCol = colIndex(headers, "Final Recommendation");
  const statusCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker Data Status");
  const betaRiskCol = colIndex(headers, "Beta Risk Group");

  let totalTickers = 0;
  let pricedTickers = 0;
  let missingPrice = 0;
  let buyCandidates = 0;
  let avoidHighRisk = 0;
  let dataWarnings = 0;
  let highRiskCount = 0;
  let veryHighRiskCount = 0;

  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {

    const row = data[r];

    if (!row[tickerCol]) continue;

    totalTickers++;

    const price = num(row[priceCol]);
    const recommendation = row[recommendationCol];
    const status = statusCol >= 0 ? row[statusCol] : "";
    const betaRisk = betaRiskCol >= 0 ? row[betaRiskCol] : "";

    if (price > 0) pricedTickers++;
    else missingPrice++;

    if (recommendation === "BUY CANDIDATE") buyCandidates++;
    if (recommendation === "AVOID / HIGH RISK") avoidHighRisk++;

    if (status && status !== "OK") dataWarnings++;

    if (betaRisk === "HIGH RISK") highRiskCount++;
    if (betaRisk === "VERY HIGH RISK") veryHighRiskCount++;
  }

  const priceCoverage = totalTickers > 0 ? pricedTickers / totalTickers : 0;

  // =====================================================
  // DETERMINE OVERALL STATUS
  // =====================================================

  let statusLabel = "HEALTHY WATCHLIST";
  let bannerColour = "#d9ead3";
  let fontColour = "#274e13";

  if (missingPrice > 0 || dataWarnings > 0) {
    statusLabel = "DATA REVIEW REQUIRED";
    bannerColour = "#fff2cc";
    fontColour = "#7f6000";
  }

  if (priceCoverage < 0.90 || missingPrice >= 10) {
    statusLabel = "DATA QUALITY WARNING";
    bannerColour = "#fce5cd";
    fontColour = "#783f04";
  }

  if (avoidHighRisk > totalTickers * 0.35 || veryHighRiskCount > totalTickers * 0.10) {
    statusLabel = "RISK REVIEW REQUIRED";
    bannerColour = "#f4cccc";
    fontColour = "#990000";
  }

  const summaryText =
    statusLabel +
    " | Total Tickers: " + totalTickers +
    " | Price Coverage: " + formatPercentText_(priceCoverage) +
    " | Missing Price: " + missingPrice +
    " | Buy Candidates: " + buyCandidates +
    " | Avoid / High Risk: " + avoidHighRisk +
    " | Data Warnings: " + dataWarnings;

  // =====================================================
  // DASHBOARD LOCATION
  // Row 6 is below KPI cards and above summary/top tables.
  // =====================================================

  const bannerRow = 6;

  dash.getRange(bannerRow, 1, 1, 13)
    .merge()
    .setValue(summaryText)
    .setBackground(bannerColour)
    .setFontColor(fontColour)
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(11)
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center")
    .setVerticalAlignment("middle")
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true, "#d9d9d9", SpreadsheetApp.BorderStyle.SOLID);

  dash.setRowHeight(bannerRow, 30);

  PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties()
    .setProperty("DASHBOARD_EXECUTIVE_BANNER_STATUS", statusLabel);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 60A — EXECUTIVE BANNER DETAIL PANEL
// PURPOSE:
// Adds a short explanation panel to the Dashboard right side.
// =====================================================

function createExecutiveBannerDetailPanel() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!dash) return;

  const props = PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties();
  const statusLabel = props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_EXECUTIVE_BANNER_STATUS") || "N/A";

  const startRow = 116;
  const startCol = 14; // Column N

  const table = [
    ["Executive Banner Logic", ""],
    ["Current Status", statusLabel],
    ["Healthy Watchlist", "Good coverage, manageable warnings"],
    ["Data Review Required", "Some missing prices / warnings"],
    ["Data Quality Warning", "Low price coverage or many missing prices"],
    ["Risk Review Required", "High avoid/high-risk concentration"]
  ];

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, 10, 4).clearContent();

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, table.length, 2)
    .setValues(table);

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, 1, 2)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  dash.getRange(startRow + 1, startCol, table.length - 1, 1)
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setBackground("#f3f6fa");

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, table.length, 2)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  dash.autoResizeColumns(startCol, 4);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 60B — FORMAT PERCENT TEXT HELPER
// PURPOSE:
// Converts decimal values into short percentage text.
// =====================================================

function formatPercentText_(value) {

  if (value === "" || value == null || isNaN(value)) {
    return "N/A";
  }

  return (Number(value) * 100).toFixed(1) + "%";
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 60C — REFRESH EXECUTIVE SUMMARY BANNER
// PURPOSE:
// Wrapper to refresh banner and detail panel together.
// =====================================================

function refreshExecutiveSummaryBanner() {
  createExecutiveSummaryBanner();
  createExecutiveBannerDetailPanel();
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 62 — DASHBOARD VIEW MODE CONTROL
// PURPOSE:
// Provides Full / Compact dashboard modes.
// Compact mode hides heavy detail sections to create a cleaner
// management review screen.
// =====================================================

function setDashboardCompactMode() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!dash) {
    throw new Error("Dashboard sheet not found.");
  }

  // Show all rows first
  dash.showRows(1, dash.getMaxRows());

  const props = PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties();

  const rankingStart = Number(props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_RANKING_START")) || 0;
  const watchlistStart = Number(props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_WATCHLIST_START")) || 0;
  const portfolioStart = Number(props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_PORTFOLIO_START")) || 0;
  const historyStart = Number(props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_HISTORY_START")) || 0;
  const unsupportedStart = Number(props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_UNSUPPORTED_START")) || 0;
  const suggestionStart = Number(props.getProperty("DASHBOARD_TICKER_SUGGESTION_START")) || 0;

  // Hide long detail tables in compact mode.
  hideSectionRows_(dash, rankingStart, 80);
  hideSectionRows_(dash, watchlistStart, 80);
  hideSectionRows_(dash, portfolioStart, 80);
  hideSectionRows_(dash, historyStart, 140);
  hideSectionRows_(dash, unsupportedStart, 60);
  hideSectionRows_(dash, suggestionStart, 60);

  dash.getRange("N2")
    .setValue("Dashboard Mode")
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  dash.getRange("O2")
    .setValue("COMPACT")
    .setBackground("#fff2cc")
    .setFontColor("#7f6000")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert("Compact Dashboard mode applied.");
}


function setDashboardFullMode() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!dash) {
    throw new Error("Dashboard sheet not found.");
  }

  dash.showRows(1, dash.getMaxRows());

  dash.getRange("N2")
    .setValue("Dashboard Mode")
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  dash.getRange("O2")
    .setValue("FULL")
    .setBackground("#d9ead3")
    .setFontColor("#274e13")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert("Full Dashboard mode applied.");
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 62A — HIDE SECTION ROW HELPER
// =====================================================

function hideSectionRows_(sheet, startRow, maxRows) {

  if (!startRow || startRow <= 0) return;

  const safeStart = Math.max(startRow - 3, 1);
  const availableRows = sheet.getMaxRows() - safeStart + 1;
  const hideRows = Math.min(maxRows, availableRows);

  if (hideRows > 0) {
    sheet.hideRows(safeStart, hideRows);
  }
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 65 — DASHBOARD FILTER VIEW BUTTONS / FILTER SHEETS
// PURPOSE:
// Creates quick filtered view sheets from Input:
// - Buy Candidates
// - Value Watch
// - High Risk
// - Missing Data
// Also adds a dashboard panel telling users which functions to run.
// =====================================================

function createDashboardFilterViews() {

  createFilteredViewSheet_("Buy Candidates", "Final Recommendation", "BUY CANDIDATE");
  createFilteredViewSheet_("Value Watch", "Final Recommendation", "VALUE WATCH");
  createFilteredViewSheet_("High Risk", "Beta Risk Group", "HIGH RISK");
  createFilteredViewSheet_("Very High Risk", "Beta Risk Group", "VERY HIGH RISK");
  createMissingDataViewSheet_();
  createDashboardFilterViewPanel();
}


function createFilteredViewSheet_(sheetName, filterHeader, filterValue) {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");

  let out = ss.getSheetByName(sheetName);
  if (!out) out = ss.insertSheet(sheetName);
  out.clear();

  const data = input.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];
  const filterCol = colIndex(headers, filterHeader);

  if (filterCol < 0) {
    out.getRange("A1").setValue("Filter column not found: " + filterHeader);
    return;
  }

  const selectedHeaders = [
    "Ticker",
    "Company",
    "Share Price",
    "PE Ratio",
    "Earnings Yield %",
    "Upside to 52W High %",
    "GoogleFinance Score",
    "Beta Risk Group",
    "Momentum Signal",
    "Portfolio Allocation %",
    "Final Recommendation",
    "Watchlist Status",
    "Remarks"
  ];

  const selectedIndexes = selectedHeaders.map(h => colIndex(headers, h));

  const rows = [selectedHeaders];

  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {
    if (data[r][filterCol] === filterValue) {
      rows.push(selectedIndexes.map(i => i >= 0 ? data[r][i] : ""));
    }
  }

  out.getRange(1, 1, rows.length, rows[0].length).setValues(rows);
  formatFilteredViewSheet_(out);
}


function createMissingDataViewSheet_() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");

  let out = ss.getSheetByName("Missing Data");
  if (!out) out = ss.insertSheet("Missing Data");
  out.clear();

  const data = input.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];

  const tickerCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker");
  const companyCol = colIndex(headers, "Company");
  const priceCol = colIndex(headers, "Share Price");
  const statusCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker Data Status");
  const suggestionCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker Format Suggestion");

  const rows = [["Ticker", "Company", "Share Price", "Ticker Data Status", "Ticker Format Suggestion"]];

  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {

    const ticker = data[r][tickerCol];
    if (!ticker) continue;

    const price = num(data[r][priceCol]);
    const status = statusCol >= 0 ? data[r][statusCol] : "";
    const suggestion = suggestionCol >= 0 ? data[r][suggestionCol] : "";

    if (!price || (status && status !== "OK")) {
      rows.push([
        ticker,
        companyCol >= 0 ? data[r][companyCol] : "",
        priceCol >= 0 ? data[r][priceCol] : "",
        status,
        suggestion
      ]);
    }
  }

  out.getRange(1, 1, rows.length, rows[0].length).setValues(rows);
  formatFilteredViewSheet_(out);
}


function formatFilteredViewSheet_(sheet) {

  const lastRow = Math.max(sheet.getLastRow(), 2);
  const lastCol = Math.max(sheet.getLastColumn(), 1);

  sheet.setFrozenRows(1);
  sheet.getDataRange().setFontFamily("Arial").setFontSize(10);

  sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, lastCol)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  sheet.getRange(1, 1, lastRow, lastCol)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  sheet.autoResizeColumns(1, lastCol);
}


function createDashboardFilterViewPanel() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!dash) return;

  const startRow = 126;
  const startCol = 14;

  const table = [
    ["Filter View Buttons", ""],
    ["Create All Views", "createDashboardFilterViews"],
    ["Buy Candidates", "Sheet: Buy Candidates"],
    ["Value Watch", "Sheet: Value Watch"],
    ["High Risk", "Sheet: High Risk"],
    ["Very High Risk", "Sheet: Very High Risk"],
    ["Missing Data", "Sheet: Missing Data"]
  ];

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, 10, 4).clearContent();
  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, table.length, 2).setValues(table);

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, 1, 2)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  dash.getRange(startRow + 1, startCol, table.length - 1, 1)
    .setBackground("#d9e2f3")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, table.length, 2)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  dash.autoResizeColumns(startCol, 4);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 66 — COLOUR THEME SELECTOR
// PURPOSE:
// Lets user switch dashboard theme:
// - Dark Finance
// - Blue Corporate
// - Gold Executive
// =====================================================

function applyThemeDarkFinance() {
  applyDashboardThemePalette_("#111827", "#1f2933", "#d9e2f3", "#ffffff", "#1f2933", "Dark Finance");
}

function applyThemeBlueCorporate() {
  applyDashboardThemePalette_("#0b5394", "#1c4587", "#d9eaf7", "#ffffff", "#073763", "Blue Corporate");
}

function applyThemeGoldExecutive() {
  applyDashboardThemePalette_("#7f6000", "#bf9000", "#fff2cc", "#ffffff", "#7f6000", "Gold Executive");
}


function applyDashboardThemePalette_(titleBg, headerBg, sectionBg, titleFont, sectionFont, themeName) {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!dash) return;

  const lastRow = Math.max(dash.getLastRow(), 1);
  const lastCol = Math.max(dash.getLastColumn(), 20);

  // Main title
  dash.getRange("A1:L1")
    .setBackground(titleBg)
    .setFontColor(titleFont)
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  // Right title strip
  dash.getRange("N1:O1")
    .setBackground(titleBg)
    .setFontColor(titleFont)
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  // Style major section title cells by known section titles
  const sectionTitles = [
    "Top 10 Decision View",
    "Clean GoogleFinance Ranking Dashboard",
    "Clean Watchlist Dashboard Table",
    "Clean Portfolio Allocation Dashboard",
    "Portfolio Concentration Check",
    "Risk Grouping Dashboard",
    "Historical Share Price Snapshot",
    "Unsupported / Missing Data Ticker Dashboard",
    "Ticker Format Suggestions",
    "Risk Heatmap — Score Band vs Beta Risk",
    "Ticker Count + Data Coverage Summary",
    "Overseer Status Panel",
    "Dashboard Navigation",
    "Latest System Log",
    "Error Log Summary",
    "User Zone",
    "Manual Input Reminder",
    "Fundamental Import Layer",
    "Fundamental Import Validation",
    "Badge Legend",
    "Row Highlight Legend",
    "Executive Banner Logic",
    "Print / PDF Guide",
    "Filter View Buttons"
  ];

  sectionTitles.forEach(title => {
    const cell = dash.createTextFinder(title).matchEntireCell(true).findNext();
    if (cell) {
      cell.setBackground(sectionBg).setFontColor(sectionFont).setFontWeight("bold");
    }
  });

  // Style rows that look like table headers
  const headerKeywords = ["Rank", "Ticker", "Metric", "Risk Group", "Score Band"];
  headerKeywords.forEach(keyword => {
    const matches = dash.createTextFinder(keyword).matchCase(false).findAll();
    matches.forEach(cell => {
      const row = cell.getRow();
      if (row <= 1) return;
      // Main dashboard table headers should be scoped to A:M only.
      // Right sidebar N:Z has its own style.
      dash.getRange(row, 1, 1, Math.min(lastCol, 13))
        .setBackground(headerBg)
        .setFontColor("#ffffff")
        .setFontWeight("bold");
    });
  });

  dash.getRange("N2")
    .setValue("Theme")
    .setBackground(headerBg)
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  dash.getRange("O2")
    .setValue(themeName)
    .setBackground(sectionBg)
    .setFontColor(sectionFont)
    .setFontWeight("bold");
}


function createDashboardThemeSelectorPanel() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!dash) return;

  const startRow = 136;
  const startCol = 14;

  const table = [
    ["Theme Selector", ""],
    ["Dark Finance", "applyThemeDarkFinance"],
    ["Blue Corporate", "applyThemeBlueCorporate"],
    ["Gold Executive", "applyThemeGoldExecutive"]
  ];

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, 8, 4).clearContent();
  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, table.length, 2).setValues(table);

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, 1, 2)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  dash.getRange(startRow + 1, startCol, table.length - 1, 1)
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setBackground("#f3f6fa");

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, table.length, 2)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  dash.autoResizeColumns(startCol, 4);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 67 — MINI ICON INDICATORS
// PURPOSE:
// Adds icon indicator columns in Input and Dashboard views.
// Icons help quickly scan status:
// ✅ good, ⚠️ caution, 🔴 avoid/missing data, 🟢 buy.
// =====================================================

function applyMiniIconIndicators() {

  applyInputMiniIconIndicators_();
  createDashboardIconLegendPanel();
}


function applyInputMiniIconIndicators_() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) return;

  ensureIconHeader_(input);

  const data = input.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];

  const tickerCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker");
  const priceCol = colIndex(headers, "Share Price");
  const recommendationCol = colIndex(headers, "Final Recommendation");
  const statusCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker Data Status");
  const iconCol = colIndex(headers, "Status Icon");

  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {

    const row = data[r];

    if (!row[tickerCol]) continue;

    const price = num(row[priceCol]);
    const recommendation = row[recommendationCol];
    const status = statusCol >= 0 ? row[statusCol] : "";

    let icon = "✅";

    if (!price || (status && status !== "OK")) {
      icon = "🔴";
    } else if (recommendation === "BUY CANDIDATE") {
      icon = "🟢";
    } else if (recommendation === "ACCUMULATE / STUDY" || recommendation === "VALUE WATCH") {
      icon = "🟡";
    } else if (recommendation === "AVOID / HIGH RISK") {
      icon = "🔴";
    } else if (recommendation === "HOLD / MONITOR") {
      icon = "⚠️";
    }

    input.getRange(r + 1, iconCol + 1).setValue(icon);
  }

  input.getRange(1, iconCol + 1)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  input.getRange(2, iconCol + 1, Math.max(input.getLastRow() - 1, 1), 1)
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center")
    .setFontSize(12);

  input.setColumnWidth(iconCol + 1, 70);
}


function ensureIconHeader_(input) {

  let headers = getHeaders(input);

  if (!headers.includes("Status Icon")) {
    const nextCol = input.getLastColumn() + 1;
    input.getRange(1, nextCol).setValue("Status Icon");
  }
}


function createDashboardIconLegendPanel() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!dash) return;

  const startRow = 144;
  const startCol = 14;

  const table = [
    ["Icon Legend", ""],
    ["🟢", "Buy candidate"],
    ["🟡", "Accumulate / Value watch"],
    ["⚠️", "Hold / Monitor"],
    ["🔴", "Avoid / Missing data"],
    ["✅", "Data OK"]
  ];

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, 10, 4).clearContent();
  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, table.length, 2).setValues(table);

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, 1, 2)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, table.length, 2)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  dash.autoResizeColumns(startCol, 4);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 68 — DASHBOARD SECTION SEPARATORS
// PURPOSE:
// Adds clean horizontal separator rows between major sections.
// Improves white-space management and visual hierarchy.
// =====================================================

function applyDashboardSectionSeparators() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!dash) return;

  const sectionTitles = [
    "Top 10 Decision View",
    "Clean GoogleFinance Ranking Dashboard",
    "Clean Watchlist Dashboard Table",
    "Clean Portfolio Allocation Dashboard",
    "Portfolio Concentration Check",
    "Risk Grouping Dashboard",
    "Historical Share Price Snapshot",
    "Unsupported / Missing Data Ticker Dashboard",
    "Ticker Format Suggestions",
    "Risk Heatmap — Score Band vs Beta Risk"
  ];

  sectionTitles.forEach(title => {
    const cell = dash.createTextFinder(title).matchEntireCell(true).findNext();

    if (!cell) return;

    const row = cell.getRow();

    if (row > 2) {
      dash.getRange(row - 1, 1, 1, 13)
        .setBackground("#e5e7eb")
        .setBorder(false, false, true, false, false, false, "#9ca3af", SpreadsheetApp.BorderStyle.SOLID_MEDIUM);
      dash.setRowHeight(row - 1, 10);
    }

    dash.getRange(row, 1, 1, 13)
      .setBackground("#d9e2f3")
      .setFontColor("#1f2933")
      .setFontWeight("bold");
  });
}


function refreshUiEnhancementModules() {
  createDashboardFilterViews();
  createDashboardThemeSelectorPanel();
  applyMiniIconIndicators();
  applyDashboardSectionSeparators();
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 70 — MANAGEMENT ONE-PAGE VIEW
// PURPOSE:
// Creates a separate board-level "Management View" sheet.
// This is a clean one-page executive view, separate from
// the operational Dashboard.
// Includes:
// - KPI strip
// - Executive status
// - Top 10 decision table
// - Key risk / data quality notes
// - Allocation summary
// - Print-friendly formatting
// =====================================================

function createManagementViewSheet() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) {
    throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");
  }

  let mgmt = ss.getSheetByName("Management View");

  if (!mgmt) {
    mgmt = ss.insertSheet("Management View");
  }

  mgmt.clear();
  mgmt.setHiddenGridlines(true);

  const data = input.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];

  const tickerCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker");
  const companyCol = colIndex(headers, "Company");
  const priceCol = colIndex(headers, "Share Price");
  const peCol = colIndex(headers, "PE Ratio");
  const scoreCol = colIndex(headers, "GoogleFinance Score");
  const earningsYieldCol = colIndex(headers, "Earnings Yield %");
  const upsideCol = colIndex(headers, "Upside to 52W High %");
  const betaRiskCol = colIndex(headers, "Beta Risk Group");
  const momentumCol = colIndex(headers, "Momentum Signal");
  const allocationCol = colIndex(headers, "Portfolio Allocation %");
  const recommendationCol = colIndex(headers, "Final Recommendation");
  const statusCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker Data Status");

  let totalTickers = 0;
  let pricedTickers = 0;
  let missingPrice = 0;
  let scoredTickers = 0;
  let allocatedTickers = 0;
  let buyCandidates = 0;
  let avoidHighRisk = 0;
  let dataWarnings = 0;
  let highRiskCount = 0;
  let veryHighRiskCount = 0;

  const stocks = [];
  const missingTickers = [];

  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {

    const row = data[r];

    if (!row[tickerCol]) continue;

    totalTickers++;

    const ticker = row[tickerCol];
    const company = companyCol >= 0 ? row[companyCol] : "";
    const price = num(row[priceCol]);
    const score = num(row[scoreCol]);
    const allocation = num(row[allocationCol]);
    const recommendation = row[recommendationCol];
    const betaRisk = betaRiskCol >= 0 ? row[betaRiskCol] : "";
    const status = statusCol >= 0 ? row[statusCol] : "";

    if (price > 0) pricedTickers++;
    else {
      missingPrice++;
      missingTickers.push(ticker);
    }

    if (score > 0) scoredTickers++;
    if (allocation > 0) allocatedTickers++;
    if (recommendation === "BUY CANDIDATE") buyCandidates++;
    if (recommendation === "AVOID / HIGH RISK") avoidHighRisk++;

    if (status && status !== "OK") dataWarnings++;
    if (betaRisk === "HIGH RISK") highRiskCount++;
    if (betaRisk === "VERY HIGH RISK") veryHighRiskCount++;

    if (ticker && price && score) {
      stocks.push({
        ticker: ticker,
        company: company,
        price: price,
        pe: num(row[peCol]),
        score: score,
        earningsYield: num(row[earningsYieldCol]),
        upside: num(row[upsideCol]),
        betaRisk: betaRisk,
        momentum: momentumCol >= 0 ? row[momentumCol] : "",
        allocation: allocation,
        recommendation: recommendation
      });
    }
  }

  const priceCoverage = totalTickers > 0 ? pricedTickers / totalTickers : 0;
  const scoreCoverage = totalTickers > 0 ? scoredTickers / totalTickers : 0;
  const allocationCoverage = totalTickers > 0 ? allocatedTickers / totalTickers : 0;

  const status = buildManagementStatus_(priceCoverage, missingPrice, dataWarnings, avoidHighRisk, veryHighRiskCount, totalTickers);

  // =====================================================
  // TITLE
  // =====================================================

  mgmt.getRange("A1:J1")
    .merge()
    .setValue("Stocks Overseer Advisor — Management One-Page View")
    .setBackground("#111827")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(16)
    .setHorizontalAlignment("left");

  mgmt.getRange("A2")
    .setValue("Generated");

  mgmt.getRange("B2")
    .setValue(new Date())
    .setNumberFormat("dd/mm/yyyy hh:mm");

  mgmt.getRange("H2")
    .setValue("Executive Status");

  mgmt.getRange("I2:J2")
    .merge()
    .setValue(status.label)
    .setBackground(status.colour)
    .setFontColor(status.font)
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  // =====================================================
  // KPI STRIP
  // =====================================================

  const kpi = [
    ["Total Tickers", totalTickers],
    ["Price Coverage", priceCoverage],
    ["Missing Price", missingPrice],
    ["Buy Candidates", buyCandidates],
    ["Avoid / High Risk", avoidHighRisk],
    ["Data Warnings", dataWarnings]
  ];

  let kpiCol = 1;

  kpi.forEach(item => {

    mgmt.getRange(4, kpiCol, 1, 2)
      .merge()
      .setValue(item[0])
      .setBackground("#1f2933")
      .setFontColor("#ffffff")
      .setFontWeight("bold")
      .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

    mgmt.getRange(5, kpiCol, 2, 2)
      .merge()
      .setValue(item[1])
      .setBackground("#f3f6fa")
      .setFontWeight("bold")
      .setFontSize(14)
      .setHorizontalAlignment("center")
      .setVerticalAlignment("middle")
      .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

    if (item[0] === "Price Coverage") {
      mgmt.getRange(5, kpiCol).setNumberFormat("0.00%");
    }

    kpiCol += 2;
  });

  // =====================================================
  // EXECUTIVE SUMMARY NOTES
  // =====================================================

  const notes = [
    ["Executive Summary", ""],
    ["Universe Coverage", pricedTickers + " priced out of " + totalTickers + " tickers (" + formatPercentText_(priceCoverage) + ")"],
    ["Decision Opportunity", buyCandidates + " buy candidates identified from current GoogleFinance-derived screen"],
    ["Risk Watch", avoidHighRisk + " avoid/high-risk recommendations; " + highRiskCount + " high risk and " + veryHighRiskCount + " very high risk beta groups"],
    ["Data Quality", missingPrice + " missing price records and " + dataWarnings + " ticker data warnings"],
    ["Missing Tickers", missingTickers.slice(0, 8).join(", ") || "None"]
  ];

  mgmt.getRange(8, 1, notes.length, 2)
    .setValues(notes);

  mgmt.getRange(8, 1, 1, 2)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  mgmt.getRange(9, 1, notes.length - 1, 1)
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setBackground("#f3f6fa");

  mgmt.getRange(8, 1, notes.length, 2)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  // =====================================================
  // TOP 10 DECISION TABLE
  // =====================================================

  const recommendationRank = {
    "BUY CANDIDATE": 5,
    "ACCUMULATE / STUDY": 4,
    "VALUE WATCH": 3,
    "HOLD / MONITOR": 2,
    "AVOID / HIGH RISK": 1
  };

  stocks.sort((a, b) => {
    const recA = recommendationRank[a.recommendation] || 0;
    const recB = recommendationRank[b.recommendation] || 0;

    if (recB !== recA) return recB - recA;
    if (b.score !== a.score) return b.score - a.score;
    return b.allocation - a.allocation;
  });

  const top10 = stocks.slice(0, 10);

  const topTable = [
    [
      "Rank",
      "Ticker",
      "Company",
      "Price",
      "PE",
      "Score",
      "Earnings Yield %",
      "52W Upside %",
      "Beta Risk",
      "Recommendation"
    ]
  ];

  top10.forEach((s, i) => {
    topTable.push([
      i + 1,
      s.ticker,
      s.company,
      s.price,
      s.pe,
      s.score,
      s.earningsYield,
      s.upside,
      s.betaRisk,
      s.recommendation
    ]);
  });

  mgmt.getRange(16, 1)
    .setValue("Top 10 Decision View")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(12)
    .setBackground("#d9e2f3")
    .setFontColor("#1f2933");

  mgmt.getRange(18, 1, topTable.length, topTable[0].length)
    .setValues(topTable);

  mgmt.getRange(18, 1, 1, topTable[0].length)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  mgmt.getRange(19, 4, Math.max(topTable.length - 1, 1), 3)
    .setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");

  mgmt.getRange(19, 7, Math.max(topTable.length - 1, 1), 2)
    .setNumberFormat("0.00%");

  mgmt.getRange(18, 1, topTable.length, topTable[0].length)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  // =====================================================
  // ALLOCATION SUMMARY
  // =====================================================

  const allocatedStocks = [...stocks]
    .filter(s => s.allocation > 0)
    .sort((a, b) => b.allocation - a.allocation)
    .slice(0, 5);

  const allocationTable = [["Top Allocation", "Allocation %"]];

  allocatedStocks.forEach(s => {
    allocationTable.push([s.ticker, s.allocation]);
  });

  mgmt.getRange(31, 1)
    .setValue("Top Allocation Summary")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(12)
    .setBackground("#d9e2f3")
    .setFontColor("#1f2933");

  mgmt.getRange(33, 1, allocationTable.length, allocationTable[0].length)
    .setValues(allocationTable);

  mgmt.getRange(33, 1, 1, allocationTable[0].length)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  mgmt.getRange(34, 2, Math.max(allocationTable.length - 1, 1), 1)
    .setNumberFormat("0.00%");

  mgmt.getRange(33, 1, allocationTable.length, allocationTable[0].length)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  // =====================================================
  // MANAGEMENT VIEW FORMATTING
  // =====================================================

  formatManagementViewSheet_(mgmt);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 70A — MANAGEMENT STATUS HELPER
// PURPOSE:
// Generates board-level status label and colour.
// =====================================================

function buildManagementStatus_(priceCoverage, missingPrice, dataWarnings, avoidHighRisk, veryHighRiskCount, totalTickers) {

  let label = "HEALTHY WATCHLIST";
  let colour = "#d9ead3";
  let font = "#274e13";

  if (missingPrice > 0 || dataWarnings > 0) {
    label = "DATA REVIEW REQUIRED";
    colour = "#fff2cc";
    font = "#7f6000";
  }

  if (priceCoverage < 0.90 || missingPrice >= 10) {
    label = "DATA QUALITY WARNING";
    colour = "#fce5cd";
    font = "#783f04";
  }

  if (totalTickers > 0 && (avoidHighRisk > totalTickers * 0.35 || veryHighRiskCount > totalTickers * 0.10)) {
    label = "RISK REVIEW REQUIRED";
    colour = "#f4cccc";
    font = "#990000";
  }

  return {
    label: label,
    colour: colour,
    font: font
  };
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 70B — FORMAT MANAGEMENT VIEW SHEET
// PURPOSE:
// Makes the Management View print/report friendly.
// =====================================================

function formatManagementViewSheet_(sheet) {

  sheet.setHiddenGridlines(true);
  sheet.setFrozenRows(1);

  sheet.getDataRange()
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setFontSize(10)
    .setVerticalAlignment("middle");

  sheet.setRowHeight(1, 36);
  sheet.setRowHeights(2, Math.max(sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 1), 24);

  sheet.setColumnWidth(1, 80);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(2, 120);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(3, 220);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(4, 90);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(5, 80);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(6, 90);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(7, 120);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(8, 120);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(9, 130);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(10, 170);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(11, 90);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(12, 90);

  sheet.getRange("A1:J1")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("left");

  sheet.getRange("A4:L6")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center")
    .setVerticalAlignment("middle");

  sheet.getRange("A8:B13")
    .setWrap(true);

  sheet.getRange("A18:J28")
    .setVerticalAlignment("middle");

  // Recommendation colour badges
  const rules = [];

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("BUY CANDIDATE")
      .setBackground("#38761d")
      .setFontColor("#ffffff")
      .setBold(true)
      .setRanges([sheet.getRange("J19:J28")])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("ACCUMULATE / STUDY")
      .setBackground("#6aa84f")
      .setFontColor("#ffffff")
      .setBold(true)
      .setRanges([sheet.getRange("J19:J28")])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("VALUE WATCH")
      .setBackground("#3c78d8")
      .setFontColor("#ffffff")
      .setBold(true)
      .setRanges([sheet.getRange("J19:J28")])
      .build()
  );

  sheet.setConditionalFormatRules(rules);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 70C — MANAGEMENT VIEW REFRESH WRAPPER
// PURPOSE:
// Refreshes the one-page management sheet.
// =====================================================

function refreshManagementView() {
  createManagementViewSheet();
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 71 — INVESTMENT COMMITTEE VIEW
// PURPOSE:
// Creates a separate Investment Committee sheet focused on
// Buy / Accumulate / Hold / Avoid decisions.
// This is designed for review meetings and decision logging.
// =====================================================

function createInvestmentCommitteeView() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) {
    throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");
  }

  let ic = ss.getSheetByName("Investment Committee");

  if (!ic) {
    ic = ss.insertSheet("Investment Committee");
  }

  ic.clear();
  ic.setHiddenGridlines(true);

  const data = input.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];

  const tickerCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker");
  const companyCol = colIndex(headers, "Company");
  const priceCol = colIndex(headers, "Share Price");
  const peCol = colIndex(headers, "PE Ratio");
  const scoreCol = colIndex(headers, "GoogleFinance Score");
  const earningsYieldCol = colIndex(headers, "Earnings Yield %");
  const upsideCol = colIndex(headers, "Upside to 52W High %");
  const betaRiskCol = colIndex(headers, "Beta Risk Group");
  const momentumCol = colIndex(headers, "Momentum Signal");
  const allocationCol = colIndex(headers, "Portfolio Allocation %");
  const recommendationCol = colIndex(headers, "Final Recommendation");
  const watchlistCol = colIndex(headers, "Watchlist Status");
  const remarksCol = colIndex(headers, "Remarks");

  const decisionRows = [
    [
      "Decision Group",
      "Ticker",
      "Company",
      "Price",
      "PE",
      "Score",
      "Earnings Yield %",
      "52W Upside %",
      "Beta Risk",
      "Momentum",
      "Allocation %",
      "Watchlist",
      "Remarks",
      "Committee Decision",
      "Decision Notes"
    ]
  ];

  const recommendationOrder = {
    "BUY CANDIDATE": 1,
    "ACCUMULATE / STUDY": 2,
    "VALUE WATCH": 3,
    "HOLD / MONITOR": 4,
    "AVOID / HIGH RISK": 5
  };

  const stocks = [];

  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {

    const row = data[r];
    const ticker = row[tickerCol];

    if (!ticker) continue;

    stocks.push({
      recommendation: row[recommendationCol] || "UNCLASSIFIED",
      ticker: ticker,
      company: companyCol >= 0 ? row[companyCol] : "",
      price: num(row[priceCol]),
      pe: num(row[peCol]),
      score: num(row[scoreCol]),
      earningsYield: num(row[earningsYieldCol]),
      upside: num(row[upsideCol]),
      betaRisk: betaRiskCol >= 0 ? row[betaRiskCol] : "",
      momentum: momentumCol >= 0 ? row[momentumCol] : "",
      allocation: num(row[allocationCol]),
      watchlist: watchlistCol >= 0 ? row[watchlistCol] : "",
      remarks: remarksCol >= 0 ? row[remarksCol] : ""
    });
  }

  stocks.sort((a, b) => {
    const aRank = recommendationOrder[a.recommendation] || 99;
    const bRank = recommendationOrder[b.recommendation] || 99;
    if (aRank !== bRank) return aRank - bRank;
    return b.score - a.score;
  });

  stocks.forEach(s => {
    decisionRows.push([
      s.recommendation,
      s.ticker,
      s.company,
      s.price,
      s.pe,
      s.score,
      s.earningsYield,
      s.upside,
      s.betaRisk,
      s.momentum,
      s.allocation,
      s.watchlist,
      s.remarks,
      "",
      ""
    ]);
  });

  ic.getRange("A1:O1")
    .merge()
    .setValue("Stocks Overseer Advisor — Investment Committee View")
    .setBackground("#111827")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(16);

  ic.getRange("A2").setValue("Generated");
  ic.getRange("B2").setValue(new Date()).setNumberFormat("dd/mm/yyyy hh:mm");

  ic.getRange(4, 1, decisionRows.length, decisionRows[0].length)
    .setValues(decisionRows);

  formatInvestmentCommitteeView_(ic);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 71A — FORMAT INVESTMENT COMMITTEE VIEW
// =====================================================

function formatInvestmentCommitteeView_(sheet) {

  const lastRow = Math.max(sheet.getLastRow(), 2);
  const lastCol = Math.max(sheet.getLastColumn(), 15);

  sheet.setFrozenRows(4);
  sheet.getDataRange().setFontFamily("Arial").setFontSize(10).setVerticalAlignment("middle");

  sheet.getRange(4, 1, 1, lastCol)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  sheet.getRange(5, 7, Math.max(lastRow - 4, 1), 2).setNumberFormat("0.00%");
  sheet.getRange(5, 11, Math.max(lastRow - 4, 1), 1).setNumberFormat("0.00%");
  sheet.getRange(5, 4, Math.max(lastRow - 4, 1), 3).setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");

  sheet.getRange(4, 1, Math.max(lastRow - 3, 1), lastCol)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  sheet.setColumnWidth(1, 160);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(2, 120);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(3, 220);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(13, 320);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(14, 180);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(15, 300);

  const rules = [];

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("BUY CANDIDATE")
      .setBackground("#d9ead3")
      .setFontColor("#274e13")
      .setRanges([sheet.getRange(5, 1, Math.max(lastRow - 4, 1), lastCol)])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("AVOID / HIGH RISK")
      .setBackground("#f4cccc")
      .setFontColor("#990000")
      .setRanges([sheet.getRange(5, 1, Math.max(lastRow - 4, 1), lastCol)])
      .build()
  );

  sheet.setConditionalFormatRules(rules);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 72 — SCORE EXPLANATION PANEL
// PURPOSE:
// Creates a Score Explanation sheet explaining why each stock
// received its GoogleFinance-derived score.
// =====================================================

function createScoreExplanationPanel() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) {
    throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");
  }

  let scoreSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Score Explanation");

  if (!scoreSheet) {
    scoreSheet = ss.insertSheet("Score Explanation");
  }

  scoreSheet.clear();
  scoreSheet.setHiddenGridlines(true);

  const data = input.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];

  const tickerCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker");
  const companyCol = colIndex(headers, "Company");
  const peCol = colIndex(headers, "PE Ratio");
  const betaCol = colIndex(headers, "Beta");
  const earningsYieldCol = colIndex(headers, "Earnings Yield %");
  const positionCol = colIndex(headers, "52W Price Position %");
  const scoreCol = colIndex(headers, "GoogleFinance Score");
  const betaRiskCol = colIndex(headers, "Beta Risk Group");
  const momentumCol = colIndex(headers, "Momentum Signal");
  const recommendationCol = colIndex(headers, "Final Recommendation");

  const rows = [
    [
      "Ticker",
      "Company",
      "Score",
      "PE",
      "Earnings Yield %",
      "Beta",
      "Beta Risk",
      "52W Position %",
      "Momentum",
      "Recommendation",
      "Score Explanation"
    ]
  ];

  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {

    const row = data[r];
    const ticker = row[tickerCol];

    if (!ticker) continue;

    const pe = num(row[peCol]);
    const earningsYield = num(row[earningsYieldCol]);
    const beta = num(row[betaCol]);
    const position = num(row[positionCol]);
    const score = num(row[scoreCol]);
    const betaRisk = row[betaRiskCol];
    const momentum = row[momentumCol];
    const recommendation = row[recommendationCol];

    rows.push([
      ticker,
      companyCol >= 0 ? row[companyCol] : "",
      score,
      pe,
      earningsYield,
      beta,
      betaRisk,
      position,
      momentum,
      recommendation,
      buildScoreExplanation_(pe, earningsYield, beta, position, score, recommendation)
    ]);
  }

  scoreSheet.getRange("A1:K1")
    .merge()
    .setValue("Stocks Overseer Advisor — Score Explanation Panel")
    .setBackground("#111827")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(16);

  scoreSheet.getRange(3, 1, rows.length, rows[0].length)
    .setValues(rows);

  formatScoreExplanationPanel_(scoreSheet);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 72A — BUILD SCORE EXPLANATION TEXT
// =====================================================

function buildScoreExplanation_(pe, earningsYield, beta, position, score, recommendation) {

  const parts = [];

  if (pe > 0 && pe <= 15) parts.push("Low/moderate PE supports valuation score");
  else if (pe > 30) parts.push("High PE reduces valuation attractiveness");
  else if (!pe) parts.push("PE unavailable or not meaningful");

  if (earningsYield >= 0.08) parts.push("High earnings yield supports value case");
  else if (earningsYield > 0 && earningsYield < 0.04) parts.push("Low earnings yield weakens value case");

  if (beta > 0 && beta <= 0.7) parts.push("Low beta improves risk profile");
  else if (beta >= 1.5) parts.push("High beta increases risk adjustment");

  if (position <= 0.25 && position !== "") parts.push("Price near 52W low; potential value/watch zone");
  else if (position >= 0.80) parts.push("Price near 52W high; momentum strong but entry risk higher");

  if (score >= 80) parts.push("Overall score is strong");
  else if (score >= 60) parts.push("Overall score is moderate");
  else if (score > 0) parts.push("Overall score is weak");

  if (recommendation) parts.push("Final recommendation: " + recommendation);

  return parts.join(" | ");
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 72B — FORMAT SCORE EXPLANATION PANEL
// =====================================================

function formatScoreExplanationPanel_(sheet) {

  const lastRow = Math.max(sheet.getLastRow(), 2);
  const lastCol = Math.max(sheet.getLastColumn(), 11);

  sheet.setFrozenRows(3);
  sheet.getDataRange().setFontFamily("Arial").setFontSize(10).setVerticalAlignment("top");

  sheet.getRange(3, 1, 1, lastCol)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  sheet.getRange(4, 5, Math.max(lastRow - 3, 1), 1).setNumberFormat("0.00%");
  sheet.getRange(4, 8, Math.max(lastRow - 3, 1), 1).setNumberFormat("0.00%");
  sheet.getRange(4, 3, Math.max(lastRow - 3, 1), 4).setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");

  sheet.getRange(3, 1, Math.max(lastRow - 2, 1), lastCol)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  sheet.setColumnWidth(1, 120);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(2, 220);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(10, 170);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(11, 520);
  sheet.getRange(1, 1, lastRow, lastCol).setWrap(true);
}
