// =====================================================
// MODULE 76 — THEME + BRANDING PRESET SHEET
// PURPOSE:
// Creates a Branding Presets sheet where titles, firm name,
// and visual theme notes can be controlled.
// This is a lightweight branding control layer.
// =====================================================

function createThemeBrandingPresetSheet() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

  let branding = ss.getSheetByName("Branding Presets");

  if (!branding) {
    branding = ss.insertSheet("Branding Presets");
  }

  branding.clear();
  branding.setHiddenGridlines(true);

  const rows = [
    ["Branding Presets", "Value", "Notes"],
    ["Dashboard Title", "Stocks Overseer Advisor Dashboard", "Used as main dashboard title"],
    ["Management View Title", "Stocks Overseer Advisor — Management One-Page View", "Board-level report title"],
    ["Firm / Project Name", "Stocks Overseer Advisor", "Change to your advisory/project name"],
    ["Preferred Theme", "Dark Finance", "Options: Dark Finance, Blue Corporate, Gold Executive"],
    ["Primary Colour", "#111827", "Dark header colour"],
    ["Secondary Colour", "#1f2933", "Table header colour"],
    ["Accent Colour", "#d9e2f3", "Section title colour"],
    ["Positive Colour", "#d9ead3", "Positive/healthy indicators"],
    ["Warning Colour", "#fff2cc", "Review/caution indicators"],
    ["Negative Colour", "#f4cccc", "Risk/missing data indicators"],
    ["Prepared By", "", "Optional"],
    ["Report Footer", "Generated from GoogleFinance and Apps Script-derived metrics.", "Footer note"]
  ];

  branding.getRange(1, 1, rows.length, rows[0].length).setValues(rows);

  branding.getRange(1, 1, 1, 3)
    .setBackground("#111827")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  branding.getRange(2, 1, rows.length - 1, 1)
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setBackground("#f3f6fa");

  branding.getRange(1, 1, rows.length, 3)
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true)
    .setVerticalAlignment("middle");

  branding.setColumnWidth(1, 240);
  branding.setColumnWidth(2, 320);
  branding.setColumnWidth(3, 520);
  branding.setFrozenRows(1);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 76A — APPLY BRANDING PRESETS
// PURPOSE:
// Applies title and preferred theme from Branding Presets.
// =====================================================

function applyThemeBrandingPresets() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const branding = ss.getSheetByName("Branding Presets");
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);
  const mgmt = ss.getSheetByName("Management View");

  if (!branding) {
    createThemeBrandingPresetSheet();
  refreshBrandingPresetsUiEffects();
    return;
  }

  const data = branding.getDataRange().getValues();
  const map = {};

  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {
    map[data[r][0]] = data[r][1];
  }

  if (dash && map["Dashboard Title"]) {
    dash.getRange("A1")
      .setValue(map["Dashboard Title"]);
  }

  if (mgmt && map["Management View Title"]) {
    mgmt.getRange("A1")
      .setValue(map["Management View Title"]);
  }

  const theme = map["Preferred Theme"];

  if (theme === "Blue Corporate") {
    applyThemeBlueCorporate();
  } else if (theme === "Gold Executive") {
    applyThemeGoldExecutive();
  } else {
    applyThemeDarkFinance();
  }
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 71/72/75/76 REFRESH WRAPPER
// PURPOSE:
// Runs all decision-support and control sheets together.
// =====================================================

function refreshDecisionSupportSheets() {
  createInvestmentCommitteeView();
  createScoreExplanationPanel();
  refreshCommitteeAndScoreUiUpgrade();
  createDashboardControlPanel();
  refreshControlPanelUiEffects();
  createThemeBrandingPresetSheet();
  applyThemeBrandingPresets();
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 78 — EXECUTIVE CHARTS SHEET
// PURPOSE:
// Creates a separate chart-only management sheet.
// This avoids overloading the operational Dashboard and gives
// a cleaner executive visual review page.
// Includes:
// - Recommendation mix chart
// - Risk group chart
// - Score band chart
// - Top 10 score chart
// - Allocation chart
// - Data quality chart
// =====================================================

function createExecutiveChartsSheet() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) {
    throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");
  }

  let charts = ss.getSheetByName("Executive Charts");

  if (!charts) {
    charts = ss.insertSheet("Executive Charts");
  }

  charts.clear();
  charts.setHiddenGridlines(true);

  // Remove old charts
  charts.getCharts().forEach(chart => charts.removeChart(chart));

  const data = input.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];

  const tickerCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker");
  const companyCol = colIndex(headers, "Company");
  const priceCol = colIndex(headers, "Share Price");
  const scoreCol = colIndex(headers, "GoogleFinance Score");
  const allocationCol = colIndex(headers, "Portfolio Allocation %");
  const recommendationCol = colIndex(headers, "Final Recommendation");
  const betaRiskCol = colIndex(headers, "Beta Risk Group");
  const statusCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker Data Status");

  const recommendationCounts = {};
  const riskCounts = {};
  const scoreBandCounts = {
    "80–100": 0,
    "60–79": 0,
    "40–59": 0,
    "20–39": 0,
    "0–19": 0,
    "No Score": 0
  };

  let totalTickers = 0;
  let pricedTickers = 0;
  let missingPrice = 0;
  let dataWarnings = 0;

  const stocks = [];

  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {

    const row = data[r];

    if (!row[tickerCol]) continue;

    totalTickers++;

    const ticker = row[tickerCol];
    const company = companyCol >= 0 ? row[companyCol] : "";
    const price = num(row[priceCol]);
    const score = num(row[scoreCol]);
    const allocation = num(row[allocationCol]);
    const recommendation = row[recommendationCol] || "UNCLASSIFIED";
    const betaRisk = row[betaRiskCol] || "NO BETA DATA";
    const status = statusCol >= 0 ? row[statusCol] : "";

    if (price > 0) pricedTickers++;
    else missingPrice++;

    if (status && status !== "OK") dataWarnings++;

    recommendationCounts[recommendation] = (recommendationCounts[recommendation] || 0) + 1;
    riskCounts[betaRisk] = (riskCounts[betaRisk] || 0) + 1;
    scoreBandCounts[getScoreBandForHeatmap_(score)]++;

    if (price && score) {
      stocks.push({
        ticker: ticker,
        company: company,
        score: score,
        allocation: allocation,
        recommendation: recommendation,
        betaRisk: betaRisk
      });
    }
  }

  // =====================================================
  // TITLE
  // =====================================================

  charts.getRange("A1:L1")
    .merge()
    .setValue("Stocks Overseer Advisor — Executive Charts")
    .setBackground("#111827")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(16);

  charts.getRange("A2")
    .setValue("Generated");

  charts.getRange("B2")
    .setValue(new Date())
    .setNumberFormat("dd/mm/yyyy hh:mm");

  // =====================================================
  // BUILD CHART DATA TABLES
  // =====================================================

  const recommendationTable = [["Recommendation", "Count"]];
  Object.keys(recommendationCounts).forEach(k => {
    recommendationTable.push([k, recommendationCounts[k]]);
  });

  const riskTable = [["Risk Group", "Count"]];
  Object.keys(riskCounts).forEach(k => {
    riskTable.push([k, riskCounts[k]]);
  });

  const scoreBandTable = [["Score Band", "Count"]];
  Object.keys(scoreBandCounts).forEach(k => {
    scoreBandTable.push([k, scoreBandCounts[k]]);
  });

  const dataQualityTable = [
    ["Metric", "Count"],
    ["Total Tickers", totalTickers],
    ["Priced Tickers", pricedTickers],
    ["Missing Price", missingPrice],
    ["Data Warnings", dataWarnings]
  ];

  const top10ScoreTable = [["Ticker", "Score"]];
  [...stocks]
    .sort((a, b) => b.score - a.score)
    .slice(0, 10)
    .forEach(s => {
      top10ScoreTable.push([s.ticker, s.score]);
    });

  const allocationTable = [["Ticker", "Allocation %"]];
  [...stocks]
    .filter(s => s.allocation > 0)
    .sort((a, b) => b.allocation - a.allocation)
    .slice(0, 10)
    .forEach(s => {
      allocationTable.push([s.ticker, s.allocation]);
    });

  // Place data tables below charts area
  writeExecutiveChartTable_(charts, 40, 1, "Recommendation Mix Data", recommendationTable);
  writeExecutiveChartTable_(charts, 40, 4, "Risk Group Data", riskTable);
  writeExecutiveChartTable_(charts, 40, 7, "Score Band Data", scoreBandTable);
  writeExecutiveChartTable_(charts, 40, 10, "Data Quality Data", dataQualityTable);
  writeExecutiveChartTable_(charts, 60, 1, "Top 10 Score Data", top10ScoreTable);
  writeExecutiveChartTable_(charts, 60, 4, "Top Allocation Data", allocationTable);

  // =====================================================
  // CREATE CHARTS
  // =====================================================

  createExecutiveChartsVisuals_(charts);

  formatExecutiveChartsSheet_(charts);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 78A — WRITE EXECUTIVE CHART DATA TABLE
// PURPOSE:
// Writes compact chart source data to fixed cells.
// =====================================================

function writeExecutiveChartTable_(sheet, row, col, title, table) {

  sheet.getRange(row, col)
    .setValue(title)
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setBackground("#d9e2f3")
    .setFontColor("#1f2933");

  sheet.getRange(row + 1, col, table.length, table[0].length)
    .setValues(table);

  sheet.getRange(row + 1, col, 1, table[0].length)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  sheet.getRange(row + 1, col, table.length, table[0].length)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 78B — CREATE EXECUTIVE CHART VISUALS
// PURPOSE:
// Creates all charts using the compact source tables.
// =====================================================

function createExecutiveChartsVisuals_(charts) {

  // Recommendation Mix Pie Chart
  const recRows = detectTableLength(charts, 42, 1);
  if (recRows > 1) {
    const chart = charts.newChart()
      .setChartType(Charts.ChartType.PIE)
      .addRange(charts.getRange(42, 1, recRows, 2))
      .setPosition(4, 1, 0, 0)
      .setOption("title", "Recommendation Mix")
      .setOption("height", 320)
      .setOption("width", 440)
      .build();

    charts.insertChart(chart);
  }

  // Risk Group Column Chart
  const riskRows = detectTableLength(charts, 42, 4);
  if (riskRows > 1) {
    const chart = charts.newChart()
      .setChartType(Charts.ChartType.COLUMN)
      .addRange(charts.getRange(42, 4, riskRows, 2))
      .setPosition(4, 7, 0, 0)
      .setOption("title", "Risk Group Distribution")
      .setOption("legend", { position: "none" })
      .setOption("height", 320)
      .setOption("width", 520)
      .build();

    charts.insertChart(chart);
  }

  // Score Band Column Chart
  const scoreRows = detectTableLength(charts, 42, 7);
  if (scoreRows > 1) {
    const chart = charts.newChart()
      .setChartType(Charts.ChartType.COLUMN)
      .addRange(charts.getRange(42, 7, scoreRows, 2))
      .setPosition(22, 1, 0, 0)
      .setOption("title", "GoogleFinance Score Band Distribution")
      .setOption("legend", { position: "none" })
      .setOption("height", 320)
      .setOption("width", 520)
      .build();

    charts.insertChart(chart);
  }

  // Data Quality Bar Chart
  const dqRows = detectTableLength(charts, 42, 10);
  if (dqRows > 1) {
    const chart = charts.newChart()
      .setChartType(Charts.ChartType.BAR)
      .addRange(charts.getRange(42, 10, dqRows, 2))
      .setPosition(22, 7, 0, 0)
      .setOption("title", "Data Quality Summary")
      .setOption("legend", { position: "none" })
      .setOption("height", 320)
      .setOption("width", 520)
      .build();

    charts.insertChart(chart);
  }

  // Top 10 Score Bar Chart
  const topRows = detectTableLength(charts, 62, 1);
  if (topRows > 1) {
    const chart = charts.newChart()
      .setChartType(Charts.ChartType.BAR)
      .addRange(charts.getRange(62, 1, topRows, 2))
      .setPosition(4, 13, 0, 0)
      .setOption("title", "Top 10 Scores")
      .setOption("legend", { position: "none" })
      .setOption("height", 320)
      .setOption("width", 520)
      .build();

    charts.insertChart(chart);
  }

  // Top Allocation Pie Chart
  const allocRows = detectTableLength(charts, 62, 4);
  if (allocRows > 1) {
    const chart = charts.newChart()
      .setChartType(Charts.ChartType.PIE)
      .addRange(charts.getRange(62, 4, allocRows, 2))
      .setPosition(22, 13, 0, 0)
      .setOption("title", "Top 10 Allocation")
      .setOption("height", 320)
      .setOption("width", 520)
      .build();

    charts.insertChart(chart);
  }
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 78C — FORMAT EXECUTIVE CHARTS SHEET
// PURPOSE:
// Applies print/presentation-friendly styling.
// =====================================================

function formatExecutiveChartsSheet_(sheet) {

  sheet.setHiddenGridlines(true);
  sheet.setFrozenRows(1);

  sheet.getDataRange()
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setFontSize(10)
    .setVerticalAlignment("middle");

  sheet.setRowHeight(1, 36);

  for (let c = 1; c <= 18; c++) {
    sheet.setColumnWidth(c, 110);
  }

  sheet.setColumnWidth(1, 140);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(4, 150);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(7, 150);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(10, 150);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 78D — REFRESH EXECUTIVE CHARTS
// PURPOSE:
// Wrapper for menu and master runner.
// =====================================================

function refreshExecutiveCharts() {
  createExecutiveChartsSheet();
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 79 — GAIN + DIVIDEND CALCULATOR SHEET
// PURPOSE:
// Creates a separate Calculator sheet for quick what-if
// investment calculations.
// User selects ticker from dropdown and manually inputs:
// - Buy Price
// - Desired Buy Price
// - Target Sell Price
// - Shares Bought
// - Desired Increase %
// - Dividend Yield %
// - Dividend Per Share
// - Holding Period Years
// The sheet calculates:
// - Target price
// - Capital gain
// - Dividend income
// - Total return amount
// - Total return %
// - Yield on cost
// - Break-even price after dividend
// =====================================================

function createGainDividendCalculatorSheet() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) {
    throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");
  }

  let calc = ss.getSheetByName("Calculator");

  if (!calc) {
    calc = ss.insertSheet("Calculator");
  }

  calc.clear();
  calc.setHiddenGridlines(true);

  // =====================================================
  // TITLE
  // =====================================================

  calc.getRange("A1:H1")
    .merge()
    .setValue("Stocks Overseer — Gain + Dividend Calculator")
    .setBackground("#111827")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(16)
    .setHorizontalAlignment("left");

  calc.getRange("A2:H2")
    .merge()
    .setValue("Select a ticker, key in your assumptions, and review projected capital gain, dividend income, and total return.")
    .setFontStyle("italic")
    .setFontColor("#666666");

  // =====================================================
  // SECTION 1 — TICKER SELECTOR
  // =====================================================

  const selector = [
    ["Ticker Selection", ""],
    ["Selected Ticker", ""],
    ["Company", ""],
    ["Currency", ""],
    ["Current Share Price", ""],
    ["PE Ratio", ""],
    ["EPS", ""],
    ["GoogleFinance Score", ""],
    ["Final Recommendation", ""],
    ["Dividend Yield % from Input", ""],
    ["Dividend Per Share from Input", ""]
  ];

  calc.getRange(4, 1, selector.length, 2)
    .setValues(selector);

  // Dropdown ticker input at B5
  const tickerRange = input.getRange("A2:A");
  const tickerRule = SpreadsheetApp.newDataValidation()
    .requireValueInRange(tickerRange, true)
    .setAllowInvalid(false)
    .setHelpText("Select ticker from Input sheet.")
    .build();

  calc.getRange("B5")
    .setDataValidation(tickerRule)
    .setBackground("#d9eaf7")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setNote("MANUAL INPUT: Select ticker from dropdown.");

  // Auto formulas from Input using header-based lookup.
  // This prevents blanks/wrong values if Input columns move.
  calc.getRange("B6").setFormula(calculatorLookupFormula_("Input", "Company"));
  calc.getRange("B7").setFormula(calculatorLookupFormula_("Input", "Currency"));
  calc.getRange("B8").setFormula(calculatorLookupFormula_("Input", "Share Price"));
  calc.getRange("B9").setFormula(calculatorLookupFormula_("Input", "PE Ratio"));
  calc.getRange("B10").setFormula(calculatorLookupFormula_("Input", "EPS"));
  calc.getRange("B11").setFormula(calculatorLookupFormula_("Input", "GoogleFinance Score"));
  calc.getRange("B12").setFormula(calculatorLookupFormula_("Input", "Final Recommendation"));

  // Dividend values use fallback headers because different workbooks may name them differently.
  calc.getRange("B13").setFormula(
    `=IFERROR(INDEX(Input!$A:$ZZ,MATCH($B$5,Input!$A:$A,0),MATCH("Dividend Yield %",Input!$1:$1,0)),` +
    `IFERROR(INDEX(Input!$A:$ZZ,MATCH($B$5,Input!$A:$A,0),MATCH("Dividend Yield",Input!$1:$1,0)),` +
    `IFERROR(INDEX(Input!$A:$ZZ,MATCH($B$5,Input!$A:$A,0),MATCH("Yield on Cost %",Input!$1:$1,0)),"")))`
  );

  calc.getRange("B14").setFormula(
    `=IFERROR(INDEX(Input!$A:$ZZ,MATCH($B$5,Input!$A:$A,0),MATCH("Dividend Per Share",Input!$1:$1,0)),` +
    `IFERROR(INDEX(Input!$A:$ZZ,MATCH($B$5,Input!$A:$A,0),MATCH("Dividend Per Share from Input",Input!$1:$1,0)),` +
    `IFERROR(INDEX(Input!$A:$ZZ,MATCH($B$5,Input!$A:$A,0),MATCH("DPS",Input!$1:$1,0)),"")))`
  );

  // =====================================================
  // SECTION 2 — USER ASSUMPTIONS
  // =====================================================

  const assumptions = [
    ["User Assumptions", ""],
    ["Buy Price", ""],
    ["Desired Buy Price", ""],
    ["Target Sell Price", ""],
    ["Shares Bought", ""],
    ["Desired Increase %", ""],
    ["Dividend Yield %", ""],
    ["Dividend Per Share", ""],
    ["Holding Period Years", ""]
  ];

  calc.getRange(4, 4, assumptions.length, 2)
    .setValues(assumptions);

  const manualCells = ["E5", "E6", "E7", "E8", "E9", "E10", "E11", "E12"];

  manualCells.forEach(cell => {
    calc.getRange(cell)
      .setBackground("#d9eaf7")
      .setFontWeight("bold")
      .setNote("MANUAL INPUT CELL");
  });

  // Default formulas / placeholders
  calc.getRange("E5").setFormula(`=IFERROR($B$8,"")`);
  calc.getRange("E6").setFormula(`=IFERROR($B$8*0.90,"")`);
  calc.getRange("E7").setFormula(`=IFERROR($B$8*1.20,"")`);
  calc.getRange("E8").setValue(100);
  calc.getRange("E9").setValue(0.20);
  calc.getRange("E10").setFormula(`=IFERROR($B$13,"")`);
  calc.getRange("E11").setFormula(`=IFERROR($B$14,"")`);
  calc.getRange("E12").setValue(1);

  // =====================================================
  // SECTION 3 — CALCULATOR 1: TARGET PRICE GAIN
  // All result formulas are self-contained and use B-column values.
  // =====================================================

  const targetGain = [
    ["Calculator 1 — Target Price Gain", ""],
    ["Buy Price", "=E5"],
    ["Shares Bought", "=E8"],
    ["Desired Increase %", "=E9"],
    ["Target Price", "=IFERROR(B17*(1+B19),\"\")"],
    ["Capital Gain Per Share", "=IFERROR(B20-B17,\"\")"],
    ["Total Invested Cost", "=IFERROR(B17*B18,\"\")"],
    ["Total Capital Gain", "=IFERROR(B21*B18,\"\")"],
    ["Capital Return %", "=IFERROR(B23/B22,\"\")"]
  ];

  calc.getRange(16, 1, targetGain.length, 2)
    .setValues(targetGain);

  // =====================================================
  // SECTION 4 — CALCULATOR 2: DESIRED BUY PRICE PROJECTION
  // =====================================================

  const desiredBuy = [
    ["Calculator 2 — Desired Buy Price Projection", ""],
    ["Desired Buy Price", "=E6"],
    ["Target Sell Price", "=E7"],
    ["Shares Bought", "=E8"],
    ["Capital Gain Per Share", "=IFERROR(B29-B28,\"\")"],
    ["Total Invested Cost", "=IFERROR(B28*B30,\"\")"],
    ["Total Capital Gain", "=IFERROR(B31*B30,\"\")"],
    ["Return on Cost %", "=IFERROR(B33/B32,\"\")"],
    ["Margin to Current Price %", "=IFERROR(($B$8-B28)/$B$8,\"\")"]
  ];

  calc.getRange(27, 1, desiredBuy.length, 2)
    .setValues(desiredBuy);

  // =====================================================
  // SECTION 5 — DIVIDEND INCOME CALCULATOR
  // =====================================================

  const dividendCalc = [
    ["Calculator 3 — Dividend Income", ""],
    ["Buy Price", "=E5"],
    ["Shares Bought", "=E8"],
    ["Total Invested Cost", "=IFERROR(B39*B40,\"\")"],
    ["Dividend Yield %", "=E10"],
    ["Dividend Per Share", "=E11"],
    ["Annual Dividend Income by Yield", "=IFERROR(B41*B42,\"\")"],
    ["Annual Dividend Income by DPS", "=IFERROR(B40*B43,\"\")"],
    ["Selected Annual Dividend Income", "=IF(B44<>\"\",B44,B45)"],
    ["Holding Period Years", "=E12"],
    ["Total Dividend Income", "=IFERROR(B46*B47,\"\")"],
    ["Yield on Cost %", "=IFERROR(B46/B41,\"\")"]
  ];

  calc.getRange(38, 1, dividendCalc.length, 2)
    .setValues(dividendCalc);

  // =====================================================
  // SECTION 6 — TOTAL RETURN SUMMARY
  // Canonical output rows:
  // B57 = Total Invested
  // B58 = Capital Gain
  // B59 = Dividend Income
  // B60 = Total Return Amount
  // B61 = Total Return %
  // B62 = Break-even Price After Dividend
  // B63 = Decision Note
  // =====================================================

  const totalReturn = [
    ["Total Return Summary", ""],
    ["Scenario Buy Price", "=E5"],
    ["Scenario Target Price", "=E7"],
    ["Shares Bought", "=E8"],
    ["Total Invested", "=IFERROR(B54*B56,\"\")"],
    ["Capital Gain", "=IFERROR((B55-B54)*B56,\"\")"],
    ["Dividend Income", "=B48"],
    ["Total Return Amount", "=IFERROR(B58+B59,\"\")"],
    ["Total Return %", "=IFERROR(B60/B57,\"\")"],
    ["Break-even Price After Dividend", "=IFERROR(B54-(B59/B56),\"\")"],
    ["Decision Note", "=IF(B61>=0.25,\"Strong projected return\",IF(B61>=0.1,\"Moderate projected return\",IF(B61>0,\"Low positive return\",\"Negative projected return\")))"]
  ];

  calc.getRange(53, 1, totalReturn.length, 2)
    .setValues(totalReturn);

  // =====================================================
  // SECTION 7 — QUICK RESULT BOX
  // =====================================================

  const resultBox = [
    ["Quick Result", ""],
    ["Selected Ticker", "=B5"],
    ["Company", "=B6"],
    ["Total Invested", "=B57"],
    ["Capital Gain", "=B58"],
    ["Dividend Income", "=B59"],
    ["Total Return Amount", "=B60"],
    ["Total Return %", "=B61"],
    ["Decision Note", "=B63"]
  ];

  calc.getRange(16, 4, resultBox.length, 2)
    .setValues(resultBox);

  // =====================================================
  // FORMAT CALCULATOR SHEET
  // =====================================================

  formatGainDividendCalculatorSheet(calc);

  if (typeof refreshCalculatorTickerSelectionAutoFillPatch === "function") {
    refreshCalculatorTickerSelectionAutoFillPatch();
  }
}




// =====================================================
// CALCULATOR LOOKUP HELPER
// PURPOSE:
// Creates header-based lookup formulas from Input sheet so
// Calculator does not break when Input columns are moved.
// =====================================================

function inputLookupFormula_(headerName) {
  return `=IFERROR(INDEX(Input!$A:$ZZ,MATCH($B$5,Input!$A:$A,0),MATCH("${headerName}",Input!$1:$1,0)),"")`;
}

// =====================================================
// MODULE 79A — FORMAT GAIN + DIVIDEND CALCULATOR
// PURPOSE:
// Applies visual design, manual input highlights, and formats.
// =====================================================

function formatGainDividendCalculatorSheet(calc) {

  calc.setHiddenGridlines(true);
  calc.setFrozenRows(1);

  calc.getDataRange()
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setFontSize(10)
    .setVerticalAlignment("middle");

  const sectionHeaders = [
    "A4",
    "D4",
    "A16",
    "A27",
    "A38",
    "A53",
    "D16"
  ];

  sectionHeaders.forEach(cell => {
    calc.getRange(cell)
      .setBackground("#1f2933")
      .setFontColor("#ffffff")
      .setFontWeight("bold");
  });

  // Manual input cells
  ["B5", "E5", "E6", "E7", "E8", "E9", "E10", "E11", "E12"].forEach(cell => {
    calc.getRange(cell)
      .setBackground("#d9eaf7")
      .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true, "#0b5394", SpreadsheetApp.BorderStyle.SOLID)
      .setFontWeight("bold");
  });

  // Output/result cells
  calc.getRange("B20:B24").setBackground("#f3f6fa");
  calc.getRange("B31:B35").setBackground("#f3f6fa");
  calc.getRange("B41:B49").setBackground("#f3f6fa");
  calc.getRange("B57:B63").setBackground("#fff2cc");

  calc.getRange("D16:E24")
    .setBackground("#d9ead3")
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  // Borders for sections
  calc.getRange("A4:B14").setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);
  calc.getRange("D4:E12").setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);
  calc.getRange("A16:B24").setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);
  calc.getRange("A27:B35").setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);
  calc.getRange("A38:B49").setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);
  calc.getRange("A53:B63").setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);
  calc.getRange("D16:E24").setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  // Number formats
  calc.getRange("B8:B11").setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");
  calc.getRange("B13").setNumberFormat("0.00%");
  calc.getRange("B14").setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");

  calc.getRange("E5:E8").setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");
  calc.getRange("E9:E10").setNumberFormat("0.00%");
  calc.getRange("E11:E12").setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");

  calc.getRange("B17:B18").setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");
  calc.getRange("B19").setNumberFormat("0.00%");
  calc.getRange("B20:B23").setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");
  calc.getRange("B24").setNumberFormat("0.00%");

  calc.getRange("B28:B33").setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");
  calc.getRange("B34:B35").setNumberFormat("0.00%");

  calc.getRange("B39:B41").setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");
  calc.getRange("B42").setNumberFormat("0.00%");
  calc.getRange("B43:B48").setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");
  calc.getRange("B49").setNumberFormat("0.00%");

  calc.getRange("B54:B60").setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");
  calc.getRange("B61").setNumberFormat("0.00%");
  calc.getRange("B63").setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");

  calc.getRange("E19:E22").setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");
  calc.getRange("E23").setNumberFormat("0.00%");

  // Column widths
  calc.setColumnWidth(1, 260);
  calc.setColumnWidth(2, 180);
  calc.setColumnWidth(3, 40);
  calc.setColumnWidth(4, 260);
  calc.setColumnWidth(5, 190);
  calc.setColumnWidth(6, 40);
  calc.setColumnWidth(7, 220);
  calc.setColumnWidth(8, 180);

  // Row heights
  calc.setRowHeight(1, 36);
  calc.setRowHeights(2, 70, 24);

  // Decision note highlight
  calc.getRange("B63")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setBackground("#d9ead3");
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 79B — REFRESH CALCULATOR
// PURPOSE:
// Wrapper for menu and master runner.
// =====================================================

function refreshGainDividendCalculator() {
  createGainDividendCalculatorSheet();
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 79C — CALCULATOR USER GUIDE PANEL
// PURPOSE:
// Adds a small guide section to the Calculator sheet.
// =====================================================

function addCalculatorUserGuide() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const calc = ss.getSheetByName("Calculator");

  if (!calc) return;

  const guide = [
    ["Calculator Guide", ""],
    ["Blue cells", "Manual input / user assumption"],
    ["Ticker dropdown", "Select ticker from Input sheet"],
    ["Buy Price", "Defaults to current price; can override"],
    ["Desired Buy Price", "Use to test lower entry price"],
    ["Target Sell Price", "Use your own target or 52W high"],
    ["Dividend Yield", "Manual or imported if available"],
    ["Total Return", "Capital gain + dividend income"]
  ];

  calc.getRange(4, 7, guide.length, 2)
    .setValues(guide);

  calc.getRange(4, 7, 1, 2)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  calc.getRange(5, 7, guide.length - 1, 1)
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setBackground("#d9eaf7");

  calc.getRange(4, 7, guide.length, 2)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  calc.autoResizeColumns(7, 2);
}


function refreshGainDividendCalculatorWithGuide() {
  refreshGainDividendCalculator();
  addCalculatorUserGuide();
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 80 — CALCULATOR UI + GRAPHICS UPGRADE
// PURPOSE:
// Enhances the Calculator sheet with a more visual interface:
// - large result cards
// - scenario summary banner
// - visual data bars
// - section icons / labels
// - improved colour zones
// - chart-style return breakdown
// - manual input emphasis
// =====================================================

function applyCalculatorUiGraphicsUpgrade() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const calc = ss.getSheetByName("Calculator");

  if (!calc) {
    throw new Error("Calculator sheet not found. Run refreshGainDividendCalculatorWithGuide() first.");
  }

  // =====================================================
  // BASE UI STYLE
  // =====================================================

  calc.setHiddenGridlines(true);

  calc.getDataRange()
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setFontSize(10)
    .setVerticalAlignment("middle");

  // Main title upgrade
  calc.getRange("A1:H1")
    .merge()
    .setValue("Stocks Overseer — Gain + Dividend Scenario Calculator")
    .setBackground("#111827")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(16)
    .setHorizontalAlignment("left");

  calc.getRange("A2:H2")
    .merge()
    .setValue("Use blue cells for manual assumptions. Outputs update automatically from selected ticker, target price, dividend yield, and holding period.")
    .setBackground("#f3f6fa")
    .setFontColor("#374151")
    .setFontStyle("italic");

  calc.setRowHeight(1, 38);
  calc.setRowHeight(2, 28);

  // =====================================================
  // SECTION ICON TITLES
  // =====================================================

  setCalculatorSectionTitle_(calc, "A4", "① Ticker Selection");
  setCalculatorSectionTitle_(calc, "D4", "② User Assumptions");
  setCalculatorSectionTitle_(calc, "A16", "③ Target Price Gain");
  setCalculatorSectionTitle_(calc, "A27", "④ Desired Buy Price Projection");
  setCalculatorSectionTitle_(calc, "A38", "⑤ Dividend Income");
  setCalculatorSectionTitle_(calc, "A53", "⑥ Total Return Summary");
  setCalculatorSectionTitle_(calc, "D16", "⑦ Quick Result");

  // =====================================================
  // MANUAL INPUT CELLS — BLUE ZONE
  // =====================================================

  const manualCells = ["B5", "E5", "E6", "E7", "E8", "E9", "E10", "E11", "E12"];

  manualCells.forEach(cell => {
    calc.getRange(cell)
      .setBackground("#d9eaf7")
      .setFontColor("#000000")
      .setFontWeight("bold")
      .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true, "#0b5394", SpreadsheetApp.BorderStyle.SOLID_MEDIUM)
      .setNote("MANUAL INPUT / USER ASSUMPTION");
  });

  // Automated output fields
  calc.getRange("B6:B14")
    .setBackground("#f7f7f7")
    .setFontColor("#111827");

  // =====================================================
  // RESULT CARD PANEL
  // =====================================================

  createCalculatorResultCards_(calc);

  // =====================================================
  // RETURN BREAKDOWN MINI GRAPHICS
  // =====================================================

  createCalculatorReturnBreakdownGraphics_(calc);

  // =====================================================
  // SCENARIO BANNER
  // =====================================================

  createCalculatorScenarioBanner_(calc);

  // =====================================================
  // DECISION COLOUR BANDS
  // =====================================================

  applyCalculatorDecisionConditionalFormatting_(calc);

  // =====================================================
  // FINAL WIDTH / LAYOUT
  // =====================================================

  calc.setColumnWidth(1, 260);
  calc.setColumnWidth(2, 180);
  calc.setColumnWidth(3, 28);
  calc.setColumnWidth(4, 260);
  calc.setColumnWidth(5, 190);
  calc.setColumnWidth(6, 28);
  calc.setColumnWidth(7, 260);
  calc.setColumnWidth(8, 190);
  calc.setColumnWidth(9, 28);
  calc.setColumnWidth(10, 220);
  calc.setColumnWidth(11, 190);

  calc.setFrozenRows(1);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 80A — CALCULATOR SECTION TITLE HELPER
// =====================================================

function setCalculatorSectionTitle_(sheet, cell, title) {

  sheet.getRange(cell)
    .setValue(title)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(11);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 80B — CALCULATOR RESULT CARDS
// PURPOSE:
// Adds large KPI-style result cards on the right side.
// =====================================================

function createCalculatorResultCards_(calc) {

  const startRow = 16;
  const startCol = 7; // Column G

  const cards = [
    ["Total Invested", "=B57", "#d9e2f3"],
    ["Capital Gain", "=B58", "#d9ead3"],
    ["Dividend Income", "=B59", "#fff2cc"],
    ["Total Return", "=B60", "#d9ead3"],
    ["Total Return %", "=B61", "#d9ead3"],
    ["Break-even Price", "=B62", "#f3f6fa"],
    ["Decision Note", "=B63", "#fff2cc"]
  ];

  calc.getRange(startRow, startCol, 18, 4).clearContent();

  calc.getRange(startRow, startCol, 1, 2)
    .merge()
    .setValue("Scenario Result Cards")
    .setBackground("#111827")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(12);

  let row = startRow + 2;

  cards.forEach(card => {

    calc.getRange(row, startCol, 1, 2)
      .merge()
      .setValue(card[0])
      .setBackground("#1f2933")
      .setFontColor("#ffffff")
      .setFontWeight("bold")
      .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

    calc.getRange(row + 1, startCol, 2, 2)
      .merge()
      .setFormula(card[1])
      .setBackground(card[2])
      .setFontColor("#111827")
      .setFontWeight("bold")
      .setFontSize(card[0] === "Decision Note" ? 11 : 15)
      .setHorizontalAlignment("center")
      .setVerticalAlignment("middle")
      .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

    row += 4;
  });

  // Formatting by result card rows
  calc.getRange(startRow + 3, startCol, 2, 2).setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");
  calc.getRange(startRow + 7, startCol, 2, 2).setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");
  calc.getRange(startRow + 11, startCol, 2, 2).setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");
  calc.getRange(startRow + 15, startCol, 2, 2).setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");
  calc.getRange(startRow + 19, startCol, 2, 2).setNumberFormat("0.00%");
  calc.getRange(startRow + 23, startCol, 2, 2).setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 80C — RETURN BREAKDOWN GRAPHICS
// PURPOSE:
// Adds mini bar visuals using SPARKLINE for key return items.
// =====================================================

function createCalculatorReturnBreakdownGraphics_(calc) {

  const startRow = 53;
  const startCol = 4; // Column D

  const rows = [
    ["Return Breakdown Visuals", ""],
    ["Capital Gain Bar", `=IFERROR(SPARKLINE(B58,{"charttype","bar";"max",MAX(ABS(B58),ABS(B59),1)}),"")`],
    ["Dividend Income Bar", `=IFERROR(SPARKLINE(B59,{"charttype","bar";"max",MAX(ABS(B58),ABS(B59),1)}),"")`],
    ["Total Return Bar", `=IFERROR(SPARKLINE(B60,{"charttype","bar";"max",MAX(ABS(B60),1)}),"")`],
    ["Return % Bar", `=IFERROR(SPARKLINE(B61,{"charttype","bar";"max",0.5}),"")`]
  ];

  calc.getRange(startRow, startCol, rows.length, 2)
    .setValues(rows);

  calc.getRange(startRow, startCol, 1, 2)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  calc.getRange(startRow + 1, startCol, rows.length - 1, 1)
    .setBackground("#f3f6fa")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  calc.getRange(startRow, startCol, rows.length, 2)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  calc.setColumnWidth(startCol + 1, 220);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 80D — SCENARIO BANNER
// PURPOSE:
// Adds visual banner for calculator result status.
// =====================================================

function createCalculatorScenarioBanner_(calc) {

  calc.getRange("D27:E29")
    .merge()
    .setFormula(`=IFERROR("Scenario: "&B5&" | Invested: "&TEXT(B57,"#,##0.00")&" | Return: "&TEXT(B61,"0.00%")&" | "&B63,"Scenario not ready")`)
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(11)
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center")
    .setVerticalAlignment("middle")
    .setBackground("#d9e2f3")
    .setFontColor("#1f2933")
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  calc.setRowHeight(27, 28);
  calc.setRowHeight(28, 28);
  calc.setRowHeight(29, 28);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 80E — CALCULATOR CONDITIONAL FORMATTING
// PURPOSE:
// Adds visual status colours to return %, decision note,
// and scenario banner.
// =====================================================

function applyCalculatorDecisionConditionalFormatting_(calc) {

  const rules = [];

  // Total return % cell
  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenNumberGreaterThanOrEqualTo(0.25)
      .setBackground("#d9ead3")
      .setFontColor("#274e13")
      .setRanges([calc.getRange("B61"), calc.getRange("G35:H36")])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenNumberBetween(0.10, 0.2499)
      .setBackground("#fff2cc")
      .setFontColor("#7f6000")
      .setRanges([calc.getRange("B61"), calc.getRange("G35:H36")])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenNumberLessThan(0)
      .setBackground("#f4cccc")
      .setFontColor("#990000")
      .setRanges([calc.getRange("B61"), calc.getRange("G35:H36")])
      .build()
  );

  // Decision text
  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextContains("Strong")
      .setBackground("#d9ead3")
      .setFontColor("#274e13")
      .setRanges([calc.getRange("B63"), calc.getRange("G39:H40"), calc.getRange("D27:E29")])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextContains("Moderate")
      .setBackground("#fff2cc")
      .setFontColor("#7f6000")
      .setRanges([calc.getRange("B63"), calc.getRange("G39:H40"), calc.getRange("D27:E29")])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextContains("Negative")
      .setBackground("#f4cccc")
      .setFontColor("#990000")
      .setRanges([calc.getRange("B63"), calc.getRange("G39:H40"), calc.getRange("D27:E29")])
      .build()
  );

  calc.setConditionalFormatRules(rules);
}

function createCalculatorGraphicsLegend() {

    ["Sparkline Bars", "Visual comparison of gain and income"]

  calc.getRange(35, 7, legend.length, 2)
    .setValues(legend);

  calc.getRange(35, 7, 1, 2)
    .setBackground("#111827")

  calc.getRange(37, 7).setBackground("#f7f7f7");
  calc.getRange(38, 7).setBackground("#d9ead3");
  calc.getRange(39, 7).setBackground("#fff2cc");
  calc.getRange(40, 7).setBackground("#f4cccc");
}

// =====================================================
// MODULE 79B — CALCULATOR SENSITIVITY TABLE
// PURPOSE:
// Adds a sensitivity table to the Calculator sheet showing
// total return % at different buy-price discounts and target
// return assumptions.
// This helps answer: "At what buy price does this become attractive?"
// =====================================================

function createCalculatorSensitivityTable() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const calc = ss.getSheetByName("Calculator");

  if (!calc) {
    throw new Error("Calculator sheet not found.");
  }

  const startRow = 66;
  const startCol = 1;

  const table = [
    ["Sensitivity Table — Total Return %", "Target +10%", "Target +20%", "Target +30%", "Target +40%"],
    ["Current Price", "", "", "", ""],
    ["5% Lower Buy", "", "", "", ""],
    ["10% Lower Buy", "", "", "", ""],
    ["15% Lower Buy", "", "", "", ""],
    ["20% Lower Buy", "", "", "", ""]
  ];

  calc.getRange(startRow, startCol, table.length, table[0].length)
    .setValues(table);

  // Buy price assumptions based on current price B8.
  const buyMultipliers = [1, 0.95, 0.90, 0.85, 0.80];
  const targetMultipliers = [1.10, 1.20, 1.30, 1.40];

  for (let r = 0; r < buyMultipliers.length; r++) {
    for (let c = 0; c < targetMultipliers.length; c++) {

      const row = startRow + 1 + r;
      const col = startCol + 1 + c;
      const buyMultiplier = buyMultipliers[r];
      const targetMultiplier = targetMultipliers[c];

      // Formula:
      // Buy = Current Price * buy multiplier
      // Target = Buy * target multiplier
      // Capital gain = (Target - Buy) * shares
      // Dividend income = Buy * shares * dividend yield * years
      // Total return % = (capital gain + dividend income) / invested
      calc.getRange(row, col).setFormula(
        `=IFERROR((((($B$8*${buyMultiplier})*${targetMultiplier})-($B$8*${buyMultiplier}))*$E$8 + (($B$8*${buyMultiplier})*$E$8*$E$10*$E$12))/(($B$8*${buyMultiplier})*$E$8),"")`
      );
    }
  }

  formatCalculatorSensitivityTable(calc, startRow, startCol);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 79B-A — FORMAT CALCULATOR SENSITIVITY TABLE
// =====================================================

function formatCalculatorSensitivityTable(calc, startRow, startCol) {

  calc.getRange(startRow, startCol, 1, 5)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  calc.getRange(startRow + 1, startCol, 5, 1)
    .setBackground("#f3f6fa")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  calc.getRange(startRow + 1, startCol + 1, 5, 4)
    .setNumberFormat("0.00%")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  calc.getRange(startRow, startCol, 6, 5)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  const rules = calc.getConditionalFormatRules();

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .setGradientMinpointWithValue("#f4cccc", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "-0.10")
      .setGradientMidpointWithValue("#fff2cc", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "0.10")
      .setGradientMaxpointWithValue("#d9ead3", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "0.30")
      .setRanges([calc.getRange(startRow + 1, startCol + 1, 5, 4)])
      .build()
  );

  calc.setConditionalFormatRules(rules);

  calc.setColumnWidth(startCol, 180);
  for (let c = startCol + 1; c <= startCol + 4; c++) {
    calc.setColumnWidth(c, 120);
  }
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 80B — CALCULATOR BULL / BASE / BEAR SCENARIO CARDS
// PURPOSE:
// Adds three visual scenario cards to the Calculator:
// Bear, Base, and Bull.
// Each card estimates target price and total return %.
// =====================================================

function createCalculatorScenarioCards() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const calc = ss.getSheetByName("Calculator");

  if (!calc) {
    throw new Error("Calculator sheet not found.");
  }

  const startRow = 66;
  const startCol = 7; // G

  const cards = [
    ["Bear Case", "-10% target", `=IFERROR(($E$5*0.90),"")`, `=IFERROR(((($E$5*0.90)-$E$5)*$E$8 + ($E$5*$E$8*$E$10*$E$12))/($E$5*$E$8),"")`, "#f4cccc"],
    ["Base Case", "Current target", `=IFERROR($E$7,"")`, `=IFERROR(((($E$7)-$E$5)*$E$8 + ($E$5*$E$8*$E$10*$E$12))/($E$5*$E$8),"")`, "#fff2cc"],
    ["Bull Case", "+30% target", `=IFERROR(($E$5*1.30),"")`, `=IFERROR(((($E$5*1.30)-$E$5)*$E$8 + ($E$5*$E$8*$E$10*$E$12))/($E$5*$E$8),"")`, "#d9ead3"]
  ];

  calc.getRange(startRow, startCol, 14, 5).clearContent();

  calc.getRange(startRow, startCol, 1, 5)
    .merge()
    .setValue("Bull / Base / Bear Scenario Cards")
    .setBackground("#111827")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(12);

  let col = startCol;

  cards.forEach(card => {

    calc.getRange(startRow + 2, col, 1, 1)
      .setValue(card[0])
      .setBackground("#1f2933")
      .setFontColor("#ffffff")
      .setFontWeight("bold")
      .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

    calc.getRange(startRow + 3, col)
      .setValue(card[1])
      .setBackground(card[4])
      .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

    calc.getRange(startRow + 4, col)
      .setValue("Target Price")
      .setFontWeight("bold")
      .setBackground("#f3f6fa")
      .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

    calc.getRange(startRow + 5, col)
      .setFormula(card[2])
      .setNumberFormat("#,##0.00")
      .setFontWeight("bold")
      .setFontSize(13)
      .setBackground(card[4])
      .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

    calc.getRange(startRow + 6, col)
      .setValue("Total Return %")
      .setFontWeight("bold")
      .setBackground("#f3f6fa")
      .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

    calc.getRange(startRow + 7, col)
      .setFormula(card[3])
      .setNumberFormat("0.00%")
      .setFontWeight("bold")
      .setFontSize(13)
      .setBackground(card[4])
      .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

    calc.getRange(startRow + 2, col, 6, 1)
      .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

    col += 2;
  });
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 81 — CALCULATOR MINI SENSITIVITY HEATMAP
// PURPOSE:
// Creates a visual return heatmap using buy-price discounts
// and target-price increases.
// Similar to a small investment scenario matrix.
// =====================================================

function createCalculatorMiniSensitivityHeatmap() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const calc = ss.getSheetByName("Calculator");

  if (!calc) {
    throw new Error("Calculator sheet not found.");
  }

  const startRow = 76;
  const startCol = 1;

  const headers = [
    ["Buy Price ↓ / Target Price →", "+5%", "+10%", "+15%", "+20%", "+30%", "+40%"]
  ];

  const labels = [
    ["Current"],
    ["5% Lower"],
    ["10% Lower"],
    ["15% Lower"],
    ["20% Lower"],
    ["25% Lower"]
  ];

  calc.getRange(startRow, startCol, 1, headers[0].length).setValues(headers);
  calc.getRange(startRow + 1, startCol, labels.length, 1).setValues(labels);

  const buyMultipliers = [1, 0.95, 0.90, 0.85, 0.80, 0.75];
  const targetMultipliers = [1.05, 1.10, 1.15, 1.20, 1.30, 1.40];

  for (let r = 0; r < buyMultipliers.length; r++) {
    for (let c = 0; c < targetMultipliers.length; c++) {

      calc.getRange(startRow + 1 + r, startCol + 1 + c).setFormula(
        `=IFERROR((((($B$8*${buyMultipliers[r]})*${targetMultipliers[c]})-($B$8*${buyMultipliers[r]}))*$E$8 + (($B$8*${buyMultipliers[r]})*$E$8*$E$10*$E$12))/(($B$8*${buyMultipliers[r]})*$E$8),"")`
      );
    }
  }

  calc.getRange(startRow, startCol, 1, headers[0].length)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  calc.getRange(startRow + 1, startCol, labels.length, 1)
    .setBackground("#f3f6fa")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  calc.getRange(startRow + 1, startCol + 1, labels.length, targetMultipliers.length)
    .setNumberFormat("0.00%")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  calc.getRange(startRow, startCol, labels.length + 1, headers[0].length)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  const rules = calc.getConditionalFormatRules();

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .setGradientMinpointWithValue("#f4cccc", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "-0.10")
      .setGradientMidpointWithValue("#fff2cc", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "0.10")
      .setGradientMaxpointWithValue("#d9ead3", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "0.30")
      .setRanges([calc.getRange(startRow + 1, startCol + 1, labels.length, targetMultipliers.length)])
      .build()
  );

  calc.setConditionalFormatRules(rules);

  calc.setColumnWidth(startCol, 190);
  for (let c = startCol + 1; c <= startCol + targetMultipliers.length; c++) {
    calc.setColumnWidth(c, 90);
  }
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 72C — REFRESH SCORE EXPLANATION VISUAL SUMMARY
// PURPOSE:
// Adds a visual summary block to the Score Explanation sheet.
// This complements Module 72.
// =====================================================

function enhanceScoreExplanationVisualSummary() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const scoreSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Score Explanation");

  if (!scoreSheet) return;

  const lastRow = Math.max(scoreSheet.getLastRow(), 4);

  let strong = 0;
  let moderate = 0;
  let weak = 0;

  const scores = scoreSheet.getRange(4, 3, lastRow - 3, 1).getValues();

  scores.forEach(row => {
    const score = num(row[0]);
    if (score >= 80) strong++;
    else if (score >= 60) moderate++;
    else if (score > 0) weak++;
  });

  const table = [
    ["Score Explanation Summary", ""],
    ["Strong Score ≥ 80", strong],
    ["Moderate Score 60–79", moderate],
    ["Weak Score < 60", weak]
  ];

  scoreSheet.getRange("M3:N6")
    .setValues(table);

  scoreSheet.getRange("M3:N3")
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  scoreSheet.getRange("M4:M6")
    .setBackground("#f3f6fa")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  scoreSheet.getRange("M3:N6")
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  scoreSheet.autoResizeColumns(13, 2);
}

// =====================================================
// MODULE 85 — WATCHLIST PIPELINE FUNNEL
// PURPOSE:
// Creates a separate visual funnel sheet:
// Universe → Priced → Scored → Watchlist → Buy Candidates
// =====================================================

function createWatchlistPipelineFunnelSheet() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");

  let funnel = ss.getSheetByName("Watchlist Funnel");

  if (!funnel) funnel = ss.insertSheet("Watchlist Funnel");

  funnel.clear();
  funnel.setHiddenGridlines(true);

  const data = input.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];

  const tickerCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker");
  const priceCol = colIndex(headers, "Share Price");
  const scoreCol = colIndex(headers, "GoogleFinance Score");
  const watchlistCol = colIndex(headers, "Watchlist Status");
  const recommendationCol = colIndex(headers, "Final Recommendation");

  let total = 0;
  let priced = 0;
  let scored = 0;
  let watchlist = 0;
  let buy = 0;

  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {
    const row = data[r];
    if (!row[tickerCol]) continue;

    total++;

    if (num(row[priceCol]) > 0) priced++;
    if (num(row[scoreCol]) > 0) scored++;
    if (row[watchlistCol]) watchlist++;
    if (row[recommendationCol] === "BUY CANDIDATE") buy++;
  }

  const table = [
    ["Pipeline Stage", "Count", "Conversion %"],
    ["Universe", total, 1],
    ["Priced", priced, safeDiv(priced, total)],
    ["Scored", scored, safeDiv(scored, total)],
    ["Watchlist", watchlist, safeDiv(watchlist, total)],
    ["Buy Candidates", buy, safeDiv(buy, total)]
  ];

  funnel.getRange("A1:F1")
    .merge()
    .setValue("Stocks Overseer — Watchlist Pipeline Funnel")
    .setBackground("#111827")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(16);

  funnel.getRange(3, 1, table.length, table[0].length)
    .setValues(table);

  funnel.getRange(3, 1, 1, table[0].length)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  funnel.getRange(4, 3, table.length - 1, 1).setNumberFormat("0.00%");

  funnel.getRange(3, 1, table.length, table[0].length)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  // Visual funnel bars
  const barStartRow = 12;
  funnel.getRange(barStartRow, 1).setValue("Visual Funnel").setFontWeight("bold").setFontSize(12);

  const stages = [
    ["Universe", total, "#d9e2f3"],
    ["Priced", priced, "#d9ead3"],
    ["Scored", scored, "#fff2cc"],
    ["Watchlist", watchlist, "#cfe2f3"],
    ["Buy Candidates", buy, "#b6d7a8"]
  ];

  for (let i = 0; i < stages.length; i++) {
    const row = barStartRow + 2 + i;
    funnel.getRange(row, 1).setValue(stages[i][0]).setFontWeight("bold");
    funnel.getRange(row, 2).setValue(stages[i][1]);
    funnel.getRange(row, 3).setFormula(`=IFERROR(SPARKLINE(B${row},{"charttype","bar";"max",$B$${barStartRow + 2}}),"")`);
    funnel.getRange(row, 3).setBackground(stages[i][2]);
  }

  funnel.setColumnWidth(1, 180);
  funnel.setColumnWidth(2, 100);
  funnel.setColumnWidth(3, 420);

  funnel.autoResizeColumns(1, 3);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 89 — PRINT COVER SHEET
// PURPOSE:
// Creates a professional report cover sheet.
// =====================================================

function createPrintCoverSheet() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  let cover = ss.getSheetByName("Print Cover");

  if (!cover) cover = ss.insertSheet("Print Cover");

  cover.clear();
  cover.setHiddenGridlines(true);

  const branding = ss.getSheetByName("Branding Presets");

  let projectName = "Stocks Overseer Advisor";
  let preparedBy = "";
  let footer = "Generated from GoogleFinance and Apps Script-derived metrics.";

  if (branding) {
    const data = branding.getDataRange().getValues();
    const map = {};
    for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {
      map[data[r][0]] = data[r][1];
    }
    projectName = map["Firm / Project Name"] || projectName;
    preparedBy = map["Prepared By"] || preparedBy;
    footer = map["Report Footer"] || footer;
  }

  cover.getRange("A1:H1")
    .merge()
    .setValue(projectName)
    .setBackground("#111827")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(20)
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  cover.getRange("A4:H4")
    .merge()
    .setValue("Investment Dashboard Report")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(18)
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  cover.getRange("A6:H6")
    .merge()
    .setValue("Prepared for management review")
    .setFontSize(12)
    .setFontStyle("italic")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  cover.getRange("B9:C9").merge().setValue("Generated Date").setFontWeight("bold");
  cover.getRange("D9:F9").merge().setValue(new Date()).setNumberFormat("dd/mm/yyyy hh:mm");

  cover.getRange("B10:C10").merge().setValue("Prepared By").setFontWeight("bold");
  cover.getRange("D10:F10").merge().setValue(preparedBy);

  cover.getRange("B12:F12").merge()
    .setValue("Included Sheets: Management View, Executive Charts, Dashboard, Calculator, Watchlist Funnel")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  cover.getRange("A18:H18")
    .merge()
    .setValue(footer)
    .setFontColor("#666666")
    .setFontStyle("italic")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  cover.getRange("A1:H20")
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setVerticalAlignment("middle");

  cover.setColumnWidths(1, 8, 110);
  cover.setRowHeight(1, 48);
  cover.setRowHeight(4, 42);
}

// =====================================================
// MODULE 84 — CALCULATOR SCENARIO COMPARISON CHART
// PURPOSE:
// Adds a visual chart comparing Bear / Base / Bull scenarios
// in the Calculator sheet.
// Compares:
// - Capital Gain
// - Dividend Income
// - Total Return Amount
// - Total Return %
// =====================================================

function createCalculatorScenarioComparisonChart() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const calc = ss.getSheetByName("Calculator");

  if (!calc) {
    throw new Error("Calculator sheet not found.");
  }

  // Remove existing scenario comparison charts only by clearing target area.
  // Existing sheet charts are retained unless manually removed.
  const startRow = 86;
  const startCol = 9; // I

  calc.getRange(startRow, startCol, 12, 5).clearContent();

  const table = [
    ["Scenario", "Capital Gain", "Dividend Income", "Total Return Amount", "Total Return %"],
    [
      "Bear",
      `=IFERROR((($E$5*0.90)-$E$5)*$E$8,"")`,
      `=IFERROR($E$5*$E$8*$E$10*$E$12,"")`,
      `=IFERROR(J${startRow + 1}+K${startRow + 1},"")`,
      `=IFERROR(L${startRow + 1}/($E$5*$E$8),"")`
    ],
    [
      "Base",
      `=IFERROR(($E$7-$E$5)*$E$8,"")`,
      `=IFERROR($E$5*$E$8*$E$10*$E$12,"")`,
      `=IFERROR(J${startRow + 2}+K${startRow + 2},"")`,
      `=IFERROR(L${startRow + 2}/($E$5*$E$8),"")`
    ],
    [
      "Bull",
      `=IFERROR((($E$5*1.30)-$E$5)*$E$8,"")`,
      `=IFERROR($E$5*$E$8*$E$10*$E$12,"")`,
      `=IFERROR(J${startRow + 3}+K${startRow + 3},"")`,
      `=IFERROR(L${startRow + 3}/($E$5*$E$8),"")`
    ]
  ];

  calc.getRange(startRow, startCol, table.length, table[0].length)
    .setValues(table);

  calc.getRange(startRow, startCol, 1, table[0].length)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  calc.getRange(startRow + 1, startCol + 1, 3, 3)
    .setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");

  calc.getRange(startRow + 1, startCol + 4, 3, 1)
    .setNumberFormat("0.00%");

  calc.getRange(startRow, startCol, table.length, table[0].length)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  // Remove old charts placed around this area if too many exist is risky;
  // therefore we simply add the chart and rely on sheet refresh clearing cells.
  const chart = calc.newChart()
    .setChartType(Charts.ChartType.COLUMN)
    .addRange(calc.getRange(startRow, startCol, table.length, 4))
    .setPosition(startRow + 6, startCol, 0, 0)
    .setOption("title", "Scenario Comparison: Capital Gain vs Dividend Income")
    .setOption("height", 320)
    .setOption("width", 620)
    .build();

  calc.insertChart(chart);

  const returnChart = calc.newChart()
    .setChartType(Charts.ChartType.BAR)
    .addRange(calc.getRange(startRow, startCol, table.length, 1))
    .addRange(calc.getRange(startRow, startCol + 4, table.length, 1))
    .setPosition(startRow + 23, startCol, 0, 0)
    .setOption("title", "Scenario Total Return %")
    .setOption("height", 260)
    .setOption("width", 620)
    .setOption("legend", { position: "none" })
    .build();

  calc.insertChart(returnChart);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 84A — SCENARIO CHART REFRESH WITH CLEANUP
// PURPOSE:
// Removes existing Calculator charts before rebuilding scenario
// charts to reduce duplicate chart build-up.
// =====================================================

function refreshCalculatorScenarioComparisonChart() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const calc = ss.getSheetByName("Calculator");

  if (!calc) return;

  calc.getCharts().forEach(chart => {
    calc.removeChart(chart);
  });

  createCalculatorScenarioComparisonChart();
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 91 — ALERT CENTRE SHEET
// PURPOSE:
// Creates a single Alert Centre sheet for all important
// review items:
// - Missing price data
// - Data warnings
// - Avoid / High Risk recommendations
// - Very high beta risk
// - Weak score
// - Negative / missing EPS or PE
// This becomes the "red flag control room".
// =====================================================

function createAlertCentreSheet() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) {
    throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");
  }

  let alert = ss.getSheetByName("Alert Centre");

  if (!alert) {
    alert = ss.insertSheet("Alert Centre");
  }

  alert.clear();
  alert.setHiddenGridlines(true);

  const data = input.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];

  const tickerCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker");
  const companyCol = colIndex(headers, "Company");
  const priceCol = colIndex(headers, "Share Price");
  const peCol = colIndex(headers, "PE Ratio");
  const epsCol = colIndex(headers, "EPS");
  const betaCol = colIndex(headers, "Beta");
  const scoreCol = colIndex(headers, "GoogleFinance Score");
  const betaRiskCol = colIndex(headers, "Beta Risk Group");
  const recommendationCol = colIndex(headers, "Final Recommendation");
  const statusCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker Data Status");
  const suggestionCol = colIndex(headers, "Ticker Format Suggestion");

  const rows = [
    [
      "Severity",
      "Alert Type",
      "Ticker",
      "Company",
      "Price",
      "PE",
      "EPS",
      "Beta",
      "Score",
      "Recommendation",
      "Details",
      "Suggested Action"
    ]
  ];

  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {

    const row = data[r];
    const ticker = row[tickerCol];

    if (!ticker) continue;

    const company = companyCol >= 0 ? row[companyCol] : "";
    const price = num(row[priceCol]);
    const pe = peCol >= 0 ? row[peCol] : "";
    const eps = epsCol >= 0 ? row[epsCol] : "";
    const beta = betaCol >= 0 ? row[betaCol] : "";
    const score = num(row[scoreCol]);
    const betaRisk = betaRiskCol >= 0 ? row[betaRiskCol] : "";
    const recommendation = recommendationCol >= 0 ? row[recommendationCol] : "";
    const status = statusCol >= 0 ? row[statusCol] : "";
    const suggestion = suggestionCol >= 0 ? row[suggestionCol] : "";

    if (!price) {
      rows.push([
        "CRITICAL",
        "Missing Price",
        ticker,
        company,
        price,
        pe,
        eps,
        beta,
        score,
        recommendation,
        "No valid GoogleFinance share price.",
        suggestion || "Check ticker format / exchange prefix."
      ]);
    }

    if (status && status !== "OK") {
      rows.push([
        "HIGH",
        "Data Status Warning",
        ticker,
        company,
        price,
        pe,
        eps,
        beta,
        score,
        recommendation,
        status,
        suggestion || "Review ticker data status."
      ]);
    }

    if (recommendation === "AVOID / HIGH RISK") {
      rows.push([
        "HIGH",
        "Avoid / High Risk",
        ticker,
        company,
        price,
        pe,
        eps,
        beta,
        score,
        recommendation,
        "Watchlist engine classified this ticker as avoid/high risk.",
        "Review score, beta, PE, EPS, and 52W position before action."
      ]);
    }

    if (betaRisk === "VERY HIGH RISK") {
      rows.push([
        "HIGH",
        "Very High Beta Risk",
        ticker,
        company,
        price,
        pe,
        eps,
        beta,
        score,
        recommendation,
        "Beta risk group is VERY HIGH RISK.",
        "Reduce allocation or require stronger conviction/fundamental review."
      ]);
    }

    if (score > 0 && score < 40) {
      rows.push([
        "MEDIUM",
        "Weak Score",
        ticker,
        company,
        price,
        pe,
        eps,
        beta,
        score,
        recommendation,
        "GoogleFinance Score below 40.",
        "Review valuation, risk, earnings yield and momentum."
      ]);
    }

    if (pe === "" || pe == null || pe === 0) {
      rows.push([
        "MEDIUM",
        "Missing / Invalid PE",
        ticker,
        company,
        price,
        pe,
        eps,
        beta,
        score,
        recommendation,
        "PE ratio missing or invalid.",
        "Check if earnings are negative or PE is unsupported."
      ]);
    }

    if (eps === "" || eps == null || eps === 0) {
      rows.push([
        "MEDIUM",
        "Missing / Invalid EPS",
        ticker,
        company,
        price,
        pe,
        eps,
        beta,
        score,
        recommendation,
        "EPS missing or zero.",
        "Manual fundamentals may be required."
      ]);
    }
  }

  alert.getRange("A1:L1")
    .merge()
    .setValue("Stocks Overseer Advisor — Alert Centre")
    .setBackground("#111827")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(16);

  alert.getRange("A2")
    .setValue("Generated");

  alert.getRange("B2")
    .setValue(new Date())
    .setNumberFormat("dd/mm/yyyy hh:mm");

  alert.getRange(4, 1, rows.length, rows[0].length)
    .setValues(rows);

  formatAlertCentreSheet_(alert);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 91A — FORMAT ALERT CENTRE SHEET
// =====================================================

function formatAlertCentreSheet_(sheet) {

  const lastRow = Math.max(sheet.getLastRow(), 5);
  const lastCol = Math.max(sheet.getLastColumn(), 12);

  sheet.setFrozenRows(4);
  sheet.getDataRange()
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setFontSize(10)
    .setVerticalAlignment("middle")
    .setWrap(true);

  sheet.getRange(4, 1, 1, lastCol)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  sheet.getRange(5, 5, Math.max(lastRow - 4, 1), 5)
    .setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");

  sheet.getRange(4, 1, Math.max(lastRow - 3, 1), lastCol)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  sheet.setColumnWidth(1, 100);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(2, 180);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(3, 120);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(4, 220);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(10, 170);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(11, 320);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(12, 360);

  const rules = [];
  const severityRange = sheet.getRange(5, 1, Math.max(lastRow - 4, 1), 1);

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("CRITICAL")
      .setBackground("#cc0000")
      .setFontColor("#ffffff")
      .setBold(true)
      .setRanges([severityRange])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("HIGH")
      .setBackground("#f4cccc")
      .setFontColor("#990000")
      .setBold(true)
      .setRanges([severityRange])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("MEDIUM")
      .setBackground("#fff2cc")
      .setFontColor("#7f6000")
      .setBold(true)
      .setRanges([severityRange])
      .build()
  );

  sheet.setConditionalFormatRules(rules);
}

// Adds alert count summary to dashboard sidebar.
// =====================================================

function createDashboardAlertCentrePanel() {
  createDashboardAlertCentreUiPanel();
}

// =====================================================
// MODULE 95A — FORMAT ONBOARDING WIZARD SHEET
// PURPOSE:
// Formats the updated onboarding workflow sheet.
// =====================================================

function formatOnboardingWizardSheet_(wizard, workflowRows) {

  wizard.setHiddenGridlines(true);
  wizard.setFrozenRows(4);

  wizard.getDataRange()
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setFontSize(10)
    .setVerticalAlignment("middle")
    .setWrap(true);

  // Workflow table header
  wizard.getRange(4, 1, 1, 8)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  wizard.getRange(5, 1, workflowRows - 1, 1)
    .setBackground("#d9e2f3")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  wizard.getRange(5, 2, workflowRows - 1, 1)
    .setBackground("#f3f6fa")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  wizard.getRange(4, 1, workflowRows, 8)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true, "#d9d9d9", SpreadsheetApp.BorderStyle.SOLID);

  // Quick start panel
  wizard.getRange(4, 10, 1, 2)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  wizard.getRange(5, 10, 6, 1)
    .setBackground("#d9ead3")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  wizard.getRange(4, 10, 7, 2)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  // Navigation panel
  wizard.getRange(13, 10, 1, 2)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  wizard.getRange(14, 10, 8, 1)
    .setBackground("#d9eaf7")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  wizard.getRange(13, 10, 9, 2)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  // Function guide panel
  wizard.getRange(24, 10, 1, 2)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  wizard.getRange(25, 10, 8, 1)
    .setBackground("#fff2cc")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  wizard.getRange(24, 10, 9, 2)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  // Phase colouring
  const phaseRange = wizard.getRange(5, 2, workflowRows - 1, 1);
  const rules = [];

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextContains("One-Time")
      .setBackground("#cfe2f3")
      .setFontColor("#073763")
      .setRanges([phaseRange])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextContains("Fast")
      .setBackground("#d9ead3")
      .setFontColor("#274e13")
      .setRanges([phaseRange])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextContains("Data Quality")
      .setBackground("#fce5cd")
      .setFontColor("#783f04")
      .setRanges([phaseRange])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextContains("Health")
      .setBackground("#fff2cc")
      .setFontColor("#7f6000")
      .setRanges([phaseRange])
      .build()
  );

  wizard.setConditionalFormatRules(rules);

  // Column sizing
  wizard.setColumnWidth(1, 60);
  wizard.setColumnWidth(2, 150);
  wizard.setColumnWidth(3, 260);
  wizard.setColumnWidth(4, 260);
  wizard.setColumnWidth(5, 260);
  wizard.setColumnWidth(6, 300);
  wizard.setColumnWidth(7, 100);
  wizard.setColumnWidth(8, 280);
  wizard.setColumnWidth(9, 30);
  wizard.setColumnWidth(10, 230);
  wizard.setColumnWidth(11, 330);

  wizard.setRowHeight(1, 46);
  wizard.setRowHeight(2, 34);
  wizard.setRowHeights(4, workflowRows, 32);
}

// =====================================================
// MODULE 100 — MASTER UI POLISH + CLEANUP
// PURPOSE:
// Final workbook-wide UI cleanup and polish module.
// This module is designed to make the workbook feel complete,
// organised, and easier to use after all prior modules.
// Includes:
// - Sheet ordering
// - Key sheet tab colours
// - Dashboard duplicate chart cleanup
// - Workbook health check sheet
// - Missing sheet check
// - Visual theme consistency pass
// - Menu/help panel refresh
// - Workbook index refresh
// =====================================================

function runMasterUiPolishCleanup() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

  // 1. Ensure important sheets exist where possible.
  ensureCoreUiSheetsExist_();

  // 2. Reorder sheets into a logical workflow sequence.
  organiseWorkbookSheetOrder_();

  // 3. Apply tab colours to improve navigation.
  applyWorkbookTabColours_();

  // 4. Clean up duplicate / excessive charts on key visual sheets.
  cleanupDuplicateCharts_();

  // 5. Apply final visual consistency pass.
  applyMasterThemeConsistency_();

  // 6. Create / refresh workbook health check sheet.
  createWorkbookHealthCheckSheet_();

  // 7. Refresh home page and control panel if those modules exist.
  if (typeof createWorkbookHomePage === "function") {
    createWorkbookHomePage();
  }

  if (typeof createDashboardControlPanel === "function") {
    createDashboardControlPanel();
  }

  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert("Master UI Polish + Cleanup completed.");
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 100A — ENSURE CORE UI SHEETS EXIST
// PURPOSE:
// Creates or refreshes major UI sheets if related functions exist.
// =====================================================

function ensureCoreUiSheetsExist_() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

  const safeCalls = [
    "createWorkbookHomePage",
    "createManagementViewSheet",
    "createExecutiveChartsSheet",
    "createGainDividendCalculatorSheet",
    "createInvestmentCommitteeView",
    "createScoreExplanationPanel",
    "createDashboardControlPanel",
    "createThemeBrandingPresetSheet",
    "createAlertCentreSheet",
    "createOnboardingWizardSheet",
    "createPrintCoverSheet",
    "createWatchlistPipelineFunnelSheet"
  ];

  safeCalls.forEach(fn => {
    if (typeof globalThis[fn] === "function") {
      try {
        globalThis[fn]();
      } catch (err) {
        // Do not stop polish if one optional sheet fails.
        Logger.log("Optional UI sheet refresh skipped: " + fn + " | " + err);
      }
    }
  });
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 100B — ORGANISE WORKBOOK SHEET ORDER
// PURPOSE:
// Places sheets in a logical user workflow order.
// =====================================================

function organiseWorkbookSheetOrder_() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

  const desiredOrder = [
    "Home",
    "Onboarding Wizard",
    "Control Panel",
    "Input",
    "Dashboard",
    "Management View",
    "Executive Charts",
    "Calculator",
    "Watchlist Funnel",
    "Investment Committee",
    "Score Explanation",
    "Alert Centre",
    "Buy Candidates",
    "Value Watch",
    "High Risk",
    "Very High Risk",
    "Missing Data",
    "History Summary",
    "History",
    "Executive Summary",
    "Print Cover",
    "Fundamental Import",
    "Fundamental Import Validation",
    "System Log",
    "Error Log",
    "User Guide",
    "Visual Legend",
    "Branding Presets",
    "Workbook Health Check"
  ];

  desiredOrder.forEach((sheetName, index) => {
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(sheetName);

    if (sheet) {
      ss.setActiveSheet(sheet);
      ss.moveActiveSheet(index + 1);
    }
  });
}
