// =====================================================
// MODULE 100D — CLEANUP DUPLICATE CHARTS
// PURPOSE:
// Prevents visual sheets from accumulating duplicate charts.
// Keeps charts on major sheets within a practical limit.
// =====================================================

function cleanupDuplicateCharts_() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

  const chartLimits = {
    "Dashboard": 8,
    "Executive Charts": 6,
    "Calculator": 3,
    "Management View": 2,
    "Executive Summary": 2
  };

  Object.keys(chartLimits).forEach(sheetName => {
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(sheetName);
    if (!sheet) return;

    const charts = sheet.getCharts();
    const maxCharts = chartLimits[sheetName];

    if (charts.length > maxCharts) {
      const chartsToRemove = charts.slice(0, charts.length - maxCharts);
      chartsToRemove.forEach(chart => sheet.removeChart(chart));
    }
  });
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 100E — MASTER THEME CONSISTENCY PASS
// PURPOSE:
// Applies consistent fonts, hidden gridlines, title bars,
// frozen rows, and column widths across important UI sheets.
// =====================================================

function applyMasterThemeConsistency_() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

  const uiSheets = [
    "Home",
    "Onboarding Wizard",
    "Control Panel",
    "Dashboard",
    "Management View",
    "Executive Charts",
    "Calculator",
    "Watchlist Funnel",
    "Investment Committee",
    "Score Explanation",
    "Alert Centre",
    "Executive Summary",
    "Print Cover",
    "User Guide",
    "Visual Legend",
    "Branding Presets",
    "Workbook Health Check"
  ];

  uiSheets.forEach(sheetName => {
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(sheetName);
    if (!sheet) return;

    sheet.setHiddenGridlines(true);

    const lastRow = Math.max(sheet.getLastRow(), 1);
    const lastCol = Math.max(sheet.getLastColumn(), 1);

    sheet.getRange(1, 1, lastRow, lastCol)
      .setFontFamily("Arial")
      .setVerticalAlignment("middle");

    sheet.setFrozenRows(1);

    // Style first row if it appears to be a title/header.
    sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, Math.min(lastCol, 12))
      .setBackground("#111827")
      .setFontColor("#ffffff")
      .setFontWeight("bold");

    sheet.setRowHeight(1, 36);
  });

  // Data/log sheets keep gridlines optional but still get readable format.
  const dataSheets = [
    "Input",
    "History Summary",
    "History",
    "System Log",
    "Error Log",
    "Fundamental Import",
    "Fundamental Import Validation"
  ];

  dataSheets.forEach(sheetName => {
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(sheetName);
    if (!sheet) return;

    const lastRow = Math.max(sheet.getLastRow(), 1);
    const lastCol = Math.max(sheet.getLastColumn(), 1);

    sheet.getRange(1, 1, lastRow, lastCol)
      .setFontFamily("Arial")
      .setVerticalAlignment("middle");

    sheet.setFrozenRows(1);

    sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, lastCol)
      .setBackground("#1f2933")
      .setFontColor("#ffffff")
      .setFontWeight("bold");
  });
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 100F — WORKBOOK HEALTH CHECK SHEET
// PURPOSE:
// Checks whether important sheets and functions exist.
// Helps diagnose broken setup after many module updates.
// =====================================================

function createWorkbookHealthCheckSheet_() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

  let health = ss.getSheetByName("Workbook Health Check");

  if (!health) {
    health = ss.insertSheet("Workbook Health Check");
  }

  health.clear();
  health.setHiddenGridlines(true);

  const requiredSheets = [
    "Home",
    "Onboarding Wizard",
    "Control Panel",
    "Input",
    "Dashboard",
    "Management View",
    "Executive Charts",
    "Calculator",
    "Watchlist Funnel",
    "Investment Committee",
    "Score Explanation",
    "Alert Centre",
    "History Summary",
    "System Log",
    "Error Log",
    "Print Cover"
  ];

  const requiredFunctions = [
    "runFullOverseerUpdate",
    "createCleanDashboard",
    "refreshManagementView",
    "refreshExecutiveCharts",
    "refreshGainDividendCalculatorWithGuide",
    "refreshCalculatorUiGraphics",
    "refreshAdvancedUiGraphicsPackage",
    "refreshScenarioAlertsOnboardingPackage",
    "createAlertCentreSheet",
    "createOnboardingWizardSheet",
    "createWorkbookHomePage",
    "runMasterUiPolishCleanup"
  ];

  const rows = [
    ["Workbook Health Check", "", "", ""],
    ["Generated", new Date(), "", ""],
    ["", "", "", ""],
    ["Sheet Check", "Status", "Notes", ""]
  ];

  requiredSheets.forEach(sheetName => {
    const exists = ss.getSheetByName(sheetName) ? "OK" : "MISSING";
    rows.push([
      sheetName,
      exists,
      exists === "OK" ? "Sheet found" : "Sheet missing — run related refresh function",
      ""
    ]);
  });

  rows.push(["", "", "", ""]);
  rows.push(["Function Check", "Status", "Notes", ""]);

  requiredFunctions.forEach(fn => {
    const exists = typeof globalThis[fn] === "function" ? "OK" : "MISSING";
    rows.push([
      fn,
      exists,
      exists === "OK" ? "Function found" : "Function missing or renamed",
      ""
    ]);
  });

  rows.push(["", "", "", ""]);

  // Chart count check
  rows.push(["Chart Count Check", "Count", "Status", ""]);

  ["Dashboard", "Executive Charts", "Calculator"].forEach(sheetName => {
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(sheetName);
    const count = sheet ? sheet.getCharts().length : 0;
    rows.push([
      sheetName,
      count,
      count <= 10 ? "OK" : "REVIEW - Too many charts",
      ""
    ]);
  });

  health.getRange(1, 1, rows.length, 4)
    .setValues(rows);

  formatWorkbookHealthCheck_(health);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 100G — FORMAT WORKBOOK HEALTH CHECK
// =====================================================

function formatWorkbookHealthCheck_(sheet) {

  const lastRow = Math.max(sheet.getLastRow(), 2);

  sheet.getRange("A1:D1")
    .merge()
    .setBackground("#111827")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(16);

  sheet.getRange("A4:D4")
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  sheet.getDataRange()
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setFontSize(10)
    .setVerticalAlignment("middle")
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  sheet.setFrozenRows(4);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(1, 300);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(2, 120);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(3, 420);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(4, 80);

  const rules = [];

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("OK")
      .setBackground("#d9ead3")
      .setFontColor("#274e13")
      .setRanges([sheet.getRange(1, 2, lastRow, 1), sheet.getRange(1, 3, lastRow, 1)])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("MISSING")
      .setBackground("#f4cccc")
      .setFontColor("#990000")
      .setRanges([sheet.getRange(1, 2, lastRow, 1)])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextContains("REVIEW")
      .setBackground("#fff2cc")
      .setFontColor("#7f6000")
      .setRanges([sheet.getRange(1, 3, lastRow, 1)])
      .build()
  );

  sheet.setConditionalFormatRules(rules);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 100H — FINAL MENU REFRESH PANEL
// PURPOSE:
// Adds a simple visual note to Control Panel showing that
// Module 100 is the final cleanup / polish tool.
// =====================================================

function addMasterUiPolishNoteToControlPanel() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const control = ss.getSheetByName("Control Panel");

  if (!control) return;

  const startRow = Math.max(control.getLastRow() + 2, 22);

  const rows = [
    ["Master UI Polish", "runMasterUiPolishCleanup", "Final cleanup: sheet order, tab colours, health check, chart cleanup, theme consistency"]
  ];

  control.getRange(startRow, 1, rows.length, 3).setValues(rows);

  control.getRange(startRow, 1, rows.length, 3)
    .setBackground("#fff2cc")
    .setFontColor("#7f6000")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  control.autoResizeColumns(1, 3);
}

function createPerformanceOptimisationGuideSheet() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  let guide = ss.getSheetByName("Performance Guide");

  if (!guide) guide = ss.insertSheet("Performance Guide");

  guide.clear();
  guide.setHiddenGridlines(true);

  const rows = [
    ["Stocks Overseer Advisor — Performance Guide", ""],
    ["Use Case", "Recommended Function"],
    ["First-time setup / reset", "runOneTimeWorkbookSetup"],
    ["Normal daily stock refresh", "runFastDailyRefresh"],
    ["Full workbook rebuild", "runFullOverseerUpdate"],
    ["Only UI cleanup", "refreshMasterUiPolishPackage"],
    ["Only calculator rebuild", "refreshGainDividendCalculatorWithGuide"],
    ["Only executive charts", "refreshExecutiveCharts"],
    ["Important note", "Avoid running heavy full rebuild repeatedly when only prices need refresh."],
    ["Optimisation note", "v44 full runner refreshes History Summary before Dashboard historical snapshot to avoid stale data."],
    ["Protection note", "Input protection is best run during setup, not every daily refresh."],
    ["Chart note", "Master cleanup limits duplicate charts on visual sheets."]
  ];

  guide.getRange(1, 1, rows.length, 2).setValues(rows);

  guide.getRange("A1:B1")
    .merge()
    .setBackground("#111827")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")

  guide.getRange(3, 1, rows.length - 2, 1)
    .setBackground("#f3f6fa")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  guide.getRange(1, 1, rows.length, 2)
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true)
    .setWrap(true);

  guide.setColumnWidth(1, 260);
  guide.setColumnWidth(2, 620);
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 101 — EXECUTION MODE SELECTOR
// PURPOSE:
// Adds clear run modes so the workbook does not always need
// to execute every heavy module.
// Modes:
// - Fast Daily Refresh
// - Full Rebuild
// - Data Only
// - Visual Only
// - Repair / Audit Only
// - Calculator Only
// - History Only
// =====================================================

function runExecutionModeSelector() {

  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();

  const response = ui.prompt(
    "Stocks Overseer Execution Mode",
    "Type one mode: FAST, FULL, DATA, VISUAL, REPAIR, CALCULATOR, HISTORY",
    ui.ButtonSet.OK_CANCEL
  );

  if (response.getSelectedButton() !== ui.Button.OK) return;

  const mode = String(response.getResponseText()).trim().toUpperCase();

  if (mode === "FAST") {
    runFastDailyRefresh();
  } else if (mode === "FULL") {
    runFullOverseerUpdate();
  } else if (mode === "DATA") {
    runDataOnlyRefresh();
  } else if (mode === "VISUAL") {
    runVisualOnlyRefresh();
  } else if (mode === "REPAIR") {
    runRepairAndAudit();
  } else if (mode === "CALCULATOR") {
    runCalculatorOnlyRefresh();
  } else if (mode === "HISTORY") {
    runHistoryOnlyRefresh();
  } else {
    ui.alert("Unknown mode. Use FAST, FULL, DATA, VISUAL, REPAIR, CALCULATOR, or HISTORY.");
  }
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 101A — DATA ONLY REFRESH
// PURPOSE:
// Refreshes core Input calculations only.
// Does not rebuild heavy dashboard/chart/report sheets.
// =====================================================

function runDataOnlyRefresh() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

  startRuntimeTimer_("DATA_ONLY_REFRESH");

  if (typeof addCleanGoogleFinanceColumns === "function") addCleanGoogleFinanceColumns();
  if (typeof ensureExpandedGoogleFinanceHeaders === "function") ensureExpandedGoogleFinanceHeaders();
  if (typeof recalculateCleanGoogleFinanceMetrics === "function") recalculateCleanGoogleFinanceMetrics();
  if (typeof runTickerDataQualityCheck === "function") runTickerDataQualityCheck();
  if (typeof runTickerFormatSuggestionEngine === "function") runTickerFormatSuggestionEngine();
  if (typeof updateErrorLogSheet === "function") updateErrorLogSheet();
  if (typeof updateSystemLog === "function") updateSystemLog();

  endRuntimeTimer_("DATA_ONLY_REFRESH");

  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert("Data-only refresh completed.");
}

// =====================================================
// MODULE 102 — HEADER INDEX CACHE HELPERS
// PURPOSE:
// Reduces repeated header scanning by building a reusable
// header map for each sheet.
// NOTE:
// Existing modules can continue using colIndex().
// New/optimised modules can use getHeaderMap_() and hcol_().
// =====================================================

function getHeaderMap_(sheet) {

  const cache = CacheService.getDocumentCache();
  const cacheKey = "HEADER_MAP_" + sheet.getSheetId() + "_" + sheet.getLastColumn();

  const cached = cache.get(cacheKey);

  if (cached) {
    try {
      return JSON.parse(cached);
    } catch (err) {
      // If cache corrupted, rebuild.
    }
  }

  const headers = sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, sheet.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
  const map = {};

  headers.forEach((header, index) => {
    if (header !== "" && header != null) {
      map[String(header).trim()] = index;
    }
  });

  cache.put(cacheKey, JSON.stringify(map), 600);

  return map;
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 102A — HEADER COLUMN HELPER
// PURPOSE:
// Returns 0-based column index from map.
// =====================================================

function hcol_(headerMap, headerName) {
  return headerMap.hasOwnProperty(headerName) ? headerMap[headerName] : -1;
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 102B — HEADER COLUMN A1 HELPER
// PURPOSE:
// Returns 1-based column index from map.
// =====================================================

function hcol1_(headerMap, headerName) {
  const c = hcol_(headerMap, headerName);
  return c >= 0 ? c + 1 : 0;
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 102C — CLEAR HEADER CACHE
// PURPOSE:
// Use if headers are changed and cache needs refreshing.
// =====================================================

function clearHeaderMapCache() {
  CacheService.getDocumentCache().removeAll([]);
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert("Header cache refresh requested. Cache will rebuild automatically.");
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 102D — FAST HEADER CHECK SHEET
// PURPOSE:
// Creates a diagnostic sheet showing important Input headers.
// =====================================================

function createHeaderIndexDiagnosticSheet() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");

  let sheet = ss.getSheetByName("Header Index Check");
  if (!sheet) sheet = ss.insertSheet("Header Index Check");

  sheet.clear();

  const map = getHeaderMap_(input);
  const rows = [["Header", "0-Based Index", "1-Based Column"]];

  Object.keys(map).forEach(key => {
    rows.push([key, map[key], map[key] + 1]);
  });

  sheet.getRange(1, 1, rows.length, rows[0].length).setValues(rows);

  sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 3)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  sheet.getDataRange()
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  sheet.autoResizeColumns(1, 3);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 103 — BATCH WRITE OPTIMISATION UTILITIES
// PURPOSE:
// Provides reusable helpers to reduce repeated setValue()
// calls and improve Apps Script performance.
// Existing modules can gradually migrate to these helpers.
// =====================================================

function batchWriteTable_(sheet, startRow, startCol, values, options) {

  if (!values || values.length === 0) return;

  options = options || {};

  const numRows = values.length;
  const numCols = values[0].length;

  const range = sheet.getRange(startRow, startCol, numRows, numCols);
  range.setValues(values);

  if (options.headerRows && options.headerRows > 0) {
    sheet.getRange(startRow, startCol, options.headerRows, numCols)
      .setBackground(options.headerBg || "#1f2933")
      .setFontColor(options.headerFont || "#ffffff")
      .setFontWeight("bold");
  }

  if (options.border) {
    range.setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);
  }

  if (options.fontFamily) {
    range.setFontFamily(options.fontFamily);
  }
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 103A — BATCH CLEAR + WRITE
// PURPOSE:
// Clears a target block then writes values in one setValues.
// =====================================================

function batchClearAndWriteTable_(sheet, startRow, startCol, clearRows, clearCols, values, options) {

  if (clearRows > 0 && clearCols > 0) {
    sheet.getRange(startRow, startCol, clearRows, clearCols).clearContent();
  }

  batchWriteTable_(sheet, startRow, startCol, values, options);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 103B — BATCH WRITE NOTES
// PURPOSE:
// Applies notes in fewer logical operations.
// notesArray format: [[row, col, note], ...]
// =====================================================

function batchWriteNotes_(sheet, notesArray) {

  if (!notesArray || notesArray.length === 0) return;

  notesArray.forEach(item => {
    sheet.getRange(item[0], item[1]).setNote(item[2]);
  });
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 103C — OPTIMISED TICKER STATUS WRITE
// PURPOSE:
// Faster replacement for row-by-row status writing where used.
// It writes status and remarks arrays in bulk.
// =====================================================

function runTickerDataQualityCheckOptimised() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);

  if (!input) throw new Error("Input sheet not found.");

  const data = input.getDataRange().getValues();
  const headers = data[0];
  const map = getHeaderMap_(input);

  const tickerCol = hcol_(map, "Ticker");
  const priceCol = hcol_(map, "Share Price");
  const marketCapCol = hcol_(map, "Market Cap");
  const epsCol = hcol_(map, "EPS");
  const peCol = hcol_(map, "PE Ratio");
  const betaCol = hcol_(map, "Beta");
  const high52Col = hcol_(map, "52 Week High");
  const low52Col = hcol_(map, "52 Week Low");
  const statusCol = hcol_(map, "Ticker Data Status");
  const remarksCol = hcol_(map, "Remarks");

  if (tickerCol < 0 || statusCol < 0) {
    if (typeof ensureExpandedGoogleFinanceHeaders === "function") {
      ensureExpandedGoogleFinanceHeaders();
    }
    return runTickerDataQualityCheckOptimised();
  }

  const statusValues = [];
  const remarksValues = remarksCol >= 0 ? [] : null;

  for (let r = 1; r < data.length; r++) {

    const row = data[r];

    if (!row[tickerCol]) {
      statusValues.push([""]);
      if (remarksValues) remarksValues.push([row[remarksCol] || ""]);
      continue;
    }

    const price = num(row[priceCol]);
    const marketCap = num(row[marketCapCol]);
    const eps = row[epsCol];
    const pe = row[peCol];
    const beta = row[betaCol];
    const high52 = num(row[high52Col]);
    const low52 = num(row[low52Col]);

    let status = "OK";
    let issues = [];

    if (!price) issues.push("NO PRICE DATA");
    if (!marketCap) issues.push("NO MARKET CAP");
    if (eps === "" || eps == null) issues.push("NO EPS DATA");
    if (pe === "" || pe == null) issues.push("NO PE DATA");
    if (beta === "" || beta == null) issues.push("NO BETA DATA");
    if (!high52 || !low52) issues.push("NO 52W RANGE DATA");

    if (issues.length > 0) status = issues.join(" | ");

    if (!price && !marketCap && !high52 && !low52) {
      status = "CHECK TICKER FORMAT";
    }

    statusValues.push([status]);

    if (remarksValues) {
      remarksValues.push([
        status !== "OK" ? "Data quality warning: " + status : row[remarksCol] || ""
      ]);
    }
  }

  input.getRange(2, statusCol + 1, statusValues.length, 1).setValues(statusValues);

  if (remarksValues && remarksCol >= 0) {
    input.getRange(2, remarksCol + 1, remarksValues.length, 1).setValues(remarksValues);
  }

  if (typeof formatTickerDataQualityStatus === "function") {
    formatTickerDataQualityStatus(input);
  }
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 104 — CONDITIONAL FORMATTING RESET CONTROL
// PURPOSE:
// Prevents conditional formatting rules from accumulating
// endlessly after repeated full refreshes.
// =====================================================

function resetWorkbookConditionalFormatting() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

  const targetSheets = [
    SHEET_NAME,
    DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME,
    "Calculator",
    "Management View",
    "Executive Charts",
    "Investment Committee",
    "Score Explanation",
    "Alert Centre",
    "System Log",
    "Error Log",
    "Fundamental Import Validation",
    "History Summary",
    "Workbook Health Check"
  ];

  targetSheets.forEach(sheetName => {
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(sheetName);
    if (sheet) {
      sheet.setConditionalFormatRules([]);
    }
  });

  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert("Conditional formatting reset completed for main workbook sheets.");
}

function resetWorkbookConditionalFormattingQuiet() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

    SHEET_NAME,
    DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME,
    "Calculator",
    "Management View",
    "Executive Charts",
    "Investment Committee",
    "Score Explanation",
    "Alert Centre",
    "System Log",
    "Error Log",
    "Fundamental Import Validation",
    "History Summary",
    "Workbook Health Check"
  ];

  targetSheets.forEach(sheetName => {
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(sheetName);
    if (sheet) {
      sheet.setConditionalFormatRules([]);
    }
  });
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 104B — CONDITIONAL FORMATTING RULE COUNT CHECK
// PURPOSE:
// Creates a diagnostic sheet showing rule count by sheet.
// =====================================================

function createConditionalFormattingDiagnosticSheet() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  let diag = ss.getSheetByName("Conditional Formatting Check");

  if (!diag) diag = ss.insertSheet("Conditional Formatting Check");

  diag.clear();

  const rows = [["Sheet", "Conditional Format Rule Count", "Status"]];

  ss.getSheets().forEach(sheet => {
    const count = sheet.getConditionalFormatRules().length;
    rows.push([
      sheet.getName(),
      count,
      count > 80 ? "REVIEW - Too many rules" : "OK"
    ]);
  });

  diag.getRange(1, 1, rows.length, rows[0].length).setValues(rows);

  diag.getRange(1, 1, 1, 3)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  diag.getDataRange()
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  diag.autoResizeColumns(1, 3);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 105 — CHART CLEANUP BEFORE REBUILD
// PURPOSE:
// Removes charts from selected sheets before rebuilding visual
// modules. Prevents duplicate chart accumulation and slow sheets.
// =====================================================

function cleanupChartsBeforeRebuild() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

  const chartSheets = [
    DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME,
    "Executive Charts",
    "Calculator",
    "Management View",
    "Executive Summary",
    "Watchlist Funnel"
  ];

  chartSheets.forEach(sheetName => {
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(sheetName);

    if (sheet) {
      sheet.getCharts().forEach(chart => {
        sheet.removeChart(chart);
      });
    }
  });
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 105A — TARGETED CHART CLEANUP
// PURPOSE:
// Allows cleanup of one specific sheet's charts.
// =====================================================

function cleanupChartsOnSheet_(sheetName) {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(sheetName);

  if (!sheet) return;

  sheet.getCharts().forEach(chart => {
    sheet.removeChart(chart);
  });
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 105B — CHART DIAGNOSTIC SHEET
// PURPOSE:
// Shows chart count per sheet.
// =====================================================

function createChartDiagnosticSheet() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  let diag = ss.getSheetByName("Chart Check");

  if (!diag) diag = ss.insertSheet("Chart Check");

  diag.clear();

  const rows = [["Sheet", "Chart Count", "Status"]];

  ss.getSheets().forEach(sheet => {
    const count = sheet.getCharts().length;
    rows.push([
      sheet.getName(),
      count,
      count > 8 ? "REVIEW - Many charts" : "OK"
    ]);
  });

  diag.getRange(1, 1, rows.length, rows[0].length).setValues(rows);

  diag.getRange(1, 1, 1, 3)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  diag.getDataRange()
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  diag.autoResizeColumns(1, 3);
}

  createHeaderIndexDiagnosticSheet();
  createConditionalFormattingDiagnosticSheet();
  createChartDiagnosticSheet();
}

// PURPOSE:
// Runs optimisation support tasks that are safe to run anytime.
// =====================================================

function refreshOptimisationSupportPackage() {
  createOptimisationDiagnosticsPackage();

  if (typeof createPerformanceOptimisationGuideSheet === "function") {
    createPerformanceOptimisationGuideSheet();
  }
}

// =====================================================
// MODULE 95A — ONBOARDING TABLE STYLE HELPER
// PURPOSE:
// Reusable formatter for onboarding wizard tables.
// =====================================================

function styleOnboardingTable_(sheet, startRow, startCol, numRows, numCols, headerColour) {

  sheet.getRange(startRow, startCol, 1, numCols)
    .setBackground(headerColour)
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  sheet.getRange(startRow + 1, startCol, Math.max(numRows - 1, 1), 1)
    .setBackground("#f3f6fa")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  sheet.getRange(startRow, startCol, numRows, numCols)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true)
    .setVerticalAlignment("middle");
}

// Wrapper for menu and full runner.

// =====================================================
// MODULE 106 — CALCULATOR AUTO-FILL ENHANCEMENT
// PURPOSE:
// Expands the Calculator sheet so more fields are auto-filled
// once a ticker is selected from the dropdown.
// Pulls available data from:
// - Input
// - History Summary
// - Alert Centre
// - Score Explanation
// - Investment Committee
// Keeps only true assumptions as manual input.
// =====================================================

function enhanceCalculatorAutoFillFromSheets() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const calc = ss.getSheetByName("Calculator");

  if (!calc) {
    throw new Error("Calculator sheet not found. Run refreshGainDividendCalculatorWithGuide() first.");
  }

  // Ensure calculator base exists
  if (!calc.getRange("B5").getValue() && !calc.getRange("B5").getDataValidation()) {
    if (typeof refreshGainDividendCalculatorWithGuide === "function") {
      refreshGainDividendCalculatorWithGuide();
    }
  }

  createCalculatorAutoMarketDataPanel_();
  createCalculatorAutoHistoryPanel_();
  createCalculatorAutoRiskDecisionPanel_();
  createCalculatorAutoAlertPanel_();
  createCalculatorAutoDefaultsPanel_();
  applyCalculatorAutoFillFormatting_();
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 106A — AUTO MARKET DATA PANEL
// PURPOSE:
// Auto-fills core ticker data from Input using header names.
// =====================================================

function createCalculatorAutoMarketDataPanel_() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const calc = ss.getSheetByName("Calculator");
  const input = ss.getSheetByName(SHEET_NAME);

  if (!calc || !input) return;

  const startRow = 4;
  const startCol = 10; // Column J

  const fields = [
    ["Auto-Filled Market Data", ""],
    ["Company", calculatorLookupFormula_("Input", "Company")],
    ["Currency", calculatorLookupFormula_("Input", "Currency")],
    ["Current Share Price", calculatorLookupFormula_("Input", "Share Price")],
    ["Market Cap", calculatorLookupFormula_("Input", "Market Cap")],
    ["PE Ratio", calculatorLookupFormula_("Input", "PE Ratio")],
    ["EPS", calculatorLookupFormula_("Input", "EPS")],
    ["Beta", calculatorLookupFormula_("Input", "Beta")],
    ["52W High", calculatorLookupFormula_("Input", "52 Week High")],
    ["52W Low", calculatorLookupFormula_("Input", "52 Week Low")],
    ["Average Volume", calculatorLookupFormula_("Input", "Average Volume")],
    ["GoogleFinance Score", calculatorLookupFormula_("Input", "GoogleFinance Score")]
  ];

  calc.getRange(startRow, startCol, fields.length, 2).clearContent();
  calc.getRange(startRow, startCol, fields.length, 2).setValues(fields);
}

// =====================================================
// MODULE 106D — AUTO ALERT PANEL
// PURPOSE:
// Pulls alert status from Alert Centre where ticker appears.
// Uses COUNTIF/FILTER formulas so it updates when ticker changes.
// =====================================================

function createCalculatorAutoAlertPanel_() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const calc = ss.getSheetByName("Calculator");
  const alert = ss.getSheetByName("Alert Centre");

  if (!calc || !alert) return;

  const startRow = 40;
  const startCol = 10; // J

  const fields = [
    ["Auto-Filled Alert Status", ""],
    ["Alert Count", `=IFERROR(COUNTIF('Alert Centre'!C:C,$B$5),0)`],
    ["Critical Alerts", `=IFERROR(COUNTIFS('Alert Centre'!C:C,$B$5,'Alert Centre'!A:A,"CRITICAL"),0)`],
    ["High Alerts", `=IFERROR(COUNTIFS('Alert Centre'!C:C,$B$5,'Alert Centre'!A:A,"HIGH"),0)`],
    ["Medium Alerts", `=IFERROR(COUNTIFS('Alert Centre'!C:C,$B$5,'Alert Centre'!A:A,"MEDIUM"),0)`],
    ["Main Alert Type", `=IFERROR(INDEX(FILTER('Alert Centre'!B:B,'Alert Centre'!C:C=$B$5),1),"No alert")`],
    ["Alert Suggested Action", `=IFERROR(INDEX(FILTER('Alert Centre'!L:L,'Alert Centre'!C:C=$B$5),1),"No alert action")`]
  ];

  calc.getRange(startRow, startCol, fields.length, 2).clearContent();
  calc.getRange(startRow, startCol, fields.length, 2).setValues(fields);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 106E — AUTO DEFAULTS PANEL
// PURPOSE:
// Uses selected ticker data to provide smarter calculator defaults.
// These are suggested values; user can still override manual inputs.
// =====================================================

function createCalculatorAutoDefaultsPanel_() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const calc = ss.getSheetByName("Calculator");

  if (!calc) return;

  const startRow = 49;
  const startCol = 10; // J

  const fields = [
    ["Suggested Defaults", ""],
    ["Suggested Buy Price", `=IFERROR(B8,"")`],
    ["Suggested Desired Buy Price", `=IFERROR(MIN(B8*0.9,K13*1.05),"")`],
    ["Suggested Target Sell Price", `=IFERROR(MAX(B8*1.2,K12),"")`],
    ["Suggested Dividend Yield %", `=IFERROR(IF(B13<>"",B13,K34),"")`],
    ["Suggested Dividend Per Share", `=IFERROR(B14,"")`],
    ["Suggested Holding Years", `=IFERROR(IF(K28>0.15,3,1),1)`],
    ["Suggested Decision Note", `=IFERROR(IF(K41>0,"Review alerts before action",IF(K32="BUY CANDIDATE","Scenario suitable for further review","Use calculator as watchlist scenario")),"")`]
  ];

  calc.getRange(startRow, startCol, fields.length, 2).clearContent();
  calc.getRange(startRow, startCol, fields.length, 2).setValues(fields);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 106F — HEADER-BASED LOOKUP FORMULA BUILDER
// PURPOSE:
// Creates safer formulas that locate columns by header text.
// This avoids hard-coded column references like Input!AI:AI.
// =====================================================

function calculatorLookupFormula_(sheetName, headerName) {

  return `=IFERROR(INDEX('${sheetName}'!$A:$ZZ,MATCH($B$5,'${sheetName}'!$A:$A,0),MATCH("${headerName}",'${sheetName}'!$1:$1,0)),"")`;
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 106G — APPLY AUTO-FILL FORMATTING
// PURPOSE:
// Formats the auto-filled panels and separates them visually
// from manual blue input zones.
// =====================================================

function applyCalculatorAutoFillFormatting_() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const calc = ss.getSheetByName("Calculator");

  if (!calc) return;

  const panels = [
    ["J4:K15", "J4:K4"],
    ["J18:K26", "J18:K18"],
    ["J29:K37", "J29:K29"],
    ["J40:K46", "J40:K40"],
    ["J49:K56", "J49:K49"]
  ];

  panels.forEach(item => {
    calc.getRange(item[0])
      .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true)
      .setFontFamily("Arial")
      .setFontSize(10)
      .setVerticalAlignment("middle")
      .setWrap(true);

    calc.getRange(item[1])
      .setBackground("#1f2933")
      .setFontColor("#ffffff")
      .setFontWeight("bold");

    const range = calc.getRange(item[0]);
    const startRow = range.getRow();
    const numRows = range.getNumRows();

    if (numRows > 1) {
      calc.getRange(startRow + 1, range.getColumn(), numRows - 1, 1)
        .setBackground("#f3f6fa")
        .setFontWeight("bold");

      calc.getRange(startRow + 1, range.getColumn() + 1, numRows - 1, 1)
        .setBackground("#f7f7f7");
    }
  });

  // Number formats for auto-fill panels
  calc.getRange("K7:K14").setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");
  calc.getRange("K19:K22").setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");
  calc.getRange("K23:K26").setNumberFormat("0.00%");
  calc.getRange("K32:K34").setNumberFormat("0.00%");
  calc.getRange("K50:K52").setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");
  calc.getRange("K53").setNumberFormat("0.00%");
  calc.getRange("K54").setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");

  calc.setColumnWidth(10, 240);
  calc.setColumnWidth(11, 260);

  // Re-highlight true manual input cells
  ["B5", "E5", "E6", "E7", "E8", "E9", "E10", "E11", "E12"].forEach(cell => {
    calc.getRange(cell)
      .setBackground("#d9eaf7")
      .setFontWeight("bold")
      .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true, "#0b5394", SpreadsheetApp.BorderStyle.SOLID_MEDIUM);
  });
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 106H — CALCULATOR AUTO-FILL GUIDE
// PURPOSE:
// Adds a guide explaining which fields are automated and which
// remain manual.
// =====================================================

function createCalculatorAutoFillGuideSheet() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

  let guide = ss.getSheetByName("Calculator Auto-Fill Guide");

  if (!guide) {
    guide = ss.insertSheet("Calculator Auto-Fill Guide");
  }

  guide.clear();
  guide.setHiddenGridlines(true);

  const rows = [
    ["Calculator Auto-Fill Guide", "Source Sheet", "Auto / Manual", "Notes"],
    ["Selected Ticker", "Calculator", "Manual", "Dropdown from Input ticker list"],
    ["Company / Currency / Price / PE / EPS / Beta", "Input", "Auto", "Pulled using selected ticker"],
    ["52W High / 52W Low / Average Volume", "Input", "Auto", "GoogleFinance-derived where available"],
    ["Score / Recommendation / Watchlist / Risk / Momentum", "Input", "Auto", "Derived by existing scoring modules"],
    ["Historical Prices and Returns", "History Summary", "Auto", "Requires History Summary to be refreshed"],
    ["Alert Count / Alert Type / Suggested Action", "Alert Centre", "Auto", "Requires Alert Centre to be refreshed"],
    ["Suggested Buy Price", "Calculator + Input", "Auto suggestion", "Defaults to current price"],
    ["Suggested Desired Buy Price", "Calculator + 52W Low", "Auto suggestion", "Uses current price and 52W low logic"],
    ["Suggested Target Sell Price", "Calculator + 52W High", "Auto suggestion", "Uses current price and 52W high logic"],
    ["Buy Price / Target / Shares / Dividend / Holding Period", "Calculator", "Manual", "True scenario assumptions remain editable blue cells"]
  ];

  guide.getRange(1, 1, rows.length, rows[0].length)
    .setValues(rows);

  guide.getRange(1, 1, 1, rows[0].length)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  guide.getRange(2, 3, rows.length - 1, 1)
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  guide.getRange(1, 1, rows.length, rows[0].length)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true)
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setWrap(true);

  guide.setColumnWidth(1, 260);
  guide.setColumnWidth(2, 160);
  guide.setColumnWidth(3, 140);
  guide.setColumnWidth(4, 520);
  guide.setFrozenRows(1);
}

// PURPOSE:
// Runs all auto-fill enhancement functions.
// =====================================================

function refreshCalculatorAutoFillEnhancement() {
  enhanceCalculatorAutoFillFromSheets();
  createCalculatorAutoFillGuideSheet();
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 107 — CALCULATOR TICKER SELECTION AUTO-FILL FIX
// PURPOSE:
// Ensures the main Calculator section ① Ticker Selection
// auto-fills correctly after selecting ticker from dropdown.
// Uses header-based lookup instead of hard-coded columns.
// This fixes blank cells for:
// - Company
// - Currency
// - Current Share Price
// - PE Ratio
// - EPS
// - GoogleFinance Score
// - Final Recommendation
// - Dividend Yield % from Input
// - Dividend Per Share from Input
// =====================================================

function fixCalculatorTickerSelectionAutoFill() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const calc = ss.getSheetByName("Calculator");

  if (!calc) {
    throw new Error("Calculator sheet not found. Run refreshGainDividendCalculatorWithGuide() first.");
  }

  // Keep the ticker dropdown at B5 and use selected ticker as lookup key.
  // The formula searches the header row in Input, so it will still work
  // even if columns move in the Input sheet.

  const formulas = [
    ["B6", calculatorLookupFormula_("Input", "Company")],
    ["B7", calculatorLookupFormula_("Input", "Currency")],
    ["B8", calculatorLookupFormula_("Input", "Share Price")],
    ["B9", calculatorLookupFormula_("Input", "PE Ratio")],
    ["B10", calculatorLookupFormula_("Input", "EPS")],
    ["B11", calculatorLookupFormula_("Input", "GoogleFinance Score")],
    ["B12", calculatorLookupFormula_("Input", "Final Recommendation")],
    ["B13", calculatorLookupFormula_("Input", "Dividend Yield %")],
    ["B14", calculatorLookupFormula_("Input", "Dividend Per Share")]
  ];

  formulas.forEach(item => {
    calc.getRange(item[0]).setFormula(item[1]);
  });

  // Formatting
  calc.getRange("B6:B14")
    .setBackground("#f7f7f7")
    .setFontColor("#111827")
    .setFontWeight("normal");

  calc.getRange("B8:B11").setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");
  calc.getRange("B13").setNumberFormat("0.00%");
  calc.getRange("B14").setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");

  calc.getRange("A4:B14")
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  calc.getRange("A4")
    .setValue("① Ticker Selection")
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  calc.getRange("A5:A14")
    .setBackground("#f3f6fa")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  calc.getRange("B5")
    .setBackground("#d9eaf7")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setNote("MANUAL INPUT: Select ticker from dropdown.");

  calc.autoResizeColumns(1, 2);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 107A — CALCULATOR DIVIDEND HEADER FALLBACK
// PURPOSE:
// Some workbooks may use slightly different dividend headers.
// This function improves B13 and B14 by trying multiple possible
// header names before returning blank.
// =====================================================

function fixCalculatorDividendAutoFillFallback() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const calc = ss.getSheetByName("Calculator");

  if (!calc) return;

  calc.getRange("B13").setFormula(
    `=IFERROR(INDEX(Input!$A:$ZZ,MATCH($B$5,Input!$A:$A,0),MATCH("Dividend Yield %",Input!$1:$1,0)),` +
    `IFERROR(INDEX(Input!$A:$ZZ,MATCH($B$5,Input!$A:$A,0),MATCH("Dividend Yield",Input!$1:$1,0)),` +
    `IFERROR(INDEX(Input!$A:$ZZ,MATCH($B$5,Input!$A:$A,0),MATCH("Yield on Cost %",Input!$1:$1,0)),"")))`
  );

  calc.getRange("B14").setFormula(
    `=IFERROR(INDEX(Input!$A:$ZZ,MATCH($B$5,Input!$A:$A,0),MATCH("Dividend Per Share",Input!$1:$1,0)),` +
    `IFERROR(INDEX(Input!$A:$ZZ,MATCH($B$5,Input!$A:$A,0),MATCH("Dividend Per Share from Input",Input!$1:$1,0)),` +
    `IFERROR(INDEX(Input!$A:$ZZ,MATCH($B$5,Input!$A:$A,0),MATCH("DPS",Input!$1:$1,0)),"")))`
  );

  calc.getRange("B13").setNumberFormat("0.00%");
  calc.getRange("B14").setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 107B — CALCULATOR AUTO-FILL FULL PATCH WRAPPER
// PURPOSE:
// Runs the full calculator ticker-selection auto-fill patch.
// =====================================================

function refreshCalculatorTickerSelectionAutoFillPatch() {
  fixCalculatorTickerSelectionAutoFill();
  fixCalculatorDividendAutoFillFallback();
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 108 — DASHBOARD SIDEBAR COLOUR CLASH FIX
// PURPOSE:
// Fixes colour clashes in Dashboard columns N:Z.
// The dashboard uses columns A:M for main tables and N:Z for
// side panels. Previous theme/row styling could accidentally
// colour entire rows across the sidebar, causing visual clashes.
// This module creates a dedicated right-sidebar style zone.
// =====================================================

function fixDashboardSidebarColourClash() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!dash) {
    throw new Error("Dashboard sheet not found.");
  }

  const lastRow = Math.max(dash.getLastRow(), 160);
  const sidebarStartCol = 14; // Column N
  const sidebarEndCol = 26;   // Column Z
  const sidebarCols = sidebarEndCol - sidebarStartCol + 1;

  // =====================================================
  // STEP 1 — RESET SIDEBAR BACKGROUND ONLY
  // Do not clear contents/formulas. Only reset visual clash.
  // =====================================================

  dash.getRange(1, sidebarStartCol, lastRow, sidebarCols)
    .setBackground("#ffffff")
    .setFontColor("#111827")
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setFontSize(10)
    .setVerticalAlignment("middle")
    .setWrap(true);

  // =====================================================
  // STEP 2 — SIDEBAR TITLE / MODE AREA
  // =====================================================

  dash.getRange("N1:Z1")
    .setBackground("#111827")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  dash.getRange("N2:Z2")
    .setBackground("#f3f6fa")
    .setFontColor("#1f2933")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  // =====================================================
  // STEP 3 — STYLE KNOWN SIDEBAR PANELS ONLY IN N:Z
  // =====================================================

  const sidebarPanelTitles = [
    "Ticker Count + Data Coverage Summary",
    "Overseer Status Panel",
    "Dashboard Navigation",
    "Latest System Log",
    "Error Log Summary",
    "User Zone",
    "Manual Input Reminder",
    "Fundamental Import Layer",
    "Fundamental Import Validation",
    "Badge Legend",
    "Row Highlight Legend",
    "Executive Banner Logic",
    "Print / PDF Guide",
    "Filter View Buttons",
    "Theme Selector",
    "Icon Legend",
    "Alert Centre",
    "Manual Input Reminder",
    "Calculator UI Legend",
    "Print / PDF Guide"
  ];

  sidebarPanelTitles.forEach(title => {
    styleDashboardSidebarPanelByTitle_(dash, title);
  });

  // =====================================================
  // STEP 4 — RESTORE TOP 10 MINI VISUALS AREA IF PRESENT
  // This area starts around N and should not use sidebar panel
  // colours if it belongs to the Top 10 mini charts.
  // =====================================================

  const miniTitle = dash.createTextFinder("Top 10 Mini Visuals")
    .matchEntireCell(true)
    .findNext();

  if (miniTitle && miniTitle.getColumn() >= sidebarStartCol) {

    const row = miniTitle.getRow();
    const col = miniTitle.getColumn();

    dash.getRange(row, col, 1, 5)
      .setBackground("#d9e2f3")
      .setFontColor("#1f2933")
      .setFontWeight("bold");

    dash.getRange(row + 1, col, 1, 5)
      .setBackground("#1f2933")
      .setFontColor("#ffffff")
      .setFontWeight("bold")
      .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

    const rows = detectTableLength(dash, row + 2, col);
    if (rows > 0) {
      dash.getRange(row + 2, col, rows, 5)
        .setBackground("#ffffff")
        .setFontColor("#111827")
        .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true, "#d9d9d9", SpreadsheetApp.BorderStyle.SOLID);
    }
  }

  // =====================================================
  // STEP 5 — COLUMN WIDTHS N:Z
  // =====================================================

  dash.setColumnWidth(14, 210); // N labels
  dash.setColumnWidth(15, 250); // O values
  dash.setColumnWidth(16, 120);
  dash.setColumnWidth(17, 120);
  dash.setColumnWidth(18, 120);
  dash.setColumnWidth(19, 120);
  dash.setColumnWidth(20, 120);
  dash.setColumnWidth(21, 120);
  dash.setColumnWidth(22, 120);
  dash.setColumnWidth(23, 120);
  dash.setColumnWidth(24, 120);
  dash.setColumnWidth(25, 120);
  dash.setColumnWidth(26, 120);

  // =====================================================
  // STEP 6 — ADD LIGHT SIDEBAR DIVIDER
  // =====================================================

  dash.getRange(1, sidebarStartCol, lastRow, 1)
    .setBorder(null, true, null, null, null, null, "#9ca3af", SpreadsheetApp.BorderStyle.SOLID_MEDIUM);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 108A — STYLE DASHBOARD SIDEBAR PANEL BY TITLE
// PURPOSE:
// Finds a panel title in N:Z and styles a compact card.
// =====================================================

function styleDashboardSidebarPanelByTitle_(dash, title) {

  const matches = dash.createTextFinder(title)
    .matchEntireCell(true)
    .findAll();

  if (!matches || matches.length === 0) return;

  matches.forEach(cell => {

    const row = cell.getRow();
    const col = cell.getColumn();

    // Only affect sidebar area N:Z.
    if (col < 14 || col > 26) return;

    const maxRows = 8;
    const maxCols = Math.min(2, 27 - col);

    // Panel title
    dash.getRange(row, col, 1, maxCols)
      .setBackground("#111827")
      .setFontColor("#ffffff")
      .setFontWeight("bold")
      .setHorizontalAlignment("left");

    // Panel body
    dash.getRange(row + 1, col, maxRows - 1, maxCols)
      .setBackground("#ffffff")
      .setFontColor("#111827")
      .setFontWeight("normal")
      .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true, "#e5e7eb", SpreadsheetApp.BorderStyle.SOLID);

    // Left labels inside panel
    dash.getRange(row + 1, col, maxRows - 1, 1)
      .setBackground("#f3f6fa")
      .setFontColor("#1f2933")
      .setFontWeight("bold");

    // Right values inside panel
    if (maxCols >= 2) {
      dash.getRange(row + 1, col + 1, maxRows - 1, 1)
        .setBackground("#ffffff")
        .setFontColor("#111827")
        .setFontWeight("normal");
    }

    // Full panel border
    dash.getRange(row, col, maxRows, maxCols)
      .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true, "#d9d9d9", SpreadsheetApp.BorderStyle.SOLID);
  });
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 108B — LIMIT MAIN TABLE HEADER STYLING TO A:M
// PURPOSE:
// Re-applies main dashboard row header styling only to A:M,
// avoiding accidental colouring of N:Z sidebar panels.
// =====================================================

function fixDashboardMainTableStylingScope() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!dash) return;

  const keywords = ["Rank", "Ticker", "Metric", "Risk Group", "Score Band"];

  keywords.forEach(keyword => {
    const matches = dash.createTextFinder(keyword)
      .matchCase(false)
      .findAll();

    matches.forEach(cell => {
      const row = cell.getRow();

      if (row <= 1) return;

      // Main dashboard area only: A:M.
      if (cell.getColumn() <= 13) {
        dash.getRange(row, 1, 1, 13)
          .setBackground("#1f2933")
          .setFontColor("#ffffff")
          .setFontWeight("bold");
      }
    });
  });
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 108C — DASHBOARD SIDEBAR FIX WRAPPER
// PURPOSE:
// Runs all sidebar colour clash fixes.
// =====================================================

function refreshDashboardSidebarColourFix() {
  fixDashboardMainTableStylingScope();
  fixDashboardSidebarColourClash();
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 109 — INVESTMENT COMMITTEE + SCORE EXPLANATION UI UPGRADE
// PURPOSE:
// Improves the visual design and conditional formatting of:
// - Investment Committee sheet

// Adds:

// - colour badges
// - score heatmaps
// - risk highlights
// - decision input zones
// - row banding
// - better column widths and wrapping
