function refreshCommitteeAndScoreUiUpgrade() {
  improveInvestmentCommitteeUi();
  improveScoreExplanationUi();
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 109A — INVESTMENT COMMITTEE UI UPGRADE
// PURPOSE:
// Makes Investment Committee sheet easier for meeting review.
// =====================================================

function improveInvestmentCommitteeUi() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName("Investment Committee");

  if (!sheet) {
    if (typeof createInvestmentCommitteeView === "function") {
      createInvestmentCommitteeView();
    }
  }

  const ic = ss.getSheetByName("Investment Committee");
  if (!ic) return;

  const lastRow = Math.max(ic.getLastRow(), 5);
  const lastCol = Math.max(ic.getLastColumn(), 15);

  ic.setHiddenGridlines(true);
  ic.setFrozenRows(4);

  ic.getDataRange()
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setFontSize(10)
    .setVerticalAlignment("middle")
    .setWrap(true);

  // Main title
  ic.getRange(1, 1, 1, Math.min(lastCol, 15))
    .merge()
    .setValue("Stocks Overseer Advisor — Investment Committee Decision View")
    .setBackground("#111827")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(16)
    .setHorizontalAlignment("left");

  ic.setRowHeight(1, 38);

  // Subtitle / guidance
  ic.getRange(2, 1, 1, Math.min(lastCol, 15))
    .merge()
    .setValue("Use this sheet during review meetings. System fields are automated; Committee Decision and Decision Notes are manual review fields.")
    .setBackground("#f3f6fa")
    .setFontColor("#374151")
    .setFontStyle("italic")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("left");

  ic.setRowHeight(2, 28);

  // Header row
  ic.getRange(4, 1, 1, lastCol)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center")
    .setVerticalAlignment("middle");

  ic.setRowHeight(4, 46);

  // Manual decision columns: N:O if present
  if (lastCol >= 15) {
    ic.getRange(4, 14, 1, 2)
      .setBackground("#0b5394")
      .setFontColor("#ffffff")
      .setFontWeight("bold");

    ic.getRange(5, 14, Math.max(lastRow - 4, 1), 2)
      .setBackground("#d9eaf7")
      .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true, "#0b5394", SpreadsheetApp.BorderStyle.SOLID)
      .setNote("Manual Investment Committee input zone.");
  }

  // Borders and row banding
  ic.getRange(4, 1, Math.max(lastRow - 3, 1), lastCol)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true, "#d9d9d9", SpreadsheetApp.BorderStyle.SOLID);

  for (let r = 5; r <= lastRow; r++) {
    const bg = r % 2 === 0 ? "#ffffff" : "#f8fafc";
    ic.getRange(r, 1, 1, Math.min(lastCol, 13)).setBackground(bg);
  }

  // Number formats
  if (lastRow >= 5) {
    ic.getRange(5, 4, lastRow - 4, 3).setNumberFormat("#,##0.00"); // Price, PE, Score
    ic.getRange(5, 7, lastRow - 4, 2).setNumberFormat("0.00%");   // Yield, upside
    ic.getRange(5, 11, lastRow - 4, 1).setNumberFormat("0.00%");  // Allocation
  }

  // Conditional formatting reset only for this sheet to avoid accumulation.
  ic.setConditionalFormatRules([]);
  const rules = [];

  const dataRange = ic.getRange(5, 1, Math.max(lastRow - 4, 1), lastCol);
  const decisionGroupRange = ic.getRange(5, 1, Math.max(lastRow - 4, 1), 1);
  const scoreRange = ic.getRange(5, 6, Math.max(lastRow - 4, 1), 1);
  const riskRange = ic.getRange(5, 9, Math.max(lastRow - 4, 1), 1);
  const momentumRange = ic.getRange(5, 10, Math.max(lastRow - 4, 1), 1);
  const committeeDecisionRange = ic.getRange(5, 14, Math.max(lastRow - 4, 1), 1);

  // Decision Group badge colours
  addIcTextRule_(rules, decisionGroupRange, "BUY CANDIDATE", "#38761d", "#ffffff");
  addIcTextRule_(rules, decisionGroupRange, "ACCUMULATE / STUDY", "#6aa84f", "#ffffff");
  addIcTextRule_(rules, decisionGroupRange, "VALUE WATCH", "#3c78d8", "#ffffff");
  addIcTextRule_(rules, decisionGroupRange, "HOLD / MONITOR", "#f1c232", "#000000");
  addIcTextRule_(rules, decisionGroupRange, "AVOID / HIGH RISK", "#cc0000", "#ffffff");

  // Entire row soft highlights
  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenFormulaSatisfied('=$A5="BUY CANDIDATE"')
      .setBackground("#eaf4e4")
      .setFontColor("#274e13")
      .setRanges([dataRange])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenFormulaSatisfied('=$A5="AVOID / HIGH RISK"')
      .setBackground("#fce8e6")
      .setFontColor("#990000")
      .setRanges([dataRange])
      .build()
  );

  // Score heatmap
  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .setGradientMinpointWithValue("#f4cccc", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "0")
      .setGradientMidpointWithValue("#fff2cc", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "60")
      .setGradientMaxpointWithValue("#d9ead3", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "100")
      .setRanges([scoreRange])
      .build()
  );

  // Risk badges
  addIcTextRule_(rules, riskRange, "LOW RISK", "#d9ead3", "#274e13");
  addIcTextRule_(rules, riskRange, "MODERATE RISK", "#fff2cc", "#7f6000");
  addIcTextRule_(rules, riskRange, "HIGH RISK", "#fce5cd", "#783f04");
  addIcTextRule_(rules, riskRange, "VERY HIGH RISK", "#cc0000", "#ffffff");
  addIcTextRule_(rules, riskRange, "NO BETA DATA", "#d9d9d9", "#666666");

  // Momentum badges
  addIcTextRule_(rules, momentumRange, "STRONG MOMENTUM", "#38761d", "#ffffff");
  addIcTextRule_(rules, momentumRange, "POSITIVE TREND", "#6aa84f", "#ffffff");
  addIcTextRule_(rules, momentumRange, "NEUTRAL", "#d9d9d9", "#000000");
  addIcTextRule_(rules, momentumRange, "WEAK", "#fce5cd", "#783f04");
  addIcTextRule_(rules, momentumRange, "NEAR 52W LOW", "#cfe2f3", "#073763");

  // Committee manual decision badges
  addIcTextRule_(rules, committeeDecisionRange, "APPROVE BUY", "#38761d", "#ffffff");
  addIcTextRule_(rules, committeeDecisionRange, "ACCUMULATE", "#6aa84f", "#ffffff");
  addIcTextRule_(rules, committeeDecisionRange, "HOLD", "#f1c232", "#000000");
  addIcTextRule_(rules, committeeDecisionRange, "REJECT", "#cc0000", "#ffffff");
  addIcTextRule_(rules, committeeDecisionRange, "DEFER", "#d9d9d9", "#000000");

  ic.setConditionalFormatRules(rules);

  // Data validation for Committee Decision column
  if (lastCol >= 14) {
    const decisionRule = SpreadsheetApp.newDataValidation()
      .requireValueInList(["APPROVE BUY", "ACCUMULATE", "HOLD", "REJECT", "DEFER"], true)
      .setAllowInvalid(true)
      .setHelpText("Select committee decision.")
      .build();

    ic.getRange(5, 14, Math.max(lastRow - 4, 1), 1).setDataValidation(decisionRule);
  }

  // Column widths
  ic.setColumnWidth(1, 170);
  ic.setColumnWidth(2, 120);
  ic.setColumnWidth(3, 230);
  ic.setColumnWidth(4, 95);
  ic.setColumnWidth(5, 85);
  ic.setColumnWidth(6, 95);
  ic.setColumnWidth(7, 120);
  ic.setColumnWidth(8, 120);
  ic.setColumnWidth(9, 140);
  ic.setColumnWidth(10, 150);
  ic.setColumnWidth(11, 120);
  ic.setColumnWidth(12, 140);
  ic.setColumnWidth(13, 320);
  ic.setColumnWidth(14, 160);
  ic.setColumnWidth(15, 340);

  // Meeting summary cards
  createInvestmentCommitteeSummaryCards_(ic);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 109B — SCORE EXPLANATION UI UPGRADE
// PURPOSE:
// Makes Score Explanation sheet easier to interpret visually.
// =====================================================

function improveScoreExplanationUi() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName("Score Explanation");

  if (!sheet) {
    if (typeof createScoreExplanationPanel === "function") {
      createScoreExplanationPanel();
    }
  }

  const sc = ss.getSheetByName("Score Explanation");
  if (!sc) return;

  const lastRow = Math.max(sc.getLastRow(), 4);
  const lastCol = Math.max(sc.getLastColumn(), 11);

  sc.setHiddenGridlines(true);
  sc.setFrozenRows(3);

  sc.getDataRange()
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setFontSize(10)
    .setVerticalAlignment("top")
    .setWrap(true);

  // Title
  sc.getRange(1, 1, 1, Math.min(lastCol, 11))
    .merge()
    .setValue("Stocks Overseer Advisor — Score Explanation Panel")
    .setBackground("#111827")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(16)
    .setHorizontalAlignment("left");

  sc.getRange(2, 1, 1, Math.min(lastCol, 11))
    .merge()
    .setValue("This sheet explains why each ticker receives its score using valuation, earnings yield, beta risk, 52W position, momentum and recommendation logic.")
    .setBackground("#f3f6fa")
    .setFontColor("#374151")
    .setFontStyle("italic");

  sc.setRowHeight(1, 38);
  sc.setRowHeight(2, 34);

  // Header
  sc.getRange(3, 1, 1, lastCol)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center")
    .setVerticalAlignment("middle");

  sc.setRowHeight(3, 46);

  // Borders
  sc.getRange(3, 1, Math.max(lastRow - 2, 1), lastCol)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true, "#d9d9d9", SpreadsheetApp.BorderStyle.SOLID);

  // Row banding
  for (let r = 4; r <= lastRow; r++) {
    const bg = r % 2 === 0 ? "#ffffff" : "#f8fafc";
    sc.getRange(r, 1, 1, Math.min(lastCol, 11)).setBackground(bg);
  }

  // Number formats
  if (lastRow >= 4) {
    sc.getRange(4, 3, lastRow - 3, 4).setNumberFormat("#,##0.00");
    sc.getRange(4, 5, lastRow - 3, 1).setNumberFormat("0.00%");
    sc.getRange(4, 8, lastRow - 3, 1).setNumberFormat("0.00%");
  }

  // Conditional formatting reset only for this sheet.
  sc.setConditionalFormatRules([]);
  const rules = [];

  const scoreRange = sc.getRange(4, 3, Math.max(lastRow - 3, 1), 1);
  const peRange = sc.getRange(4, 4, Math.max(lastRow - 3, 1), 1);
  const yieldRange = sc.getRange(4, 5, Math.max(lastRow - 3, 1), 1);
  const betaRange = sc.getRange(4, 6, Math.max(lastRow - 3, 1), 1);
  const riskRange = sc.getRange(4, 7, Math.max(lastRow - 3, 1), 1);
  const positionRange = sc.getRange(4, 8, Math.max(lastRow - 3, 1), 1);
  const momentumRange = sc.getRange(4, 9, Math.max(lastRow - 3, 1), 1);
  const recommendationRange = sc.getRange(4, 10, Math.max(lastRow - 3, 1), 1);
  const explanationRange = sc.getRange(4, 11, Math.max(lastRow - 3, 1), 1);

  // Score heatmap
  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .setGradientMinpointWithValue("#f4cccc", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "0")
      .setGradientMidpointWithValue("#fff2cc", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "60")
      .setGradientMaxpointWithValue("#d9ead3", SpreadsheetApp.InterpolationType.NUMBER, "100")
      .setRanges([scoreRange])
      .build()
  );

  // PE rule
  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenNumberLessThanOrEqualTo(15)
      .setBackground("#d9ead3")
      .setFontColor("#274e13")
      .setRanges([peRange])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenNumberGreaterThan(30)
      .setBackground("#f4cccc")
      .setFontColor("#990000")
      .setRanges([peRange])
      .build()
  );

  // Earnings yield rule
  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenNumberGreaterThanOrEqualTo(0.08)
      .setBackground("#d9ead3")
      .setFontColor("#274e13")
      .setRanges([yieldRange])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenNumberLessThan(0.04)
      .setBackground("#fff2cc")
      .setFontColor("#7f6000")
      .setRanges([yieldRange])
      .build()
  );

  // Beta risk colours
  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenNumberLessThanOrEqualTo(0.8)
      .setBackground("#d9ead3")
      .setFontColor("#274e13")
      .setRanges([betaRange])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenNumberGreaterThanOrEqualTo(1.5)
      .setBackground("#f4cccc")
      .setFontColor("#990000")
      .setRanges([betaRange])
      .build()
  );

  // 52W position: low can be value zone; high can be momentum/entry risk
  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenNumberLessThanOrEqualTo(0.25)
      .setBackground("#cfe2f3")
      .setFontColor("#073763")
      .setRanges([positionRange])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenNumberGreaterThanOrEqualTo(0.80)
      .setBackground("#fff2cc")
      .setFontColor("#7f6000")
      .setRanges([positionRange])
      .build()
  );

  // Badge styling
  addIcTextRule_(rules, riskRange, "LOW RISK", "#d9ead3", "#274e13");
  addIcTextRule_(rules, riskRange, "MODERATE RISK", "#fff2cc", "#7f6000");
  addIcTextRule_(rules, riskRange, "HIGH RISK", "#fce5cd", "#783f04");
  addIcTextRule_(rules, riskRange, "VERY HIGH RISK", "#cc0000", "#ffffff");
  addIcTextRule_(rules, momentumRange, "STRONG MOMENTUM", "#38761d", "#ffffff");
  addIcTextRule_(rules, momentumRange, "POSITIVE TREND", "#6aa84f", "#ffffff");
  addIcTextRule_(rules, momentumRange, "NEUTRAL", "#d9d9d9", "#000000");
  addIcTextRule_(rules, momentumRange, "WEAK", "#fce5cd", "#783f04");
  addIcTextRule_(rules, recommendationRange, "BUY CANDIDATE", "#38761d", "#ffffff");
  addIcTextRule_(rules, recommendationRange, "ACCUMULATE / STUDY", "#6aa84f", "#ffffff");
  addIcTextRule_(rules, recommendationRange, "VALUE WATCH", "#3c78d8", "#ffffff");
  addIcTextRule_(rules, recommendationRange, "HOLD / MONITOR", "#f1c232", "#000000");
  addIcTextRule_(rules, recommendationRange, "AVOID / HIGH RISK", "#cc0000", "#ffffff");

  // Explanation text highlights
  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextContains("High PE")
      .setBackground("#fff2cc")
      .setFontColor("#7f6000")
      .setRanges([explanationRange])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextContains("High beta")
      .setBackground("#fce5cd")
      .setFontColor("#783f04")
      .setRanges([explanationRange])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextContains("Overall score is strong")
      .setBackground("#d9ead3")
      .setFontColor("#274e13")
      .setRanges([explanationRange])
      .build()
  );

  sc.setConditionalFormatRules(rules);

  // Column widths
  sc.setColumnWidth(1, 120);
  sc.setColumnWidth(2, 230);
  sc.setColumnWidth(3, 90);
  sc.setColumnWidth(4, 80);
  sc.setColumnWidth(5, 120);
  sc.setColumnWidth(6, 80);
  sc.setColumnWidth(7, 140);
  sc.setColumnWidth(8, 120);
  sc.setColumnWidth(9, 150);
  sc.setColumnWidth(10, 170);
  sc.setColumnWidth(11, 560);

  // Summary panel
  createScoreExplanationSummaryCards_(sc);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 109C — TEXT RULE HELPER
// PURPOSE:
// Adds conditional formatting text rule.
// =====================================================

function addIcTextRule_(rules, range, text, bg, font) {

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo(text)
      .setBackground(bg)
      .setFontColor(font)
      .setBold(true)
      .setRanges([range])
      .build()
  );
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 109D — INVESTMENT COMMITTEE SUMMARY CARDS
// PURPOSE:
// Adds small meeting summary cards to the right side.
// =====================================================

function createInvestmentCommitteeSummaryCards_(ic) {

  const lastRow = Math.max(ic.getLastRow(), 5);

  const startRow = 4;
  const startCol = 17; // Q

  const table = [
    ["IC Summary", ""],
    ["Buy Candidates", `=COUNTIF(A5:A,"BUY CANDIDATE")`],
    ["Accumulate / Study", `=COUNTIF(A5:A,"ACCUMULATE / STUDY")`],
    ["Value Watch", `=COUNTIF(A5:A,"VALUE WATCH")`],
    ["Hold / Monitor", `=COUNTIF(A5:A,"HOLD / MONITOR")`],
    ["Avoid / High Risk", `=COUNTIF(A5:A,"AVOID / HIGH RISK")`],
    ["Approved Buy", `=COUNTIF(N5:N,"APPROVE BUY")`],
    ["Deferred", `=COUNTIF(N5:N,"DEFER")`]
  ];

  ic.getRange(startRow, startCol, table.length, 2)
    .clearContent()
    .setValues(table);

  ic.getRange(startRow, startCol, 1, 2)
    .setBackground("#111827")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  ic.getRange(startRow + 1, startCol, table.length - 1, 1)
    .setBackground("#f3f6fa")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  ic.getRange(startRow, startCol, table.length, 2)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  ic.setColumnWidth(startCol, 180);
  ic.setColumnWidth(startCol + 1, 120);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 109E — SCORE EXPLANATION SUMMARY CARDS
// PURPOSE:
// Adds score distribution cards to the right side.
// =====================================================

function createScoreExplanationSummaryCards_(sc) {

  const startRow = 3;
  const startCol = 13; // M

  const table = [
    ["Score Summary", ""],
    ["Strong ≥ 80", `=COUNTIF(C4:C,">=80")`],
    ["Moderate 60–79", `=COUNTIFS(C4:C,">=60",C4:C,"<80")`],
    ["Weak < 60", `=COUNTIFS(C4:C,">0",C4:C,"<60")`],
    ["No Score", `=COUNTBLANK(C4:C)`],
    ["Buy Candidates", `=COUNTIF(J4:J,"BUY CANDIDATE")`],
    ["High Risk", `=COUNTIF(G4:G,"HIGH RISK")`],
    ["Very High Risk", `=COUNTIF(G4:G,"VERY HIGH RISK")`]
  ];

  sc.getRange(startRow, startCol, table.length, 2)
    .clearContent()
    .setValues(table);

  sc.getRange(startRow, startCol, 1, 2)
    .setBackground("#111827")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  sc.getRange(startRow + 1, startCol, table.length - 1, 1)
    .setBackground("#f3f6fa")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  sc.getRange(startRow, startCol, table.length, 2)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  sc.setColumnWidth(startCol, 170);
  sc.setColumnWidth(startCol + 1, 120);
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 110 — CONTROL PANEL COLOUR + UI EFFECTS
// PURPOSE:
// Upgrades the Control Panel sheet into a visual command centre.
// Adds:
// - colour-coded workflow categories
// - quick action cards
// - function badges
// - speed/risk indicators
// - visual legend
// - better layout and spacing
// =====================================================

function improveControlPanelUiEffects() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

  let control = ss.getSheetByName("Control Panel");

  if (!control) {
    if (typeof createDashboardControlPanel === "function") {
      createDashboardControlPanel();
    }
  }

  control = ss.getSheetByName("Control Panel");
  if (!control) return;

  control.clear();
  control.setHiddenGridlines(true);

  // =====================================================
  // TITLE
  // =====================================================

  control.getRange("A1:F1")
    .merge()
    .setValue("Stocks Overseer Advisor — Control Panel")
    .setBackground("#111827")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(18)
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  control.getRange("A2:F2")
    .merge()
    .setValue("Use this sheet as the main command centre. Select the right function depending on whether you want a fast refresh, full rebuild, repair, calculator, visuals, or report output.")
    .setBackground("#f3f6fa")
    .setFontColor("#374151")
    .setFontStyle("italic")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  // =====================================================
  // QUICK ACTION CARDS
  // =====================================================

  const cards = [
    ["FAST DAILY", "runFastDailyRefresh", "Normal daily use", "#d9ead3", "#274e13"],
    ["FULL REBUILD", "runFullOverseerUpdate", "Major changes only", "#fff2cc", "#7f6000"],
    ["REPAIR / AUDIT", "runRepairAndAudit", "Fix warnings", "#fce5cd", "#783f04"],
    ["CALCULATOR", "runCalculatorOnlyRefresh", "Scenario testing", "#d9eaf7", "#073763"],
    ["VISUAL ONLY", "runVisualOnlyRefresh", "Refresh UI sheets", "#d9e2f3", "#1c4587"],
    ["MASTER POLISH", "runMasterUiPolishCleanup", "Final cleanup", "#eadcf8", "#351c75"]
  ];

  let col = 1;

  cards.forEach(card => {

    control.getRange(4, col, 1, 1)
      .setValue(card[0])
      .setBackground("#1f2933")
      .setFontColor("#ffffff")
      .setFontWeight("bold")
      .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

    control.getRange(5, col, 1, 1)
      .setValue(card[1])
      .setBackground(card[3])
      .setFontColor(card[4])
      .setFontWeight("bold")
      .setHorizontalAlignment("center")
      .setWrap(true);

    control.getRange(6, col, 1, 1)
      .setValue(card[2])
      .setBackground(card[3])
      .setFontColor(card[4])
      .setHorizontalAlignment("center")
      .setWrap(true);

    control.getRange(4, col, 3, 1)
      .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true, "#d9d9d9", SpreadsheetApp.BorderStyle.SOLID);

    col++;
  });

  // =====================================================
  // MAIN FUNCTION TABLE
  // =====================================================

  const rows = [
    ["Category", "Workflow Step", "Function to Run", "Purpose", "Speed", "When to Use"],
    ["DAILY", "Fast Daily Refresh", "runFastDailyRefresh", "Refresh normal daily dashboard outputs", "FAST", "Use most of the time"],
    ["SETUP", "One-Time Setup", "runOneTimeWorkbookSetup", "Initial workbook setup, guide, protection, visuals", "MEDIUM", "After first script paste"],
    ["FULL", "Full System Rebuild", "runFullOverseerUpdate", "Rebuild formulas, dashboard, logs, visuals, reports", "SLOW", "After major changes"],
    ["MODE", "Execution Mode Selector", "runExecutionModeSelector", "Prompt user to choose FAST/FULL/DATA/VISUAL/REPAIR/CALCULATOR/HISTORY", "FAST", "When unsure which mode to use"],
    ["DATA", "Data Only Refresh", "runDataOnlyRefresh", "Refresh Input metrics, status, logs only", "FAST", "When only tickers/data changed"],
    ["VISUAL", "Visual Only Refresh", "runVisualOnlyRefresh", "Rebuild Dashboard, Management View, charts and visuals", "MEDIUM", "When UI/graphics look outdated"],
    ["REPAIR", "Repair and Audit", "runRepairAndAudit", "Refresh data quality, alerts, logs and health checks", "FAST", "When errors/missing data appear"],
    ["CALCULATOR", "Calculator Refresh", "runCalculatorOnlyRefresh", "Refresh Calculator sheet and scenario visuals", "FAST", "When testing buy/target/dividend scenarios"],
    ["HISTORY", "History Refresh", "runHistoryOnlyRefresh", "Refresh History and History Summary", "SLOW", "When historical price data is needed"],
    ["ALERT", "Alert Centre", "createAlertCentreSheet", "Create red flag control room", "FAST", "Review high-risk/missing data"],
    ["REPORT", "Management View", "refreshManagementView", "Refresh board-level one-page report", "FAST", "For management review"],
    ["REPORT", "Executive Charts", "refreshExecutiveCharts", "Refresh chart-only management view", "MEDIUM", "For presentations"],
    ["IC", "Investment Committee", "createInvestmentCommitteeView", "Create committee decision review sheet", "FAST", "For Buy/Hold/Avoid meeting"],
    ["SCORE", "Score Explanation", "createScoreExplanationPanel", "Explain score drivers by ticker", "FAST", "When reviewing why a stock scored well/poorly"],
    ["UI", "Calculator Auto-Fill", "refreshCalculatorAutoFillEnhancement", "Auto-fill calculator panels after ticker selection", "FAST", "When calculator fields are blank"],
    ["UI", "Fix Calculator Auto-Fill", "refreshCalculatorTickerSelectionAutoFillPatch", "Patch main ticker selection auto-fill fields", "FAST", "When Company/Price/PE/EPS are blank"],
    ["UI", "Fix Dashboard Sidebar Colours", "refreshDashboardSidebarColourFix", "Fix colour clash from Dashboard N:Z", "FAST", "When sidebar colours clash"],
    ["UI", "Committee + Score UI", "refreshCommitteeAndScoreUiUpgrade", "Improve Investment Committee and Score Explanation UI", "FAST", "After refreshing those sheets"],
    ["DIAG", "Optimisation Diagnostics", "createOptimisationDiagnosticsPackage", "Create header, chart and conditional formatting diagnostics", "FAST", "When workbook feels slow"],
    ["CLEAN", "Chart Cleanup", "cleanupChartsBeforeRebuild", "Remove duplicate charts before rebuild", "FAST", "When charts duplicate"],
    ["CLEAN", "Reset Conditional Formatting", "resetWorkbookConditionalFormatting", "Clear formatting rules on main sheets", "FAST", "When rules accumulate or formatting breaks"],
    ["POLISH", "Master UI Polish", "runMasterUiPolishCleanup", "Sheet order, tab colours, health check and theme consistency", "MEDIUM", "Final cleanup after updates"]
  ];

  const startRow = 9;
  control.getRange(startRow, 1, rows.length, rows[0].length)
    .setValues(rows);

  formatControlPanelMainTable_(control, startRow, rows.length, rows[0].length);

  // =====================================================
  // VISUAL LEGEND
  // =====================================================

  const legendStart = startRow + rows.length + 3;

  const legend = [
    ["Control Panel Legend", ""],
    ["Green", "Fast / normal daily workflow"],
    ["Yellow", "Full rebuild / use carefully"],
    ["Orange", "Repair / warning / audit"],
    ["Blue", "Calculator / visual refresh"],
    ["Purple", "Polish / final cleanup"],
    ["Red", "Reset / destructive cleanup action"]
  ];

  control.getRange(legendStart, 1, legend.length, 2)
    .setValues(legend);

  control.getRange(legendStart, 1, 1, 2)
    .setBackground("#111827")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  control.getRange(legendStart + 1, 1).setBackground("#d9ead3").setFontColor("#274e13");
  control.getRange(legendStart + 2, 1).setBackground("#fff2cc").setFontColor("#7f6000");
  control.getRange(legendStart + 3, 1).setBackground("#fce5cd").setFontColor("#783f04");
  control.getRange(legendStart + 4, 1).setBackground("#d9eaf7").setFontColor("#073763");
  control.getRange(legendStart + 5, 1).setBackground("#eadcf8").setFontColor("#351c75");
  control.getRange(legendStart + 6, 1).setBackground("#f4cccc").setFontColor("#990000");

  control.getRange(legendStart, 1, legend.length, 2)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  // =====================================================
  // QUICK NOTES
  // =====================================================

  const notes = [
    ["Recommended Use", ""],
    ["Daily", "Use runFastDailyRefresh"],
    ["After adding many modules", "Use runFullOverseerUpdate, then runMasterUiPolishCleanup"],
    ["If workbook is slow", "Run createOptimisationDiagnosticsPackage"],
    ["If charts duplicate", "Run cleanupChartsBeforeRebuild"],
    ["If dashboard N:Z clashes", "Run refreshDashboardSidebarColourFix"],
    ["If calculator auto-fill is blank", "Run refreshCalculatorTickerSelectionAutoFillPatch"]
  ];

  control.getRange(legendStart, 4, notes.length, 2)
    .setValues(notes);

  control.getRange(legendStart, 4, 1, 2)
    .setBackground("#111827")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  control.getRange(legendStart + 1, 4, notes.length - 1, 1)
    .setBackground("#f3f6fa")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  control.getRange(legendStart, 4, notes.length, 2)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  // =====================================================
  // FINAL LAYOUT
  // =====================================================

  control.getDataRange()
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setFontSize(10)
    .setVerticalAlignment("middle")
    .setWrap(true);

  control.setFrozenRows(8);

  control.setColumnWidth(1, 120);
  control.setColumnWidth(2, 220);
  control.setColumnWidth(3, 290);
  control.setColumnWidth(4, 420);
  control.setColumnWidth(5, 110);
  control.setColumnWidth(6, 280);

  control.setRowHeight(1, 42);
  control.setRowHeight(2, 32);
  control.setRowHeights(4, 3, 42);

  control.getRange("A8:F8")
    .merge()
    .setValue("Function Command Table")
    .setBackground("#d9e2f3")
    .setFontColor("#1f2933")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(12);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 110A — FORMAT CONTROL PANEL MAIN TABLE
// PURPOSE:
// Applies category colours, speed badges and borders.
// =====================================================

function formatControlPanelMainTable_(sheet, startRow, numRows, numCols) {

  sheet.getRange(startRow, 1, 1, numCols)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  sheet.getRange(startRow, 1, numRows, numCols)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true, "#d9d9d9", SpreadsheetApp.BorderStyle.SOLID);

  for (let r = startRow + 1; r < startRow + numRows; r++) {
    const category = sheet.getRange(r, 1).getValue();
    const colour = getControlPanelCategoryColour_(category);

    sheet.getRange(r, 1)
      .setBackground(colour.bg)
      .setFontColor(colour.font)
      .setFontWeight("bold")
      .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

    const rowBg = r % 2 === 0 ? "#ffffff" : "#f8fafc";
    sheet.getRange(r, 2, 1, numCols - 1).setBackground(rowBg);
  }

  const rules = [];

  const speedRange = sheet.getRange(startRow + 1, 5, numRows - 1, 1);
  const categoryRange = sheet.getRange(startRow + 1, 1, numRows - 1, 1);

  addControlPanelTextRule_(rules, speedRange, "FAST", "#d9ead3", "#274e13");
  addControlPanelTextRule_(rules, speedRange, "MEDIUM", "#fff2cc", "#7f6000");
  addControlPanelTextRule_(rules, speedRange, "SLOW", "#f4cccc", "#990000");

  addControlPanelTextRule_(rules, categoryRange, "DAILY", "#38761d", "#ffffff");
  addControlPanelTextRule_(rules, categoryRange, "FULL", "#bf9000", "#ffffff");
  addControlPanelTextRule_(rules, categoryRange, "REPAIR", "#e69138", "#ffffff");
  addControlPanelTextRule_(rules, categoryRange, "CALCULATOR", "#3c78d8", "#ffffff");
  addControlPanelTextRule_(rules, categoryRange, "HISTORY", "#674ea7", "#ffffff");
  addControlPanelTextRule_(rules, categoryRange, "CLEAN", "#cc0000", "#ffffff");
  addControlPanelTextRule_(rules, categoryRange, "POLISH", "#351c75", "#ffffff");

  sheet.setConditionalFormatRules(rules);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 110B — CONTROL PANEL CATEGORY COLOUR HELPER
// =====================================================

function getControlPanelCategoryColour_(category) {

  const map = {
    "DAILY": { bg: "#d9ead3", font: "#274e13" },
    "SETUP": { bg: "#d9e2f3", font: "#1c4587" },
    "FULL": { bg: "#fff2cc", font: "#7f6000" },
    "MODE": { bg: "#d9eaf7", font: "#073763" },
    "DATA": { bg: "#d9ead3", font: "#274e13" },
    "VISUAL": { bg: "#d9e2f3", font: "#1c4587" },
    "REPAIR": { bg: "#fce5cd", font: "#783f04" },
    "CALCULATOR": { bg: "#d9eaf7", font: "#073763" },
    "HISTORY": { bg: "#eadcf8", font: "#351c75" },
    "ALERT": { bg: "#f4cccc", font: "#990000" },
    "REPORT": { bg: "#fff2cc", font: "#7f6000" },
    "IC": { bg: "#fff2cc", font: "#7f6000" },
    "SCORE": { bg: "#d9e2f3", font: "#1c4587" },
    "UI": { bg: "#d9eaf7", font: "#073763" },
    "DIAG": { bg: "#eadcf8", font: "#351c75" },
    "CLEAN": { bg: "#f4cccc", font: "#990000" },
    "POLISH": { bg: "#eadcf8", font: "#351c75" }
  };

  return map[category] || { bg: "#f3f6fa", font: "#111827" };
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 110C — CONTROL PANEL TEXT RULE HELPER
// =====================================================

function addControlPanelTextRule_(rules, range, text, bg, font) {

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo(text)
      .setBackground(bg)
      .setFontColor(font)
      .setBold(true)
      .setRanges([range])
      .build()
  );
}

// MODULE 110D — CONTROL PANEL UI WRAPPER
// =====================================================

// =====================================================
// MODULE 111 — BRANDING PRESETS VALUE UI EFFECTS
// PURPOSE:
// Improves the Branding Presets sheet, especially the Value column.
// Adds:
// - editable value highlight
// - colour swatches for hex colour values
// - theme badges
// - section styling
// - notes formatting
// - validation for Preferred Theme
// - visual preview panel
// =====================================================

function improveBrandingPresetsValueUiEffects() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

  let branding = ss.getSheetByName("Branding Presets");

  if (!branding) {
    if (typeof createThemeBrandingPresetSheet === "function") {
      createThemeBrandingPresetSheet();
    }
  }

  branding = ss.getSheetByName("Branding Presets");
  if (!branding) return;

  const lastRow = Math.max(branding.getLastRow(), 13);
  const lastCol = Math.max(branding.getLastColumn(), 3);

  branding.setHiddenGridlines(true);
  branding.setFrozenRows(1);

  branding.getDataRange()
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setFontSize(10)
    .setVerticalAlignment("middle")
    .setWrap(true);

  // =====================================================
  // MAIN HEADER
  // =====================================================

  branding.getRange(1, 1, 1, 3)
    .setBackground("#111827")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(12)
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  branding.setRowHeight(1, 36);

  // =====================================================
  // VALUE COLUMN EFFECTS
  // Column B is the editable value column.
  // =====================================================

  branding.getRange(2, 2, lastRow - 1, 1)
    .setBackground("#d9eaf7")
    .setFontColor("#111827")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true, "#0b5394", SpreadsheetApp.BorderStyle.SOLID)
    .setNote("Editable branding value. Update this cell to control dashboard/report branding.");

  // Field names
  branding.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 1)
    .setBackground("#f3f6fa")
    .setFontColor("#1f2933")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  // Notes
  branding.getRange(2, 3, lastRow - 1, 1)
    .setBackground("#ffffff")
    .setFontColor("#374151");

  branding.getRange(1, 1, lastRow, 3)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true, "#d9d9d9", SpreadsheetApp.BorderStyle.SOLID);

  // =====================================================
  // PREFERRED THEME VALIDATION + BADGE
  // =====================================================

  const themeRow = findBrandingPresetRow_(branding, "Preferred Theme");

  if (themeRow > 0) {
    const themeRule = SpreadsheetApp.newDataValidation()
      .requireValueInList(["Dark Finance", "Blue Corporate", "Gold Executive"], true)
      .setAllowInvalid(false)
      .setHelpText("Choose one: Dark Finance, Blue Corporate, or Gold Executive.")
      .build();

    branding.getRange(themeRow, 2)
      .setDataValidation(themeRule)
      .setNote("Dropdown: choose the workbook theme.");
  }

  // =====================================================
  // COLOUR SWATCHES FOR HEX VALUES
  // =====================================================

  addBrandingColourSwatches_(branding);

  // =====================================================
  // CONDITIONAL FORMATTING FOR VALUE COLUMN
  // =====================================================

  branding.setConditionalFormatRules([]);
  const rules = [];

  const valueRange = branding.getRange(2, 2, lastRow - 1, 1);

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextContains("Dark Finance")
      .setBackground("#111827")
      .setFontColor("#ffffff")
      .setBold(true)
      .setRanges([valueRange])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextContains("Blue Corporate")
      .setBackground("#0b5394")
      .setFontColor("#ffffff")
      .setBold(true)
      .setRanges([valueRange])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextContains("Gold Executive")
      .setBackground("#fff2cc")
      .setFontColor("#7f6000")
      .setBold(true)
      .setRanges([valueRange])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextStartsWith("#")
      .setFontColor("#000000")
      .setBold(true)
      .setRanges([valueRange])
      .build()
  );

  branding.setConditionalFormatRules(rules);

  // =====================================================
  // VISUAL PREVIEW PANEL
  // =====================================================

  createBrandingPreviewPanel_(branding);

  // =====================================================
  // FINAL LAYOUT
  // =====================================================

  branding.setColumnWidth(1, 240);
  branding.setColumnWidth(2, 320);
  branding.setColumnWidth(3, 520);
  branding.setColumnWidth(5, 160);
  branding.setColumnWidth(6, 260);

  branding.getRange("A1:C1").setHorizontalAlignment("center");
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 111A — FIND BRANDING PRESET ROW
// PURPOSE:
// Finds a preset name in column A.
// =====================================================

function findBrandingPresetRow_(sheet, presetName) {

  const values = sheet.getRange(1, 1, sheet.getLastRow(), 1).getValues();

  for (let i = 0; i < values.length; i++) {
    if (String(values[i][0]).trim() === presetName) {
      return i + 1;
    }
  }

  return 0;
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 111B — ADD COLOUR SWATCHES
// PURPOSE:
// Creates a visual swatch beside hex colour values.
// Uses columns E:F so the user can see the colour directly.
// =====================================================

function addBrandingColourSwatches_(branding) {

  const lastRow = Math.max(branding.getLastRow(), 13);

  branding.getRange("E1:F1")
    .merge()
    .setValue("Colour Preview")
    .setBackground("#111827")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  const colourFields = [
    "Primary Colour",
    "Secondary Colour",
    "Accent Colour",
    "Positive Colour",
    "Warning Colour",
    "Negative Colour"
  ];

  let previewRow = 2;

  colourFields.forEach(field => {

    const row = findBrandingPresetRow_(branding, field);
    if (row <= 0) return;

    const hex = branding.getRange(row, 2).getValue();

    branding.getRange(previewRow, 5)
      .setValue(field)
      .setBackground("#f3f6fa")
      .setFontWeight("bold");

    branding.getRange(previewRow, 6)
      .setValue(hex)
      .setFontWeight("bold")
      .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

    if (isValidHexColour_(hex)) {
      branding.getRange(previewRow, 6)
        .setBackground(hex)
        .setFontColor(getReadableFontForHex_(hex));
    } else {
      branding.getRange(previewRow, 6)
        .setBackground("#ffffff")
        .setFontColor("#990000")
        .setValue("Invalid / blank");
    }

    previewRow++;
  });

  branding.getRange(1, 5, Math.max(previewRow - 1, 1), 2)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 111C — BRANDING PREVIEW PANEL
// PURPOSE:
// Creates a mini preview of title, header, accent and status cards.
// =====================================================

function createBrandingPreviewPanel_(branding) {

  const primary = getBrandingPresetValue_(branding, "Primary Colour", "#111827");
  const secondary = getBrandingPresetValue_(branding, "Secondary Colour", "#1f2933");
  const accent = getBrandingPresetValue_(branding, "Accent Colour", "#d9e2f3");
  const positive = getBrandingPresetValue_(branding, "Positive Colour", "#d9ead3");
  const warning = getBrandingPresetValue_(branding, "Warning Colour", "#fff2cc");
  const negative = getBrandingPresetValue_(branding, "Negative Colour", "#f4cccc");
  const dashboardTitle = getBrandingPresetValue_(branding, "Dashboard Title", "Stocks Overseer Advisor Dashboard");
  const theme = getBrandingPresetValue_(branding, "Preferred Theme", "Dark Finance");

  const startRow = 10;
  const startCol = 5; // E

  branding.getRange(startRow, startCol, 12, 2).clearContent();

  branding.getRange(startRow, startCol, 1, 2)
    .merge()
    .setValue("Brand Preview")
    .setBackground(primary)
    .setFontColor(getReadableFontForHex_(primary))
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  branding.getRange(startRow + 1, startCol, 1, 2)
    .merge()
    .setValue(dashboardTitle)
    .setBackground(secondary)
    .setFontColor(getReadableFontForHex_(secondary))
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  branding.getRange(startRow + 2, startCol, 1, 2)
    .merge()
    .setValue("Theme: " + theme)
    .setBackground(accent)
    .setFontColor(getReadableFontForHex_(accent))
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  const cards = [
    ["Positive", positive],
    ["Warning", warning],
    ["Negative", negative]
  ];

  let row = startRow + 4;

  cards.forEach(card => {
    branding.getRange(row, startCol)
      .setValue(card[0])
      .setBackground("#f3f6fa")
      .setFontWeight("bold");

    branding.getRange(row, startCol + 1)
      .setValue(card[1])
      .setBackground(card[1])
      .setFontColor(getReadableFontForHex_(card[1]))
      .setFontWeight("bold")
      .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

    row++;
  });

  branding.getRange(startRow, startCol, 8, 2)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 111D — GET BRANDING PRESET VALUE
// PURPOSE:
// Reads value from Branding Presets by field name.
// =====================================================

function getBrandingPresetValue_(branding, field, fallback) {

  const row = findBrandingPresetRow_(branding, field);

  if (row <= 0) return fallback;

  const value = branding.getRange(row, 2).getValue();

  return value || fallback;
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 111E — HEX COLOUR VALIDATION
// PURPOSE:
// Checks whether a value looks like #RRGGBB.
// =====================================================

function isValidHexColour_(hex) {

  if (!hex) return false;

  return /^#[0-9A-Fa-f]{6}$/.test(String(hex).trim());
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 111F — READABLE FONT COLOUR FOR HEX
// PURPOSE:
// Chooses black/white text depending on background brightness.
// =====================================================

function getReadableFontForHex_(hex) {

  if (!isValidHexColour_(hex)) return "#111827";

  hex = String(hex).replace("#", "");

  const r = parseInt(hex.substring(0, 2), 16);
  const g = parseInt(hex.substring(2, 4), 16);
  const b = parseInt(hex.substring(4, 6), 16);

  const brightness = (r * 299 + g * 587 + b * 114) / 1000;

  return brightness > 150 ? "#111827" : "#ffffff";
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 111G — BRANDING UI EFFECTS WRAPPER
// PURPOSE:
// Refreshes Branding Presets UI effects.
// =====================================================

function refreshBrandingPresetsUiEffects() {
  improveBrandingPresetsValueUiEffects();
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 112 — STAGED FULL REBUILD RUNNER
// PURPOSE:
// Reduces Google Apps Script timeout risk by splitting the
// heavy full workbook rebuild into smaller stage functions.
// Instead of always running runFullOverseerUpdate(), users can run:
// - runStage1DataRefresh
// - runStage2DashboardRefresh
// - runStage3DecisionSheetsRefresh
// - runStage4ChartsReportsRefresh
// - runStage5UiPolishDiagnostics
//
// Also includes:
// - runStagedRebuildMenuPrompt
// - createStagedRebuildControlSheet
// - staged rebuild status logging
// =====================================================

function runStagedRebuildMenuPrompt() {

  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();

  const response = ui.prompt(
    "Staged Full Rebuild",
    "Type stage number: 1, 2, 3, 4, 5, or ALL",
    ui.ButtonSet.OK_CANCEL
  );

  if (response.getSelectedButton() !== ui.Button.OK) return;

  const mode = String(response.getResponseText()).trim().toUpperCase();

  if (mode === "1") {
    runStage1DataRefresh();
  } else if (mode === "2") {
    runStage2DashboardRefresh();
  } else if (mode === "3") {
    runStage3DecisionSheetsRefresh();
  } else if (mode === "4") {
    runStage4ChartsReportsRefresh();
  } else if (mode === "5") {
    runStage5UiPolishDiagnostics();
  } else if (mode === "ALL") {
    runAllStagedRebuildSequential();
  } else {
    ui.alert("Unknown stage. Type 1, 2, 3, 4, 5, or ALL.");
  }
}

// MODULE 112E — STAGE 5: UI POLISH + DIAGNOSTICS

// =====================================================


// Duplicate earlier definition of runStage5UiPolishDiagnostics removed by v60 cleanup.



// =====================================================
// MODULE 112F — RUN ALL STAGES SEQUENTIALLY
// PURPOSE:
// Runs all stages in sequence.
// WARNING:
// This can still time out for large ticker lists. Prefer running
// each stage separately for safer execution.
// =====================================================

function runAllStagedRebuildSequential() {

  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();

  const response = ui.alert(
    "Run All Optimised Stages?",
    "This may still exceed Apps Script execution time for large ticker lists. Safer option: run Stage 1 to Stage 5 separately. Continue?",
    ui.ButtonSet.YES_NO
  );

  if (response !== ui.Button.YES) return;

  const totalStart = new Date();

  // Use args-aware runner directly. This avoids older wrappers and ensures
  // all stage arguments are honoured.
  for (let i = 1; i <= 5; i++) {
    runOptimisedStageWithArgs_(i);
  }

  const elapsed = new Date() - totalStart;
  logOptimisedRuntime_("ALL STAGED REBUILD TOTAL", "OK", "All stages completed", elapsed);

  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert("All optimised stages completed. Review Optimised Runtime Log.");
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 112G — STAGED REBUILD CONTROL SHEET
// PURPOSE:
// Creates a visual control sheet for staged execution.
// =====================================================

function createStagedRebuildControlSheet() {
  createOptimisedStagedRebuildControlSheet();
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 112H — STAGED REBUILD STATUS LOG
// PURPOSE:
// Logs staged rebuild status in a dedicated sheet.
// =====================================================

function logStagedRebuildStatus_(stage, status, notes) {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

  let log = ss.getSheetByName("Staged Rebuild Log");

  if (!log) {
    log = ss.insertSheet("Staged Rebuild Log");
    log.getRange(1, 1, 1, 5)
      .setValues([["Timestamp", "Stage", "Status", "Notes", "User"]])
      .setBackground("#1f2933")
      .setFontColor("#ffffff")
      .setFontWeight("bold");
    log.setFrozenRows(1);
  }

  const user = Session.getActiveUser().getEmail() || "";

  log.appendRow([
    new Date(),
    stage,
    status,
    notes,
    user
  ]);

  const lastRow = log.getLastRow();

  log.getRange(lastRow, 1)
    .setNumberFormat("dd/mm/yyyy hh:mm:ss");

  log.getDataRange()
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setFontSize(10)
    .setVerticalAlignment("middle");

  log.autoResizeColumns(1, 5);
}

// =====================================================

function refreshStagedRebuildSupport() {
  createStagedRebuildControlSheet();
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 113 — CALCULATOR + ONBOARDING AUDIT CHECK
// PURPOSE:
// Creates a diagnostic sheet to verify that Calculator and
// Onboarding Wizard are correctly wired after updates.
// Checks:
// - Calculator exists
// - Ticker dropdown exists at B5
// - Key auto-fill cells have formulas
// - Calculator canonical output rows are correct
// - Onboarding Wizard exists and references staged/optimised runners
// =====================================================

function createCalculatorOnboardingAuditSheet() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

  let audit = ss.getSheetByName("Calculator Onboarding Audit");
  if (!audit) audit = ss.insertSheet("Calculator Onboarding Audit");

  audit.clear();
  audit.setHiddenGridlines(true);

  const calc = ss.getSheetByName("Calculator");
  const wizard = ss.getSheetByName("Onboarding Wizard");

  const rows = [["Check Area", "Item", "Status", "Details"]];

  if (!calc) {
    rows.push(["Calculator", "Sheet exists", "MISSING", "Run refreshGainDividendCalculatorWithGuide"]);
  } else {
    rows.push(["Calculator", "Sheet exists", "OK", "Calculator found"]);

    rows.push([
      "Calculator",
      "Ticker dropdown B5",
      calc.getRange("B5").getDataValidation() ? "OK" : "REVIEW",
      calc.getRange("B5").getDataValidation() ? "Dropdown exists" : "No data validation found"
    ]);

    const requiredFormulaCells = {
      "B6 Company": "B6",
      "B7 Currency": "B7",
      "B8 Current Price": "B8",
      "B9 PE Ratio": "B9",
      "B10 EPS": "B10",
      "B11 Score": "B11",
      "B12 Recommendation": "B12",
      "B13 Dividend Yield": "B13",
      "B14 Dividend Per Share": "B14",
      "B57 Total Invested": "B57",
      "B58 Capital Gain": "B58",
      "B59 Dividend Income": "B59",
      "B60 Total Return Amount": "B60",
      "B61 Total Return %": "B61",
      "B62 Break-even Price": "B62",
      "B63 Decision Note": "B63"
    };

    Object.keys(requiredFormulaCells).forEach(label => {
      const cell = requiredFormulaCells[label];
      const formula = calc.getRange(cell).getFormula();
      rows.push([
        "Calculator",
        label,
        formula ? "OK" : "REVIEW",
        formula || "No formula found"
      ]);
    });
  }

  if (!wizard) {
    rows.push(["Onboarding", "Sheet exists", "MISSING", "Run refreshOptimisedOnboardingWizard"]);
  } else {
    rows.push(["Onboarding", "Sheet exists", "OK", "Onboarding Wizard found"]);

    const wizardText = wizard.getDataRange().getDisplayValues().flat().join(" | ");

    const requiredTerms = [
      "runFastDailyRefresh",
      "runFullOverseerUpdate",
      "runExecutionModeSelector",
      "runStage1DataRefresh",
      "runStage2DashboardRefresh",
      "runStage3DecisionSheetsRefresh",
      "runStage4ChartsReportsRefresh",
      "runStage5UiPolishDiagnostics"
    ];

    requiredTerms.forEach(term => {
      rows.push([
        "Onboarding",
        term,
        wizardText.includes(term) ? "OK" : "REVIEW",
        wizardText.includes(term) ? "Referenced" : "Missing from onboarding guide"
      ]);
    });
  }

  audit.getRange(1, 1, rows.length, rows[0].length)
    .setValues(rows);

  audit.getRange(1, 1, 1, rows[0].length)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  audit.getRange(1, 1, rows.length, rows[0].length)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true)
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setWrap(true);

  const rules = [];

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("OK")
      .setBackground("#d9ead3")
      .setFontColor("#274e13")
      .setRanges([audit.getRange(2, 3, Math.max(rows.length - 1, 1), 1)])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("REVIEW")
      .setBackground("#fff2cc")
      .setFontColor("#7f6000")
      .setRanges([audit.getRange(2, 3, Math.max(rows.length - 1, 1), 1)])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("MISSING")
      .setBackground("#f4cccc")
      .setFontColor("#990000")
      .setRanges([audit.getRange(2, 3, Math.max(rows.length - 1, 1), 1)])
      .build()
  );

  audit.setConditionalFormatRules(rules);

  audit.setColumnWidth(1, 160);
  audit.setColumnWidth(2, 260);
  audit.setColumnWidth(3, 110);
  audit.setColumnWidth(4, 560);
  audit.setFrozenRows(1);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 113A — CALCULATOR + ONBOARDING PATCH WRAPPER
// PURPOSE:
// Refreshes Calculator/Onboarding and creates audit sheet.
// =====================================================

function refreshCalculatorOnboardingAuditAndFix() {

  if (typeof refreshGainDividendCalculatorWithGuide === "function") refreshGainDividendCalculatorWithGuide();
  if (typeof refreshCalculatorUiGraphics === "function") refreshCalculatorUiGraphics();
  if (typeof refreshCalculatorAutoFillEnhancement === "function") refreshCalculatorAutoFillEnhancement();
  if (typeof refreshCalculatorTickerSelectionAutoFillPatch === "function") refreshCalculatorTickerSelectionAutoFillPatch();
  if (typeof refreshCalculatorUserInputYellowHighlight === "function") refreshCalculatorUserInputYellowHighlight();

  if (typeof refreshOptimisedOnboardingWizard === "function") refreshOptimisedOnboardingWizard();
  else if (typeof createOnboardingWizardSheet === "function") createOnboardingWizardSheet();

  createCalculatorOnboardingAuditSheet();
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 114 — CALCULATOR USER INPUT YELLOW HIGHLIGHT
// PURPOSE:
// Makes all true Calculator user-input cells yellow.
// This separates manual assumptions from auto-filled fields.
// Yellow = user input
// Grey/white = auto-filled or calculated output
// Applies to:
// - selected ticker dropdown
// - buy price
// - desired buy price
// - target sell price
// - shares bought
// - desired increase %
// - dividend yield %
// - dividend per share
// - holding period years
// =====================================================

function applyCalculatorUserInputYellowHighlight() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const calc = ss.getSheetByName("Calculator");

  if (!calc) {
    throw new Error("Calculator sheet not found.");
  }

  const userInputCells = [
    "B5",  // Selected Ticker
    "E5",  // Buy Price
    "E6",  // Desired Buy Price
    "E7",  // Target Sell Price
    "E8",  // Shares Bought
    "E9",  // Desired Increase %
    "E10", // Dividend Yield %
    "E11", // Dividend Per Share
    "E12"  // Holding Period Years
  ];

  // Reset the main user input zones to yellow.
  userInputCells.forEach(cell => {
    calc.getRange(cell)
      .setBackground("#fff2cc")
      .setFontColor("#7f6000")
      .setFontWeight("bold")
      .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true, "#bf9000", SpreadsheetApp.BorderStyle.SOLID_MEDIUM)
      .setNote("USER INPUT: edit this yellow cell.");
  });

  // Label cells beside inputs
  calc.getRange("A5:A14")
    .setBackground("#f3f6fa")
    .setFontColor("#1f2933")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  calc.getRange("D5:D12")
    .setBackground("#f3f6fa")
    .setFontColor("#1f2933")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  // Auto-filled ticker details remain grey/white.
  calc.getRange("B6:B14")
    .setBackground("#f7f7f7")
    .setFontColor("#111827")
    .setFontWeight("normal")
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true, "#d9d9d9", SpreadsheetApp.BorderStyle.SOLID);

  // Re-apply ticker dropdown yellow after B6:B14 reset.
  calc.getRange("B5")
    .setBackground("#fff2cc")
    .setFontColor("#7f6000")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true, "#bf9000", SpreadsheetApp.BorderStyle.SOLID_MEDIUM);

  // Output sections remain soft grey/yellow for readability but not manual-input yellow.
  calc.getRange("B17:B24").setBackground("#f3f6fa").setFontColor("#111827");
  calc.getRange("B28:B35").setBackground("#f3f6fa").setFontColor("#111827");
  calc.getRange("B39:B49").setBackground("#f3f6fa").setFontColor("#111827");
  calc.getRange("B54:B63").setBackground("#f7f7f7").setFontColor("#111827");

  // Total Return Summary key outputs
  calc.getRange("B57:B63")
    .setBackground("#eaf4e4")
    .setFontColor("#274e13")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  // Quick Result panel values remain output cards, not user input.
  calc.getRange("E17:E24")
    .setBackground("#d9ead3")
    .setFontColor("#274e13")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  // Yellow input legend panel
  createCalculatorUserInputYellowLegend_();

  // Improve row/column readability
  calc.setColumnWidth(1, 260);
  calc.setColumnWidth(2, 180);
  calc.setColumnWidth(4, 260);
  calc.setColumnWidth(5, 190);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 114A — CALCULATOR YELLOW INPUT LEGEND
// PURPOSE:
// Adds a clear legend explaining yellow cells.
// =====================================================

function createCalculatorUserInputYellowLegend_() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const calc = ss.getSheetByName("Calculator");

  if (!calc) return;

  const legend = [
    ["Calculator Input Legend", ""],
    ["Yellow cells", "User input / assumptions"],
    ["Grey cells", "Auto-filled from other sheets"],
    ["Green cells", "Calculated result / output"],
    ["Important", "Only edit yellow cells unless intentionally overriding formulas"]
  ];

  calc.getRange(4, 7, legend.length, 2)
    .clearContent()
    .setValues(legend);

  calc.getRange(4, 7, 1, 2)
    .setBackground("#111827")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  calc.getRange(5, 7, 1, 1)
    .setBackground("#fff2cc")
    .setFontColor("#7f6000")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  calc.getRange(6, 7, 1, 1)
    .setBackground("#f7f7f7")
    .setFontColor("#111827")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  calc.getRange(7, 7, 1, 1)
    .setBackground("#d9ead3")
    .setFontColor("#274e13")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  calc.getRange(8, 7, 1, 1)
    .setBackground("#f4cccc")
    .setFontColor("#990000")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  calc.getRange(4, 7, legend.length, 2)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true)
    .setWrap(true);

  calc.setColumnWidth(7, 220);
  calc.setColumnWidth(8, 300);
}

// MODULE 114B — CALCULATOR YELLOW INPUT WRAPPER
// PURPOSE:
// Menu/full-run wrapper.
// =====================================================

function refreshCalculatorUserInputYellowHighlight() {
  applyCalculatorUserInputYellowHighlight();
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 115 — WHOLE SCRIPT OPTIMISATION FRAMEWORK
// PURPOSE:
// Adds a central optimisation layer for the full workbook.
// This improves how major functions are executed:
// - safeCall wrapper
// - runtime stage logger
// - skip-if-missing logic
// - optimised master runner
// - optimised visual runner
// - optimised calculator runner
// - runtime diagnostics sheet
// =====================================================

function safeRun_(functionName, label, options) {

  options = options || {};

  const start = new Date();
  const stage = label || functionName;

  try {

    if (typeof globalThis[functionName] !== "function") {
      logOptimisedRuntime_(stage, "SKIPPED", "Function not found: " + functionName, 0);
      return false;
    }

    globalThis[functionName]();

    const elapsed = new Date() - start;
    logOptimisedRuntime_(stage, "OK", "Completed", elapsed);

    return true;

  } catch (err) {

    const elapsed = new Date() - start;
    logOptimisedRuntime_(stage, "ERROR", err.message, elapsed);

    if (options.throwOnError) {
      throw err;
    }

    return false;
  }
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 115A — OPTIMISED RUNTIME LOG
// PURPOSE:
// Logs execution time and status for optimisation review.
// =====================================================

function logOptimisedRuntime_(stage, status, message, elapsedMs) {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

  let log = ss.getSheetByName("Optimised Runtime Log");

  if (!log) {
    log = ss.insertSheet("Optimised Runtime Log");
    log.getRange(1, 1, 1, 5)
      .setValues([["Timestamp", "Stage / Function", "Status", "Elapsed Seconds", "Message"]])
      .setBackground("#1f2933")
      .setFontColor("#ffffff")
      .setFontWeight("bold");
    log.setFrozenRows(1);
  }

  log.appendRow([
    new Date(),
    stage,
    status,
    elapsedMs ? elapsedMs / 1000 : 0,
    message
  ]);

  const lastRow = log.getLastRow();

  log.getRange(lastRow, 1).setNumberFormat("dd/mm/yyyy hh:mm:ss");
  log.getRange(lastRow, 4).setNumberFormat("0.00");

  if (status === "ERROR") {
    log.getRange(lastRow, 1, 1, 5).setBackground("#f4cccc").setFontColor("#990000");
  } else if (status === "SKIPPED") {
    log.getRange(lastRow, 1, 1, 5).setBackground("#fff2cc").setFontColor("#7f6000");
  } else {
    log.getRange(lastRow, 1, 1, 5).setBackground("#ffffff").setFontColor("#111827");
  }

  log.autoResizeColumns(1, 5);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 115B — OPTIMISED FULL REBUILD SAFE RUNNER
// PURPOSE:
// Safer replacement for running every module blindly.
// Uses stages and safeRun_ so one optional failure does not
// stop the whole workbook update.
// =====================================================

function runOptimisedFullRebuildSafe() {

  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();

  const response = ui.alert(
    "Optimised Full Rebuild",
    "This will run the workbook in safer grouped stages with runtime logging. For large ticker lists, Stage 1–5 separate runs are still safer. Continue?",
    ui.ButtonSet.YES_NO
  );

  if (response !== ui.Button.YES) return;

  const totalStart = new Date();

  safeRun_("resetWorkbookConditionalFormattingQuiet", "Pre-clean conditional formatting");
  safeRun_("cleanupChartsBeforeRebuild", "Pre-clean charts");

  // Stage 1 — Data
  safeRun_("addCleanGoogleFinanceColumns", "Data: clean GoogleFinance columns");
  safeRun_("ensureExpandedGoogleFinanceHeaders", "Data: ensure expanded headers");
  safeRun_("recalculateCleanGoogleFinanceMetrics", "Data: recalculate clean metrics");
  safeRun_("runTickerDataQualityCheckOptimised", "Data: optimised ticker quality check");
  safeRun_("runTickerFormatSuggestionEngine", "Data: ticker format suggestions");
  safeRun_("calculateImportedFundamentalRatios", "Data: imported fundamental ratios");
  safeRun_("updateErrorLogSheet", "Data: error log");
  safeRun_("updateSystemLog", "Data: system log");

  // Stage 2 — Dashboard
  safeRun_("createCleanDashboard", "Dashboard: base dashboard");
  safeRun_("createDashboardKpiScorecards", "Dashboard: KPI scorecards");
  safeRun_("refreshExecutiveSummaryBanner", "Dashboard: executive banner");
  safeRun_("createDashboardTop10DecisionView", "Dashboard: Top 10 decision view");
  safeRun_("refreshTop10MiniCharts", "Dashboard: Top 10 mini charts");
  safeRun_("createDashboardRiskHeatmap", "Dashboard: risk heatmap");
  safeRun_("createUnsupportedTickerDashboard", "Dashboard: unsupported tickers");
  safeRun_("createTickerSuggestionDashboard", "Dashboard: ticker suggestions");
  safeRun_("refreshDashboardSidebarColourFix", "Dashboard: sidebar colour fix");

  // Stage 3 — Decisions and Calculator
  safeRun_("createAlertCentreSheet", "Decision: alert centre");
  safeRun_("refreshManagementView", "Decision: management view");
  safeRun_("createInvestmentCommitteeView", "Decision: investment committee");
  safeRun_("createScoreExplanationPanel", "Decision: score explanation");
  safeRun_("refreshCommitteeAndScoreUiUpgrade", "Decision: committee and score UI");
  safeRun_("refreshGainDividendCalculatorWithGuide", "Calculator: base calculator");
  safeRun_("refreshCalculatorUiGraphics", "Calculator: UI graphics");
  safeRun_("refreshCalculatorAutoFillEnhancement", "Calculator: auto-fill enhancement");
  safeRun_("refreshCalculatorTickerSelectionAutoFillPatch", "Calculator: ticker auto-fill patch");
  safeRun_("refreshCalculatorUserInputYellowHighlight", "Calculator: yellow user inputs");
  safeRun_("createCalculatorSensitivityTable", "Calculator: sensitivity table");
  safeRun_("createCalculatorScenarioCards", "Calculator: scenario cards");
  safeRun_("createCalculatorMiniSensitivityHeatmap", "Calculator: heatmap");
  safeRun_("createCalculatorBreakEvenVisual", "Calculator: break-even visual");
  safeRun_("refreshCalculatorScenarioComparisonChart", "Calculator: scenario comparison chart");

  // Stage 4 — Reports and charts
  safeRun_("refreshExecutiveCharts", "Reports: executive charts");
  safeRun_("createWatchlistPipelineFunnelSheet", "Reports: watchlist funnel");
  safeRun_("createExecutivePrintSummarySheet", "Reports: executive summary");
  safeRun_("createPrintCoverSheet", "Reports: print cover");

  // Stage 5 — UI and diagnostics
  safeRun_("createThemeBrandingPresetSheet", "UI: branding presets");
  safeRun_("refreshBrandingPresetsUiEffects", "UI: branding effects");
  safeRun_("createDashboardControlPanel", "UI: control panel");
  safeRun_("refreshControlPanelUiEffects", "UI: control panel effects");
  safeRun_("createWorkbookHomePage", "UI: home page");
  safeRun_("refreshOptimisedOnboardingWizard", "UI: onboarding wizard");
  safeRun_("createStagedRebuildControlSheet", "UI: staged rebuild control");
  safeRun_("createCalculatorOnboardingAuditSheet", "Audit: calculator/onboarding audit");
  safeRun_("createOptimisationDiagnosticsPackage", "Audit: optimisation diagnostics");
  safeRun_("createWorkbookHealthCheckSheet_", "Audit: workbook health check");
  safeRun_("runMasterUiPolishCleanupQuiet", "UI: master polish");

  const totalElapsed = new Date() - totalStart;
  logOptimisedRuntime_("OPTIMISED FULL REBUILD TOTAL", "OK", "Total runtime", totalElapsed);

  ui.alert("Optimised full rebuild completed. Review 'Optimised Runtime Log' for slow/error modules.");
}

// =====================================================
// MODULE 115F — FUNCTION INVENTORY SHEET
// PURPOSE:
// Lists important functions and recommended usage.
// =====================================================

function createOptimisedFunctionInventorySheet() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

  let sheet = ss.getSheetByName("Function Inventory");
  if (!sheet) sheet = ss.insertSheet("Function Inventory");

  sheet.clear();
  sheet.setHiddenGridlines(true);

  const rows = [
    ["Category", "Function", "Recommended Use"],
    ["Optimised Runner", "runOptimisedDailySafe", "Best normal daily use"],
    ["Optimised Runner", "runOptimisedFullRebuildSafe", "Safer full rebuild with runtime logging"],
    ["Optimised Runner", "runOptimisedVisualSafe", "Refresh visuals only"],
    ["Optimised Runner", "runOptimisedCalculatorSafe", "Refresh calculator only"],
    ["Staged Runner", "runStage1DataRefresh", "Stage 1: data"],
    ["Staged Runner", "runStage2DashboardRefresh", "Stage 2: dashboard"],
    ["Staged Runner", "runStage3DecisionSheetsRefresh", "Stage 3: decisions/calculator"],
    ["Staged Runner", "runStage4ChartsReportsRefresh", "Stage 4: charts/reports"],
    ["Staged Runner", "runStage5UiPolishDiagnostics", "Stage 5: polish/diagnostics"],
    ["Diagnostics", "createOptimisationDiagnosticsPackage", "Header/chart/format diagnostics"],
    ["Diagnostics", "createCalculatorOnboardingAuditSheet", "Check Calculator and Onboarding"],
    ["Cleanup", "cleanupChartsBeforeRebuild", "Remove duplicate charts"],
    ["Cleanup", "resetWorkbookConditionalFormatting", "Clear excessive formatting rules"]
  ];

  sheet.getRange(1, 1, rows.length, rows[0].length).setValues(rows);

  sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 3)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  sheet.getRange(1, 1, rows.length, 3)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true)
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setWrap(true);

  sheet.setColumnWidth(1, 180);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(2, 300);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(3, 520);
  sheet.setFrozenRows(1);
}

// =====================================================
// MODULE 117 — OPTIMISED WORKFLOW ALIGNMENT PATCH
// PURPOSE:
// Aligns optimisation, staged rebuild, onboarding, and control
// panel workflows into one recommended operating system.
// Adds:
// - optimised stage runner using safeRun_
// - timeout-safe stage status panel
// - better stage control sheet
// - updated onboarding wizard
// - updated control panel command centre
// - runtime health summary
// =====================================================

function runOptimisedStage_(stageNumber) {
  // v63 patch: route all stage execution through args-aware runner.
  // This ensures functions such as cleanupChartsOnSheet_(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME)
  // receive their required arguments.
  runOptimisedStageWithArgs_(stageNumber);
}

}

  runOptimisedStage_(5);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 117C — SAFE RUN WITH ARGUMENT SUPPORT
// PURPOSE:
// Some stage items need arguments, such as cleanupChartsOnSheet_.
// This wrapper keeps existing safeRun_ behaviour but supports args.
// =====================================================

function safeRunWithArgs_(functionName, label, args, options) {

  options = options || {};
  args = args || [];

  const start = new Date();
  const stage = label || functionName;

  try {

    if (typeof globalThis[functionName] !== "function") {
      logOptimisedRuntime_(stage, "SKIPPED", "Function not found: " + functionName, 0);
      return false;
    }

    globalThis[functionName].apply(null, args);

    const elapsed = new Date() - start;
    logOptimisedRuntime_(stage, "OK", "Completed", elapsed);

    return true;

  } catch (err) {

    const elapsed = new Date() - start;
    logOptimisedRuntime_(stage, "ERROR", err.message, elapsed);

    if (options.throwOnError) throw err;

    return false;
  }
}


// Patch runOptimisedStage_ to use args-aware safe runner.
function runOptimisedStageWithArgs_(stageNumber) {

  const stages = getOptimisedStageDefinitions_();
  const stage = stages[String(stageNumber)];

  if (!stage) {
    SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert("Unknown stage: " + stageNumber);
    return;
  }

  const totalStart = new Date();

  logOptimisedRuntime_("STAGE " + stageNumber + " START", "OK", stage.title, 0);
  logStagedRebuildStatus_("Stage " + stageNumber, "Started", stage.title);

  stage.steps.forEach(step => {
    safeRunWithArgs_(step.fn, "Stage " + stageNumber + ": " + step.label, step.args || []);
  });

  const elapsed = new Date() - totalStart;

  logOptimisedRuntime_("STAGE " + stageNumber + " TOTAL", "OK", stage.title, elapsed);
  logStagedRebuildStatus_("Stage " + stageNumber, "Completed", stage.title + " | " + (elapsed / 1000).toFixed(2) + " sec");

  createOptimisedStagedRebuildControlSheet();

  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert("Stage " + stageNumber + " completed: " + stage.title);
}


// Final stage runner override uses args-aware runner.
function runStage1DataRefreshOptimised() { runOptimisedStageWithArgs_(1); }
function runStage2DashboardRefreshOptimised() { runOptimisedStageWithArgs_(2); }
function runStage3DecisionSheetsRefreshOptimised() { runOptimisedStageWithArgs_(3); }
function runStage4ChartsReportsRefreshOptimised() { runOptimisedStageWithArgs_(4); }
function runStage5UiPolishDiagnosticsOptimised() { runOptimisedStageWithArgs_(5); }

function getStageFunctionSuffix_(key) {
  const map = {
    "1": "DataRefreshOptimised",
    "2": "DashboardRefreshOptimised",
    "3": "DecisionSheetsRefreshOptimised",
    "4": "ChartsReportsRefreshOptimised",
    "5": "UiPolishDiagnosticsOptimised"
  };

  return map[String(key)] || "";
}


function getStageRecommendation_(key) {
  const map = {
    "1": "Run first; low timeout risk",
    "2": "Run after Stage 1; medium timeout risk",
    "3": "Run after Stage 2; calculator and decision sheets",
    "4": "Run separately; chart-heavy and slower",
    "5": "Run last; UI polish and diagnostics"
  };

  return map[String(key)] || "";
}

    ["STAGE", "runStage1DataRefreshOptimised", "Data refresh", "LOW", "First stage", "Input/calculations/logs"],
    ["STAGE", "runStage2DashboardRefreshOptimised", "Dashboard refresh", "MEDIUM", "After Stage 1", "Dashboard visuals"],
    ["STAGE", "runStage3DecisionSheetsRefreshOptimised", "Decision sheets + Calculator", "MEDIUM", "After Stage 2", "IC/Score/Calculator"],
    ["STAGE", "runStage4ChartsReportsRefreshOptimised", "Charts + reports", "HIGH", "Run separately", "Chart-heavy"],
    ["STAGE", "runStage5UiPolishDiagnosticsOptimised", "UI polish + diagnostics", "LOW", "Final stage", "Home/Control/health"],
    ["AUDIT", "createCalculatorOnboardingAuditSheet", "Check calculator and onboarding", "LOW", "After script updates", "Formula/check sheet"],
    ["AUDIT", "refreshWholeScriptOptimisationSupport", "Optimisation support sheets", "LOW", "When reviewing script", "Inventory + diagnostics"],
    ["CLEANUP", "cleanupChartsBeforeRebuild", "Remove duplicate charts", "LOW", "If charts duplicate", "Use before visual refresh"],

// =====================================================
// MODULE 118 — SAFE RUNTIME TIMER HELPERS
// PURPOSE:
// Some legacy and staged functions call startRuntimeTimer_()
// and endRuntimeTimer_(). This module defines safe helpers so
// those calls never fail. Timings are written to Optimised Runtime Log.
// =====================================================

function startRuntimeTimer_(label) {

  const props = PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties();
  const key = "RUNTIME_TIMER_" + String(label || "DEFAULT");

  props.setProperty(key, String(new Date().getTime()));

  logOptimisedRuntime_("TIMER START: " + label, "OK", "Timer started", 0);
}


function endRuntimeTimer_(label) {

  const props = PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties();
  const key = "RUNTIME_TIMER_" + String(label || "DEFAULT");
  const startValue = props.getProperty(key);

  let elapsed = 0;

  if (startValue) {
    elapsed = new Date().getTime() - Number(startValue);
  }

  logOptimisedRuntime_("TIMER END: " + label, "OK", "Timer ended", elapsed);

  return elapsed;
}

function styleHomeTable_(sheet, startRow, startCol, numRows, numCols, headerColour) {

  sheet.getRange(startRow, startCol, 1, numCols)
    .setBackground(headerColour)
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")

    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  sheet.getRange(startRow + 1, startCol, Math.max(numRows - 1, 1), 1)
    .setBackground("#f3f6fa")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  sheet.getRange(startRow, startCol, numRows, numCols)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true)
    .setVerticalAlignment("middle")
    .setWrap(true);
}

// =====================================================
// MODULE 120 — STAGED REBUILD MODULE AUDIT
// PURPOSE:
// Creates a diagnostic sheet checking the staged rebuild module.
// Verifies:
// - core staged functions exist
// - stage definitions reference existing functions
// - menu items are wired
// - recommended stage order is visible
// =====================================================

function createStagedRebuildAuditSheet() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

  let audit = ss.getSheetByName("Staged Rebuild Audit");
  if (!audit) audit = ss.insertSheet("Staged Rebuild Audit");

  audit.clear();
  audit.setHiddenGridlines(true);

  const rows = [["Audit Area", "Item", "Status", "Notes"]];

  const requiredFunctions = [
    "runStagedRebuildMenuPrompt",
    "runAllStagedRebuildSequential",
    "runOptimisedStage_",
    "runOptimisedStageWithArgs_",
    "getOptimisedStageDefinitions_",
    "runStage1DataRefresh",
    "runStage2DashboardRefresh",
    "runStage3DecisionSheetsRefresh",
    "runStage4ChartsReportsRefresh",
    "runStage5UiPolishDiagnostics",
    "runStage1DataRefreshOptimised",
    "runStage2DashboardRefreshOptimised",
    "runStage3DecisionSheetsRefreshOptimised",
    "runStage4ChartsReportsRefreshOptimised",
    "runStage5UiPolishDiagnosticsOptimised",
    "createOptimisedStagedRebuildControlSheet",
    "logStagedRebuildStatus_"
  ];

  requiredFunctions.forEach(fn => {
    rows.push([
      "Function",
      fn,
      typeof globalThis[fn] === "function" ? "OK" : "MISSING",
      typeof globalThis[fn] === "function" ? "Function found" : "Function missing"
    ]);
  });

  const stages = getOptimisedStageDefinitions_();

  Object.keys(stages).forEach(stageKey => {
    const stage = stages[stageKey];

    rows.push([
      "Stage Definition",
      "Stage " + stageKey + " — " + stage.title,
      "OK",
      stage.steps.length + " steps | Risk: " + stage.risk
    ]);

    stage.steps.forEach(step => {
      rows.push([
        "Stage Step",
        "Stage " + stageKey + ": " + step.fn,
        typeof globalThis[step.fn] === "function" ? "OK" : "MISSING",
        step.label + (step.args ? " | Args: " + JSON.stringify(step.args) : "")
      ]);
    });
  });

  audit.getRange(1, 1, rows.length, rows[0].length)
    .setValues(rows);

  audit.getRange(1, 1, 1, rows[0].length)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  audit.getRange(1, 1, rows.length, rows[0].length)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true)
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setFontSize(10)
    .setWrap(true);

  const statusRange = audit.getRange(2, 3, Math.max(rows.length - 1, 1), 1);

  const rules = [];

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("OK")
      .setBackground("#d9ead3")
      .setFontColor("#274e13")
      .setRanges([statusRange])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("MISSING")
      .setBackground("#f4cccc")
      .setFontColor("#990000")
      .setRanges([statusRange])
      .build()
  );

  audit.setConditionalFormatRules(rules);

  audit.setColumnWidth(1, 160);
  audit.setColumnWidth(2, 340);
  audit.setColumnWidth(3, 110);
  audit.setColumnWidth(4, 520);
  audit.setFrozenRows(1);
}
