  createOptimisedStagedRebuildControlSheet();
  createStagedRebuildAuditSheet();
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 121 — DASHBOARD ALERT CENTRE UI UPGRADE
// PURPOSE:
// Improves the Alert Centre panel inside the Dashboard sheet.
// Adds:
// - clear critical / high / medium alert cards
// - direct link to Alert Centre sheet
// - alert health status
// - top alert summary
// - cleaner sidebar placement in N:Z
// - colour-coded action guidance
// =====================================================

function createDashboardAlertCentreUiPanel() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);
  const alert = ss.getSheetByName("Alert Centre");

  if (!dash) {
    throw new Error("Dashboard sheet not found.");
  }

  // If Alert Centre does not exist, try to create it first.
  if (!alert && typeof createAlertCentreSheet === "function") {
    createAlertCentreSheet();
  }

  const alertSheet = ss.getSheetByName("Alert Centre");

  const startRow = 154;
  const startCol = 14; // Column N
  const panelRows = 20;
  const panelCols = 5; // N:R

  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, panelRows, panelCols)
    .clearContent()
    .setBackground("#ffffff")
    .setFontColor("#111827")
    .setBorder(false, false, false, false, false, false);

  // Title
  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, 1, panelCols)
    .merge()
    .setValue("Alert Centre — Dashboard Control")
    .setBackground("#111827")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(12)
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  if (!alertSheet) {
    dash.getRange(startRow + 2, startCol, 3, panelCols)
      .merge()
      .setValue("Alert Centre sheet not found. Run createAlertCentreSheet.")
      .setBackground("#f4cccc")
      .setFontColor("#990000")
      .setFontWeight("bold")
      .setHorizontalAlignment("center")
      .setVerticalAlignment("middle")
      .setWrap(true);

    return;
  }

  const data = alertSheet.getDataRange().getValues();

  let critical = 0;
  let high = 0;
  let medium = 0;
  let total = 0;
  let firstAlertType = "No alert";
  let firstTicker = "";
  let firstAction = "No immediate action required.";

  for (let r = 4; r < data.length; r++) {
    const severity = data[r][0];
    const alertType = data[r][1];
    const ticker = data[r][2];
    const action = data[r][11];

    if (!severity) continue;

    total++;

    if (severity === "CRITICAL") critical++;
    else if (severity === "HIGH") high++;
    else if (severity === "MEDIUM") medium++;

    if (firstAlertType === "No alert") {
      firstAlertType = alertType || "Alert";
      firstTicker = ticker || "";
      firstAction = action || "Review Alert Centre.";
    }
  }

  const healthStatus = critical > 0
    ? "CRITICAL REVIEW REQUIRED"
    : high > 0
      ? "HIGH RISK ITEMS FOUND"
      : medium > 0
        ? "MEDIUM WARNINGS FOUND"
        : "NO MAJOR ALERTS";

  const healthBg = critical > 0
    ? "#cc0000"
    : high > 0
      ? "#f4cccc"
      : medium > 0
        ? "#fff2cc"
        : "#d9ead3";

  const healthFont = critical > 0
    ? "#ffffff"
    : high > 0
      ? "#990000"
      : medium > 0
        ? "#7f6000"
        : "#274e13";

  // Summary health bar
  dash.getRange(startRow + 1, startCol, 1, panelCols)
    .merge()
    .setValue(healthStatus)
    .setBackground(healthBg)
    .setFontColor(healthFont)
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  // Alert count cards
  const cards = [
    ["Critical", critical, "#cc0000", "#ffffff"],
    ["High", high, "#f4cccc", "#990000"],
    ["Medium", medium, "#fff2cc", "#7f6000"],
    ["Total", total, "#d9e2f3", "#1c4587"]
  ];

  for (let i = 0; i < cards.length; i++) {
    const col = startCol + i;

    dash.getRange(startRow + 3, col)
      .setValue(cards[i][0])
      .setBackground("#1f2933")
      .setFontColor("#ffffff")
      .setFontWeight("bold")
      .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

    dash.getRange(startRow + 4, col)
      .setValue(cards[i][1])
      .setBackground(cards[i][2])
      .setFontColor(cards[i][3])
      .setFontWeight("bold")
      .setFontSize(14)
      .setHorizontalAlignment("center");
  }

  // Link card
  const alertGid = alertSheet.getSheetId();

  dash.getRange(startRow + 3, startCol + 4)
    .setValue("Open")
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  dash.getRange(startRow + 4, startCol + 4)
    .setFormula(`=HYPERLINK("#gid=${alertGid}","Alert Centre")`)
    .setBackground("#d9ead3")
    .setFontColor("#274e13")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  // Main alert detail
  const detail = [
    ["Top Alert", firstAlertType],
    ["Ticker", firstTicker || "-"],
    ["Suggested Action", firstAction]
  ];

  dash.getRange(startRow + 7, startCol, detail.length, 2)
    .setValues(detail);

  dash.getRange(startRow + 7, startCol, detail.length, 1)
    .setBackground("#f3f6fa")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  dash.getRange(startRow + 7, startCol + 1, detail.length, panelCols - 1)
    .mergeAcross()
    .setBackground("#ffffff")
    .setWrap(true);

  // Guidance
  const guide = [
    ["How to use", "If Critical > 0, review ticker format / missing price first."],
    ["Daily check", "Run runRepairAndAudit or Stage 1 if alerts look outdated."],
    ["Decision rule", "Do not treat BUY candidates as final until Alert Centre is clean."]
  ];

  dash.getRange(startRow + 12, startCol, guide.length, 2)
    .setValues(guide);

  dash.getRange(startRow + 12, startCol, guide.length, 1)
    .setBackground("#f3f6fa")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  dash.getRange(startRow + 12, startCol + 1, guide.length, panelCols - 1)
    .mergeAcross()
    .setBackground("#fff2cc")
    .setFontColor("#7f6000")
    .setWrap(true);

  // Formatting
  dash.getRange(startRow, startCol, panelRows, panelCols)
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setFontSize(10)
    .setVerticalAlignment("middle")
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true, "#d9d9d9", SpreadsheetApp.BorderStyle.SOLID);

  dash.setColumnWidth(startCol, 120);
  dash.setColumnWidth(startCol + 1, 150);
  dash.setColumnWidth(startCol + 2, 120);
  dash.setColumnWidth(startCol + 3, 120);
  dash.setColumnWidth(startCol + 4, 150);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 121A — DASHBOARD ALERT CENTRE UI VALIDATION
// PURPOSE:
// Creates an audit sheet checking Dashboard ↔ Alert Centre UI.
// =====================================================

function createDashboardAlertCentreUiAuditSheet() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

  let audit = ss.getSheetByName("Dashboard Alert UI Audit");
  if (!audit) audit = ss.insertSheet("Dashboard Alert UI Audit");

  audit.clear();
  audit.setHiddenGridlines(true);

  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);
  const alert = ss.getSheetByName("Alert Centre");

  const rows = [
    ["Check", "Status", "Details"],
    ["Dashboard sheet exists", dash ? "OK" : "MISSING", dash ? DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME : "Dashboard sheet missing"],
    ["Alert Centre sheet exists", alert ? "OK" : "MISSING", alert ? "Alert Centre found" : "Run createAlertCentreSheet"],
    ["Dashboard alert panel function", typeof createDashboardAlertCentreUiPanel === "function" ? "OK" : "MISSING", "createDashboardAlertCentreUiPanel"],
    ["Legacy alert panel function", typeof createDashboardAlertCentrePanel === "function" ? "OK" : "MISSING", "createDashboardAlertCentrePanel"],
    ["Sidebar colour fix", typeof refreshDashboardSidebarColourFix === "function" ? "OK" : "MISSING", "refreshDashboardSidebarColourFix"],
    ["Repair and audit function", typeof runRepairAndAudit === "function" ? "OK" : "MISSING", "runRepairAndAudit"]
  ];

  if (alert) {
    const values = alert.getDataRange().getValues();

    let total = 0;
    let critical = 0;
    let high = 0;
    let medium = 0;

    for (let r = 4; r < values.length; r++) {
      const severity = values[r][0];
      if (!severity) continue;
      total++;
      if (severity === "CRITICAL") critical++;
      else if (severity === "HIGH") high++;
      else if (severity === "MEDIUM") medium++;
    }

    rows.push(["Alert total", "INFO", total]);
    rows.push(["Critical alerts", critical > 0 ? "REVIEW" : "OK", critical]);
    rows.push(["High alerts", high > 0 ? "REVIEW" : "OK", high]);
    rows.push(["Medium alerts", medium > 0 ? "REVIEW" : "OK", medium]);
  }

  audit.getRange(1, 1, rows.length, rows[0].length)
    .setValues(rows);

  audit.getRange(1, 1, 1, rows[0].length)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  audit.getRange(1, 1, rows.length, rows[0].length)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true)
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setWrap(true);

  const statusRange = audit.getRange(2, 2, Math.max(rows.length - 1, 1), 1);
  const rules = [];

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("OK")
      .setBackground("#d9ead3")
      .setFontColor("#274e13")
      .setRanges([statusRange])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("MISSING")
      .setBackground("#f4cccc")
      .setFontColor("#990000")
      .setRanges([statusRange])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("REVIEW")
      .setBackground("#fff2cc")
      .setFontColor("#7f6000")
      .setRanges([statusRange])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("INFO")
      .setBackground("#d9e2f3")
      .setFontColor("#1c4587")
      .setRanges([statusRange])
      .build()
  );

  audit.setConditionalFormatRules(rules);

  audit.setColumnWidth(1, 260);
  audit.setColumnWidth(2, 120);
  audit.setColumnWidth(3, 520);
  audit.setFrozenRows(1);
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 121B — DASHBOARD ALERT CENTRE UI WRAPPER
// PURPOSE:
// Refreshes Alert Centre, Dashboard alert UI and audit.
// =====================================================

function refreshDashboardAlertCentreUi() {

  if (typeof createAlertCentreSheet === "function") {
    createAlertCentreSheet();
  }

  createDashboardAlertCentreUiPanel();

  if (typeof refreshDashboardSidebarColourFix === "function") {
    refreshDashboardSidebarColourFix();
  }

  createDashboardAlertCentreUiAuditSheet();
}

// =====================================================
// MODULE 122B — UPDATED STAGED REBUILD CONTROL
// PURPOSE:
// Adds Alert Centre UI status and updated workflow sequence.
// =====================================================

function createOptimisedStagedRebuildControlSheet() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

  let sheet = ss.getSheetByName("Staged Rebuild Control");
  if (!sheet) sheet = ss.insertSheet("Staged Rebuild Control");

  sheet.clear();
  sheet.setHiddenGridlines(true);

  const matrix = getWorkflowStageMatrix_();

  sheet.getRange("A1:F1")
    .merge()
    .setValue("Stocks Overseer Advisor — Staged Rebuild Control")
    .setBackground("#111827")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(16)
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  sheet.getRange("A2:F2")
    .merge()
    .setValue("Run stages separately for large ticker lists. Stage 2 now includes Dashboard Alert Centre UI. Stage 5 updates Home, Onboarding and Control Panel.")
    .setBackground("#f3f6fa")
    .setFontColor("#374151")
    .setFontStyle("italic")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  sheet.getRange(4, 1, matrix.length, matrix[0].length)
    .setValues(matrix);

  styleWorkflowTable_(sheet, 4, 1, matrix.length, matrix[0].length, "#351c75");

  // Add direct run command cards
  const cards = [
    ["Daily Safe", "runOptimisedDailySafe", "#d9ead3", "#274e13"],
    ["Full Safe", "runOptimisedFullRebuildSafe", "#fff2cc", "#7f6000"],
    ["Stage Prompt", "runStagedRebuildMenuPrompt", "#d9eaf7", "#073763"],
    ["Alert UI", "refreshDashboardAlertCentreUi", "#fce5cd", "#783f04"],
    ["Audit", "refreshStagedRebuildAuditAndControl", "#eadcf8", "#351c75"]
  ];

  for (let i = 0; i < cards.length; i++) {
    const col = i + 1;

    sheet.getRange(12, col)
      .setValue(cards[i][0])
      .setBackground("#1f2933")
      .setFontColor("#ffffff")
      .setFontWeight("bold")
      .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

    sheet.getRange(13, col)
      .setValue(cards[i][1])
      .setBackground(cards[i][2])
      .setFontColor(cards[i][3])
      .setFontWeight("bold")
      .setHorizontalAlignment("center")
      .setWrap(true);

    sheet.getRange(12, col, 2, 1)
      .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);
  }

  const rules = [];

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("LOW")
      .setBackground("#d9ead3")
      .setFontColor("#274e13")
      .setRanges([sheet.getRange(5, 4, matrix.length - 1, 1)])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("MEDIUM")
      .setBackground("#fff2cc")
      .setFontColor("#7f6000")
      .setRanges([sheet.getRange(5, 4, matrix.length - 1, 1)])
      .build()
  );

  rules.push(
    SpreadsheetApp.newConditionalFormatRule()
      .whenTextEqualTo("HIGH")
      .setBackground("#f4cccc")
      .setFontColor("#990000")
      .setRanges([sheet.getRange(5, 4, matrix.length - 1, 1)])
      .build()
  );

  sheet.setConditionalFormatRules(rules);

  sheet.getRange("A16:F16")
    .merge()
    .setValue("Recommended: Daily Safe for normal use. For major rebuilds: Stage 1 → 2 → 3 → 4 → 5. Run Stage 4 separately because charts/reports are slower.")
    .setBackground("#fff2cc")
    .setFontColor("#7f6000")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  sheet.getDataRange()
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setFontSize(10)
    .setVerticalAlignment("middle")
    .setWrap(true);

  sheet.setFrozenRows(4);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(1, 110);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(2, 310);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(3, 470);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(4, 100);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(5, 320);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(6, 120);
  sheet.setTabColor("#351c75");
}

function createOptimisedHomeSheet() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

  let home = ss.getSheetByName("Home");
  if (!home) home = ss.insertSheet("Home", 0);

  home.clear();
  home.setHiddenGridlines(true);

  home.getRange("A1:H1")
    .merge()
    .setValue("Stocks Overseer Advisor — Optimised Home")
    .setBackground("#111827")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(20)
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  home.getRange("A2:H2")
    .merge()
    .setValue("Start here. Daily Safe is for normal use; staged rebuild is for large/full updates; Alert Centre UI shows dashboard risk warnings.")
    .setBackground("#f3f6fa")
    .setFontColor("#374151")
    .setFontStyle("italic")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  const cards = [
    ["DAILY SAFE", "runOptimisedDailySafe", "Normal daily use", "#d9ead3", "#274e13"],
    ["FULL SAFE", "runOptimisedFullRebuildSafe", "Grouped rebuild", "#fff2cc", "#7f6000"],
    ["STAGED", "Stage 1–5", "Lowest timeout risk", "#eadcf8", "#351c75"],
    ["ALERT UI", "refreshDashboardAlertCentreUi", "Dashboard alert panel", "#fce5cd", "#783f04"],
    ["CALCULATOR", "runOptimisedCalculatorSafe", "Scenario analysis", "#d9eaf7", "#073763"],
    ["CONTROL", "refreshControlPanelOptimised", "Command centre", "#f3f6fa", "#1f2933"],
    ["ONBOARDING", "refreshOnboardingOptimised", "User guide", "#d9e2f3", "#1c4587"],
    ["AUDIT", "refreshStagedRebuildAuditAndControl", "Check stages", "#f4cccc", "#990000"]
  ];

  for (let i = 0; i < cards.length; i++) {
    const col = i + 1;

    home.getRange(4, col)
      .setValue(cards[i][0])
      .setBackground("#1f2933")
      .setFontColor("#ffffff")
      .setFontWeight("bold")
      .setHorizontalAlignment("center")
      .setWrap(true);

    home.getRange(5, col)
      .setValue(cards[i][1])
      .setBackground(cards[i][3])
      .setFontColor(cards[i][4])
      .setFontWeight("bold")
      .setHorizontalAlignment("center")
      .setWrap(true);

    home.getRange(6, col)
      .setValue(cards[i][2])
      .setBackground(cards[i][3])
      .setFontColor(cards[i][4])
      .setHorizontalAlignment("center")
      .setWrap(true);

    home.getRange(4, col, 3, 1)
      .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);
  }

  const nav = [
    ["Area", "Open Sheet", "Purpose", "Recommended Function"],
    ["Input", "Input", "Ticker input and automated market data", "runOptimisedDailySafe"],
    ["Dashboard", "Dashboard", "Dashboard, KPI, Top 10, risk heatmap and Alert Centre UI", "runStage2DashboardRefreshOptimised"],
    ["Alert Centre", "Alert Centre", "Red-flag control room", "refreshDashboardAlertCentreUi"],
    ["Management View", "Management View", "Board-level decision view", "refreshManagementView"],
    ["Investment Committee", "Investment Committee", "Buy / Hold / Avoid review sheet", "createInvestmentCommitteeView"],
    ["Score Explanation", "Score Explanation", "Explains score drivers", "createScoreExplanationPanel"],
    ["Calculator", "Calculator", "Gain, dividend and scenario calculator", "runOptimisedCalculatorSafe"],
    ["Executive Charts", "Executive Charts", "Presentation chart sheet", "runStage4ChartsReportsRefreshOptimised"],
    ["Staged Rebuild", "Staged Rebuild Control", "Stage 1–5 rebuild control", "createOptimisedStagedRebuildControlSheet"],
    ["Control Panel", "Control Panel", "Command centre", "refreshControlPanelOptimised"],
    ["Onboarding", "Onboarding Wizard", "Step-by-step guide", "refreshOnboardingOptimised"],
    ["Runtime", "Optimised Runtime Log", "Runtime performance log", "runOptimisedDailySafe"],
    ["Audit", "Staged Rebuild Audit", "Stage function audit", "refreshStagedRebuildAuditAndControl"],
    ["Dashboard Alert Audit", "Dashboard Alert UI Audit", "Dashboard alert panel audit", "createDashboardAlertCentreUiAuditSheet"],
    ["Health", "Workbook Health Check", "Workbook health and missing items", "createWorkbookHealthCheckSheet_"]
  ];

  const navRow = 9;
  home.getRange(navRow, 1, nav.length, nav[0].length)
    .setValues(nav);

  styleWorkflowTable_(home, navRow, 1, nav.length, nav[0].length, "#1f2933");

  for (let r = navRow + 1; r < navRow + nav.length; r++) {
    const sheetName = home.getRange(r, 2).getValue();
    const target = ss.getSheetByName(sheetName);

    if (target) {
      const gid = target.getSheetId();
      home.getRange(r, 2).setFormula(`=HYPERLINK("#gid=${gid}","${sheetName}")`);
    }
  }

  const matrix = getWorkflowStageMatrix_();
  const stageRow = 28;

  home.getRange(stageRow, 1, matrix.length, matrix[0].length)
    .setValues(matrix);

  styleWorkflowTable_(home, stageRow, 1, matrix.length, matrix[0].length, "#351c75");

  const alertGuide = [
    ["Dashboard Alert UI", "Description"],
    ["Critical", "Missing price or severe data warning; fix before decision"],
    ["High", "Avoid / high-risk or very high beta warnings"],
    ["Medium", "Weak score, missing PE/EPS or review-needed item"],
    ["Refresh", "Run refreshDashboardAlertCentreUi or Stage 2"],
    ["Audit", "Use Dashboard Alert UI Audit"]
  ];

  const alertRow = 38;
  home.getRange(alertRow, 1, alertGuide.length, alertGuide[0].length)
    .setValues(alertGuide);

  styleWorkflowTable_(home, alertRow, 1, alertGuide.length, alertGuide[0].length, "#990000");

  home.getRange("A47:H47")
    .merge()
    .setValue("Daily workflow: Input tickers → runOptimisedDailySafe → review Dashboard + Alert Centre UI → use Calculator → review Management View.")
    .setBackground("#fff2cc")
    .setFontColor("#7f6000")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  home.getRange("A49:H49")
    .merge()
    .setValue("Large rebuild workflow: Stage 1 → Stage 2 → Stage 3 → Stage 4 → Stage 5. Run Stage 4 separately due to chart/report runtime.")
    .setBackground("#eadcf8")
    .setFontColor("#351c75")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  home.getDataRange()
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setFontSize(10)
    .setVerticalAlignment("middle")
    .setWrap(true);

  home.setFrozenRows(2);
  home.setRowHeight(1, 44);
  home.setRowHeight(2, 30);
  home.setRowHeights(4, 3, 48);

  home.setColumnWidth(1, 180);
  home.setColumnWidth(2, 230);
  home.setColumnWidth(3, 500);
  home.setColumnWidth(4, 290);
  home.setColumnWidth(5, 120);
  home.setColumnWidth(6, 120);
  home.setColumnWidth(7, 120);
  home.setColumnWidth(8, 120);
  home.setTabColor("#111827");
}

// MODULE 122D — UPDATED ONBOARDING WIZARD
// PURPOSE:
// Updates onboarding with Stage, Home and Alert Centre UI guidance.
// =====================================================

function refreshOnboardingOptimised() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

  let wizard = ss.getSheetByName("Onboarding Wizard");
  if (!wizard) wizard = ss.insertSheet("Onboarding Wizard");

  wizard.clear();
  wizard.setHiddenGridlines(true);

  wizard.getRange("A1:H1")
    .merge()
    .setValue("Stocks Overseer Advisor — Optimised Onboarding Wizard")
    .setBackground("#111827")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setFontSize(18)
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  wizard.getRange("A2:H2")
    .merge()
    .setValue("Use this guide to choose between daily safe refresh, staged rebuild, dashboard alert review and calculator scenario analysis.")
    .setBackground("#f3f6fa")
    .setFontColor("#374151")
    .setFontStyle("italic")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  const quick = [
    ["Use Case", "Best Function", "Why"],
    ["Normal daily use", "runOptimisedDailySafe", "Fast; updates data, dashboard, alerts and management view"],
    ["Dashboard alert review", "refreshDashboardAlertCentreUi", "Refreshes Alert Centre and Dashboard alert cards"],
    ["Large full rebuild", "Run Stage 1–5 separately", "Lowest timeout risk"],
    ["Calculator only", "runOptimisedCalculatorSafe", "Refreshes calculator in correct order with yellow input cells"],
    ["Reports/charts only", "runStage4ChartsReportsRefreshOptimised", "Chart-heavy; run separately"],
    ["Final polish", "runStage5UiPolishDiagnosticsOptimised", "Updates Home, Onboarding, Control Panel, branding and diagnostics"]
  ];

  wizard.getRange(4, 1, quick.length, quick[0].length)
    .setValues(quick);

  styleWorkflowTable_(wizard, 4, 1, quick.length, quick[0].length, "#1f2933");

  const matrix = getWorkflowStageMatrix_();

  wizard.getRange(13, 1, matrix.length, matrix[0].length)
    .setValues(matrix);

  styleWorkflowTable_(wizard, 13, 1, matrix.length, matrix[0].length, "#351c75");

  const alertSteps = [
    ["Dashboard Alert Centre UI", "Instruction"],
    ["Where", "Dashboard sidebar, around columns N:R"],
    ["What it shows", "Critical, High, Medium and Total alert cards"],
    ["Green state", "No major alerts"],
    ["Yellow / Red state", "Review Alert Centre before buying"],
    ["Refresh function", "refreshDashboardAlertCentreUi"],
    ["Audit sheet", "Dashboard Alert UI Audit"]
  ];

  wizard.getRange(23, 1, alertSteps.length, alertSteps[0].length)
    .setValues(alertSteps);

  styleWorkflowTable_(wizard, 23, 1, alertSteps.length, alertSteps[0].length, "#990000");

  const calc = [
    ["Calculator Rule", "Meaning"],
    ["Yellow cells", "User input / assumptions only"],
    ["Grey cells", "Auto-filled market/history/alert data"],
    ["Green cells", "Calculated result/output fields"],
    ["Best function", "runOptimisedCalculatorSafe"],
    ["Audit", "createCalculatorOnboardingAuditSheet"]
  ];

  wizard.getRange(33, 1, calc.length, calc[0].length)
    .setValues(calc);

  styleWorkflowTable_(wizard, 33, 1, calc.length, calc[0].length, "#0b5394");

  wizard.getRange("A42:H42")
    .merge()
    .setValue("Best practice: Daily Safe for normal use. Stage 1–5 separately for major rebuilds. Check Dashboard Alert UI before making investment decisions.")
    .setBackground("#fff2cc")
    .setFontColor("#7f6000")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  wizard.getDataRange()
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setFontSize(10)
    .setVerticalAlignment("middle")
    .setWrap(true);

  wizard.setFrozenRows(2);
  wizard.setColumnWidth(1, 250);
  wizard.setColumnWidth(2, 340);
  wizard.setColumnWidth(3, 520);
  wizard.setColumnWidth(4, 110);
  wizard.setColumnWidth(5, 300);
  wizard.setTabColor("#0b5394");
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 122E — GENERIC WORKFLOW TABLE STYLE HELPER
// PURPOSE:
// Shared formatter for Home, Onboarding and Stage sheets.
// =====================================================

function styleWorkflowTable_(sheet, startRow, startCol, numRows, numCols, headerColour) {

  sheet.getRange(startRow, startCol, 1, numCols)
    .setBackground(headerColour)
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold")
    .setHorizontalAlignment("center");

  sheet.getRange(startRow + 1, startCol, Math.max(numRows - 1, 1), 1)
    .setBackground("#f3f6fa")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  sheet.getRange(startRow, startCol, numRows, numCols)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true)
    .setVerticalAlignment("middle")
    .setWrap(true);
}

// =====================================================
// DASHBOARD LAYOUT HELPERS
// PURPOSE:
// Used by dynamic dashboard layout, charts, and formatting.
// =====================================================

function findNextDashboardRow_(dash, startCol, endCol) {

  const lastRow = Math.max(dash.getLastRow(), 1);

  for (let r = lastRow; r >= 1; r--) {
    const values = dash.getRange(r, startCol, 1, endCol - startCol + 1).getValues()[0];
    if (values.some(v => v !== "" && v != null)) {
      return r + 3;
    }
  }

  return 3;
}

function findSectionDataStart_(dash, title, offsetRows) {

  const finder = dash.createTextFinder(title).matchEntireCell(true).findNext();

  if (!finder) return 0;

  return finder.getRow() + offsetRows + 1;
}

function styleDashboardSectionTitles_(dash) {

  const titles = [
    "Clean GoogleFinance Ranking Dashboard",
    "Clean Watchlist Dashboard Table",
    "Clean Portfolio Allocation Dashboard",
    "Portfolio Concentration Check",
    "Risk Grouping Dashboard",
    "Historical Share Price Snapshot",
    "Ticker Count + Data Coverage Summary"
  ];

  titles.forEach(title => {
    const cell = dash.createTextFinder(title).matchEntireCell(true).findNext();
    if (cell) {
      cell
        .setFontWeight("bold")
        .setFontSize(12)
        .setBackground("#d9e2f3")
        .setFontColor("#1f2933");
    }
  });
}

// =====================================================
// MODULE 15 — GENERAL HELPERS
// PURPOSE:
// Shared utility functions used across all modules.
// =====================================================

function getHeaders(sh) {
  return sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, sh.getLastColumn()).getValues()[0];
}

function colIndex(headers, headerName) {
  return headers.indexOf(headerName);
}

function getCol(headers, headerName) {
  const index = headers.indexOf(headerName);
  if (index === -1) throw new Error("Header not found: " + headerName);
  return index + 1;
}

function getValue(sh, headers, row, headerName) {
  const c = headers.indexOf(headerName) + 1;
  if (c <= 0) return "";
  return sh.getRange(row, c).getValue();
}

function setValue(sh, headers, row, headerName, value) {
  const c = headers.indexOf(headerName) + 1;
  if (c > 0) sh.getRange(row, c).setValue(value);
}

function setFormula(sh, headers, row, headerName, formula) {
  const c = headers.indexOf(headerName) + 1;
  if (c > 0) sh.getRange(row, c).setFormula(formula);
}

function setCellByIndex(sh, row, zeroBasedCol, value) {
  if (zeroBasedCol >= 0) {
    sh.getRange(row, zeroBasedCol + 1).setValue(value);
  }
}

function num(v) {
  if (v === "" || v == null || isNaN(v)) return 0;
  return Number(v);
}

function safeDiv(a, b) {
  if (a === "" || b === "" || a == null || b == null || b === 0) return "";
  return a / b;
}

function formatCleanMetricColumns(input) {
  const headers = getHeaders(input);
  const lastRow = Math.max(input.getLastRow() - 1, 1);

  const impliedSharesCol = colIndex(headers, "Implied Shares Outstanding");
  const scoreCol = colIndex(headers, "GoogleFinance Score");

  if (impliedSharesCol >= 0) {
    input.getRange(2, impliedSharesCol + 1, lastRow, 1).setNumberFormat("#,##0");
  }

  if (scoreCol >= 0) {
    input.getRange(2, scoreCol + 1, lastRow, 1).setNumberFormat("0");
  }

  [
    "Earnings Yield %",
    "Upside to 52W High %",
    "Downside to 52W Low %",
    "52W Price Position %"
  ].forEach(header => {
    const c = colIndex(headers, header);
    if (c >= 0) {
      input.getRange(2, c + 1, lastRow, 1).setNumberFormat("0.00%");
    }
  });
}



// =====================================================
// MODULE 32 — DYNAMIC DASHBOARD CHART ENGINE
// PURPOSE:
// Create adaptive dashboard charts using dynamic ranges.
// Prevents charts from breaking when table sizes change.
// =====================================================

function createDashboardVisualCharts() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const dash = ss.getSheetByName(DASHBOARD_SHEET_NAME);

  if (!dash) {
    throw new Error("Dashboard sheet not found.");
  }

  // Remove old charts
  dash.getCharts().forEach(chart => dash.removeChart(chart));

  // DETECT TABLE SIZES
  const rankingStartRow = 13;
  const portfolioStartRow = 78;
  const riskStartRow = 103;

  const rankingRows = detectTableLength(dash, rankingStartRow, 2);
  const portfolioRows = detectTableLength(dash, portfolioStartRow, 1);
  const riskRows = detectTableLength(dash, riskStartRow, 1);

  // CHART 1 — SCORE RANKING
  if (rankingRows > 1) {

    const scoreChart = dash.newChart()
      .setChartType(Charts.ChartType.BAR)
      .addRange(dash.getRange(rankingStartRow, 2, rankingRows, 1))
      .addRange(dash.getRange(rankingStartRow, 11, rankingRows, 1))
      .setPosition(2, 13, 0, 0)
      .setOption("title", "GoogleFinance Score Ranking")
      .setOption("legend", { position: "none" })
      .setOption("height", 350)
      .setOption("width", 600)
      .build();

    dash.insertChart(scoreChart);
  }

  // CHART 2 — PORTFOLIO ALLOCATION
  if (portfolioRows > 1) {

    const allocationChart = dash.newChart()
      .setChartType(Charts.ChartType.PIE)
      .addRange(dash.getRange(portfolioStartRow, 1, portfolioRows, 1))
      .addRange(dash.getRange(portfolioStartRow, 7, portfolioRows, 1))
      .setPosition(20, 13, 0, 0)
      .setOption("title", "Suggested Portfolio Allocation")
      .setOption("height", 350)
      .setOption("width", 600)
      .build();

    dash.insertChart(allocationChart);
  }

  // CHART 3 — RISK GROUPING
  if (riskRows > 1) {

    const riskChart = dash.newChart()
      .setChartType(Charts.ChartType.COLUMN)
      .addRange(dash.getRange(riskStartRow, 1, riskRows, 1))
      .addRange(dash.getRange(riskStartRow, 3, riskRows, 1))
      .setPosition(38, 13, 0, 0)
      .setOption("title", "Portfolio Allocation by Risk Group")
      .setOption("legend", { position: "none" })
      .setOption("height", 350)
      .setOption("width", 600)
      .build();

    dash.insertChart(riskChart);
  }

  // CHART 4 — EARNINGS YIELD VS UPSIDE
  if (rankingRows > 1) {

    const scatterChart = dash.newChart()
      .setChartType(Charts.ChartType.SCATTER)
      .addRange(dash.getRange(rankingStartRow, 6, rankingRows, 1))
      .addRange(dash.getRange(rankingStartRow, 7, rankingRows, 1))
      .setPosition(56, 13, 0, 0)
      .setOption("title", "Earnings Yield vs 52W Upside")
      .setOption("hAxis", { title: "Earnings Yield %" })
      .setOption("vAxis", { title: "Upside to 52W High %" })
      .setOption("height", 350)
      .setOption("width", 600)
      .build();

    dash.insertChart(scatterChart);
  }
}


// =====================================================
// MODULE 32 HELPERS
// PURPOSE:
// Detect dynamic dashboard table lengths.
// =====================================================

function detectTableLength(sheet, startRow, col) {

  let row = startRow;
  let count = 0;

  while (true) {

    const value = sheet.getRange(row, col).getValue();

    if (value === "" || value == null) {
      break;
    }

    count++;
    row++;
  }

  return count;
}

// MODULE 100J — QUIET MASTER UI POLISH FOR FULL RUNNER
// PURPOSE:
// Same cleanup steps without user alert; better for automation.
// =====================================================

function runMasterUiPolishCleanupQuiet() {

  // =====================================================
  // OPTIMISED QUIET MASTER POLISH — v44
  // PURPOSE:
  // Non-destructive final polish for full runner.
  // IMPORTANT:
  // This version intentionally does NOT call ensureCoreUiSheetsExist_()
  // because that function recreates sheets such as Calculator,
  // Executive Charts, and Management View, which can wipe advanced
  // UI elements already built earlier in the run.
  // =====================================================

  organiseWorkbookSheetOrder_();
  applyWorkbookTabColours_();
  cleanupDuplicateCharts_();
  applyMasterThemeConsistency_();
  createWorkbookHealthCheckSheet_();

  if (typeof createWorkbookHomePage === "function") {
    createWorkbookHomePage();
  }

  if (typeof createDashboardControlPanel === "function") {
    createDashboardControlPanel();
  }

  addMasterUiPolishNoteToControlPanel();

  if (typeof refreshControlPanelUiEffects === "function") {
    refreshControlPanelUiEffects();
  }

  if (typeof refreshBrandingPresetsUiEffects === "function") {
    refreshBrandingPresetsUiEffects();
  }
}




// =====================================================
// MODULE 116 — STATIC SCRIPT DUPLICATE FUNCTION REPORT
// PURPOSE:
// Records duplicate function names detected during script assembly.
// Apps Script uses the last duplicate definition, so duplicates
// should be reviewed if unexpected.
// =====================================================

function createStaticDuplicateFunctionReport() {

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

  let sheet = ss.getSheetByName("Static Function Duplicate Report");
  if (!sheet) sheet = ss.insertSheet("Static Function Duplicate Report");

  sheet.clear();

  const duplicates = [];

  const rows = [["Duplicate Function Name", "Notes"]];

  if (duplicates.length === 0) {
    rows.push(["None detected during assembly", "OK"]);
  } else {
    duplicates.forEach(name => {
      rows.push([name, "Review if this duplicate is intentional. Apps Script uses the last definition."]);
    });
  }

  sheet.getRange(1, 1, rows.length, 2).setValues(rows);
  sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 2)
    .setBackground("#1f2933")
    .setFontColor("#ffffff")
    .setFontWeight("bold");

  sheet.getRange(1, 1, rows.length, 2)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true)
    .setFontFamily("Arial")
    .setWrap(true);

  sheet.setColumnWidth(1, 300);
  sheet.setColumnWidth(2, 520);
  sheet.setFrozenRows(1);
}
